[I,1,i_I,1,iii]	vīta āvīta viṣāṇasya pakṣa tāvana sevinaḥ pravādāḥ sāṃkhya kariṇaḥ sallakīṣaṃḍa bhaṅgurāḥ ṛṣaye paramāya arka marīci sama tejase saṃsāra gahanamadhva anta sūryāya gurave namaḥ tattvam jijñāsamānāya viprāya asuraye muniḥ tat uvāca mahat tantram duḥkha traya nivṛttaye na tasya adhigamaḥ śakyaḥ kartum varṣa śataiḥ api bhūyas tvāt iti saṃcintya munibhiḥ sūkṣma buddhibhiḥ granthena alpena saṃkṣipya tadā ārṣam anuśāsanam nibaddham amala prajñaiḥ śiṣyāṇām hita kāmyayā 
[I,2,i_I,2,ii]	pratipakṣāḥ punar tasya puruṣa īśa aṇu vādinaḥ vaināśikāḥ prākṛtikāḥ vikāra puruṣāḥ tathā teṣām icchā vighāta artham ācāryaiḥ sūkṣma buddhibhiḥ racitāḥ sveṣu tantreṣu viṣamāḥ tarka gahvarāḥ śiṣyaiḥ duravagāhāḥ te tattva artha bhrānta buddhibhiḥ tasmāt īśvara kṛṣṇena saṃkṣipta artham idam kṛtam saptati ākhyam prakaraṇam sakalam śāstram eva vā yasmāt sarva padārthānām iha vyākhyā kariṣyate 
[I,3,i]	pradhāna astitvam eka tvam arthavat tvam atha anya tā pārārthyañca tathā anaikyam viyogaḥ yogaḥ eva ca śeṣa vṛttiḥ akartṛ tvam cūlikā arthāḥ smṛtāḥ daśa viparyayaḥ pañcavidhaḥ tathā uktāḥ nava tuṣṭayaḥ karaṇānām asāmarthyam aṣṭāviṃśatidhā matam iti ṣaṣṭiḥ padārthānām aṣṭābhiḥ saha siddhibhiḥ yathākramam lakṣaṇataḥ kārtsnyena iha abhidhāsyate tasmāt atas śāstram idam alam nānātva siddhaye 
[I,4,i_I,5,ii]	alpa grantham analpa artham sarvaiḥ tantra guṇaiḥ yutam pāramarṣasya tantrasya bimbam ādarśa gam yathā tasya vyākhyām kariṣyāmi yathānyāya upapattaye kāruṇyāt api ayuktām tām pratigṛhṇantu sūrayaḥ āha kariṣyati bhavān vyākhyām idam tu ādau upanyastam sarvaiḥ tantra guṇaiḥ yutam idam tantram iti ke tantra guṇāḥ kiyantaḥ vā iti 
[I,5,iii_I,6,iv]	ucyate sūtra pramāṇa avayava upapattiḥ anyūna tā saṃśaya nirṇaya uktiḥ uddeśa nirdeśam anukramaḥ ca saṃjñā upadeśau iha tantra sampad sūtrāṇi ca pramāṇāni ca avayavāḥ ca sūtra pramāṇa avayavāḥ teṣām upapattiḥ sūtra pramāṇa avayava upapattiḥ upapattiḥ sambhavaḥ iti anarthāntaram ananyaḥ arthaḥ anartha antaram upapatti śabdaḥ pratyekam parisamāpyate sūtra upapattiḥ ityādi āha lakṣaṇa upeta sūtra upapattiḥ iti vaktavyam itarathāḥ hi alakṣaṇa upetasya api sūtrasya tantra aṅga bhāvaḥ syāt iti ucyate na na antarīyaka tvāt na hi antareṇa lakṣaṇa upeta tvam sūtra tvam atas na vaktavyam etat iti āha atha sūtram iti kasmāt 
[I,6,v]	ucyate sūcanāt sūtram sūcayati tān tān artha viśeṣān iti sūtram tat yathā kāraṇam asti avyaktam bhedānām parimāṇāt iti atra pratijñā hetū kaṇṭha uktau tayoḥ upayogi dṛṣṭāntam sādhya siddhaye samartham iti kṛtvā mūla śakala ādayaḥ atra antaranabhihitāḥ api etasmāt avasīyante athavā bhikṣoḥ upasaṃhṛta bahiṣkaraṇa antaḥkaraṇasya teṣu teṣu atīndriyeṣu api pradhāna ādiṣu artheṣu buddhim sūcayati iti sūtram athavā saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ iti sūtram tat yathā alpa akṣaram asandigdham sāravat viśvatomukham astobhamanavadyam ca sūtram sūtra vidaḥ viduḥ 
[I,7,i_I,8,ii]	astobhama punaruktam iti arthaḥ tathā laghūni sūcita arthāni su alpa akṣara padāni ca sarvatas sāra bhūtāni sūtrāṇi āhuḥ manīṣiṇaḥ pramāṇāni ca pratyakṣa ādīni tāni uttaratra vakṣyati dṛṣṭam anumānam āpta vacanam ca prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭam ityādi avayavāḥ punar jijñāsā ādayaḥ pratijña ādayaḥ ca tatra jijñāsā ādayaḥ vyākhyā aṅgam pratijña ādayaḥ para pratyāyana aṅgam tān uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ 
[I,8,iii_I,8,v]	āha avayavān abhidhānam upadeśāt na hi tathā pratyakṣa ādīni pramāṇāni upadiṣṭāni tathā avayavāḥ upadiṣṭāḥ tasmāt avayava upapattiḥ iti etat asat bhāṣya kāra prāmāṇyāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi api sūtra kāreṇa avayava upadeśaḥ na kṛtaḥ tathā api bhāṣya kārāḥ kecid eṣām saṃgraham cakruḥ te ca naḥ pramāṇam tasmāt yukatam avayava upapattiḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt utsūtra tvāt na hi utsūtram vyācakṣāṇāḥ bhāṣya kārāḥ pramāṇam bhavanti tathā ca etat utsūtritam iti 
[I,9,i]	ucyate na liṅgāt na etat yuktam anupadeśāt na santi jijñāsā ādayaḥ kintarhi anupadiṣṭam api eṣām astitvam liṅgāt pratipadyāmahe yat ayam ācāryaḥ duḥkha traya abhighātāt jijñāsā tad apaghātake hetau iti jijñāsā prayojanam ācaṣṭe kāraṇam asti avyaktam iti pratijñām karoti bhedānām parimāṇāt iti hetum upadiśati naṭa vat vyavatiṣṭhate liṅgam iti dṛṣṭāntam dyotayati kṣīrasya yathā tathā pravṛttiḥ pradhānastyā iti upasaṃharati tasmāt trividham karaṇam dvārī iti nigamayati na ca anabhipretaiḥ ācāryāṇām śāstre vyavahāraḥ lakṣyate tena vayam liṅgāt pratipadyāmahe santi jijñāsā ādayaḥ avayavāḥ śāstre iti 
[I,10,i_I,10,ii]	āha satām anupadeśe prayojana vacanam evam ced manyase santi jijñāsā ādayaḥ avayavāḥ śāstre teṣām anupadeśe prayojanam vaktavyam amuṣmāt hetoḥ ācāryeṇa na upadiśyante santi ca te iti ucyate pramāṇa antarbhāvāt pramāṇeṣu antarbhāvaḥ eṣām iti ayam upadiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ asmābhiḥ anumāna aṅgam hi jijñāsā ādayaḥ tasmāt tad antarbhūtāḥ te iti na pṛthak upadiśyante kiñca tantra antara ukteḥ tantra antareṣu hi vindhya vāsi prabhṛtiḥ ācāryaiḥ upadiṣṭāḥ pramāṇam ca naḥ te ācāryāḥ iti atas ca anupadeśaḥ jijñāsā ādīnām iti 
[I,11,i]	āha na pramāṇa anupadeśa prasaṃgāt yadi ca tantra antara upadeśāt eva avayavānām anupadeśaḥ pratyakṣa ādīni api ca tantra antareṣu upadiśyante śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam sambandhāt ekasmāt śeṣa siddhiḥ anumānam yaḥ yatra abhiyuktaḥ karmaṇi ca āduṣṭassa tatra āptaḥ tasya upadeśaḥ āpta vacanam iti teṣām api anupadeśa prasaṅgaḥ atha sati tantra antara upadeśe pramāṇāni upadiśyante na avayavāḥ iti nanu etat icchā mātram iti 
[I,12,i^1]	ucyate pūrvaḥ eva tarhi parihāraḥ astu athavā punar astu tantra antara ukteḥ iti ayam api parihāraḥ yat tu uktam pramāṇa anupadeśa prasaṅgaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt prayojanavatām upadeśasya adoṣa tvāt anupadeśaḥ hi prayojanavataḥ ca udyate iti yuktam etat upadeśam eva tu sa doṣaḥ iti kṛtvā kaḥ pratyācakṣīta tasmāt na kiñcid etat kiñca anyat pradhāna upadeśe guṇa bhūta antarbhāva siddheḥ tat yathā takṣṇu hi caitraḥ iti ukte yāvadbhiḥ sādhana viśeṣaiḥ vinā takṣaṇam na upapadyate sarvāḥ tān caitraḥ upādatte tathā pratyakṣa ādiṣu pramāṇeṣu upadiṣṭeṣu yaiḥ eṣām avinābhāvaḥ sarvāṇi tāni upādāsyāmahe kiñca anyāt anyatra api tad anuṣṭhānāt na kevalam iha anyatra api ayam ācāryaḥ pradhānām eva upadeśam karoti tad aṅga bhūtāḥ tu tad upadeśāt eva pratīyante tat yathā kāraṇam asti avyaktam bhedānām parimāṇāt iti 
[I,12,i^2]	itarathāḥ hi dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt asādhanam etat syāt paśyati tu ācāryaḥ na adṛṣṭāntam sādhanam sādhyam āpnoti iti kṛtvā pratipādakāḥ pratipādana kāle tantra antara upadiṣṭān api mūla śakala ādīn ākṣepsyanti iti kiñca anyat anumāne bhūta vat upadeśāt atas ca etat evam yat ayam ācāryaḥ trividham anumānam ākhyātam iti bravīti katham kṛtvā jñāpakam ākhyātasya hi pratyāmnāye bhūta vācinā śabdena upadeśaḥ bhavati na ca anena pūrvam trividham anumānam ākhyātam ākhyātam iti ced na tat ākhyātam kvacid iti śakyam pratipādayitum saḥ ayam anākhyāya api yat bhūta vācinam śabdam upādatte tat jñāpayati ācāryaḥ tantra antara klṛptānām api iha sanniveśaḥ aṅgīkriyate kim etasya jñāpane prayojanam tantra antara upadiṣṭaḥ api karma yonīnām prāṇa bheda ādīnām ca lakṣaṇa upadeśa ssaṃgṛhītaḥ bhavati iti siddham tantra antara upadeśāt avayavān upadeśaḥ tasmāt sūktam eva avayava upapattiḥ iti 
[I,15,i_I,15,ii]	anyūna tā padārtha kārtsnyam aśeṣa tānyūnata iti abhidhīyate padārthāḥ ca daśa cūlikā arthāḥ paṃcāśat pratyayāḥ tatra astitvam eka tvam paṃcabhiḥ vītaiḥ siddham arthavat tvam kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pārārthyam saṃhatya kāriṇām para artha tvāt atas eva anya tvam cetanā śakteḥ guṇa trayāt janma maraṇa karaṇānām iti evamādibhiḥ puruṣa bahu tvam puruṣasya darśana arthaḥ iti saṃyogaḥ prāpte śarīra bhede iti viyogaḥ samyak jñāna adhigamāt iti śeṣa vṛttiḥ tasmāt ca viparyāsāt iti puruṣasya akartṛ tvam iti ete daśa cūlikā arthāḥ pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ bhavanti aśaktiḥ ca karaṇa vaikalyāt aṣṭāviṃśati bhedā tuṣṭiḥ navadhā aṣṭadhā siddhiḥ iti pañcāśat pratyayāḥ sā eṣā ṣaṣṭiḥ padārthānām tad upapattiḥ anyūna tā 
[I,16,i]	saṃśaya nirṇaya uktiḥ saṃśayaḥ ca nirṇayaḥ ca tau saṃśaya nirṇayau tayorukti ssaṃśaya nirṇaya uktiḥ sāmānya abhidhānam saṃśayaḥ tat yathā mahat ādi tat ca kāryam prakṛti virūpam sarūpam ca iti ukte saṃśayaḥ bhavati kena dharmeṇa kāryam prakṛti virūpam kena vā sarūpam iti viśeṣa abhidhānam nirṇayaḥ sa ca dvividhaḥ śabdataḥ arthataḥ ca śabdaḥ tāvat yathā hetumat ādibhiḥ kāryam prakṛti virūpam traiguṇya ādibhiḥ prakṛti sarūpam iti arthataḥ tat yathā tebhyaḥ bhūtāni pañca pañcabhyaḥ ete smṛtāḥ viśeṣāḥ kim kāraṇam yasmāt śāntāḥ ghorāḥ ca mūḍhāḥ ca aśānta ghora mūḍha tvāt tanmātrāṇi aviśeṣāḥ 
[I,17,i_I,17,ii]	uddeśa nirdeśam uddeśaḥ ca nirdeśaḥ ca uddeśa nirdeśam sarvaḥ dvandvaḥ vibhāṣaya eka vat bhavati iti dvandva eka vat bhāvaḥ saṅkṣepa vacanam uddeśaḥ tat yathā eṣa pratyaya sargaḥ viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭi siddhi ākhyaḥ vistara vacanam nirdeśaḥ tat yathā pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ bhavanti bhedaḥ tamasaḥ aṣṭavidhaḥ ityādiḥ anukramaḥ ca padārthānām ānupūrvyā sanniveśa upadeśaḥ anukramaḥ tat yathā prakṛteḥ mahān tatas ahaṃkāraḥ tasmāt gaṇaḥ ca ṣoḍaśakaḥ iti antena 
[I,17,iii]	saṃjñā upadeśau saṃjñi pratyāyana arthaḥ śabdaḥ saṃjñā sā ca dvividhā artha nibandhanā svarūpa nibandhanā ca tatra artha nibandhana artha vaśena artha kriyā apekṣā jāti ādi artha svarūpa antarbhāvī yathārthaḥ tathābhūtam eva saṃjñinam pratyāyati tat yathā pācakaḥ lāvakaḥ iti svarūpa nibandhanā punar saṃjñi pratyāyana upāya mātram sva rūpa mātra upakāriṇī vinā avayava artham samaya vaśāt atathābhūtam api saṃjñinam pratyāyati tat yathā gajakarṇaḥ aśvakarṇaḥ iti prayatnataḥ bhagavataḥ parama ṛṣeḥ ārṣeṇa jñānena sarva tattvānām svarūpam upalabhya saṃjñām vidadhataḥ na asti svarūpa nibandhanaḥ śabdaḥ tat yathā pradhīyante atra vikārāḥ iti pradhānam puri śetaḥ iti puruṣaḥ ityādi tad mata anusāriṇām api ācāryāṇām tābhiḥ eva saṃvyavahārāt na asti apūrva saṃjñā vidhānam pratyādaraḥ 
[I,19,i_I,19,iii]	upadeśaḥ itikartavya tā phala samākhyānam upadeśaḥ tat yathā evam tattva abhayasān nā asmi na me na aham iti apariśeṣam aviparyayāt viśuddham kevalam utpadyate jñānam ete sūtra upapatti ādayaḥ tantra guṇāḥ iti karaṇam prakāra artham evamprakārāḥ anye api draṣṭavyāḥ tat yathā utsargaḥ apavādaḥ atideśaḥ ityādiḥ tatra utsargaḥ prakṛti virūpam vyaktam sarūpam ca iti apavādaḥ tathā tad viparītaḥ iti utsargaḥ tathā ca pumān iti apavādaḥ sāmānyam acetanam prasava dharmi vyaktam tathā pradhānam iti atideśaḥ iti evam anyāḥ api tantra yuktayaḥ śakyāḥ iha pradarśayitum atiprasaṅgaḥ tu prakṛtam tirodadhāti iti nivartyate siddham tantra yuktīnām sambandha upapatteḥ tantram idam iti 
[I,20,i]	kiñca tantra antara avirodhāt yadi khalvapi idam api prakaraṇam syāt tantra antare pātañjala pañca adhikaraṇa vārṣa gaṇa prabhṛtīnām anyatamasya śeṣa bhūtam syāt taiḥ ca api avirodhaḥ tatra tatra iti vakṣyāmaḥ pūrva tantra śeṣa bhāvāt iti ced tulyam etāni api pūrva tantra śeṣa bhūtāni teṣām api prakaraṇa tva prasaṅgaḥ atha matam sakala padārtha saṃgrahāt tantra antarāṇi etāni evam iha api sakala padārtha saṃgrahāt tantra antara tvam abhyupagantavyam tasmāt yuktam etat tantram idam iti upodghātaḥ 
[I,22,i_I,22,iv]	āha kiṃguṇa viśiṣṭāya śiṣyāya punar idam tantram vyākhyeyam iti ucyate jijñāsave matimate mīmāṃsa kāya arthine abhyupagatāya śiṣyāya vyākhyeyam śāstram kasmāt parama ṛṣi prāmāṇyāt yasmāt bhagavān viśva agrajaḥ parama ṛṣiḥ bhagavat āsureḥ jijñāsām upalabhya uttara guṇa viśeṣa sampadam ca vyākhyātavān rajaḥ eva duḥkham tad nirākariṣṇoḥ vivekaḥ ayam sattvāt sattvam ca asmān nānā iti evamādinā vacana pratipādyaḥ ayam arthaḥ mahadbhiḥ ca uktaḥ tasmāt rajaḥ duḥkha upaghāta upaghātaka jijñāsoḥ sattvāt dharma ādi kuśala mūla vipāka utpitsoḥ duḥkha traya nivṛttayaḥ idam śāstram pravṛttam tad arthāt pariṇamate śiṣyasya iti katham nāma śiṣyasya niḥśreyasena yogaḥ syāt iti evam artham idam vyākhyānam kriyate iti 
[I,24,i_I,24,iii]	āha yat uktam jijñāsave vyākhyānam kartavyam iti tatra kutas punar iyam jijñāsā kasmin vā arthe bhavati iti ucyate yat tāvat uktam kutas punar iyam jijñāsā bhavati iti atra brūmaḥ duḥkha traya abhighātāt jijñāsā duḥkham rajaḥ iti anarthāntaram duḥkhayati iti duḥkham bhavati iti trayam iti saṃkhyā padam sarva dravya viṣayam duḥkha śabdena viśiṣyate prādhānyāt ca vyatirikta buddhyā gṛhyamāṇam sambandhi tvāt ādhārasya bheda nibandhanāyāḥ ṣaṣṭhyā nimittattvam pratipadyate duḥkhānām trayam duḥkha trayam 
[I,24,iv_I,25,iii]	abhihanyate anena iti abhighātaḥ kaḥ punar ayam abhighātaḥ nāma ucyate yaḥ asau upari ukta duḥkha trayeṇa antaḥkaraṇena cetanā śakteḥ abhisambandhaḥ tasmāt duḥkha traya abhighātāt jijñāsā yat uktam kasmin arthe bhavati iti tatra āha tad apaghātake hetau apahanti iti apaghātakaḥ tasya apaghātakaḥ tad apaghātakaḥ 
[I,25,iv_I,25,v]	āha tad apaghātake iti samāsa anupapattiḥ pratiṣedhāt kartari yau tṛjakau tābhyām saha ṣaṣṭhī na samasyate tasmāt tasya apaghātakaḥ iti vaktavyam ucyate na śāstre darśanāt tad prayojakaḥ hetuḥ ca iti śāstre dṛṣṭaḥ prayogaḥ pada kāraḥ ca āha jātivācaka tvāt tathā kadācid guṇaḥ guṇa viśeṣaḥ bhavati kadācid guṇinā guṇaḥ viśiṣyate iti cūrṇikārasya prayogaḥ tasmadanavadyam etat 
[I,26,i_I,26,ii]	ayam tu piṇḍa arthaḥ trividhena duḥkhena abhihataḥ brāhmaṇaḥ tad apaghātakam hetum jijñāsate kaḥ nāma asau hetuḥ syāt yaḥ duḥkha trayam abhihanyāt iti āha duḥkha śabdā vacanam ādau amaṅgala artha tvāt maṅgala ādīni hi śāstrāṇi prathante vīra puruṣāṇi ca bhavanti adhyetāraḥ ca maṃgalena abhihata saṃskārāḥ śāstra arthānāsu pratipadyante duḥkham iti ayam ca amaṅgala arthaḥ śabdaḥ tasmāt na ārabdhavyaḥ śāstra ādau iti 
[I,27,i^1]	ucyate na vākyasya arthe prayogāt padasya anarthakyādamaṅgala artha tva anupapattiḥ vākyam artha pratyāyana artham prayujyate viśiṣṭa artha abhidhānāt na padam tathā hi padārtha vyatirekeṇa viśiṣṭaḥ eva vākya arthaḥ pratīyate kevalam tu padam sāmānya arthāt apracyutam viśiṣṭa artha abhidhānā samartham atas eva na vivakṣita artha pratyāyana yogyatayā upādīyate tat yathā devadattā iti ayam śabdaḥ kartṛ vācaka tvena upāttaḥ sarva kriyā viṣaya tvāt na antareṇa karma kriyā śabdau viśiṣṭa arthaḥ pratīyate tathā gām iti karma sarva kriyā kartṛ abhidhāna nimitta tvāt tathā abhyāja iti kriyā sarva karma kartṛ viṣaya tvāt yadā tu devadatta gām abhyāja śuklām iti ucyate tadā devadattena go śabdena karma antarebhyaḥ vicchidya sva ātmani avasthāpyate 
[I,27,i^2]	kriyā ca go śabdaḥ ca sarva kartṛbhyaḥ devadatta karma tayā vyavasthāpyate kartṛ karmaṇī ca abhyāji kriyāyāḥ sādhana bhāvena eva niyamyete śukla śabdaḥ go śabdaḥ ca go śabdam sarva guṇa viṣayam ādheya antarebhyaḥ vyavacchedya sva ātmanaḥ ādhāra tve niyamya tat viṣaya tām pratipādayati iti anena krameṇa viśiṣṭaḥ vākya arthaḥ kevala anāntu padānām sāmānya arthāt pracyutānām viśeṣān abhidhānāt ānarthakyam āha ca pṛthak niviṣṭa tattvānām pṛthak artha abhipātinām indriyāṇām yathā kāryam ṛte dehāt na labhyate tathā eva sarva śabdānām pṛthak artha abhidhāyinām vākyebhyaḥ pravibhaktānām arthavat tā na labhyate iti
[I,27,ii]	evam sati kutas ayam niścaya pratilambhaḥ yad duḥkha śabdaḥ ayam amaṅgala arthaḥ yāvatā sandihyate eva ayam kim sva artha pratipatti artham upāttaḥ atha heya tvāya iti vākyasya tu maṅgala artha tvam duḥkha prahāṇa artham upādānāt yat hi duḥkha prahāṇa artham vākyam upādīyate tad maṅgala artham dṛṣṭam tat yathā vyādhi apagamaḥ syāt alakṣmīḥ mā bhūt iti duḥkha prahāṇa artham ca idam vākyam upāttam tasmāt maṅgala artham idam tatra yat uktam duḥkha śabdā vacanam ādau amaṅgala artha tvāt iti etat ayuktam 
[I,29,i_I,30,iii]	āha traya grahaṇa ānarthakyam guṇa eka tvāt duḥkham rajaḥ iti pratipannaḥ bhavān tat ca ekam śāstre paṭhyate tasmāt traya grahaṇam anarthakam iti nimitta bhedāt bheda upacāraḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi api ekam duḥkham tathā api nimittānām adhyātma adhibhūta adhidaiva lakṣaṇānām bhedāt asya bheda upacāraḥ kariṣyate iti tat ca na evam kasmāt 
[I,30,iv]	nimitta ānantyena guṇa ānantya prasaṅgāt ādhyātmikam hi dvividham śārīram mānasam ca śārīram tāvat vāta pitta śleṣmaṇām vaiṣamya nimittam tathā mānasam kāma krodha lobha moha viṣāda bhaya īrṣyā asūyā rati aviśeṣa darśana nimittam ādhibhautikam ca manuṣya paśu mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa sthāvara nimittam ādhidaivikam śīta uṣṇa vāta varṣa aśanyavaśyāya āveśa nimittam tatra nimitta bhedāt tritva pragijñasya guṇa ānantya prasaṅgaḥ sa ca na iṣṭaḥ tasmāt na nimitta bhedāt tri tvam 
[I,31,i]	ucyate yat uktam rajasaḥ eka tvāt tritva anupapattiḥ tasya nimitta bhedāt tritva upacāraḥ iti satyam etat yat tu uktam nimitta ān antyena guṇa ānantya prasaṅgaḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt bhede api sati varṇa saṃkhyā vat dvi avasthāna upapatteḥ tat yathā catvāraḥ varṇāḥ iti asyāḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ sati paippalādādi bhede teṣām brāhmaṇa tva ādi vyatireka abhāvāt na saṃkhyā antara hetu tvam no khalu api varṇa avyatirekāt eka tvam bhavati evam trīṇi duḥkhāni iti asyāḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ sati śarīra ādi bhede teṣām ādhyātmika ādi vyatireka asambhavāt na saṅkhyā antara hetu tvam no khalu api duḥkha avyatirekāt eka tvam bhavitum arhati kiñca anyat nimitta bhedāt bheda upacāraḥ iti bhavān eva pratipannaḥ na ca upacāraḥ parama arthaḥ iti alam asthāne yatnena 
[I,32,i^1]	āha abhighātāt jijñāsāyām ati prasaṅgaḥ sarveṣām sambhavāt yathā sureḥ duḥkha traya abhighātāt jijñāsā bhavati iti etat iṣṭam tena sarveṣām abhighātaḥ asti iti sarveṣām jijñāsā prasaṅgaḥ atha matam duḥkha abhighāte kasyacid jijñāsā bhavati kasyacid na iti nanu evam icchā mātram prāc prasaṅgāt ca prāk api āsureḥ jijñāsāyāḥ duḥkha traya abhighātaḥ na ca asya ātyantike hetau jijñāsā babhūva tena kim prāptam paścāt asya yatas babhūva tat vaktavyam yathā anyatra brahmaṇaḥ abhyāsa nimittāt adharma kṣayāt pūrva dharma anugrahāt ca vividiṣā tathā anyeṣām kuśala mūla abhyāsa paripākāt na ca apadiṣṭam atas laghu uktam etat kiñca anyat tad apaghātāt ca anirmokṣaḥ akṛtsna tvāt mokṣaḥ hi kāmarūpārūpya dhātu traya āt iṣyate daiva mānuṣya tiryagyoni trayāt vā eka deśaḥ ca saṃsārasya duḥkha trayam tasmāt prayojanam api ayuktam 
[I,32,i^2]	kiñca nimitta antara sadbhāvāt divya kāma dhyāna sukha anapekṣasya api vividiṣā sambhavati na kevalam tāpa udvignasya api tasmāt nimittam api ayuktam kiñca anyat ubhayathā ca asambhavāt parikalpyamānā khalu api iyam jijñāsā puruṣasya vā syāt guṇānām vā kiṃca atas tat na tāvat puruṣasya sambhavati kasmāt nairguṇya abhyupagamāt icchā dveṣa prayatna sukha duḥkha dharma adharma jñāna saṃskārāṇām ātma guṇa tvam na bhavadbhiḥ abhyupagamyate na guṇānām ācetanyāt na hi acetanā ghaṭa ādayaḥ hita ahita prāpti parihāram jijñāsamānā dṛśyate na ca cetanā bhavatām guṇāḥ sāmānyam acetanam prasava dharmi pradhānam iti vakṣyamāṇa vacanāt kiṃca anyat tattva antara anupapatteḥ na ca guṇa puruṣa vyatiriktam vastutas tattva antaram asti yasya jijñāsā parikalpyamānā parikalpyeta tasmāt anupapannā jijñāsā 
[I,35,i^1]	ucyate yat uktam abhighātāt jijñāsāyām ati prasaṅgaḥ sarveṣām tad sambhavāt iti atra brūmaḥ na abhighāta tvena apratipatteḥ yadi api aviśiṣṭaḥ abhighātaḥ tathā api sarve na enam abhighāta tvena pratipadyante tathā hi satsu ādhyātmika ādi duḥkheṣu arjana rakṣaṇa kṣaya saṃga hiṃsāsu ca prīti abhiṣvaṅgāt eṣām na viṣayeṣu udvega apadveṣau na ca viṣaya parityāgaḥ bhavati tasmāt na aviśiṣṭaḥ abhighātaḥ viśeṣe abhighāta buddheḥ nimitta abhidhānam iti ced atha api syādya iyam asati viśeṣe sarva prāṇabhṛtām āsureḥ eva bhagavataḥ duḥkha traya abhighāta buddhiḥ bhavati na punar anyeṣām iti atra nimittam abhidhānīyam na hi antareṇa nimittam asau viśeṣaḥ avasthāpayitum śakyate iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt praśnāsambandhāt 
[I,35,i^2]	kutas jijñāsā bhavati iti evam ca udakena pūrvam akāri praśnaḥ tasyāḥ ca sākṣāt kāraṇam abhighātaḥ kāraṇa antarāṇām anabhidhāna ādityasya eva nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ yat tu khalu idānīm kāraṇa kāraṇam api pṛcchyate tad anavasthā prasaṅga bhayāt na ucyate atha nirbandhaḥ kriyate tena pūrava dharma anugrahasya kuśala mūla abhyāsa paripākasya kāraṇa kāraṇa tvam asmābhiḥ na pratiṣidhyate iti tat eva kim na gṛhyate etena prāc prasaṅgaḥ pratyuktaḥ yat tu uktam tad abhighāte ca anirmokṣaḥ akṛtsna tvāt iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt śāstra artha an avabodhāt aṣṭa vikalpaḥ daivaḥ tairyagyoniḥ ca pañcadhā bhavati mānuṣyaḥ ca ekavidhaḥ iti etāvān asmākam saṃsāraḥ na tu tad vyatiriktāḥ kāmarūpa ārūpya dhātavaḥ kvacid api siddhāḥ caturdaśavidhe ca saṃsāre yā sukha mātrā sā duḥkha bhūyaḥ tvāt tad śabda vācyā bhavati iti tathā ca uktam 
[I,36,i_I,36,ii]	atra janma jarā maraṇa kṛtam duḥkham prāpnoti cetanaḥ puruṣaḥ liṅgasya avinivṛtteḥ tasmāt duḥkham samāsena dṛśyate ca loke bhūyasā grahaṇam tat yathā āmravanam iti tasmāt kṛtsna vikalpa pratiṣedhaḥ ayam yat punar etat uktam divya kāma dhyāna sukha anapekṣasya api vividiṣā sambhavāt nimittam ayuktam iti tat api anupapannam kasmāt uttaratra pratiṣedhāt iṣṭam eva etat saṅgṛhītam tathā ca uttara sūtreṇa pratiṣetsyati ācāryaḥ dṛṣṭa vat ānuśravikaḥ sa hi aviśuddhi kṣaya atiśaya yuktaḥ tasmāt divya sukha anapekṣasya api yuktā vividiṣā dhyāna sukham api kṣaya atiśayau na ativartate tat api atra eva saṅgṛhītam tasmāt pratiṣedhya eva ayam pakṣaḥ iti na kiñcid abhidhīyate yat api uktam ubhayathā sambhavāt jijñāsā anupapattiḥ iti astu guṇānām jijñāsā yat tu uktam ācetanyāt asambhavaḥ iti satya acetanye buddheḥ icchā ādi sadbhāvam uttaratra pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt upapannā jijñāsā 
[I,39,i_I,39,ii]	āha tat śabda ānarthakyam pratipada sambandhāt yaḥ ayam ācāryeṇa tad śabdaḥ sūtre paṭhitaḥ asya khalu pratipadam asambandhāt su alpām api arthavat tām na upalabhāmahe tasmāt ainam apuṣkala artham adhyeṣyāmahe iti ucyate katham hi nāma prayoktṛ pāratantryāt śabdasya śabda antareṇa sambandhaḥ na syāt iti 
[I,39,iii]	āha na brūmaḥ avidyamāna sambandhaḥ asambandhaḥ kintarhi ayukta sambandhaḥ yaḥ sa khalu asambandhaḥ tat yathā anācāraḥ māṇavakaḥ iti dravyeṇa kriyā śakti tvāt na śakyam kiñcid anācāravatā kṣaṇam api avasthātum ayuktam tvācaran anācāraḥ iti ucyate tathā ca asya tad śabdasya pratipadam sambandhaḥ na yuktaḥ tasmāt anarthakaḥ tad śabdaḥ 
[I,39,iv]	ānantaryāt jijñāsā śabdasya iti ced syāt matam anantarasya vidhiḥ vā bhavati pratiṣedhaḥ vā iti anayā yuktyā jijñāsā śabdasya tad śabdena abhisambandhaḥ śakyaḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt tad apaghāte prayojana asadbhāvāt na hi jijñāsā apaghāte kiñcid prayojanam asti iti sati api sambandhe na tad śabdena arthaḥ 
[I,40,i_I,40,ii]	abhighātasya iti ced atha api syāt yadi jijñāsā apaghātena kiṃcid prayojanam asti iti atas tad sambandhaḥ na iṣyate tena tarhi abhighāta śabdena asya abhisambandhaḥ kariṣyate tathā ca api tat śabda urthavān bhaviṣyati iti etad anupapannam kasmāt nimitta avasthāne punar punar utpatteḥ naimittikaḥ ayam abhighātaḥ tasya nimittavat tvāt ātyantikaḥ apaghātaḥ na syāt itarathā jvara nimittakaḥ dāhaḥ iva śīta dravya saṃsparśāt praśāntaḥ api nimitta avasthānāt punar punar pravartate iti aphala tvam asya vyāyāmasya traya śabdasya iti ced na pāratantryāt āśraya paratantrā hi saṃkhyā tasyāḥ na antareṇa āśrayeṇa upaghātam apaghātaḥ śakyaḥ kartum ānarthakyañca samānam iti sutarām tad śabdena na arthaḥ 
[I,40,iii^1]	duḥkha śabdasya iti ced sāmānyam yadi eteṣām padānām abhisambandhe yathā ukta doṣa upapattiḥ duḥkha śabdam tarhi tad śabdena abhisaṃbhantsyāmaḥ tasmin eṣa niṣedhaḥ viśati iti tat ca na evam kasmāt aneka pada vyavadhānāt katham anantara vṛttinā sarva nāmnā aneka pada vyavahitasya duḥkha śabdasya abhisambandhaḥ śakyet pratipādayitum tasmāt na kiñcid etat kiñca anyat upasarjana tvāt ayam khalu api duḥkha śabdaḥ samāse upasarjanībhūtaḥ na ca ekasmin kāle śabdasya pradhāna tvam upasarjana tvam ca yuktitaḥ sambhavati pradhānasya ca pada antareṇa abhisambandhaḥ tasmāt vivāda āspadam eva etat sūtram kiñca anyat nityānām apaghāta anupapatteḥ iha nityānām apaghātaḥ kartum na śakyate 
[I,40,iii^2]	tat yathā puruṣāṇām anityānāñca apaghātaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā jvara ādīnām nityañca duḥkham tasmāt tad apaghāte abhyutthānānarthakyam vṛtti apaghāte tad apaghātaḥ iti ced syāt punar eṣā buddhiḥ satyam nityānām apaghātaḥ na yuktitaḥ sambhavati na tu vayam guṇa lakṣaṇasya duḥkhasya apaghātam brūmaḥ kintarhi vṛttiḥ asya abhibhūyate iti tat ca na evam kasmāt ukta uttara tvāt uktam atra uttaram nimitta avasthāne punar punar utpatteḥ iti tasmāt ayam api amārgaḥ kiñca anyat aviśeṣāt kalpayitvā api vṛtti apaghātam vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ ananya tvāt vṛtti apaghāte vṛttimat apaghātaḥ prāptaḥ iti na asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ tasmāt kṛśaḥ ayam parihāraḥ iti na arthaḥ tad śabdena 
[I,43,i_I,44,i]	ucyate yat uktam tat śabda ānarthakyam pratipadam asambandha ādityaḥ tu duḥkha śabdena abhisambandhaḥ tad sambandhe yathā ukta doṣa upapattiḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi tarhi tad śabdasya duḥkha śabdena eva abhisambandhaḥ abhyupagamyate tena ye asmābhiḥ pūrvam abhihitāḥ doṣāḥ te prasajyante tasmāt pratiṣiddhasya pakṣasya parigrahe sāhasa mātram iti etat ca na evam kasmāt pratividhānāt satyam asati pratividhāne sāhasa mātram syāt pratividhīyate tu tasmāt adoṣaḥ ayam iti kintat iti ced syāt matam ucyata antarhi kintat pratividhānam yasya avaṣṭambhena aneka doṣa vyāhataḥ api ayam pakṣaḥ āśrīyate na hi anuktam asmābhiḥ ākāra mātreṇa śakyam pratipattum iti 
[I,44,ii^1]	ucyate bāḍham yat tāvat uktam aneka pada vyavadhānāt na duḥkha śabdasya tad śabdena abhisambandhaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na anabhyupagamāt yaḥ hi anantara kṛtam śabdasya śabda antareṇa saha sambandham ācaṣṭe tampratyayam upālambhaḥ syāt vayantu artha kṛtam sambandham ācakṣmahe tathā ca uktam yasya yena abhisambandhaḥ dūra sthasya api tasya saḥ arthataḥ tu asamānām ānantarye api asambhavaḥ kiñca anyat śāstre darśanāt śāstre ca vyavahitānām api sarva nāmnām abhisambandhaḥ dṛśyate yasya guṇasya hi bhāvāt dravye śabda niveśaḥ tad abhidhāne tu atalau iti atra artha kṛtaḥ ca sambandhaḥ śabdānām abhyupagataḥ ṅyāp prātipadikāt bahuṣu bahuvacanam supaḥ dhātu prātipadikayoḥ aluj uttara pade iti evamādīnām sambandha abhyupagamaḥ tathā anaḍvāham udahāriṇi bhagini vahasi yā tvam śirasi kumbham avācīnam abhidhāvantam adrākṣīḥ iti vārtike dṛṣṭāntaḥ na hi atra satya ānantarye śirasā anaḍuhaḥ vahanam kumbhasya vā saraṇam upapadyate yathā ca atra vyavahitānām abhisambandhaḥ tathā iha api draṣṭavyaḥ 
[I,44,ii^2]	yat punar etat uktam upasarjana tvāt pada antareṇa anabhisambandhaḥ iti etad anupapannam kasmāt samāsādapa uddhāre buddhayā vyavasthitasya svātantrya upapatteḥ satyam upasarjanasya pada antareṇa abhisambandhaḥ na upapadyate na tu vayam samāsa vṛtteḥ eva tad śabdena abhisambandhaḥ iti pratipadyāmahe kintarhi samāsādapa uddhṛtasya buddhi vyavasthitasya upajanita svātantryasya śabda antareṇa sambandham icchāmaḥ iti atha etat aniṣṭam yoga pramāṇe ca tad abhāve darśanam syāt atha śabda anuśāsanam keṣām śabdānām iti ca evamādīnām prayogāṇām virodhaḥ prāpnoti aniṣṭañca etat yat punar etat uktam nityānām apaghāta anupapatteḥ vṛtti apaghāte ca tad apaghāta prasaṅgāt iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt guṇa śakteḥ prayojana uparame satya ātma kalpena vyavasthāna abhyupagamāt na etat abhyupagamyate guṇasya ucchittiḥ bhavati vṛttiḥ vā asyā abhibhūyate kintarhi puruṣa artha nibandhanā caritārtha śaktiḥ asya puruṣa artha pravṛttau prayojana asadbhāvāt ātma kalpena vyavatiṣṭhate iti etat vivakṣitam tasmāt yuktam etat tad apaghātake hetau jijñāsā pravartate iti 
[I,48,i_I,49,i]	dṛṣṭe sā apārthā ced syāt etat pratyakṣaḥ duḥka pratīkāra hetuḥ asti tasya samatikrame kim prayojanam tat yathā śārīrasya tāvat ayam apagama hetuḥ aneka dravya rasāyana upabhogaḥ mānasasya api manojña strī pāna vilepana bhojana vastra alaṅkāra ādi viṣaya samprāptiḥ ādhibhautikasya nīti śāstra abhyāsaḥ śastra astra kuśala tā viṣama sthāna an adhyāsanam ca ādhidaivikasya api yathākālam vividha nivasana āstaraṇa garbha gṛha prāsāda jāla antara candana vyajana maṇi hāra ādi sevā vividha auṣadha maṃgala stuti mantra prayoga anuṣṭhānam iti dṛṣṭe hetau sā jijñāsā apārtha iti ced na ekānta atyatataḥ abhāvāt 
[I,49,ii_I,50,i]	etat ca na evam kasmāt ekānta atyantataḥ abhāvāt ekāntaḥ nāma niyamena bhāvaḥ atyantam bhūtasya avināśaḥ ekāntaḥ ca atyantam ca te ekānta atyante tayoḥ abhāvaḥ ekānta atyantataḥ abhāvaḥ tasmāt ṣaṣṭhī sthāne pañcamī ṣaṣṭhyā eva vā tasiḥ ṣaṣṭhyā vyāśrayaḥ iti yoga vibhāgāt asamāsa karaṇam vṛtta pūraṇa artham mānasasya ca duḥkhasya pratīkāre doṣa antara upasaṃgraha artham tathā hi strī ādīnām sati etasmin doṣa dvaye aśakya marjjanam kartum asvābhāvika tvāt sati arjane rakṣaṇam aśakyam sādhāraṇa tvāt sati ca rakṣaṇe kṣayaḥ kṛtaka tvāt saṅgāt ca anupaśamaḥ bhūta upaghātam antareṇa ca asambhavaḥ iti ete doṣāḥ āha katham etat avagamyate yat dṛṣṭasya hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam anātyantika tvam ca iti 
[I,50,ii]	ucyate pratyakṣaḥ eva etat upalabhyate yat ā āyurveda vihitasya kriyā kramasya abhiyuktam ātmavantam bheṣaja bhiṣaj paricāraka sampannam pratyānarthakyam āha ca sarveṣām vyādhi rūpāṇām nidānam trividham smṛtam āhāraḥ ca vihāraḥ ca karma pūrva kṛtam tathā tatra āhāra vihāra utthān rogān dravyam apohati yaḥ tu karma kṛtaḥ vyādhiḥ maraṇāt sa nivartate punar api āha sa upadravaḥ sarva rūpaḥ bala māṃsa indriya apahaḥ sāriṣṭhaḥ ca eva yaḥ vyādhiḥ tam bhiṣaj parivarjayet iti evam anaikāntika tvam anātyantika tvam tu nivṛttānām api vyādhīnāmpunar utpatti darśanāt mahatā khalu api prayatnena nivartitāḥ vyādhayaḥ punar utpadyante tathā ca uktam punar jvare samutpanne kriyā pūrva jvara anugā iti
[I,51,i]	tasmāt yathā eva asya āyurveda ādeḥ pratīkāra hetu tvam pratyakṣa siddham evam ekānta atyantataḥ abhāvaḥ api tathā mānasasya ca yathā ca śārīra duḥkha pratīkāra hetavaḥ anaikāntikāḥ tathā strī ādayaḥ api kasmāt tad sannidhāne viṣaya antara abhilāṣa darśanāt yadi hi strī ādayaḥ viṣayāḥ sarvadā duḥkha pratīkāra samarthāḥ bhaveyuḥ kim ati teṣu sannihiteṣu viṣayiṇaḥ viṣaya antara jighṛkṣā syāt evam anaikāntika tvam anātyantika tvam api nivṛtta icchānām api bhūyas prārthanā sambhavāt yadi hi viṣaya upabhogaḥ atyantam eva mānasam duḥkham apahanyāt kim prāptam yena bhūyas tam prati viṣayiṇaḥ abhilāṣaḥ syāt kim kāraṇam yasmāt na hi avidyamāne tamasi devadattasya pradīpam pratyapekṣā bhavati dṛśyate ca nivṛtta icchānām api viṣaya upabhogāt viṣayiṇām bhūyas viṣaya abhilāṣaḥ tena manyāmahe na ayam dṛṣṭaḥ hetuḥ duḥkham ahapanti kintarhi sutarām vṛddhim karoti āha ca na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmā iva bhūyas eva abhivardhate 
[I,51,ii_I,52,i]	aparaḥ āha saṃvedya tvāt guru tvāt ca nindita tvāt ca sādhubhiḥ sarvatra āsat nidhānāt ca na dṛṣṭaḥ hetuḥ iṣyate saṃvedya tvāt bhoga sādhana vikalānām arthinām madhye viṣayiṇā upayujyamānāḥ taiḥ saṃvedyante teṣām apradāya upayujyamānam nairghṛṇyam āviṣkuryāt viṣayiṇā pradīyamānaḥ vā arthibhyaḥ parimita tvāt avacchidyeta iti anupāyaḥ ayam duḥkha apaghāte buddhimatām kim ca guru tvāt bhogānām vividha nivasana strī pāna bhojana vilepana alaṃkāra ādīnām samagrye sukham utpadyate na anyatara vaikalye sāmagryam ca eṣām svābhāvika tvāt anupapannam āha ca nābhi jātim na vijñānam na ca śauryam apekṣate lakṣmī saṃskāra yogāt ca kvacid eva avatiṣṭhate 
[I,52,ii_I,52,iii]	iti evam aneka artha āśraya tvāt guruḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ kim ca nindita tvāt ca sādhubhiḥ ninditaḥ khalu api sādhubhiḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ yasmāt āha āyāsāḥ ca vighātaḥ ca vipralambha bhayāni ca yat ca anyat aśivam loke tad kāmebhyaḥ pravartate punar api āha ayam sa kṣetriyaḥ vyādhiḥ ayam ātyantikaḥ jvaraḥ idam āspadamītīnām eṣa yoniḥ sa pāpmanām agādham etat pātālam eṣa paṅkaḥ duruttaraḥ kleśa vyādhi bhaya ākīrṇam etat śvabhram bhaya āvaham vividha āyāsa śokānām etat āyatanam mahat dainya śrama viṣādānām etat kṣetram apāvṛtam yasmāt viṣaya sambhogāt vihagaḥ pañjarau iva gataḥ vaneṣu ramate sa sukhāni samaśnute 
[I,52,iv]	tasmāt sādhubhiḥ apākṛta tvāt asādhuḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ kim ca sarvatra asat nidhānāt na hi su pratiniviṣṭasya api kāminaḥ sarvatra viṣaya sannidhānena bhavitavyam no khalu api ekasmin deśe avasthānam sambhavati viṣaya abhāva prasaṅgāt tasmāt avaśyam viyogena bhavitavyam viyoge ca sati dhruvaḥ aniṣṭa anubandhaḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ viṣaya parigraheṇa tatra yat uktam dṛṣṭasya hetoḥ sadbhāvāt apārthakāḥ jijñāsā iti etat ayuktam 
[I,57,i]	āha yadi ekānta atyantataḥ abhāvāt dṛṣṭe hetau aparitoṣaḥ tena tarhi astyayam anyaḥ hetuḥ ubhaya doṣa varjitaḥ sa kasmāt na parigṛhyate kaḥ asau iti ced ucyate śāstra uktaḥ karma vidhiḥ sa hi aikāntikaḥ katham evam hi āha paśu bandhena sarvān lokān jayati na tu uktam kadācid jayati kadācid na iti phalasya pratyakṣa anupalabdheḥ anaikāntika tvam iti ced syāt matam pratyakṣatas eva idam vihitasya karmaṇaḥ phalam na upalabhyate tathā hi putra kāmaḥ iṣṭim nirūpya duhitaram api na prāpnoti artha kāmaḥ ca karma kṛtvā māṣakam api na labhate tasmāt na ayam anaikāntikaḥ iti etat ca na evam kasmāt sādhana vaikalyāt tad anupapatteḥ aneka sādhana sādhyaḥ hi karma vidhiḥ yatra phalam na upalabhyate tatra sādhana vaikalyam anumātavyam kasmāt na hi etat iṣṭam sati kāraṇe kāryam na bhavati kim ca anyat saṃsāra abhāva prasaṅgāt yadi khalu api karmaṇaḥ phalavat tvam na iṣyate tena tad nimittasya saṃsāsarasya abhāva prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt siddham asya aikāntika tvam 
[I,57,ii_I,59,ii]	ātyantika tvam api siddham eva yasmāt āha apāma somam amṛtā abhūma iti atra soma pānāt amṛta tva avāptiḥ śrūyate tasmāt tat eva anuṣṭhātavyam kim anyena hetunā parikalpitena iti jijñāsā apārtha eva iti ucyate dṛṣṭa vat ānuśravikaḥ anuśrūyate iti anuśravaḥ anuśrave bhavaḥ ānuśravikaḥ dṛṣṭena tulyam vartate dṛṣṭa vat kim asau anabhipretaḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ 
[I,59,iii_I,60,i]	āha kaḥ punar ayam anuśravaḥ ucyate mantra brāhmaṇam yāvat vā purātanam anuśrūyamāṇam prāmāṇyena abhyupagamyate tatrabhavadbhiḥ yathā śruti nibandhanāḥ smṛtayaḥ aṅgāni vedāḥ tarkā vā yathā āha veda vedāṅga tarkeṣu veda saṃjñā nirucyate iti āha kim pūrvasmāt eva hetoḥ ayam ānuśravikaḥ hetuḥ anabhipretaḥ iti 
[I,60,ii_I,60,iv]	na iti ucyate kintarhi sa hi aviśuddhi kṣaya atiśaya yuktaḥ iti saḥ iti ānuśravikasya hetoḥ pratinirdeśaḥ hi śabdaḥ yasmāt arthe aviśuddhiḥ ca kṣayaḥ ca atiśayaḥ ca taiḥ yuktaḥ etat uktam bhavati yasmāt ayam ānuśravikaḥ hetuḥ aviśuddhaḥ anityaḥ tāratamyavān ca atas dṛṣṭaḥ iva anabhipretaḥ tatra aviśuddhi yuktaḥ tāvat hiṃsā vidhānāt yat āha brāhmaṇe brāhmaṇam ālabheta ityādi tathā ṣaṣ śatāni niyujyante paśūnām madhyame ahani aśvamedhasya vacanāt ūnāni paśubhiḥ tribhiḥ 
[I,60,v_I,61,ii]	iti hiṃsā ca aviśuddhiḥ prāṇinām iṣṭa śarīra vyāpādanāt āha tad anupapattiḥ śāstra codita tvāt yadi śāstreṇa coditā iyam hiṃsā na syāt mukta saṃśayam aviśuddhi tvam asyāḥ pratipadyāmahe śāsra coditā tu tasmāt na iyam aviśuddhiḥ tad prāmāṇya anabhyupagamāt aviśuddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam veda prāmāṇyam abhyupagacchatām asaṃśayam etat evam syāt hetu vāda kuśalāḥ tu vayam tasmāt adhīyatām yadi kaścid asti ubhaya pakṣa prasiddhaḥ hetuḥ yatas nissaṃśayaḥ pratyayaḥ syāt iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt abhyupagama virodhāt dṛṣṭam anumānam āpta vacanam ca iti prāmāṇya trayam abhyupagatam bhavadbhiḥ idānīm vedasya āpta vacana tve satya prāmāṇyam bruvataḥ sva mata vyāghātaḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat 
[I,61,iii]	vedasya āpta vacana tva anupapatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam āpta vacana tvam prāc prasādhya asya vedasya paścāt ayam upālambhaḥ yuktam abhidhātum syāt tattva siddham tasmāt anupālambhaḥ ayam iti etat api uktam kasmāt puruṣa buddhi pūrvaka tve sati rāga ādi yogāt śabdaḥ vicāra arhaḥ syāt kim āpta vacanam na vā iti apuruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ tu āmnāyaḥ svatantraḥ puruṣa niśśreyasa artham pravartate tasmāt na evaṃvidham aniṣṭam vicāram arhati kim ca anyat aviśuddhi tva anupapatti prasaṅgāt yadi ca etasmin arthe bhavān api paryanupayujyeta katham idam niścīyate yat uta prāṇinām iṣṭa śarīra vyāpāda nāda viśuddhi hiṃsā iti avaśyam abhidhānīyam śāstrate iti tat eva ca śāstram kratau hiṃsām āha tasmāt kaḥ atra hetuḥ anyatra pramāṇam iha eva etat apramāṇam bhavitum arhati hiṃsātaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
[I,62,i]	anugraha upaghāta lakṣaṇa tvāt ahiṃsā hiṃsayoḥ pratyakṣa siddhiḥ iti ced atha api syāt ahiṃsātaḥ ca anugrahaḥ bhavati iṣṭa śarīra vyāpādana lakṣaṇaḥ hiṃsātaḥ ca upaghātaḥ bhavati abhipreta śarīra vyāpādana lakṣaṇaḥ kriyā anurūpam ca phalam anumātum yuktam iti pratyakṣa siddham anayoḥ iṣṭa aniṣṭa phala hetu tvam tasmāt kaḥ atra śāstra vyāpāraḥ iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt aniṣṭa prasaṃgāt evam hi parikalpyamāne guru bhāryā gamane api sattva antara anugraha sāmartha ādiṣṭa phala sambandhaḥ syāt māṇavakam ca upanīya vrata ādeśa śauca brahmacaryya svādhyāya abhyāsa bhaikṣa agni paricaraṇa guru śuśrūṣā ādiṣu pravartayataḥ aniṣṭa phala sambandhaḥ syāt tasmāt loka śāstra viruddhaḥ asat tarkaḥ na iṣṭaḥ iti 
[I,62,ii]	ubhaya abhidhānāt śāstra virodha prasaṅgaḥ iti ced syāt matam tat eva śāstram ahiṃsām āha tat eva hiṃsām evam sati paraspara viruddhayoḥ arthayoḥ ca udita tvāt ubhaya anugrahā sambhave śāstra virodha prasaṅgaḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt utsarga apavādayoḥ viṣaya bhedāt sāmānye hi śāstram ahiṃsām utsṛjya viśeṣe kratu lakṣaṇe apavādam śāsti sāmānya vihitam ca viśeṣa vihitena bādhyate tat yathā dadhi brāhmaṇa ibhaḥ dīyatām takram kauṇḍinyāya iti tasmāt utsarga apavādayoḥ viṣaya bhedāt na asti śāstra virodhaḥ iti kim ca anyat kanyā gamana vat punar vidhāne doṣa abhāvāt yathā khalu api śāsre pratiṣiddham kanyā gamanam iti na idānīm abhirūpaḥ pratigṛhya tām abhigamya adharma bhāj bhavati 
[I,62,iii_I,66,i]	gṛhasthaḥ sadṛśīm bhāryām vindeta ananya pūrvikām iti śāstra antara sadbhāvāt evam śāstre pratiṣiddhā hiṃsā na idānīm kratau hiṃsāyām pravartamānaḥ aniṣṭa phala bhāj syāt pūrva uktāt eva śāstra antara sadbhāvāt tara yat uktam prāṇinām iṣṭa śarīra vyāpāda nāda viśuddhiḥ hiṃsā iti etat ayuktam ucyate na abhiprāyānavabodhāt citram api bahu etat abhidhīyamānaḥ na abhi prāyam veda bhavān kim kāraṇam yasmāt na vayam vedasya prāmāṇyam pratyācakṣmahe no khalu api brūmaḥ śāstra coditāyām hiṃsāyām pravartamānasya aniṣṭa phala sambandhaḥ bhavati kintarhi sati svarga prāpti nimitta tve veda vihitasya karmaṇaḥ samanuṣṭhānam prāṇi jam upaghātam antareṇa na sambhavati iti hita kāmaiḥ abhyupekṣyate yasmāt na hi etat uktam yat anyeṣām upaghātena ātma anugrahaḥ kāryaḥ iti āha na tad parasya sandadhyāt pratikūlam yadātmanaḥ eṣa saṅkṣepataḥ dharmaḥ kāmāt anyaḥ pravartate 
[I,66,ii_I,67,i]	āha yadi etat na abhyupagamyate katham pūrvam uktam prāṇinām iṣṭa śarīra vyāpāda nāda viśuddhiḥ hiṃsā iti ucyate kārye kāraṇa upacārāt yaḥ asau hiṃsā nimittakaḥ kāruṇyāt manasi naḥ paritāpaḥ utpadyate sā khalu aviśuddhiḥ abhipretā tasyām kāraṇam upacarya uktam aviśuddhiḥ hiṃsā iti yathā mudgaiḥ tṛptāḥ gobhiḥ sukhinaḥ iti 
[I,67,ii_I,67,iii]	āha katham etat avagamyate hiṃsā kāryam paritāpa mātram aviśuddhiḥ ācāryasya abhipretā na punar hiṃsā eva iti ucyate prakarṣa pratyaya upalabdheḥ vakṣyati upadiṣṭāt tad viparītaḥ śreyān iti samāna jātīyam ca pratiyoginam apekṣya prakarṣa pratyayaḥ utpadyate yadi ca ānuśravikasya praśasyatā na abhi pretā syāt prakarṣa pratyaya anupapatti prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt na utsūtram etat 
[I,67,iv_I,68,i]	āha sannyāsa anupapattiḥ aviyoga śravaṇāt na hi karmaṇaḥ atyāga sannyāsayoḥ tvam īśiṣe kintarhi śāstram yat āha tat avaśyam kartavyam tat ca amaraṇāt karmabhiḥ aviyogam śāsti kasmāt evam hi āha jarā maryam etat satram yat agnihotra dārśa paurṇamāsau jarayā ha etasmāt satrāt vimucyate mṛtyunā ca punar api āha kurvan eva iha karmāṇi jijīviṣet śatam samāḥ tasmāt āmaraṇāt karmaṇā ām atyāgaḥ tasmin sati hetu antara karmaṇām ānarthakyam ucyate na sādhanānām asvabhāvika tvāt patnī saṃyoga ādibhiḥ anekaiḥ sādhanaiḥ ayam karma vidhiḥ prasādhyate teṣām ca asvābhāvika tvāt aśakyam arjanam prayogataḥ pūrvam kartum iti pratipāditam tasmāt anityāni karmāṇi 
[I,68,ii]	hetu śāstra vipratipattau śāstra balīyaḥ tvam iti ced syāt matam yatra hetu śāstrayoḥ vipratipattiḥ bhavati tatra vipralambha bhūyiṣṭha tvāt anumānasya balīyaḥ śāstram iti avaśayam abhyupagantavyam iti tat ca anupapannam kasmāt śaktitas viniyogāt śaktim apekṣya śāstram agnihotra ādīni karmāṇi vidadhat teṣām anitya tām jñāpayati katham evam hi āha yaḥ alam san agni hotrāya agnihotram na juhoti tam eṣā devatā paruṇaddhi asmāt lokāt amuṣmāt ca ubhābhyām tasmāt anityāni karmāṇi kim ca anyat jarā grahaṇa sāmarthyāt tvadīyaḥ eva jñāpake jarā grahaṇam asti atas anumīyate śakti apekṣam anityam ca karma kim ca anyat śāstra hāneḥ ubhayam hi śāstre nirdiṣṭam karmāṇi sannyāsaḥ ca yadi punar karmāṇi nityakartavyatayā īṣi ante tena sannyāsa śāstram hīyate tasmāt viṣaya rāga āviṣkaraṇam etat vaḥ 
[I,70,i_I,70,ii]	āha na śruti balīyaḥ tvāt tulya balayoḥ hi śāstrayoḥ eka viṣaya sannipāte dvayoḥ yugapad anugrahā sambhave vikalpa paryāyau bhavataḥ śruti smṛti sannipāte ca śrutiḥ balīyasī smṛti vihitaḥ ca sannyāsaḥ tasmāt na anayoḥ vikalpaḥ na khalu api paryāyaḥ nyāyyaḥ ucyate tat itaratra tulyam yathā eva karmaṇām samanuṣṭhānam śāsti śāstram tathā sannyāsam api katham evam hi āha na karmaṇā na prajayā dhanena tyāgena ekena amṛta tva mānaśuḥ pareṇa nākam nihitam guhāyām vibhrājate yat yatayaḥ viśanti na karmaṇā mṛtyum ṛṣayaḥ niṣeddhuḥ prajāvantaḥ draviṇam icchamāṇāḥ atha apare ṛṣayaḥ manīṣiṇaḥ param karmabhyaḥ amṛta tva mānaśuḥ 
[I,70,iii]	brāhmaṇam ca atra bhavati tat yaḥ idam viduḥ ye ca ime araṇyāḥ śraddhā ātapaḥ iti upāsate te arciṣam abhisambhavanti arciṣaḥ harahnaḥ āpūryamāṇa pakṣam āpūryamāṇa pakṣāt yan ṣaṣ udaḍḍa iti māsān tān māsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaram saṃvatsarāt ādityam ādityāt candramasam candramasaḥ vidyutam tatpuruṣaḥ amāṇavaḥ saḥ etān brahma gamayati punar api āha etam eva viditvā muniḥ bhavati etam eva pravrājinaḥ lokam icchantaḥ pravrajanti etat ha sma vai pūrve vidvāṃsaḥ prajām na akāmayanta prajayā kim kariṣyāmaḥ yeṣām na ayam ātmā na ayam lokaḥ iti te ha sma putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca loka eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya atha bhikṣā caryam caranti iti tasmāt ete tyāga sannyāsayoḥ ubhayoḥ liṅgam 
[I,72,i_I,72,iii]	āha yadi api evam śāstram tathā api samanuṣṭhāne vidhiḥ asti vihitam ca avaśyam kartavyam sannyāse tu artha vāda mātram iti anayoḥ ayam viśeṣaḥ tasmin sati samanuṣṭhānam jyāyaḥ na tyāgaḥ ucyate kaḥ ayam vidhiḥ kaḥ ayam artha vādaḥ āha vidhiḥ tad artha tvena apūrva upadeśaḥ yaḥ hi vidhi arthena liṅā loṭā kṛtyaiḥ vā apūrva upadeśaḥ kriyate sa vidhiḥ yathā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ vāyavyam śvetam ajam ālabheta bhūti kāmaḥ iti stutiḥ artha vādaḥ tasya tu vihitasya prarocana artham yā stutiḥ saḥ artha vādaḥ tat yathā vāyuḥ vai kṣepiṣṭhā devatāḥ vāyum eva tena bhāgadheyena upadhāvati saḥ eva enam bhūtim gamayati iti evaṃvidhām hi stutim upaśrutya phala arthine hi yajamānāya vidhiḥ prarocate etasmin hita kāmaḥ pravartate iti 
[I,73,i^1]	ucyate na atas eva sannyāsa siddhiḥ evam ced manyase yama āmnāyaḥ śreyāṃsam artham manyate tam prarocanāya stauti tathā sannyāsa siddhiḥ kasmāt stuta tvāt bahula arthinām sannyāsam āmnāyaḥ stauti sa kasmāt na prarocate itarathāḥ hi ānarthakyam yadi khalu api artha vādaḥ stuvan api na prarocayet yat uktam prarocana arthaḥ artha vādaḥ iti tat bhavadbhiḥ hāpitavyam syāt anarthakaḥ hi evam satyartha vādaḥ na prarocana arthaḥ artha antara vacanam vā yadi prarocana artha tvam asya na iṣyate tena tarhi artha antaram vaktavyam mā bhūt anarthaka tvam veda eka deśasya iti tasmāt na anayā vibhīṣikayā vayam śakyāḥ sat mārgāt apanetum kiṃca anyat ubhayathā vikalpe aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt iha ayam āmnāyaḥ vidheya tvena vā sannyāsam stūyāt avidheya tvena vā kiṃca atas tat yadi tāvat vidheya tvena stauti kim anyat vicāryate siddhaḥ sannyāsaḥ atha vidheya tvena stutau asya prayojanam kartavyam yat hi kartavya tayā na iṣṭam tad apuruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ svatantraḥ puruṣa niśśreyasa artham pravartamānaḥ āmnāyaḥ kim iti prarocayeta 
[I,73,i^2]	tasmāt etām api kalpanām kṛtvā kṛśam eva etat athavā ubhathāḥ vikalpaḥ iti asya ayam anyaḥ arthaḥ iha ayam āmnāyaḥ bhūta arthena vā sannyāsam prarocayet abhūta arthena vā kim ca atas tat yadi tāvat bhūtārthena prarocayati tathā sati amṛta tva prāpakasya sannyāsasya aparigrahe viṣaya ārāgāt anyaḥ hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ atha abhūta arthena puruṣaḥ niḥśreyasāt hīyate kasmāt na hi etat yuktam yat aśreyasi mārge pramāṇa bhūtaḥ āmnāyaḥ mātṛmodaka nyāyena īhita arthinaḥ prāṇinaḥ pratārayet tasmāt ayuktam etat kiñca anyat anekāntāt naca ayam ekāntaḥ yat vihitam eva kartavyam tathā ca śābarāḥ paṭhanti grāma gamanam bhavataḥ śobhanam iti atra antareṇa vidhim stutiḥ eva devadattam grāma gamanāya prarocayati iti kiñca anyat āśaṅkā prasaṅgāt yadi khalu api kiñcid satyam kiñcid anṛtam brūyāt vedaḥ tathā sati pauruṣeya vākyavat veda vākye api āśaṃkā prasajyeta tathā ca sati yat uktam eva prasaṃgaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat 
[I,73,i^3]	kim ca vidhi anumānam vā tat evam eka deśa bhūta tvāt athavā vidhi eka deśaḥ artha vādaḥ iti atisṛṣṭam bhavatā tatra sannyāse artha vādam upalabhya vidhiḥ api asti iti anumātavyam anupalambhāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt ca evam yadi asau vidhiḥ upalabhyate tasmāt anupalambha āt ayam doṣān nivartiṣyate iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt aneka bheda tvāt upalabdhau yatnaḥ kriyatām aneka bhedaḥ hi prativedam āmnāyaḥ tatra yat uktam vidhi sadbhāvāt kriyā prādhānyam iti etat api ayuktam itikarta vya tā anupadeśāt sannyāsa anupapattiḥ iti ced atha api syāt yadi sannyāsam api āmnāyaḥ vidheyam manyeta tena yathā gārhasthyasya itikartavyatām bhāryā udvahana ādikām mantravat upadiśati tathā sannyāsam api upadiśet na tu upadiṣṭavān tasmāt na asti sannyāsaḥ iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt abhāvāt itikartavya tānām hi sarvāsām abhāvaḥ sannyāsaḥ tatra kim śāstram upadekṣyati yāvatī khalu iti kartavya tā sannyāsa aṅgam tām upadiśati śāstram katham 
[I,73,i^4]	evam hi āha tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi upavasanti araṇye śāntāḥ vidvāṃsaḥ bhaikṣa caryā carantaḥ sūrya dvāreṇa te virajasaḥ prayānti yatra amṛtaḥ sa puruṣaḥ avyaya ātmā tatra tapaḥ śraddhe ye hi apavasanti iti enam śraddhayā upetam yama niyama lakṣaṇam dharmam āha araṇyaḥ iti gṛhebhyaḥ vinissṛtim śāntāḥ iti indriyāṇām antaḥkaraṇasya ca viṣaya abhilāṣāt vi nivartanam vidvāṃsaḥ iti pūrva rātra apararātra ādiṣu kāleṣu anirviṇṇasya yoginaḥ jñāna abhyāsam bhaikṣa caryām carantaḥ iti śarīra sthiti nimittam parimitam abhyavahāra niyogam uttara ardhena ca phalam ācaṣṭe tat nibandhanaḥ ca vistaraḥ sanyāsa itikartavyatāyām manu ādibhiḥ abhihitaḥ śruti nirvacanāḥ ca smṛtayaḥ bhavatām pramāṇam iti pakṣaḥ tatra yat ukta miti kartavya tā anupadeśāt na asti sannyāsaḥ iti eda yuktam evam ca nityāni karmāṇi yat tu anena etat uktam ānuśravikaḥ hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ iti satyam etat avaśyam hi karmaṇaḥ phalam abhyupagantavyam itarathāḥ hi tad nimittasya saṃsārasya abhāvāt aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt aniṣṭām eva etat ācāryasya 
[I,78,i_I,78,iv]	āha katham etat anumātavyam iti ucyate kṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyāt yadi pūrva sūtra uktam iha anuvartate kṣaya grahaṇam anarthakam syāt kasmāt atyanta abhāva paryāyaḥ hi kṣayaḥ iti kṛtvā evam siddhaḥ aviśuddhi yogaḥ āha kṣaya yogaḥ idānīm katham anumātavyaḥ iti ucyate kṣaya yogaḥ aṅga parimāṇāt kṣaya yogaḥ punar asya hetoḥ aṅga parimāṇāt veditavyaḥ yāni hi yajeḥ aṅgāni paśu puroḍāśa ādīni tāni parimitāni parimitānām sādhanānām tantu ādīnām parimitam kāryam paṭa ādi dṛṣṭam parimitam kṣaya dharmi dṛṣṭam tadvat eva kiñca anyat saṃsāra upalambhāt dṛśyate ca ayam vāc buddhi svabhāva āhāra vihāra bheda bhinna karma vihāra vaicitrya nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ yadi punar sākṣāt kṛtam karma akṣaya phalam syāt sa punarāvṛtti abhāvāt prāṇinām na upalabhyeta 
[I,79,i]	śabda sāmarthyāt nitya tvam iti ced syāt etat śabda pramāṇakāḥ vayam yat śabdaḥ āha tat asmākam pramāṇam sa ca asya hetoḥ amṛta tvam āha tarati mṛtyum tarati pāpmānam ityādi tasmāt anicchatā api etat avaśyam abhyupagantavyam anabhyupagame vā pratijñā ahāniḥ vedaḥ pramāṇam iti etat ca na evam kasmāt śabda antareṇa virodhāt anitya tvam asya hetoḥ śabdaḥ anumanyate tasya evam sati virodhaḥ prāpnoti katham evam hi āha atha ye ime grāme iṣṭāpūrte dattam iti upāsate atha etam eva adhvānam punar nivartante yathā etam ākāśam ākāśāt vāyum te dhūmam abhisambhavanti dhūmaḥ bhūtvā abhram bhavati meghaḥ bhūtvā pravarṣati te iha vrīhi yavāḥ oṣadhi vanaspatayaḥ tilāḥ māṣāḥ iti jāyante tatas vai yaḥ annamati yaḥ retaḥ siñcati sa bhūyas eva bhavati iti tatra yat uktam śabda sāmarthyāt nitya tvam iti et ayuktam 
[I,81,i^1]	ubhayathā abhidhānāt śāstra virodha prasaṅgaḥ iti ced syāt matam tat eva śāstram nitya tvam āha tat eva anitya tvam evam sati paraspara virodhinoḥ arthayoḥ ca udita tvāt ubhaya anugrahā sambhave sati śāstra virodha prasaṅgaḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt asambhave satyartha antara klṛpteḥ yatra hi pramāṇa bhūtā śrutiḥ asambhavinam artham codayati tatra artha antaram kalpayati tat yathā saḥ ātmanaḥ vapām udakhidat stenam manaḥ anṛta vādinaḥ vāc iti evamādiṣu evam iha api na asti sambhavaḥ yat ekaḥ arthaḥ nityaḥ ca syāt anityaḥ ca iti tasmāt nitya tva vācakasya śāstra antarasya bhaktyā artha antaram parikalpayiṣyāmaḥ 
[I,81,i^2]	tat vat itaratrāpi iti ced syāt matam yathā eva bhavatā nitya anityayoḥ ekatra asambhavān nitya tvasya bhaktyā kalpanā kṛtā tathā eva anitya tvasya api kariṣyate iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt sarva pramāṇa virodha prasaṅgāt vināśe hi bhaktyā kalpyamāne sarva pramāṇa virodhaḥ prasajyeta katham pratyakṣa virodhaḥ tāvat saṃsāra upalambhāt anumāna virodhaḥ aṅga parimāṇe sati aṅginaḥ nitya tva anupapatteḥ śabda virodhaḥ te dhūmam abhisambhavanti iti vacanāt na tu nitya tve bhaktyā kalpyamāne doṣaḥ ayam upadyate tasmāt viṣam etat 
[I,82,i_I,83,i]	āha katham idānīm bhaktyā kalpayitavyam śāstram iti ucyate prakṛṣṭa artha tayā yathā khalu api amṛtam vā mṛtam atijīvaḥ mā te hāsiṣuḥ asavaḥ śarīram iti abhidhīyate na ca prāṇinām atyantāya āsavaḥ jahati kintarhi prakṛṣṭam kālam evam iha api ucyate tarati mṛtyum iti na atyantāya mṛtyum tarati kintarhi prakṛṣṭam kālam upacaryate hi loke prakṛṣṭe nitya śabdaḥ tat yathā nitya prahasitaḥ nitya prajalpitaḥ iti evam siddhaḥ kṣaya yogaḥ 
[I,83,ii_I,83,iv]	āha atiśaya yogaḥ idānīm asya hetoḥ katham anumātavyaḥ iti ucyate atiśaya yogaḥ kriyā abhyāsāt yatra hi kriyā sakṛt pravartate yatra ca asakṛt āvartate tatra atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā kṛṣi ādiṣu yajñe ca dravya upādāna śakti apekṣā kvacid sakṛt eva pravṛttiḥ kvacid punar punarāvṛttiḥ tasmāt atiśayena bhavitavyam kim ca anyat aṅga atiśayāt iha aṅgānām atiśayāt aṅginaḥ api ghaṭa ādeḥ atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ asti ca ayam pratiyajñam aṅgānām dakṣiṇa ādīnām atiśayaḥ tasmāt atra api atiśayena bhavitavyam 
[I,84,i^1]	devatā aṅga bhāva gamanāt kṣaya atiśaya anupapattiḥ iti ced atha api syāt yaḥ hi yajñe dravya mātrasya sādhana bhāvam anumanyate tam prati kṣaya atiśaya doṣa a aparihāryau syātām vayantu dravya samavāyinīm devatām kratau aṅga bhāvam upagacchantīm vidmaḥ tasmāt adoṣaḥ ayam iti tat ca anupapannam kasmāt sādhya tvāt devatānām a parimita tvam sādhyam tad aṅga bhāva gamanāt ca doṣa abhāvaḥ na ca ātma kriyā aṅga tvam udāsīna tvāt iti naḥ siddhāntaḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat upetya vā kratu samanuṣṭhānānarthakya prasaṅgāt 
[I,84,i^2]	yadi dravya samavāyinīm devatām upalabhya tad aṅga bhāva gamanāt akṣayaḥ niratiśayaḥ ca hetuḥ avāpyate iti iṣṭam vaḥ tena tarhi yat vā tat vā veda uktam karma kṛtvā śakyaḥ avāptum arthaḥ kim prāṇi vināśa hetubhiḥ kratubhiḥ katham na hi kiṃcid karma vidyate yatra śarīrasya aṅga bhāvaḥ na syāt sarva devatā mayam ca śarīram yasmāt āha tasmāt vai vidvān puruṣam idam brahma iti manyate sarvāḥ hi asmin devatāḥ śarīre adhi samāhitāḥ tatra yat uktam devatā aṅga bhāva gamanāt kṣaya atiśaya anupapattiḥ iti etat ayuktam evam ayam hetuḥ tridoṣaḥ tena yaḥ phala viśeṣaḥ abhinirvartyate saḥ api tathājātīyakaḥ iti śakyam anumātum tasmāt na asya jijñāsoḥ atra samādhiḥ 
[I,85,i_I,86,ii]	āha yadi na ayam śreyān iti kṛtvā asya jijñāsoḥ na atra samādhiḥ tena tarhi yaḥ śreyān phala viśeṣaḥ saḥ upadeṣṭa vayaḥ iti ucyate tad viparītaḥ śreyān tat iti anena karma vidhi niṣpāditasya svarga prāpti lakṣaṇasya phalasya abhisambandhaḥ tasmāt viparītaḥ śuddhaḥ akṣayaḥ niratiśayaḥ iti arthaḥ kaḥ asau iti ucyate mokṣaḥ śreyān etat uktam bhavati ubhau api etau praśasyau svarga apavargau āmnāya vihita tvāt mokṣaḥ tu praśasyataraḥ kasmāt yathā ukta doṣa anupapatteḥ sa hi avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt aikāntikaḥ atīndriya tvāt asaṃvedyaḥ sva ātmani avasthi tvāt laghuḥ sarvatra sannihitaḥ ca āmnāya stuta tvāt praśastaḥ sadbhiḥ āsevita tvāt aninditaḥ yama niyama vairāgya jñāna abhyupāya śuddheḥ viśuddhaḥ adravya tvāt akṣayaḥ niratiśayaḥ ca 
[I,87,i_I,87,ii]	āha katham punar ayam apavargaḥ prāpyate iti ucyate saṃyoga abhāvāt duḥkham ca pradhānam tathā ca tantra antareṣu api uktam duḥkha hetuḥ kārya karaṇa śaktiḥ iti tena yadā puruṣasya saṃyogaḥ tadā aviśuddhi tvam asya sva śakti viśeṣa yogāt teṣu teṣu jāti antara parivarteṣu dharma ādi nimitta sāmarthyāt āyāsam anubhavati yadā tu pradhāna saṃyogaḥ vinivartate tadā nimitta abhāve naimittikasya api abhāvaḥ iti kṛtvā na punar dvandvāni anubhavati 
[I,88,i_I,88,iv]	āha kimarthaḥ punar ayam pradhānasya puruṣeṇa saha saṃyogaḥ ucyate na etat iha abhidhānīyam vakṣyati ayam upariṣṭāt ācāryaḥ puruṣasya darśana arthaḥ kaivalya arthaḥ tathā pradhānasya paṅgu andhavat ubhayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ iti āha viyogaḥ tarhi kasmāt nimittāt bhavati iti ucyate vyakta avyakta jña vijñānāt 
[I,88,v]	vyaktam ca avyaktam ca jñaḥ ca vyakta avyakta jñāḥ teṣām vijñānam vyakta avyakta jña vijñānam tasmāt bahuṣu aniyamāt alpācaḥ api jña śabdasya na pūrva nipātaḥ athavā jñānasya sādhakatamam vyaktam tad pūrvaka tvāt avyakta samadhigamasya iti abhihitam yat vā vyaktam ca avyaktam ca te vyakta avyakte te vijānāti iti vyakta avyakta jñaḥ tad vijñānāt saṃyogaḥ nivartate vakṣyati ca etat dṛṣṭā mayā iti upekṣate ekaḥ dṛṣṭā aham iti uparamati anyāḥ iti 
[I,89,i]	tatra rūpa pravṛtti phala lakṣaṇam vyaktam rūpam punar mahān ahaṃkāraḥ pañca tanmātrāṇi ekādaśa indriyāṇi pañca mahābhūtāni sāmānyatas pravṛttiḥ dvividhā hita kāma prayojanā ca ahita pratiṣedha prayojanā ca viśeṣataḥ paṃca karma yonayaḥ vṛtti ādyāḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ ca pañca vāyavaḥ phalam dvividham dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam ca tatra dṛṣṭam siddhi tuṣṭi aśakti viparyaya lakṣaṇam adṛṣṭam brahma ādau stamba paryante saṃsāre śarīra pratilambhaḥ iti etat vyaktam eṣām guṇānām sattva rajaḥ tamasāmaṅga aṅgibhāva gamanāt viśeṣa gṛhītiḥ yadā tu aṅga bhāvam agacchantaḥ nirlikhita viśeṣāḥ vyavatiṣṭhante tadā avyaktam iti ucyante cetanā śakti rūpa tvāt citram guṇa vṛttam jānāti iti jñaḥ 
[I,90,i]	eṣām trayāṇām bhedam abhedam ca vijñāya saṃyoga nivṛttim labhate kasmāt saṃyoga nimitta pratidvandvi bhūta tvāt yoga nimittasya iha yadā adarśana nimittaḥ pradhāna puruṣayoḥ saṃyogaḥ tasmāt asya pratidvandvi bhūtena jñānena viyoga hetunā bhavitavyam kaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ tamaḥ prakāśa vat yathā tamasā tirohitāni dravyāṇi ghaṭa ādīni na upalabhyante tad pratidvandvi bhūtena tu pradīpena prakaśitānām eṣām upalabdhiḥ bhavati tadvat iha api draṣṭavyam iti siddham jñānāt mokṣaḥ uktam ca vṛkṣa agrāt cyuta pādaḥ yadvat anicchat naraḥ patati eva tadvat guṇa puruṣa jñaḥ anicchan api kevalī bhavati 
[I,91,i_I,91,iii]	kim ca anyat āmnāya abhihita tvāt āmnāya nibandhanaḥ hi ayam arthaḥ jñānāt mokṣaḥ iti na yādṛcchikaḥ katham evam hi āha satyam jñānam anantam brahma yaḥ veda nihitam guhāyām parame vyoman saḥ aśnute sarvān kāmān saha brahmaṇā vipaścitā yatas vācaḥ nivartante aprāpya manasā saha ānandam brahmaṇaḥ vidvān na bibheti kutaścana tam eva viditvā amṛta tvam eti na anyaḥ panthāḥ ayanāya vidyate tathā brāhmaṇe api uktam tarati śokam ātma vid brahma vid brahmā eva bhavati iti tasmāt āmnāya prāmāṇyāt api manyāmahe jñānāt mokṣaḥ iti 
[I,92,i]	āha jñāna vācinaḥ amṛta tva nimitta abhyupagamāt mahataḥ āmnāya antarasya ānarthakyam yadi jñāna vācinaḥ āmnāya khaṇḍakāt amṛta tvam avāpyate iti etat abhyupagamyate tena kriyā vācinaḥ mahataḥ āmnāya antarasya ānarthakyam prāptam kim kāraṇam na hi anāyāsena iṣṭa avāptau satyām āyāsa bhūyiṣṭhe karmaṇi pravartamānaḥ kṛtī bhavati iti āha ca akke ced madhu vindeta kim artham parvatam vrajet iṣṭasya arthasya saṃprāptau kaḥ vidvān yatnam ācaret 
[I,93,i_I,93,ii]	ucyate yadi punar karmāṇi atyanta kartavyatayā īṣyante jñāna vācinaḥ āmnāyasya katham arthavat tā siddhā bhavati āha samuccaye tu ubhaya arthavat tvam jñāna karmaṇoḥ tu samuccaye abhyupagamyamāne dvayoḥ api āmnāya arthavattā siddhā bhavati vidvān yajeta vidvān yājayet iti vacanāt tathā sarva puruṣāṇām kratau adhikāraḥ aśrotriya ṣaṇḍha śūdra varjam iti nyāyāt tasmāt jñāna karmaṇoḥ samuccayāt iṣṭa prasiddhiḥ 
[I,94,i]	ucyate na pūrva doṣa aparihārāt yadi niyamataḥ viduṣā eva karmāṇi kartavyāni iti abhyupagamyate tena yaḥ pūrva uktaḥ doṣaḥ saṃsāra abhāva prasaṅgaḥ tasya aparihāraḥ kim ca śāstra hāneḥ ca yaḥ ca śāstram iṣṭāpūrte samupāsyate te dhūmam abhisaṃbhavanti iti tat etasyām kalpanāyām hīyate kim ca anyat bhinna phala tvāt iha abhinna phalāni dravyāṇi samuccīyante tat yathā bhujyaṅgāni sūpa ādīni abhinnam teṣām tṛpti lakṣaṇam phalam iti na ca etat jñāna karmaṇoḥ abhinnam phalam svarga apavarga hetu tvāt jñāna sāmarthāt kaivalyam abhinnam phalam iti ced pūrveṇa aviśeṣaḥ yat uktam saṃsāra abhāva prasaṃgaḥ iti tat anapahṛtam eva bhavati kiṃca anyat śrūyamāṇa phala virodhaḥ ca yat ca kriyāyāḥ phalam śrūyate agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ rāṣṭram agniṣṭomena jayati iti tat virudhyate karmaṇaḥ ca śeṣa bhāvaḥ sva artha upasarjana tve satyartha antara niṣpādaka tvāt yathā avahanti iti evamādyāḥ kriyāḥ svam phalam upasarjanīkṛtya tad dvāreṇa yajeḥ upakurvantyaḥ tad śeṣa bhūtāḥ bhavanti evam kriyā api jñāna phala bhūta tvāt tad śeṣa bhūtā syāt 
[I,96,i]	vidhi sadbhāvāt kriyā prādhānyam iti ced na ukta tvāt katham etat na asti vidhi kṛtaḥ viśeṣaḥ upetya vā tatra api tad utpatteḥ asti hi jñānasya api vidhāyakam śāstram katham evam hi āha yaḥ ātma apahata pāpmā vijighatsaḥ vipipāsaḥ vijaraḥ vimṛtyuḥ viśokaḥ sannyasta saṃkalpaḥ saḥ anveṣṭavyaḥ sa jijñāsitavyaḥ sarvān ca kāmān avāpnoti yaḥ ātmānam anuvidya vijānāti iti prajāpateḥ vacanam śrūyate punar api āha dve vidye veditavye parā ca eva aparā ca yā tasmāt vidhi sadbhāvāt kriyā prādhānyam iti sva pakṣa anurāga mātram etat 
[I,97,i]	dṛṣṭa artha tvāt iti eke eke punar ācāryāḥ manyante dṛṣṭam eva jñānasya ajñāna nivṛtti lakṣaṇam phalam tasmāt na śāstreṇa vidhīyate kim kāraṇam dṛṣṭa arthasya hi karmaṇaḥ na śāstram prayojakam svayam eva arthita tvāt tatra pravṛtteḥ bhujya ādi vat teṣām jñāna vidhāyakāni vākyāni tāni upāya guṇa vidhāna artham anuvāda bhūtāni āśrīyante tat yathā dadhnā juhoti payasā juhoti iti 
[I,97,ii_I,98,i]	yat tu khalu idam ucyate vidvān yajeta vidvān yājayet śrotriyasya ca karmaṇi adhikāraḥ iti tasya ām ayam arthaḥ adhītya vedam kriyā anupūrvaḥ ca jñātvā karmaṇi pravartitavyam evam ca sati na kaścid doṣaḥ yadi punar niyamataḥ eva ātmavidhām karmaṇi adhikāraḥ tena saṃsāra abhāva prasaṃgaḥ svābhāvika tvāt vijñānasya śāsrasya sarva adhikāra virodhaḥ tasmāt na asti samuccayaḥ jñāna karmaṇoḥ aparaḥ āha satyam na asti anayoḥ samuccayaḥ kintarhi sarva arthā kriyā jñānam pratiṣiddha artham ye hi ṣaṇḍhān dhava badhira ādayaḥ karmaṇaḥ atyantam nirākṛtāḥ teṣām jñānāt āśrama antare amṛta tva avāptiḥ itareṣām tū mūla āśrame karmaṇaḥ eva iti tasya na ayam vādinaḥ parihāraḥ iti 
[I,98,ii]	ucyate na sva samaya virodhāt evam bruvāṇasya asya vādinaḥ sva samayaḥ eva virudhyate yat uktam vidvāṃsaḥ prajām na akāmayanta kim prajayā kariṣyāmaḥ atha yat uktam putra eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vitta eṣaṇāyāḥ ca vyutthāya bhaikṣa caryām caranti iti na ca ṣaṇḍānām putra eṣaṇā vyutthānam athavat bhavati deva kṛta tvāt kim ca anyat rahasya bhūta tvāt rahasya bhūtam hi vedānām jñānam yasmāt āha tat ha sma etat āruṇiḥ auddālakiḥ jyeṣṭhāya putrāya provāca idam jyeṣṭha putrāya pitā brahma prabrūyāt praṇāyya antevāsine na anyasmai yasmai kasmaicana yaḥ imāmadbhiḥ parigṛhītām vasunā vasumatīm pūrṇām dadyāt etat eva tatas bhūyaḥ iti 
[I,99,i]	bhavati ca atra param rahasyam vedānām avasāneṣu paṭhyate ṣaṇḍa ādi artham tat iṣṭam ced hiṣṭyā saphala tā śrute vidvān karmāṇi kurvīta iti etat uktam kila śrutau sa ca paṇḍa ādiḥ evasya ādyaḥ atyantam karmaṇaḥ cyutaḥ saḥ eva vartyatām prājñaiḥ kim nyāyyaḥ atha mati bhramaḥ indriya artha anurāgaḥ vā dveṣaḥ vā mokṣa vartmani kaivalya prāpti hetu tva ādyāḥ veda vihitā stutiḥ praśastā yājñavalkya ādyaiḥ viśiṣṭaiḥ tattva niścayāt sā iyam viṣaya rāga andhaiḥ viparīta artha vādibhiḥ vidyā kanyā iva ṣaṇḍāya dīyamānā na śobhate tasmāt rāga anugaiḥ uktām kuhetu pṛtanām imām apohya matimān yuvatyā hi āśramāt āśramam vrajet 
[I,102,i_I,102,ii]	āha samyak upadiṣṭam bhavatā vyakta avyakta jña vijñānāt mokṣaḥ avāpyate idānīm upadeṣṭavyam katham etat trayam pratipattavyam iti ucyate trayasya asya pratipattim dvedhā samāmananti samāsatas vistarataḥ ca tat eva trayam paṃcabhiḥ adhikaraṇaiḥ bhidyate kāni punar adhikaraṇāni iti ucyate prakṛti vikāra vṛttam kārya kāraṇa vṛttam atiśayān atiśaya vṛttam nimitta naimittika vṛttam viṣaya viṣayi vṛttam iti tatra prakṛti vikāra vṛtta pūrvaka tvāt itareṣām adhikaraṇānām tad bhedān vakṣyāmaḥ tat punar caturdhā bhidyate kiṃcid kāraṇam eva na kāryam kiṃcid kāraṇam ca kāryam ca kiṃcid kāryam eva na kāraṇam kiṃcid na eva kāraṇam na ca api kāryam iti 
[I,103,i_I,103,iii]	āha atisāmānya upadiṣṭam etat na asmākam buddhau avatiṣṭhate tasmāt vibhajya upadiśyatām kasya padārthasya kim vṛttam iti ucyate bāḍham upadiśyate mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ mūlam ādhāraḥ pratiṣṭhā iti anartha antaram prakaroti iti prakṛtiḥ mūlam ca asau prakṛtiḥ mūlaprakṛtiḥ mūlaprakṛtiḥ kasya mūlam mahat ādīnām saṃjñā khalu iyam pradhānasya mūlaprakṛtiḥ iti sā ca avikṛtiḥ avikārānutpādya iti arthaḥ 
[I,104,i]	āha samāsa anupapattiḥ viśeṣaṇa antara upādānāt mūlam iti ayam śabdaḥ prakṛti viśeṣaṇa artham upāttaḥ mahat ādi viśeṣaṇa antaram upādatte tatra sa viśeṣaṇānām vṛttiḥ na iti samāsa pratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti samāsa antara vidhānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi etasmin samāse doṣaḥ ayam upapadyate samāsa antaram atra vidhāsyate mūlam prakṛtīnām mūlaprakṛtiḥ iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt doṣa antara upapatteḥ evam api upasarjanam pūrvam nipatati iti ṣaṣṭhyā uktasya upasarjana tvāt pūrva nipātaḥ tatra evam bhavitavyam mūlam prakṛtīnām prakṛti mūlam iti tasmāt idam api asāram iti 
[I,105,i]	ucyate pūrvaḥ eva samāsaḥ astu sambandhi śabdaḥ sa apekṣaḥ nityam vṛttau samasyate yat tu uktam viśeṣaṇa antara upādānāt samāsa anupapattiḥ iti tatra brūmaḥ sambandhi śabdānām sambandhi antaram anapekṣya svarūpa pratilambhaḥ eva na asti iti ākāṃkṣāvatām eva vṛttyā bhavitavyam tat yathā devadattasya guru kulam iti sambandhi śabda tvāt devadatta śabdam apekṣamāṇaḥ api guru śabdaḥ kula śabdena saha vṛttim pratipadyate evam iha api mūlam iti ayam śabdaḥ sambandhi śabda tvāt mahat ādi apekṣaḥ api prakṛti śabdena saha vṛttim pratipadyate iti kiñca anyat vākya pratipādyasya arthasya vṛttau upalabdheḥ yatra hi vākya pratipādyaḥ arthaḥ vṛttyā na labhyate yathā ṛddhasya rājñasya puruṣaḥ iti tatra sa viśeṣaṇānām vṛttiḥ na iti vyavasthitam śāstre gamyate ca iha vākya pratipādyaḥ arthaḥ vṛttau api satyām tasmāt adoṣaḥ ayam iti kim ca jñāpakāt jñāpakam khalu api karma vat karmaṇā tulya kriyaḥ tathā akārasya vivṛtta upadeśaḥ ityādi tasmāt na atra asūyā kartavyā iti 
[I,106,i_I,107,i]	āha avayavasya pratyavamarśa anupapattiḥ saṃjñā śabda tvāt saṃjñā śabdeṣu hi na avayavasya parāmarśaḥ bhavati tat yathā gajakarṇaḥ aśvakarṇaḥ kasya gajasya kasya aśvasya iti ucyate na artha upapatteḥ yatra hi arthaḥ upapadyate bhavati eva tatra saṃjñā śabdeṣu ayava parāmarśaḥ tat yathā saptaparṇāni asya parvaṇi parvaṇi aṣṭau padāni asya paṅktau paṅktau saptaparṇaḥ aṣṭāpadam iti upapadyate ca iha ayam arthaḥ tasmāt adoṣaḥ ayam 
[I,107,ii_I,108,i]	āha mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ prakṛtiḥ iti vaktavyam yat āha mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta iti ucyate prakṛti tva avacanam prakṛti tvam ca mūlaprakṛteḥ na vaktavyam kim kāraṇam arthāt āpatteḥ mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti eva siddham ucyamānam hi tad anarthakam syāt āha prakṛti tva anupapattiḥ satkārya vāda abhyupagamāt prakaroti iti prakṛtiḥ tad bhāvaḥ prakṛti tvam tat ca sati kārye na ghaṭate kasmāt na hi satām ātma ādīnām kāraṇam upapadyate iti 
[I,108,ii]	ucyate tat itaratra api tulyam yathā eva hi satām ātma ādīnām kāraṇam na upapannam evam asatām śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām api iti na asti kaścid viśeṣaḥ tṛtīyā tu viṣāda āvalyā eva koṭiḥ evam ubhaya pakṣa vyudāsāt svapakṣa siddhiḥ iti ced atha api syāt sat asatoḥ kriyā sambandham pratyaviśeṣaḥ upadarśyate bhavatā tena ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ vyudāsaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati na ca ubhaya pakṣa vyudāsāt svapakṣa siddhiḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt uttaratra pratiṣedhāt sa khalu eṣa vādī satkārya vādam pratyācaṣṭe tasmāt svakaḥ eva enam adhikāre nivartayiṣyāmaḥ 
[I,109,i]	āha avikṛti abhidhāna ānarthakyam mūlaprakṛti tvāt tad siddheḥ yadi mūlam sarvāsām prakṛtīnām avikṛtya eva tayā bhavitavyam itarathā hi mūlaprakṛti tva anupapattiḥ yadi khalu api pradhānasya api prakṛti antaram syāt mūlaprakṛti tvam na upapannam bhavet tasmāt mūlaprakṛti tva vacanāt eva tad siddheḥ avikṛti grahaṇam anarthakam iti 
[I,109,ii_I,110,i]	ucyate na anavasthā prasaṃga nivṛtti artha tvāt yathā hi mūla ādīnām bījam prakṛtiḥ tasya api anyat tasya api anyat iti anavasthā evam mahat ādīnām pradhānam mūlaprakṛtiḥ tasya api anyat iti anavasthā prasajyeta sā mā bhūt iti atas tad nivṛtti artham tat abhidhānam āha na hetu anupadeśāt asaṃśayam etat evam syāt na tu hetuḥ atra upadiṣṭaḥ bhavadbhiḥ na ca anupadiṣṭa hetukam vipaścidbhiḥ pratipattum nyāyyam tasmāt ayuktam etat 
[I,110,ii]	ucyate kāraṇa antara pratiṣedhāt puruṣākartṛ tvāt pradhāna ākhyānām guṇānām ca avasthā antara anupapatteḥ avikṛti tva siddhiḥ iha ārabhyamāṇā prakṛtiḥ kāraṇa antaraiḥ īśvara ādibhiḥ ārabhyate puruṣeṇa vā guṇaiḥ vā kiñcātas tat na tāvat kāraṇa antaraiḥ īśvara ādibhiḥ ārabhyate kasmāt pratiṣedhāt yathā kāraṇa antarāṇi na santi tathā uttaratra pratiṣedhaḥ kariṣyate idānīm sattvam rajaḥ tamaḥ puruṣaḥ iti padārtha catuṣṭayam pratijñāyate tatra api puruṣa kartṛ tvam pratyākhyāyate tasmin pratyākhyāte guṇānām eva avasthā antara apekṣaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sūkṣmāṇām mūrti lābhaḥ kāryam nivṛta viśeṣāṇām avibhāga ātmanā avasthānam kāraṇam iti ayam siddhāntaḥ tatra astaṅgata viśeṣāṇām nivṛtta pariṇāma vyāpārāṇām aṅga aṅgi bhāvam anupagacchatām upasaṃhṛta śaktīnām sarva vikāra sāmyam sarva śakti pralayam nissattā sattam nissadasat avyakta lakṣaṇam avasthā antaram upasaṃprāptānām na asti anyat sūkṣmataram avasthā antaram yasya idam pradhāna lakṣaṇam avasthā antaram kāryam syāt tasmāt suṣṭhu ucyate mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti 
[I,12,i_I,12,ii]	mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta mahān ādyaḥ yāsām tāḥ mahat ādyāḥ avayavena vigrahaḥ samudāyaḥ samāsārthaḥ anyathā mahān eva atra aparigṛhītaḥ syāt prakṛtayaḥ ca vikṛtayaḥ ca prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ kāraṇāni kāryāṇi ca iti arthaḥ tatra mahān ahaṃkārasya prakṛtiḥ pradhānasya vikṛtiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ api tanmātra indriya parvaṇoḥ prakṛtiḥ vikṛtiḥ mahataḥ tanmātrāṇi ca bhūtaparvaṇaḥ prakṛtiḥ ahaṃkārasya vikṛtiḥ 
[I,113,i_I,113,iii]	āha sapta grahaṇam kim artham ucyate sapta grahaṇam avadhi pariccheda artham akriyamāṇe hi sapta grahaṇe na jñāyate kriyān prakṛti gaṇaḥ prakṛti vikṛti saṃjñaḥ bhavati tatra mahābhūta indriya parvaṇoḥ api prakṛti tvam prasajyeta āha na etat asti prayojanam pariśeṣa siddheḥ iha bhavatām pañcaśikhānām pañcaviṃśatiḥ tattvāni tatra mūlaprakṛtiḥ avikṛtiḥ iti uktam ṣoḍaśakaḥ tu vikāraḥ na prakṛtiḥ na vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ iti vakṣyati pariśeṣataḥ sapta eva avaśiṣyante tasmāt na arthaḥ tad arthena sapta grahaṇena 
[I,114,i_I,114,ii]	ucyate ahaṃkāra parigraha artham evam tarhi na eva ahaṃkāraḥ vidyate iti patañjaliḥ mahataḥ asmi pratyaya rūpa tva abhyupagamāt tad parihāra artham etat bhaviṣyati āha na uttaratra parigrahāt etat asti na asti prayojanam vakṣyati hi mahatā kaṇṭhena upariṣṭāt ācāryaḥ prakṛteḥ mahān tatas ahaṅkāraḥ iti tena eva idam siddham na arthaḥ tad arthena api sapta grahaṇena 
[I,114,iii_I,115,i]	ucyate rūpa bhede api tattva abheda jñāpana artham evam tarhi dharma ādīni aṣṭau rūpāṇi buddheḥ vakṣyamāṇāni ahaṃkāraḥ ca vaikārika taijasa bhūta ādi rūpa tvāt tri lakṣaṇaḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ tatra rūpa bhedāt tattva bhedaḥ mā bhūt iti evam artham sapta grahaṇam kriyate āha hetum antareṇa apratipatteḥ kaṇṭha uktam api yuktim antareṇa na tarka śīlāḥ pratipadyante kimpunaḥ kleśa upapāditam tasmāt atra samādhiḥ vācyaḥ katham aneka rūpā buddhiḥ ekā eva iti 
[I,115,ii_I,116,iii]	ucyate na uttaratra vicāraṇāt uttaratra etat vicārayiṣyāmaḥ kim aneka rūpa āvirbhāve api tat eva tat vastu bhavati āhosvit rūpa bhedāt tattva bhedaḥ tasmāt iha tāvat dṛśyatām iti siddham mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta iti ṣoḍaśakaḥ tu vikāraḥ ṣoḍaśa parimāṇasya saḥ ayam ṣoḍaśakaḥ saṃghaḥ tasya parimāṇam saṃkhyāyāḥ saṃjñā saṃgha sūtra adhyayaneṣu iti kan pratyayaḥ āha kaḥ punar ayam ṣoḍaśakaḥ iti ucyate pañca mahābhūtāni ekādaśa indriyāṇi tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ 
[I,116,iv^1]	āha śakyaḥ punar ayam arthaḥ antareṇa api tuśabdam avāptum katham mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta iti hi upadiṣṭam purastāt tatas ahaṅkārata mātra pūrvaka tve siddhe sati indriya mahābhūta parvaṇoḥ punar śruteḥ niyamaḥ bhaviṣyati tat yathā pañca pañcanakhāḥ bhakṣyāḥ iti atra kṣudh pratīkāra samarthānām dravyāṇām arthāt eva sarveṣām bhakṣaṇe samprāpte punar śruteḥ niyamaḥ bhavati tadvat idam draṣṭavyam iṣṭataḥ avadhāraṇa artham iti ced syāt matam iṣṭataḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ tarhi tuśabdaḥ bhaviṣyati katham nāma ṣoḍaśakaḥ vikāraḥ eva iti yathā vijñāyate ṣoḍaśakaḥ tu vikāraḥ iti evam mā jñāyi iti 
[I,116,iv^2]	yadi evam asthāne tarhi tuśabdaḥ paṭhitaḥ ṣoḍaśakaḥ vikāraḥ tu iti vaktavyam atha matam vṛtta paripūrana artha m ayam asmin pradeśe paṭhitaḥ tuśabdaḥ yatra nirdoṣaḥ tatra eva ayam draṣṭavyaḥ iti etad anupapannam kasmāt asandehāt mahat ādyāḥ prakṛti vikṛtayaḥ sapta iti apadiṣṭe kim iti sāṃśayikā bhaviṣyāmaḥ tasmāt pelavam asya pāṭhe prayojanam paśyāmaḥ atha ayam abhiprāyaḥ syāt yadi api etat arthataḥ siddham tathā api ayam ācāryaḥ sphuṭa pratipatti artham avadhāraṇam pratyādriyate kim kāraṇam yasmāt vicitrāḥ sūtra kārāṇām abhiprāya gatayaḥ 
[I,116,iv^3]	tat yathā bhagavān pāṇiniḥ na kye rātsasya iti evamādiṣu antareṇa prayatnam iṣṭataḥ avadhāraṇe siddhe anyatra aja ādī guṇa vacanāt eva stautiṇyoḥ eva ṣaṇya bhāsāt iti evamādiṣu yatnam karoti tadvat iha api draṣṭavyam iti etad anupapannam kasmāt aśakya tvāt sati vā punar avadhāraṇa artha tve tuśabdasya katham iva atra śakyam avadhāraṇam pratipattum yāvatā mahābhūtānām api śarīra ādi lakṣaṇam kāryam upalabhyate iti tatra kecid samādhim āhuḥ śarīra ādīnām anartha antara bhāvāt pṛthivī ādīnām aprakṛti tvam yasmāt kila pṛthivī ādīnām sanniveśa viśeṣa mātram kāryam muṣṭi granthi kuṇḍala ādi vanna artha antara bhūtam 
[I,116,iv^4_I,117,i]	atas eṣām aprakṛti tvam iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt aviśeṣāt sarvam eva hi sāṃkhyānām kāryam anartha antara bhūtam tatra etasyām kalpanāyām sarva tattvānām aprakṛti tvam prasajyeta atha etat aniṣṭam satkārya vyāghātaḥ anye punar āhuḥ apariṇāmi tvāt mahābhūtānām vikāritvā anavadhāraṇam iti tat api anupapannam kasmāt pratyakṣa upalabdheḥ pratyakṣatas eva upalabhyate mahābhūtānām kalila aṅkura kṣīra ādi pariṇāmaḥ anumāna grāhyaḥ tu tattva antarāṇām tat etat adhara uttaram bhavati tasmāt ayuktam etat na tarhi idam pratipattavyam ṣoḍaśakaḥ vikāraḥ eva iti 
[I,120,i]	ucyate pratipattavyam kim kāraṇam tattva antara anupapatteḥ iha puruṣa arthena hetunā sāmyāt pracyutānām guṇānām yaḥ ayam mahat ādiḥ viśeṣa antaḥ vipariṇāmaḥ sa tattva antara utpatti niyamena vyavatiṣṭhate na tu pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ tattva antara utpattiḥ asti tasmāt eteṣām vikāra tvam eva iti kim ca anyat grāhaka antara abhāvāt yathā tanmātraiḥ ārabdheṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu ahaṃkārāt tat yogyam grāhaka antaram indriya lakṣaṇam utpadyate na evam pṛthivī ādi vikārāṇām ghaṭa ādīnām grāhaka antaram asti tasmāt na tattva antaram atas ca pṛthivī ādayaḥ vikārāḥ eva iti kim ca anyat pradhāne prakṛti bhāva pratyasta mayavat teṣu vikāra bhāva pratyasta mayāt yathā pradhānāt sūkṣmataram avasthā antaram na asti iti tatra prakṛti bhāvasya pratyasta mayaḥ tathā teṣu vikāra bhāva pratyasta mayaḥ tasmāt yuktam ucyate ṣoḍaśakaḥ ayam vikāraḥ eva iti 
[I,121,i_I,122,ii]	āha puruṣe tarhi kā pratipattiḥ iti ucyate na prakṛtiḥ na vikṛtiḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ na hi ayam avasthā antaram pratipadyate no khalu api avasthā antarasya avasthā antaram bhavati iti āha na etat yuktim antareṇa śraddhīyate tasmāt upapādyatām katham asya aprakṛti tvam avikṛti tvam ca iti 
[I,122,iii_I,123,i]	ucyate prakṛti tva anupapattiḥ uttaratra pratividhānāt tasmāt ca viparyāsāt iti atra yuktim upadekṣyāmaḥ tasmāt tāvat asya aprakṛti tvam avikṛti tvam pradhāna vat yathā pradhānam evam ayam api puruṣaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ kāraṇa antaraiḥ īśvara ādibhiḥ na ārabhyate kasmāt pratiṣedhāt yathā kāraṇa antarāṇi na santi tathā uttaratra pratiṣedhaḥ kariṣyate puruṣa antaraiḥ samatvāt samāḥ sarve puruṣāḥ na ca samānām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kim ca niṣkriya tvāt śuddha tvāt ca eṣām vipariṇāma lakṣaṇā parispanda lakṣaṇā vā kriyā vibhu tvāt anupapannā kasmāt eṣām itaretara anārambhaka tvāt na guṇaiḥ bhinna jātīyaka tvāt iha acetanāḥ guṇāḥ iti etat pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ yat ca yena ārabhyate tat ca tad mayam bhavati yadi guṇaiḥ puruṣāṇām ārambhaḥ tadā teṣām api acetana tvam syāt cetanāḥ tu te tasmāt na guṇaiḥ ārabhyante iti siddham etat kiṃcid kāraṇam eva na kāryam kiṃcid kāraṇam kāryam ca kiṃcid kāryam eva kiṃcid na eva kāraṇam na eva kāryam iti caturvidham kāraṇa vṛttam pratipāditam etet pratijñā piṇḍasūtram atra yat apadiṣṭam bhavadbhiḥ asmin śāstre prameyam iti avagantavyam 
[I,124,i_I,125,ii]	āha atha asya prameyasya kutas siddhiḥ iti ucyate prameya siddhiḥ pramāṇāt hi pramīyate tat iti prameyam prameyasya siddhiḥ prameya siddhiḥ siddhiḥ adhigamaḥ avabodhaḥ iti arthaḥ pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam karaṇa sādhanaḥ lyuṭ tat ekam eva buddheḥ eka tva abhyupagamāt upādhi vaśāt tu bhinnam āśrīyate pratyakṣam anumānam ityādi tasya yaḥ asau upādhikṛtaḥ bhedaḥ tam anāśritya prameya paricchedaka tva sāmānyam aṅgīkṛtya ekavacana nirdeśaḥ kriyate pramāṇāt iti etasmāt prameya siddhiḥ iti avagantavyam katham vrīhi ādi vat yathā vrīhyā ati prameyam prastha ādinā pramāṇena paricchidyate evam iha api vyakta ādi prameyam pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇena paricchidyate iti iha hi śabdaḥ idānīm kimarthaḥ syāt avadhāraṇa arthaḥ iti 
[I,125,iii]	āha yadi evam hi śabda avacanam avadhāraṇa anupapatteḥ na hi etasmin sūtre kathaṃcid avadhāraṇam upapadyate tasmāt avacanam eva hi śabdasya nyāyyam prameyasya eva iti ced na anyasya asambhavāt sati hi vyabhicāra sambhave vastu avadhāryate tat yathā gauḥ eva ayam na aśvaḥ devadattaḥ eva ayam na yajñadattaḥ iti na ca prameya aprameyayoḥ pramāṇa paricchedya tve asti prasaṃgaḥ yat nivṛtti artham prameyasya eva iti avadhāryate pramāṇebhyaḥ eva iti ced na ārṣa jñāna virodha prasaṃgāt parama ṛṣeḥ hi bhagavataḥ jñānam sāṃsiddhi kam apramāṇa pūrvakam iti vaḥ pakṣaḥ sāṃsiddhikāḥ ca bhāvāḥ prākṛtikāḥ vaikṛtāḥ ca dharma ādyāḥ iti vacanāt ubhaya avadhāraṇe sati ubhayoḥ api pakṣayoḥ ye doṣāḥ te prasajyante tasmāt ayuktam etat siddhiḥ eva iti ced na anekāntāt kadācid dyayam pramātā sannihite api āt itya ādau liṅge diś niścaya ādiṣu artheṣu pratihanyate tasmāt anekāntāt siddhiḥ eva iti etat ayuktam avadhāraṇam 
[I,127,i^1]	ucyate yat uktam hi śabda āvacanam avadhāraṇa anupapatteḥ iti astu pramāṇebhyaḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam yat tu uktam ārṣa jñāna virodha prasaṃgaḥ iti ayama doṣaḥ kasmāt siddha rūpa tvāt sādhya māna rūpāṇi hi vastūni na antarīyaka tvāt sva rūpa niṣpattaye sādhana sambandham pratyākāṃkṣāvanti bhavanti siddha rūpam tu bhagavataḥ parama ṛṣeḥ jñānam tasmāt asya sādhana sambandham pratyākāṅkṣā na upapadyate iti athavā punar astu siddhiḥ eva iti avadhāraṇam yat tu uktam anekāntāt iti tad anupapannam kasmāt sattva ādīnām aṅga aṅgi bhāva aniyamāt tamaḥ prakarṣasāmagryāt pramāṇa vaikalya upapatteḥ 
[I,127,i^2]	iha sattva ādīnām aniyataḥ aṅga aṅgi bhāvaḥ deśa kāla nimitta sāmarthyāt hi kadācid sattvam prakṛṣyate kadācid rajaḥ kadācid tamaḥ sattva prakarṣaḥ ca prakāśa rūpa tvāt pramāṇam tatra yadā tamaḥ prakṛṣyate tadā tena abhibhūta tvāt sattvasya tad kāryam anumānam tri kāla aṅgam uttiṣṭhate iti atas satyām api āditya ādi liṅga pravṛttau diś niścaya ādiṣu artheṣu pratihanyate itarathā tu na svarūpa hānam yasya tu niṣpatti vaikalyāt pramāṇa pratibandhaḥ na iṣṭaḥ tasya svarūpa hānam pramāṇānām prāptam katham etāvat hi teṣām svarūpam yat uta prameya paricchedaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat avadhāraṇa arthaḥ hi śabdaḥ 
[I,129,i_I,129,iii]	āha bahūni pramāṇāni ācāryaiḥ abhyupagamyante tāni sarvāṇi kim bhavān anumanyate na iti ucyate trividham pramāṇam iṣṭam kintarhi vidhānam vidhā tisraḥ vidhāḥ asya tat trividham tri prakāram iti arthaḥ anena etat ācaṣṭe ekam eva buddhi lakṣaṇam sattvam nimitta antara anugraha upajanitābhiḥ kārya viśeṣa paricchinna rūpa bhedābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upakārāt bhinnam iva pratyavabhāsamānam dṛṣṭa ādi śabda vācyam bhavati na tu yathā tantra antarīyāṇām viṣaya upanipātibhiḥ indriyaiḥ upajanita avadhyaḥ buddhayaḥ tathā iha vidyante yāḥ parikalpyamānāḥ svatantrāṇi trīṇi pramāṇāni syuḥ 
[I,130,i_I,130,ii]	syāt matam katham punar pramāṇa lakṣaṇānām śaktī nāmaka vastu sanniveśa rūpa bhedāḥ bhavanti iti ucyate sattva ādi vat yathā sattva ādīnām guṇānām eka śabda ādi vastu sanniveśe api prakāśa ādi kārya bhedāt rūpa saṃkaraḥ na bhavati yathā vā śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām eka dravya sanniveśe api grāhaka antara gamyaka tvāt yathā vā kartṛ karaṇa adhikaraṇa sampradāna apādāna karma lakṣaṇānām śaktīnām eka dravya sanniveśe api kārya viśeṣa paricchinnāni svarūpāṇi na saṃkīryante tadvat idam draṣṭavyam śakti antara upajanane vastu antara upapattiḥ iti ced na anabhyupagamāt na hi kṣaṇa bhaṅga sāhasam yuktim antareṇa daṇḍa bhayāt api pratipadyāmahe na tu tasyām avasaraḥ iti sthīyatām tāvat 
[I,131,i_I,131,iii]	āha katham punar etat gamyate yathā trividham eva pramāṇam na punar anekavidham api iti ucyate sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt sarvāṇi ca tāni pramāṇāni sarva pramāṇāni siddhasya bhāvaḥ siddha tvam sarva pramāṇānām siddhatvam sarva pramāṇa siddha tvam siddha tvam antarbhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ tasmāt sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt tasmin eva trividhe pramāṇaḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ sarveṣām para parikalpitānām pramāṇānām asmin eva trividhe pramāṇe antarbhāvāt iti yāvat uktam syāt tāvat idam ucyate sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt iti athavā sarva pramāṇeṣu siddham sarva pramāṇa siddham saptamī siddha śuṣka pakva bandhaiḥ iti samāsaḥ yathā sāṃkāśya siddhaḥ pāṭaliputra siddhaḥ iti tad bhāvaḥ pramāṇa siddha tvam tasmāt sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt kasya trividhasya pramāṇasya iti vākya śeṣaḥ 
[I,132,i_I,133,iii]	kena punar ākāreṇa trividham pramāṇam siddham iti ucyate paraspara viśeṣāt anyāni punar asmāt trayāt yathā abhinnāni tathā pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ āha kimpunaḥ tat trividham pramāṇam iti ucyate dṛṣṭam anumānam āpta vacanam ca iti tatra dṛṣṭam nāma upātta viṣaya indriya vṛtti upanipātī yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ anumānam dvayoḥ avinābhā vinoḥ ekam pratyakṣeṇa pramāya tad pūrvakam sambandī antare yat paścāt mānam bhavati āpta vacanam tu pramāṇa bhūta dvārakaḥ atyanta parokṣe arthe niścayaḥ iti uddeśa mātram idam mūla lakṣaṇam tu ācāryaḥ vakṣyati svayam eva prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭam ityādi 
[I,134,i_I,134,iv]	āha traividya anupapattiḥ nyūna adhika śravaṇāt tantra antarīyāḥ kecid catvāri pramāṇāni icchanti pratyakṣa anumāna upamāna śabdāḥ pramāṇāni iti vacanāt tathā ṣaṣ iti anye pratyakṣam anumānam ca śabdam ca upamayā saha artha āpattiḥ abhāvaḥ ca hetavaḥ sadhya sādhakāḥ iti abhidhānāt etāni sambha vaitihya ceṣṭā sahitāni navā iti apare pratyakṣa anumāne eva iti vaiśeṣika bauddhāḥ tatra katham idam niścīyate trividham eva pramāṇam na punar nyūnam adhikam vā iti ucyate kimpunar idam upamānam nāma 
[I,135,i]	āha prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam prasiddhaḥ prajñātaḥ tena sādharmyāt sādhyasya aprasiddhasya sādhanam adhigamaḥ yaḥ tad upamānam avabodha vidhiḥ tu yena anupalabdhaḥ gavayaḥ sa tasya upalabdhi artham adhigata gavayam paryanuyuṅkte kiṃrūpaḥ gavayaḥ iti sa tasmai ācaṣṭe yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti tatra pratipattyā atyanta anupalakṣita gavaya svarūpaḥ vyākhyātṛ pratipādita prasiddha vastu sādharmya jñānāhita saṃskāraḥ pratipadyate nūnam evaṃrūpaḥ gavayaḥ iti aparaḥ āha pratirāpta vacana upajanita prasiddha vastu sādharmya jñānāhita saṃskārasya uttara kālam pratyakṣeṇa tam upalabhya yā samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ ayam asau arthaḥ asya śabdasya samākhyāḥ iti tat upamānam ucyate 
[I,135,ii]	yadi evam upamā aitihi āvacanam āpta upadeśa siddheḥ yathā gauḥ evam gavayaḥ iti ca āpta upadeśa balāt pratipattā aprasiddham gavayam upalabhate na sādharmya mātrāt tasmāt na śabdāt pṛthak upamā yat tu khalu iti ha uvāca yājñavalkyasya iti etat aitihyam nāma pramāṇa antaram upakalpyate tat api vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣa tvāt na śabdāt artha antaram
