[I,13,i]	āha na sādharmya apekṣa tvāt yadi hi āpta upadeśaḥ upamā syāt tena yathā svarge apsarasaḥ uttarāḥ kuravaḥ iti evamādiṣu antareṇa sādharmya upādānam pratipattiḥ bhavati evam iha api syāt gavayantu ayam ākhyātā pratipādayiṣyan prasiddha sādharmya garbham śabdam upādatte na kevalam pratipattā api tasmāt eva pratipadyate na śabda mātrāt tasmāt pṛthak eva asya upadeśaḥ kartavyaḥ śabda vyāpārāt tad antarbhāvaḥ iti ced syāt matam śabda vyāpāra sahitaḥ ayam prasiddha sādharmya lakṣaṇa arthaḥ gavaya pratipattau na kevalaḥ tasmāt asya tatra antarbhāvaḥ iti tat api anupapannam kasmāt vīta āvītayoḥ api tad prasaṅgāt vīta a ītau api hetū para pratipādana artham upādīyamānau śabda vyāpāram apekṣete tayoḥ api āpta vacana tva prasaṃgaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt na upamānam āpta upadeśaḥ 
[I,137,i^1]	ucyate sādharmya avyatireka upāya bhūta tvāt ākhyātṛ prāmāṇyāt eva pratipattuḥ gavaya vijñānam upapadyate sa tu kauśalāt durupapādaḥ ayam arthaḥ iti kṛtvā prasiddha sādharmyam upādatte tasmāt ākhyātuḥ gavaya pratipādana artham upāya bhūtam sādharmyam upādadānasya śabdāt artha antaram udbhavati atha evaṃjātīyakānām api pramāṇa antara tvam iṣyate tena atyalpam idam ucyate catvāri pramāṇāni iti kim tarhi pāṇi vihāra akṣi nikoca prabhṛtīnām api upasaṃkhyānam kartavyam kiṃca vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣa tvāt yatra hi artha vaśāt pratipattiḥ utpadyate na tatra pratipattā vaktṛ viśeṣam apekṣate dṛṣṭa arthaḥ ayam adṛṣṭa arthaḥ ayam iti tat yathā anumāne asti ca upamāne vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣā tasmāt na śabdāt artha antaram tat avaśyam ca etat evam vijñeyam 
[I,137,i^2]	yaḥ hi manyate prasiddha sādharmyāt eva gavaya pratipattiḥ iti yathāśvaḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti etasmāt api tasya sampratipattiḥ syāt na ca arhati bhavitum mithyājñāna tvāt yat tu khalu idam ucyate yatas samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ iti tad upamānam iti etad anupapannam kasmāt anavasthā prasaṃgāt tat yathā bahuṣu niṣaṇṇeṣu kaḥ atra devadattaḥ iti ukte yaḥ mukuṭī kuṃḍalī vyūḍha uraskaḥ tāmra āyata akṣaḥ iti pratyāha tatas ca samākhyā sambandha pratipattiḥ iti pramāṇa antara tva prasaṅgaḥ iti evam anavasthā pramāṇānām syāt aniṣṭam ca etat evam hi na tāvat paratas upamānam pramāṇa antaram yadā svayam eva gām gavayam ca upalabhya vikalpayati yathā ayam tathā ayam iti tadā tasya arthasya pramāṇa antareṇa adhigata tvāt pramāṇam eva tat na bhavati iti tasmāt suṣṭhu uktam ayam aitihi āpta vacanam āpta upadeśāt siddheḥ iti 
[I,140,i^1]	kiñca anyat arthāpatti saṃbhava abhāva ceṣṭānām anumāna siddheḥ avacanam iti anuvartate tatra arthāpattiḥ nāma yatra arthayoḥ pūrvam avyabhicāram upalabhya paścāt anyatarasya darśanāt śravaṇāt vā anyatarasmi pratipattiḥ bhavati darśana ādyāḥ guḍam upalabhya mādhuryam indriya antara viṣayam pratipadyate śravaṇāt yathā guḍa śabdam śrutvā mādhuryam aśabdakam pratipadyate iti aparā khalva artha āpattiḥ yatra dharmayoḥ avyabhicāram upalabhya tat pratidvandvinoḥ api sāhacarya kalpanā sā tu dvividhā vyabhicāriṇī ca avyabhicāriṇī ca tatra vyabhicāriṇī yathā sāvayavam anityam iti ukte arthāt āpannam niravayavam nityam iti 
[I,140,i^2]	tat ca karma ādiṣu adṛṣṭam iti eṣānaikāntika tvāt pramāṇam eva na bhavati iti yā tu avinā bhāvinī avyabhicāriṇī yathā kesari vara ahayoḥ upagahvare sannipātam upalabhya uttara kālam kevalam kesariṇam varāha vraṇa aṃkita śarīram prayāntam upalabhya pratipadyate jitaḥ varāhaḥ iti tad anumānam katham yasmāt kesarivarāhaya uḥ yau jaya parājayau tayoḥ avyabhicārī sambandhaḥ tatra yadā kesariṇaḥ jayam upalabhya avyabhicāriṇam itarasya parājayam pratipadyate kim anyat syāt ṛte anumānāt adhigata ubhaya sambandhi samudāyasya hi pratipattuḥ pratyakṣībhūta anyatara sambandhinaḥ yā sambandhi antara pratipattiḥ tad anumānam ittham ca artha āpattiḥ atas na tasmāt pṛthak bhavitum arhati 
[I,141,i]	sambhavaḥ nāma droṇaḥ prasthaḥ iti ukte ardha droṇa ādīnām sannidhānam avasīyate iti ayam api sāhacarya kalpanayā artha āpattiḥ eva katham yasmāt ukta parimāṇe dravye droṇa śabdaḥ vartate na nyūne na adhike tatra droṇaḥ iti ukte yat atyanta saha bhuvām tad avayavānām anya śabda vācyānām api sannidhānam tad artha āpattiḥ eva sa ca anumānam iti uktam 
[I,142,i]	abhāvaḥ nāma tat yathā dhūmasya bhāvāt agneḥ bhāvaḥ pratīyate evam dhūma abhāvāt agni abhāvaḥ iti ayam pratidvandvi sāha carya kalpa naya arthāpattiḥ abhihitaḥ tatra yadā vyabhicāra sāhacarya kalpanā tadā pramāṇa abhāvaḥ eva tat yathā yaḥ guṇa aṅgāra ādiṣu dhūma abhāvaḥ na agni abhāvaḥ yatra tu kvacid ekāntaḥ syāt yathākṛtaka tvāt nityaḥ iti tatra anumānam katham sāhacarya upapatteḥ kṛtaka tva anitya tva vat 
[I,143,i]	anye tu abhāvam anyathā varṇayanti tat yathā gehe na asti caitraḥ iti ukte bahis asti iti sampratyayaḥ bhavati tatra geha abhāvaḥ bahirbhāva sampratipatti hetuḥ artha antara āpattiḥ eva pratidvandvi sāha carya kalpanayā katham yathā eva hi divā na bhuṅkte devadattaḥ pīne iti atra abhojana pratiyoginaḥ medura tvasya upalambhāt divā pratiyogini kāle rātrau bhujiḥ avasīyate evam iha api geha abhāva abhidhāna sāmarthyāt tad pratiyogini viparyayaḥ kalpyate anyathā tu yadi abhāvaḥ eva abhipretaḥ syāt na asti caitraḥ eva iti brūyāt arthāpattiḥ ca anumānam 
[I,143,ii_I,144,ii]	ceṣṭā nāma abhiprāya sūcakaḥ kaścid eva udara tāḍana añjali karaṇa ādiḥ śarīra vyāpāraḥ sa hi bubhukṣā ādīni apratīyamānāni pratipādayati iti pramāṇam iti ucyate sa ca anumānam eva kasmāt yasmāt bhojana icchā ādi sahacaraḥ hi vyāpāraḥ anuṣṭhīyamānaḥ yadi sahacāriṇam gamayati tadā na anumānāt pṛthak iti śakyam pratijñātum āha pratibhā tarhi pramāṇa antaram bhaviṣyati ucyate kā iyam pratibhā nāma 
[I,144,iii]	āha yaḥ ayam anādau saṃsāre deva manuṣyatiraśca āma bhinne arthe bāhye strī ādau pratyaye pūrva abhyāsa vāsanā apekṣaḥ kuṇapa kāminī bhakṣya ādi ākāra bheda bhinna pratyayaḥ itikartavyatā aṅgam utpadyate sā hi pratibhā tathā ca uktam yathā abhyāsam hi vākyebhyaḥ vinā api arthena jāyate sva pratyaya anukāreṇa pratipattiḥ anekadhā 
[I,144,iv]	yena hi yaḥ arthaḥ abhyastassukha ādi tvena tasya vinā api tena arthena śabda mātrāt pratipattiḥ utpadyate tat yathā vyāghraḥ atra prativasati iti ukte vinā api bāhyena arthena abhyāsa vaśāt eva sveda vepathu prabhṛtayaḥ bhavanti tasmāt pratibhā eva deva manuṣya tiraḥ ca amiti kartavyatā aṅga tvāt pramāṇam iti āha ca pramāṇa tvena tām lokaḥ sarvaḥ samanugacchati vyavahārāḥ pravartante tiraścām api tad vaśāt 
[I,145,i^1]	ucyate pratibhāyāḥ dṛṣṭa ādi vyatirekena rūpa antara anupapatteḥ avacanam iti anuvartate yadi pūrva abhyāsa vāsanā apekṣaḥ pratyayaḥ pratibhā iti upagamyate tena tarhi asau pratyakṣam anumānam āpta vacanam ca iti etat āpannam kasmāt yatas na dṛṣṭa ādi vyatirekeṇa pratyakṣa rūpam kadācid api upalabhāmahe tasmāt na tebhyaḥ artha antaram pratibhā ārṣa pratyaya sambhavāt ayuktam iti ced syāt etat asti ārṣaḥ hi dṛṣṭa ādi vyatirekeṇa sarva padārtheṣu sāṃsiddhikaḥ pratyayaḥ sa prātibho bhaviṣyati iti etat ca api ayuktam kasmāt ukta tvāt uktam etat siddha rūpam bhagavataḥ parama ṛṣeḥ jñānam atas na pramāṇa apekṣam iti yoginām iti ced na anabhyupagamāt na hi yogi nām apramāṇa pūrvakam jñānam iti yathā tathā vakṣyāmaḥ sa laukikaḥ iti ced na aniścita tvāt syāt etat asti laukikaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭa ādi vyatirekeṇa 
[I,145,i^2]	tat yathā santamase vrajataḥ drāk iti vijñānam utpadyate asti me pratīghāti dravyam purastāt ūrdhvam avasthitam iti tat ca na evam kasmāt aniścita tvāt na hi tatra niścayaḥ utpadyate idam tat dravyam asti puratas vā vyaktam asti iti na ca aniścitam pramāṇa jñānam iṣyate kiṃca anyat anavasthā prasaṃgāt yadi ca evaṃjātīyataḥ api pratyayaḥ pramāṇam abhyupagamyate tena anavasthā prāpnoti kim kāraṇam anavasthānāt vikaraṇasya kāma krodha la ubhaya viṣāda dvārakaḥ vikalpaḥ samyak mithyā vā yasmāt anekaḥ utpadyate tasmāt na laukikaḥ pratyayaḥ pratibhā yat tu khalu idam ucyate abhyāsa vāsana apekṣā satsu api vyāghra ādiṣu pratipattiḥ utpadyate iti satyam etat sā tu mithyājñāna tvāt pramāṇa tvena na parigṛhyate iti ayam adoṣaḥ tasmāt siddham dṛṣṭa ādi vyatirekeṇa rūpa antar anupapatteḥ pratibhāyāḥ pṛthak anabhidhānam tatas ca sarva pramāṇa siddha tvāt trividham pramāṇam iṣṭam iti sthitam etat 
[I,149,i_I,150,i]	āha astu evam etat lakṣaṇa anabhidhānāt tad apratipattiḥ tasmāt tat abhidhānam anavasthitam hi dṛṣṭa ādīnām lakṣaṇam dṛṣṭi vaicitryāt indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam iti kecid tathā ātma indriya manaḥ artha sannikarṣāt yat niṣpadyate tat anyat iti eke sat samprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma tat pratyakṣam iti apare śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ iti vārṣa gaṇāḥ kalpanā apoḍham iti anye ittham anavasthitam lakṣaṇam iti dṛṣṭa ādīnām apratipattiḥ tasmāt lakṣaṇam abhidhānīyam ucyate prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭam
[I,150,ii]	viṣiṇvanti iti viṣayāḥ śabda ādayaḥ athavā viṣīyante upalabhyante iti arthaḥ te ca dvividhāḥ viśiṣṭāḥ aviśiṣṭāḥ ca viśiṣṭāḥ pṛthivī ādi lakṣaṇāḥ asmad ādi gamyāḥ aviśiṣṭāḥ ca tanmātra lakṣaṇāḥ yoginām ūrdhvasrotasām ca gamyāḥ vakṣyati ca etat upariṣṭāt buddhīndriyāṇi teṣām pañca viśeṣa aviśeṣa viṣayāṇi adhyavasāyaḥ buddhiḥ iti ca vakṣyati viṣayam prati vartate iti prativiṣayam kintat indriyam tasmin yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ sa prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ upātta viṣayāṇām indriyāṇām vṛtti upanipāti sattva udreka āt arajaḥ tamaskam yat prakāśa rūpam tat dṛṣṭam iti yāvat tat dṛṣṭam pratyakṣam iti arthaḥ etad pramāṇam anena yaḥ cetanā śakteḥ anugrahaḥ tad phalam prameyāḥ śabda ādayaḥ evam uttaratra api pramāṇa phala bhāvaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ 
[I,152,i_I,152,v]	āha kim punar idam pramāṇāt phalam artha antaram āhosvidh anarthāntaram katham tāvat bhavitum arhati anartha antaram iti āha kasmāt adhigama rūpa tvāt adhigama rūpam hi jñānam tasya utpattyā eva adhigataḥ arthaḥ iti kutas phala bhedaḥ iti ucyate karaṇa bhāvaḥ idānīm katham syāt āha karaṇa bhāvaḥ tu prasiddhi vaśāt viṣaya nirbhāsā hi jñānasya utpattiḥ adhigama rūpā api loke sa vyāpārā iva pratītā iti kalpanayā karaṇa bhāvaḥ abhyupagamyate na paramārthataḥ 
[I,153,i]	ucyate phalasya artha antara bhāvaḥ adhikaraṇa bhedāt buddhi āśrayam hi pramāṇa madhyavasāya ākhyam puruṣa āśrayam phalam anugraha lakṣaṇam na ca bhinna adhikaraṇayoḥ ekatvam arhati bhavitum yat tu uktam adhigama rūpa tvāt jñānam eva phalam iti tad anupapannam kasmāt asiddha tvāt yathā eva hi ghaṭa ādayaḥ arthāḥ jñānam antareṇa na tad rūpāḥ na atad rūpāḥ iti na śakyam pratipattum evam jñānam api puruṣa pratyayam antareṇa na viṣaya rūpam na aviṣaya rūpam tathā ca śāstram tad saṃyogāt acetanam cetanāvat iva liṅgam iti vacanāt atas puruṣa pratyayam antareṇa jñānam adhigama rūpam iti sāṃkhyam pratyasiddham etat ubhaya pakṣa prasiddhena ca vyavahāraḥ puruṣa abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced naḥ uttaratra pratipādanāt saṃghāta para artha tvāt iti atra puruṣa astitvam pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt siddha madhya vasāya pramāṇa vādinaḥ pramāṇāt phalam artha antaram iti 
[I,154,i_I,154,iii]	āha yadi hi adhyavasāyaḥ pramāṇam katham laukikaḥ prayogaḥ arthavān bhavati pratyakṣam vastu iti ucyate viṣaye pratyakṣa śabdaḥ tad pramita tvāt tad kāraṇā tvāt ca yathā prastha pramitaḥ vrīhi rāśiḥ prastha śabda vācyaḥ bhavati evam pratyakṣa pramitaḥ arthaḥ pratyakṣa śabda vācyaḥ syāt āha na anyatra api tad prasaṅgāt yadi pratyakṣa pramita tvāt viṣaye pratyakṣa śabdaḥ tena tarhi anumāmapramitaḥ arthaḥ anumānam iti syāt śabda pramitaḥ arthaḥ śabdaḥ iti na ca agni svarga ādayaḥ pramāṇa śabda vācyāḥ bhavanti tasmāt viṣama liṅga liṅgi pūrvakam yoginām ca dhyāna bhūmikāsu viharatām anumāna āgama atītam prātibham yat vijñānam utpadyate tad upasaṃkhyeyam syāt kutas na hi sukha ādayaḥ śrotra ādi vṛtti grāhyāḥ yoginām ca atindriyam jñānam iti yathānyāsam tu kriyamāṇe te api viṣayāḥ teṣām yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tasya pratyakṣa tvam kena vāryate 
[I,156,i_I,156,iii]	ucyate tad abhāvāditaratra apravṛttiḥ pramāṇa antare tu na asti sāmānyam nimittam katham anumīyate anena iti anumānam na ca agni ādibhiḥ kaścid anumīyate iti atas tulya śabda vācya tā na bhavati āha adhyavasāya grahaṇam kim artham ucyate atiprasaṃga nivṛtti artham prativiṣayam dṛṣṭa mitīyati ucyamāne yāvat kiṃcid prativiṣayam vartate anugrāhaka tvena upaghāta tvena vā tat sarvam dṛṣṭam iti etat āpadyate adhyavasāya grahaṇe punar kriyamāṇe na doṣaḥ bhavati 
[I,156,iv]	āha na pramāṇa adhikārāt na adhyavasāya śabdasya prayojanam kutas pramāṇa adhikāraḥ ayam na ca adhyavasāyāt ṛte yat kiṃcid viṣayam pratipadyate tena kiṃcid pramīyate tena vayam sāmarthyāt adhyavasāyam eva abhisaṃbhanti asyāmaḥ tat yathā adhyayana adhikāre brāhmaṇāḥ ānīyantām iti ukte ye eva ādhīyante te eva ānīyante 
[I,157,i_I,157,ii]	ucyate karaṇa antarāṇām tu sandeha nivṛtti artham evam tarhi śrotra ādīnām anyatamam antaḥkaraṇam ca iti etat dvāra dvāri bhāvena catuṣṭayam viṣayam prati vartate tasmāt adhyavasāya grahaṇam kriyate sandehaḥ mā bhūt iti āha astu atra sandehaḥ na ekena kenacid kaścid viṣayaḥ upādīyate tena vayam sarveṣām pratyakṣa tvam pratipatsyāmahe 
[I,158,i]	ucyate sarva abhyupagame hi śāstra hāniḥ yadi punar sarveṣām eva pramāṇa tvam abhyupagamyate tena yat śāstram ekam eva darśanam khyātiḥ eva darśanam iti tat hīyate vakṣyati ca ācāryaḥ ete pradīpa kalpāḥ sarvam pratyupabhogam yasmāt puruṣasya sādhayati buddhiḥ iti tat virudyate tasmāt adhyavasāya grahaṇam kartavyam sandehaḥ mā bhūt iti 
[I,159,i_I,159,ii]	āha na sandeha mātram etat bhavati sarva sandeheṣu ca etat upatiṣṭhate vyākhyānataḥ viśeṣa pratipattiḥ na hi saṃdehāt alakṣaṇam tatra adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭam iti vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ucyate mukta saṃśayam ca indriya vṛtti pratipatteḥ syāt etat yadi atra sandehaḥ syāt na eva atra sandehaḥ prāptaḥ kintarhi śrotra ativṛtteḥ eva grahaṇam 
[I,159,iii_I,160,i]	āha kim punar kāraṇam yena nimitta aviśeṣe api śrotra ādi vṛtteḥ eva atra grahaṇam prāpnoti na antaḥkaraṇasya eva pratyakṣa tvam ucyate tatra ca mukhyā śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ kasmāt sākṣāt viṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyāt na antaḥkaraṇam tad dvāreṇa pratipatteḥ gauṇa mukhyayoḥ ca mukhye sampratipattiḥ tat yathā gauḥ anubandhyaḥ ajaḥ agnīṣomīya iti vāhīkaḥ na anubadhyate 
[I,160,ii_I,160,iii]	āha yadi iyam śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ eva pratyakṣam iti abhupeyate kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ syāt ucyate rāga ādi viṣayam yat vijñānam liṅga liṅgi pūrvakam yoginām ca dhyāna bhūmikāsu viharatām anumānāgam atītam prātibham yat vijñānam utpadyate tad upasaṃkhyeyam syāt kutas na hi sukha ādayaḥ śrotra ādi vṛtti bāhyāḥ yoginām ca atīndriyam jñānam iti yathānyāsam tu kriyamāne te api viṣayāḥ teṣām yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tasya pratyakṣa tvam kena vāryate 
[I,161,i_I,161,iii]	āha prativiṣaya grahaṇam tarhi kimartham ucyate prativiṣaya grahaṇam asat vyudāsa artham adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭa mitīyati ucyamāne mṛgatṛṣṇikā alāta cakra gandharvanagara ādiṣu api yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tat dṛṣṭam iti prativiṣaya grahaṇāt tu teṣām vyudāsaḥ kṛtaḥ bhavati āha yadi evam viṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ iti eva ca ucyatām kimpratigrahaṇena 
[I,161,iv_I,162,i]	ucyate pratigrahaṇam sannikarṣa artham viṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ dṛṣṭa mitīyati ucyamāne viṣaya mātre sampratyayaḥ syāt pratigrahaṇe punar kriyamāṇe pratirābhi mukhye vartate tena sannikṛṣṭa indriya vṛtti upanipātī yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tat dṛṣṭam iti upalabhyate āha kasya punar atīndriya sannikarṣe pratyakṣa tvam prāpnoti 
[I,162,ii_I,162,iii]	ucyate anumānasya kasmāt tat hi liṅga darśanāt asannikṛṣṭe viṣaye bhavati āha anumānasya aprasaṅgaḥ sāmānya vihitasya viśeṣa vihitena bādhanāt sāmānye hi viṣaya mātre adhyavasāyasya pratyakṣa tvam vidhāya viśeṣe liṅga liṅgi pūrvake anumānam śāsti sāmānya vihitam ca viśeṣa vihitena bādhyate yathā tat hi brāhmaṇebhyaḥ dīyatām takram kauṇḍinyāya iti 
[I,163,i_I,163,iv]	ucyate smṛteḥ tarhi pratyakṣa tvam prāpnoti tatra ayam apavādaḥ na abhiniviśate iti āha na smṛteḥ pramāṇa adhikārāt pramāṇa adhikāraḥ ayam na ca smṛtyā kiṃcid pramīyate smṛteḥ pramite arthe prādurbhāvāt ucyate saṃśayasya tarhi prāpnoti na saṃśayasya adhyavasāya grahaṇāt adhyavasāyaḥ hi dṛṣṭam iti ucyate na ca saṃśayaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ aniścita tvāt 
[I,163,v_I,164,ii]	ucyate indriya antara ākūta viṣaye tu prasaṅgaḥ evam tarhi indriya artha sannikṛṣṭa indriya vṛtti upanipātī iti doṣaḥ na bhavati āha rāga ādi upasaṃkhyānam yadi sannikṛṣṭa indriya vṛtti upanipātī yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tat dṛṣṭam iti abhyupeyate tena rāga ādi viṣayam vijñānam atīndriya tvāt pratyakṣam na prāpnoti tasya upasaṃkhyānam kartavyam ucyate na tarhi idam pratigrahaṇam indriya viśeṣaṇam viṣayam viṣayam prati yaḥ vartate tasmin yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tat dṛṣṭam iti kintarhi adhyavasāya viśeṣaṇam viṣayam viṣayam prati yaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ iti 
[I,164,iii]	āha adhyavasāya viśeṣaṇam iti ced śabda ādi upasaṃkhyānam śabda ādīnām eva tena pratyakṣa tvam prāpnoti teṣām upasaṃkhyānam kartavyam prāpnoti kim kāraṇam antaḥkaraṇasya taiḥ sannikarṣa anupapatteḥ pratigrahaṇam sannikarṣa artham iti pūrvam atisṛṣṭam bhavatā tat ca idānīm antaḥkaraṇa viśeṣaṇam na ca antaḥkaraṇasya śabda ādibhiḥ sannikarṣaḥ upapadyate śrotra ādi vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt dvāri dvāra bhāvasya apaghāta prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt su dūram api gatvā pratigrahaṇam pratyākhyānāt na mucyate rāga ādi upasaṃkhyānāt vā iti 
[I,165,i]	ucyate astu tarhi indriyāṇām prati viṣaya grahaṇam viśeṣaṇam yat tu uktam rāga ādīnām upasaṃkhyānam kartavyam iti tatra brūmaḥ eka śeṣa nirdeśāt siddham evam tarhi prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ ca prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ ca prativiṣaya adhyavasāyaḥ iti sarūpāṇām eka śeṣaḥ kariṣyate tatra ekena bahis aṅgasya aindriyasya pratyakṣasya parigrahaḥ dvitīyena antaraṅgasya prātibhasya iti rāga ādi viṣayam yoginām ca yat vijñānam tat saṃgṛhītam bhavati iti vyākhyātam pratyakṣam 
[I,166,i_I,166,iii]	āha anumānam idānīm vaktavyam ucyate trividham anumāmam ākhyātam anumānam tri prakāram ācāryaiḥ ākhyātam pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ca tatra pūrvam iti kāraṇam ucyate yasya hi yat kāraṇam sa loke tad pūrvakaḥ iti ucyate yathā tantu pūrvakaḥ paṭaḥ devadatta pūrvakaḥ yajñadattaḥ iti pūrvam asya asti iti pūrvavat śeṣaḥ iti vikāra nāma śiṣyate iti kṛtvā tathā ca uktam na śeṣaḥ agneḥ anyasya jātam iti asti na apatyam anyena jātam sambhavati iti arthaḥ śeṣaḥ asya asti iti śeṣavat 
[I,167,i_I,167,iii]	tatra pūrvavat yadā kāraṇam abhyuditam bhaviṣayat tvam kāryasya pratipadyate tat yathā megha udaye bhaviṣyat tvam vṛṣṭeḥ āha na etat asti udāharaṇam anekāntāt na hi megha udayaḥ avaśyam vṛṣṭeḥ kāraṇam bhavati vāyu ādi nimitta pratibandha sambhavāt ucyate yadi tarhi kāraṇa śaktim sahakāri śakti antara anugṛhītām apratiyoginīm dṛṣṭvā kāryasya vyaktim pratipadyate tat yathā yadā lauha daṇḍa ādi sādhana sampanne vyāpāravatā kumbhakāreṇa adhiṣṭhitām mṛdam upalabhya ghaṭasya tadā pūrvavat 
[I,167,iv_I,168,ii]	śeṣavat yadā kārya nirvṛtim dṛṣṭvā kāraṇa sadbhāvam pratipadyate tat yathā kumārakam dṛṣṭvā dvaya samāpattim āha na etat asti udāharaṇam anekāntāt na hi dvaya samāpatti pūrvakaḥ eva prāṇabhṛtām prādurbhāvaḥ droṇa ādīnām anyathā utpatti viśeṣa śravaṇāt ucyate yadā tarhi prabhā anuraṃjitam antarikṣam dṛṣṭvā candra arkayoḥ udayam pratipadyate tadā śeṣavat 
[I,168,iii_I,168,vi]	āha etat api na asti udāharaṇam anekāntāt na hi prabhā anurāgaḥ antarikṣe candra arka nimittaḥ eva bhavati kintarhi digdāha ādi nimittaḥ api ucyate yadā tu nadī pūram dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṭim pratipadyate tadā śeṣavat āha etat api na asti udāharaṇam anekāntāt nadī pūrasya hi nimittam anekavidham bhavati iti himilayana setu bhaṃga gaja krīḍā ādi tasmāt ayuktam etat ucyate yadā tarhi parṇam dṛṣṭvā śālūkam pratipadyate aṃkuram vā dṛṣṭvā bījam iti tadā śeṣavat 
[I,169,i]	athavā punar astu pūrvakam eva udāharaṇam yat tu uktam anekāntāt iti atra brūmaḥ vīta avīta sāmarthyāt vīta avītābhyām hetu bhūtābhyām abhipreta artha siddhiḥ iti vakṣyāmaḥ prasaṃgi dharma antara nivṛtti mukhena ca avīta prayogaḥ tatra yadā prasaṃginām hima vilayana ādīnām deśa kāla liṅgaiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate tadā mukta saṃśayam pratipattiḥ bhavati deśaḥ tāvat tat yathā dakṣiṇāpathe na asti hima vilayana sambhavaḥ kālataḥ yathā prāvṛṣ kāle liṅgataḥ api yasmāt mudga gavedhuka śyāmāka kāṣṭha sūtra śakṛt prabhṛtīnām anupalambhaḥ tathā ūṣma kaluṣa tva ādīnām upalambhaḥ tasmāt pariśeṣataḥ medhyāḥ eva apaḥ iti tasmāt na anekāntaḥ evam kṛtvā pūrvāṇi api udāharaṇāni upapannāni bhavanti deśa ādi vicāra sāmarthyāt 
[I,170,i_I,170,ii]	sāmānyatodṛṣṭam nāma yatra ekadārthayoḥ avyabhicāram upalabhya deśa antare kāla antare ca tad jātīyayoḥ avyabhicāram pratipadyate tat yathā kvacid dhūma agni sambandham dṛṣṭvā kvacid dhūma antareṇa agni antarasya astitvam pratipadyate āha na etat asti udāharaṇam aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt sarvatra eva hi anumāne kvacid arthayoḥ avyabhicāram upalabhya anyatra tad jātīyayoḥ arthayoḥ avī abhicāram pratipadyate tat yathā kvacid sādhanavataḥ mṛd piṇḍāt ghaṭa niṣpattim upalabhya ani atra sādhanavataḥ piṇḍa antarāt ghaṭa antara niṣpattim pratipadyate tathā ekatra nadī pūrāt vṛṣṭim upalabhya anyatra nadī pūra antarāt vṛṣṭi antaram avasīyate tathā ca sati trayāṇām a viśeṣa prasaṃgaḥ 
[I,171,i_I,171,ii]	ucyate yadā tarhi sahabhuvām ekasya viśiṣṭa guṇam upalabhya śeṣāṇām api tadvat tvam anumīyate tadā sāmānyatodṛṣṭam tat yathā vṛkṣāt ekasya phalasya pākam upalabhya śeṣāṇām vṛkṣa antarāṇām ca pākaḥ anumīyate āha etat api na asti udāharaṇam anekātantāt na hi sarveṣām phalānām tulya kālam pākaḥ bhavati pūrva apara kāla niṣpanna tvāt nimitta bhedāt ca 
[I,171,iii_I,172,i]	ucyate yadā tarhi samudrāt ekam udababindum prāśya śeṣasya lavaṇatā anumīyate sthālyām vā ekam pulākam upalabhya śeṣāṇām pākaḥ anumīyate tadā sāmānyatodṛṣṭam āha na etat asti udāharaṇam akṛtsna saṅgrahāt vakṣyati ayam upariṣṭāt ācāryaḥ sāmānyatas tu dṛṣṭāt ati indriyāṇām pratītiḥ anumānāt iti tatra evam pramāṇe parikalpyamāne kārya kāraṇayoḥ tad saṃghātānām ca sukha duḥkha moha svabhāva upalambhāt tanmātrā ahaṅa kāra pradhānānām samadhigamaḥ syāt na puruṣasya tad jātīya artha anupalambhāt 
[I,172,ii_I,173,i]	ucyate yadā tarhi kvacid dharmeṇa dharma antarasya avyabhicāram upalabhya eka dharma upalambhāt bhinna jātīye atyanta anupalabdhasya dharma antarasya pratipattiḥ tadā sāmānyatodṛṣṭam tat yathā devadatte gamanāt deśa antara prāptim upalabhya atyanta adṛṣṭa jyotiṣām deśa antara prāpteḥ gamanam anumīyate tathā prāsāda ādīnām vṛddhi pūrvakam dīrgha tvam upalabhya oṣadhi vanaspatīnām dīrgha tva darśanāt vṛddhiḥ anumīyate āha na etat api asti udāharaṇam pūrveṇa aviśeṣāt kāryāt kāraṇasya adhigamaḥ śeṣavat iti pūrvam atisṛṣṭam bhavatā atra api ca deśa antara prāpti lakṣaṇāt kāryāt gati lakṣaṇasya kāraṇasya adhigamaḥ tasmāt śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭayā uḥ abheda prasaṃgaḥ 
[I,173,ii_I,173,iv]	ucyate na aniyamāt yatra hi niyamataḥ kāryeṇa kāraṇam adhigamyate tat śeṣa vat iti ayam asmad abhisandhiḥ na tu tat asti sāmānyatodṛṣṭe kasmāt saṃghāta tva sāmānyāt pārārthya sāmānya sādhanam api dṛśyate yathā āha avyabhicārāt viśeṣāḥ tu pratītāḥ pratipādakāḥ iti sādhya sādhana sāmānyayoḥ api dṛśyate yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti tatra evam sati niyama vādinaḥ pratijñā hāniḥ etena asiddha viruddha anaikāntika sādhana ābhāsāḥ pratyuktāḥ te hi saṃśaya viparyaya ajñāna hetuka tvāt agamakāḥ iti vyākhyātam anumānam āha āpta vacanasya kim lakṣaṇam iti ucyate āpta śrutiḥ āpta vacanantu 
[I,173,v_I,175,i]	āptā nāma rāga ādi viyuktasya agṛhyamāṇa kāraṇa para arthāḥ vyāhṛtiḥ śravaṇam śrutiḥ āptā ca asau śrutiḥ āpta śrutiḥ athavā āpta āsya asti iti āptaḥ akāraḥ matu arthīyaḥ tat yathā tundaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti āptebhyaḥ śrutiḥ āpta śrutiḥ āpta śrutiḥ ca āpta śrutiḥ sarūpa aṇim iti eka śeṣaḥ tatra pūrveṇa āpta śruti grahanena pratipādayati apuruṣa buddhi pūrvakaḥ āmnāyaḥ svatantraḥ puruṣa niḥśreyasa artham pravartamānaḥ niḥsaṃśayam pramāṇam iti dvitīyena manu ādi nibandhanānām ca smṛtīnām vedāṅga tarka itihāsa purāṇānām śiṣṭānām nānā śilpa abhiyuktānām ca aduṣṭa manasām yat vacaḥ tad pramāṇam iti eta siddham bhavati tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ āpta śrutiḥ eva āpta vacanam na śabda mātram evam sati yat uktam tantra antarīyaiḥ śiṃśapā ādi śabdānām nirvikalpam anumāne antar bhāvaḥ tri lakṣaṇa tvāt iti tad ayatnatas pratikṣiptam bhavati iti vyākhyātāni pramāṇāni etaiḥ pūrva uktam prameyam yathāsvam pratipattavyam iti 
[I,177,i_I,177,iii]	āha astu tāvat akṣarāt nikarṣa bhājām arthānām pratyakṣeṇa upalabdhiḥ asannikā ṛṣa bhājām api ca upalabdha sambandhānām anumānena ye tu ati indriyāḥ bhāvāḥ teṣām ubhaya vailakṣaṇyāt na asti pratyakṣa anumānābhyām upalabdhiḥ āgamika tve sarva vāda siddhi prasaṃgaḥ iti atas atyantam eva agrahaṇam prāptam tatra yat uktam etāvadbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ sakala padārtha avabodhaḥ iti etat ayuktam ucyate syāt etat evam yadi eka rūpam eva anumānam adhītam syāt kim tarhi trividham tatra satyam eva pūrvavat śeṣavatī prāk anubhūta sambandha viṣaya phale iti kṛtvā na tābhyām aśeṣa padārtha adhigamaḥ abhyupagamyate sāmānyatas tu dṛṣṭāt ati indriyāṇām prasiddhiḥ anumānāt 
[I,178,i^1]	yat tu etat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam anumānam etasmāt atīndriyāṇām arthānām samadhigamaḥ pratyavagantavyaḥ katham yathā hi kṛtaka tva anitya tvayoḥ ghaṭe sahabhāvam upalabhya ani atra śabda ādau kṛtaka tva darśanāt anitya tvam anumīyate evam śakala ādīnām tad jātīya tā candana ādi pūrvakatva siddheḥ kārya kāraṇasya sukha ādi jātīya tayā tad pūrvakatva siddheḥ śayana ādīnām ca saṃghāta tvāt pāra arthya siddheḥ kārya kāraṇasya api saṃghāta tvāt pārārthya siddhiḥ iti sarvam iṣṭam saṅgṛhītam bhavati iti yeṣām tu śeṣavat eva sāmānyatodṛṣṭam teṣām tasya kārya dvāreṇa samadhigama hetu tvāt puruṣasya agrahaṇa prasaṃgaḥ 
[I,178,i^2_I,180,i]	vṛttau kārya upacārāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi api puruṣasya kārya abhāvaḥ tathā api puruṣa avyakta mahat ahaṅkāra viśeṣāṇām sāmprate kāle sva vṛttibhyaḥ teṣām grahaṇam iti uktam kasmāt vṛtti śaktiḥ eṣām kāryatvena upacaritā svam ātmānam yunakti iti tat ca ayuktam kasmāt hetu antara abhidhānāt yadi vṛttyā grahaṇam puruṣasya sūpa pādam abhaviṣyat saṃhata pāra arthyam ācāryaḥ hetu tvena na avakṣyat tat ca avṛtti bhūtam iti avaśyam śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭayoḥ artha antara bhāvaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tasmāt siddham sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt ati indriyāṇām arthānām samadhigamaḥ tasya prayoga mātra bhedāt dvaividhyam vītaḥ avītaḥ iti tayoḥ lakṣaṇam āmananti yadā hetuḥ sva rūpeṇa sādhya siddhau prayujyate sa vītaḥ arthānara ākṣepāditaraḥ pariśeṣitaḥ 
[I,180,ii]	svarūpam hi sādhanasya dvividham sādhāraṇam asādhāraṇam ca tatra sādhāraṇam sādhya sahabhāvī tad pratipatti hetutvena yathāvat āśrīyamāṇaḥ artha ātmā asādhāraṇam punar parimāṇam anvayaḥ saṃghāta parārtha tvam ityādi tatra yadā hetuḥ para pakṣam apekṣya yathārthena svarūpeṇa sādhya siddhau upadiśyate tadā vīta ākhyaḥ bhavati yadā tu sva sādhyāt artha antara bhūtānām prasaṃginām kṣepam apoham kṛtvā pariśeṣataḥ sādhya siddhau apadiśyate tadāvīta ākhyaḥ bhavati tat yathā na ced paramāṇu puruṣa īśvara karma daiva kāla svabhāva yadṛcchābhyaḥ jagat utpattiḥ sambhavati pariśeṣataḥ pradhānāt iti tadā punar avīta ākhyaḥ bhavati tatra yadā vītaḥ hetuḥ sva buddhau avahita vijñāna sarūpam vijñāna antaram ādadhānena vaktrā pratipādya ādau vākya bhāvam upanīyate vākyam antareṇa arthasya buddhi antare saṃkrāmayitum aśakyatvāt tad ā avaya vi vākyam parikalpyate 
[I,181,i_I,182,i^1]	tasya punar avayavāḥ jijñāsā saṃśaya prayojana śakya prāpti saṃśaya vyudāsa lakṣaṇāḥ ca vyākhyā aṅgam pratijñā hetu dṛṣṭānta upasaṃhāra nigamanāni para pratipādana aṅgam iti tatra jñātum icchā jijñāsā kaścid kaṃcid upasadya āha puruṣam jñātum icchāmi kim asti na asti iti kutas saṃśayaḥ iti paryanuyuktaḥ pratyāha anupalabhyamānasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iha anupalabhyamānam ubhayathā dṛṣṭam sat bhūtam asat bhūtam ca iti sadbhūtam ca arka indu maṇḍalāpara bhāga ādi asat bhūtam ca śaśaviṣāṇa ādi ayam api ca ātmā na upalabhyate atas saṃśayaḥ kim asti na asti iti kim asyāḥ cintāyāḥ prayojanam iti pṛṣṭaḥ vyācaṣṭe śāstra tattva adhigamaḥ tatas ca mokṣa avāptiḥ katham iti 
[I,182,i^2]	yadi tāvat ayam ātmā asti tatas asya aprakṛti tva audāsīnya vibhutva ādi sattva vijñānāt nairātmya bhrānti vipakṣa bhūtāt apavarga prāptiḥ avaśyaṃbhāvinī iti yat uktam vyakta avyakta jña vijñānāt mokṣaḥ avāpyate iti tat śāstram arthavat bhavati iti atha na asti iti niścīyate tena sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anumānāt tadvat anye api padārthāḥ na santi iti vipralambha bhūyiṣṭham ārṣam darśanam apahāya ātma graha dṛṣṭi vigamāt loka uttarmavalambanam śūnyam dhyāna viṣayam upasamprāptaḥ traidhātuka kleśa nirodha lakṣaṇam ātyantikam nirvāṇam avāpsyati iti śakyaḥ ca ayam arthaḥ niścetum pramāṇa traya parigrahāt iti vyavasthite vyudāsya saṃśayam sādhya avadhāraṇam pratijñā sādhyasya yat avadhāraṇam asti puruṣaḥ iti sā pratijñā 
[I,183,i]	sādhana samāsa vacanam hetuḥ sādhyate anena iti sādhanam liṅgam samāsaḥ saṃkṣepaḥ sādhanasya samāsa vacanam sādhana samāsa vacanam sādhana grahaṇam tad ābhāsa pratiṣedha artham na hi tāni sādhanam saṃśaya viparyaya hetu tvāt samāsa grahaṇam avayava antara avakāśa pradāna artham liṅga nirdeśa mātram hetuḥ yaḥ tu tasya sādhya sahabhāvi tva lakṣaṇaḥ prapañcaḥ saḥ avayava antarāṇi iti uktam bhavati 
[I,184,i]	udāharaṇantu atra nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ tasya sādhanasya sādhyena sahabhāvi tva nidarśanam yat asau dṛṣṭāntaḥ tat yathā saṃhatya kāriṇām parārtha tvam dṛṣṭam yathā śayana āsana ratha śaraṇānām vyatirekaḥ tu avītasya prasaṅgi dharma antara nivṛtti rūpa tvāt tad antarbhūtaḥ iti tad artham vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ ucyate 
[I,185,i]	sādhya dadṛṣṭāntayoḥ eka kriyā upasaṃhāraḥ upanayaḥ sādhyasya cakṣuḥ ādi pāra arthya lakṣaṇasya dṛṣṭāntasya ca śayana ādeḥ eka kriyā upasaṃhāraḥ tatra artha antara bhūta tvāt sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ añjasā na eka kriyā upapadyate tena eva tasya anidarśanāt iti ataḥ dharma sāmānyāt yathā idam tathā idam iti eka kriyā upacaryate yathā śayana ādayaḥ saṃhata tvāt para arthāḥ evam cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ api para arthaiḥ bhavitavyam yaḥ asau paraḥ sa puruṣaḥ 
[I,185,ii]	tad vaśāt pratijñā abhyāsaḥ nigamanam hetu dṛṣṭānta upasaṃhāra apekṣayā yaḥ punar abhyāsaḥ tad nigamanam tat yathā tasmāt asti puruṣaḥ iti eṣām avayavānām paraspara sambandhāt viśiṣṭa arthaḥ samudāyaḥ vākyam iti upadiśyate vākyam api anekam yadā guṇībhūta sva artham artha antara upakāri tva āditareṇa saṃsṛjyate tadā śāstram api ekam vākyam iti avasīyate 
[I,186,i^1]	āha jijñāsā ādi anabhidhānam tad vyatirekeṇa api svayam artha gateḥ sva niścaya vat ca para pratipādanāt yathā hi svayam utpadyate niścetuḥ pratyayaḥ tathā eva anyaḥ pratyāyya iti etat nyāyyam na ca svayam eva artham pratipadyamānasya jijñāsā ādīnām tatra vyāpāraḥ tasmāt para artham api eṣām upādānam na kalpyate saṃśaya vacana ānarthakyam ca pratīta artha tvāt niścitau hi vādi prativādinau sva pakṣayoḥ tayoḥ itaretara saṃśaya paryanuyoge na asti prayojanam kiṃca anyat prayojana śakya prāpti avacanam ca sādhana abhyupagamāt eva tad pratīteḥ na hi mahatām niṣprayojanā pravṛttiḥ upapadyate na ca aśakye arthe himavat samīkaraṇa ādiṣu pravṛtteḥ tasmāt anarthakam tat abhidhānam tad bhāve bhāvāt iti ced syāt etat satsu jijñāsā ādiṣu tattva adhigamam prati pravṛttiḥ bhavati asatsu na bhavati 
[I,186,i^2]	tasmāt etāni api sādhanam bhaviṣyanti iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt atiprasaṃgāt satsvātma antaḥkaraṇa indriya āloka viṣayeṣu pravṛtti darśanāt teṣām api sādhana tvam syāt aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt jijñāsā ādayaḥ anarthakāḥ pratijña ādayaḥ durvihitāḥ katham sādhya avadhāraṇasya avayava antareṣu api upapatteḥ yadi sādhya avadhāraṇam pratijñā iti ucyate tena sādhyasya hetoḥ dṛṣṭāntasya vā yat avadhāraṇam tat api pratijñā prāpnoti nimitta aviśeṣāt sādhya śabdaḥ hi ayam sāmānya vṛttiḥ na yatnam antareṇa viśeṣe avasthāpayitum śakyate iti kim ca hetu lakṣaṇa anupapattiḥ ca sādhana anupadeśāt yaḥ hi sādhana samāsa vacanam hetuḥ iti etat lakṣaṇam ācaṣṭe tena prāc sādhanam abhidheyam syāt 
[I,186,i^3]	tatas vaktavyam amuṣya samāsa vacanam hetuḥ iti na ca evam uktam tasmāt alakṣaṇam etat kiṃca anyat samāsa vacanam ca vistara niṣedha prasaṅgāt yadi hi samāsa grahaṇam kriyate kim prāptam yaḥ ayam ādhyātmikānām bhedānām kārya kāraṇa ātmakānām ca eka jāti samanvayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti evamādiḥ sādhana prapañcaḥ saḥ ahetuḥ iti uktam bhavati tasmāt samāsa grahaṇam aniṣṭam liṅga abhidhānāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam liṅgam hi naḥ sādhanam tasya atra nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ tasmāt svam ati jāḍyāt idam aniṣṭam adhyāropyate na tu asmad pramādāt iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt tasya dvidhā bhinnasya pañcadhā sādhana bhāvāt tat hi liṅgam vītāvīta tvena iṣṭam tena dvidhā bhinnam 
[I,186,i^4]	tatra api vītaḥ pañca prabhedaḥ iti atas samudāyāt niṣkṛṣṭasya ekasya liṅga tvam aśakyam vaktum iti kiñca anyat dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ ca śabda artha lakṣaṇe aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt tat nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti atra śabdaḥ vā yena sādhya sādhane nidarśyete sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ syāt arthaḥ vā yatra nidarśyate kiñcātas na tat yadi tāvat śabdaḥ parigṛhyate tatas upanaya lakṣaṇam bādhyate kasmāt na hi yathā abhidhānam tathā sādhyam iti eka kriyā yujyate iti atha arthaḥ parigṛhyate tena abhidheyasya vākya an avayava tvāt pañca avayava tva virodhaḥ kiñca anyat dṛṣṭānta upanaya nigamana abhedaḥ ca hetu pratijñā artha abhidhānāt sādhana tvam eva sādhya avinābhau i tva lakṣaṇam dṛṣṭānta upanayayoḥ pratyāyayate pratijñā artham ca nigamanasya na avayava antara tvam yujyate 
[I,190,i^1]	ucyate yat ucyate sva niścayena aṅga bhāva gamanāt para pratyāyana artham jijñāsā ādi anabhidhānam iti atra brūmaḥ na ukta tvāt uktam etat purastāt vyākhya aṅgam jijñāsā ādayaḥ sarvasya ca anugrahaḥ kartavyaḥ iti evam artham śāstra vyākhyānam vipaścidbhiḥ pratāyate na sva artham sva sadṛṣa buddhi artham vā tatra evam kalpyamāne ye vyutpādyāḥ tān prati na eva eṣām ānarthakyam atha etat aniṣṭam yat uktam sandigdha viparyasta avyutpanna buddhi anugraha arthaḥ hi satām viniścayaḥ śāstra kathā iti asya vyāghātaḥ kim ca niyama anabhyupagamāt 
[I,190,i^2]	na hi vayam eṣām āvaśyakam abhidhānam ācakṣmahe kintarhi yadā prativādī paryanuyuṅkte kim jijñāsasaḥ iti avaśyam abhidhānīyam śabdam iti kena dharmeṇa kim nityaḥ anityaḥ iti kutas saṃśayaḥ mūrta tvāt yaḥ tu na paryanuyuṅkte na tam pratyete vācyāḥ kvacid ānarthakyāt sarvatra prasaṅgaḥ iti ced naḥ itareṣām api tad prasaṅgāt pratijña ādīnām api tarhi kvacid anabhidhānam atas teṣām api sarvatra āvacanam prasajyate tathā ca bhavatā uktam kasyacid tu kiñcid prasiddham eva bhavati iti anyataroktiḥ api sādhanam bhavati śabdaḥ iva artha dvaya pratīta tvāt ubhayān abhidhānam iti 
[I,190,i^3]	yat api uktam niścita tvāt saṃśaya avacanam iti asat etat kasmāt ukta tvāt uktam etat sati paryanuyoge tat vacanam iti etena prayojana śakya prāptī pratyukte yaḥ hi paryanuyuñjīta kim prayojanaḥ ayam śakyaḥ vā ayam arthaḥ iti tam prati vācyam etat yat api uktam tad bhāve bhāvāt iti na anabhyupagamāt na brūmaḥ yasmāt satsu jijñāsā ādiṣu tattva adhigama sadbhāvaḥ tasmāt eteṣām avayava tvam iti kintarhi yam pratyeṣām pratipattau aṅga bhāva gamanam tam pratyetāni sādhanam iti yat api uktam sādhya abhidhāyinaḥ pratijñā abhyupagamāt hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ api tad prasaṅgaḥ iti ayuktam etat 
[I,190,i^4]	kasmāt jijñāsā ādeḥ sadbhāve sati tad pratīteḥ yadi api sādhya śabdaḥ ayam aviśeṣeṇa siddha tvāt artha antaram ācaṣṭe tathā api yam prati jijñāsā saṃśaya prayojana śakya prāptayaḥ tasya vyudasya saṃśayam sādhyasya avadhāraṇam pratijñā na hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ tat asti iti asat etat kiṃca anyat tad bhāve avirodhāt yadā tu jijñāsā ādayaḥ hetau dṛṣṭānte vā bhavanti tadā kim kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ atha na kṛtakaḥ atha buddhiḥ nityā kṣaṇikā vā iti bhavati eva tad avadhāraṇam pratijñā yat api uktam sādhana anupadeśāt hetu lakṣaṇā yogaḥ iti asat etat kasmāt loka prasiddha tvāt 
[I,190,i^5]	yathā sādhyavatvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ iti pratijñā lakṣaṇam ācakṣāṇaḥ bhavān na sādhya lakṣaṇam ācaṣṭe kasmāt sādhanīyam sādhyam iti loke siddha tvāt evam sādhana samāsa vacanam hetu lakṣaṇam ācakṣāṇāḥ vayam na sādhanam ācakṣmahe kasmāt sādhyate anena iti kṛtvā sādhanam iti loke siddha tvāt upetya vā anumāna nirdeśāt liṅgam hi naḥ sādhanam tat ca nirdiṣṭaim iti yat tu uktam vīta avīta bhede sati pañcadhā sādhana bhāvāt iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt samāsa grahaṇa sāmarthyāt atas eva samāsa grahaṇam kriyate sādhana svarūpa abhidhāna mātram hetuḥ iti yathā vijñāyate 
[I,190,i^6]	prapañcaḥ tu avayava antarāṇi iti etena vistara pratiṣedha prasaṅgaḥ prayuktaḥ katham na hi samāsa śabdasya ayam arthaḥ iti kṛtvā yat punar etat uktam śabda artha kalpane aniṣṭa prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇa ayogaḥ iti astu tāvat śabdaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ yat tu uktam upanaya lakṣaṇam bādhyate iti anupapannam etat kasmāt asambhave sati sambandhi antare kārya vijñānāt śabde asambhavāt arthe kāryam vijñāsyāmaḥ athavā punar aḥ tu arthaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ yat tu uktam abhidheyasya vākya an avayava tvāt pañca avayava tva virodhaḥ iti arthe asambhavāt śabde kāryam vijñāsyāmaḥ 
[I,190,i^7]	yat api uktam pratijñā hetu artha abhidhānāt dṛṣṭānta upanaya nigamanānām na avayava antara tvam iti ayama doṣaḥ kasmāt apratijñānāt na hi etat asmābhiḥ pratijñāyate kim tarhi prameya vacanam pratijñā pramāṇa rūpa mātra vacanam hetuḥ tasya prameya sahabhāvi tva nidarśanam dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma sāmānyāt eka kriyā upasaṃhāraḥ upanayaḥ samudāyasya sādhya siddhaye vyāpāra nirdeśaḥ nigamanam tasmāt ayuktam etat kiṃca anyat ekasya sādhana bhāva parikalpanā vat tat parikalpane doṣa abhāvāt 
[I,190,i^8]	yathā vākyam evam ca tad arthaḥ ca mukhyau śabda arthau tayoḥ abhinna artha tvāt iti abhyupagamāt ekam eva artham abhāgama kramam ca buddhau avasthāpya śrotra grāhya tva anitya tva kṛtaka tva prameya tva ādi lakṣaṇānām śaktīnām apa uddhārāt sādhya sādhana saṃśaya rūpa āpannam vaktāraḥ bhinnam ācakṣate na ca eka artha dharma tvāt sādhya sādhana saṃśaya abhidhānānām ekatvam anuṣajyate tathā ekasya sādhanasya sādhya dharma tad sahabhāvi tva lakṣaṇānām śaktīnām abhidhānam hetu dṛṣṭānta ādinā avayava antaram naḥ syāt tatra yat uktam pratijñā hetu artha abhidhānāt dṛṣṭānta upanaya nigamanānām na avayava antara tvam iti etat ayuktam tasmāt sūktam daśa avayavaḥ vītaḥ 
[I,197,i]	tasya purastāt prayogam nyāyyam ācāryāḥ manyante kim kāraṇam avīta lakṣaṇa avirodhāt avītasya hi lakṣaṇam pariśeṣataḥ sādhya anugrahaḥ tatra anvaya dinā sva rūpeṇa adhigate pradhāna lakṣaṇe dharmiṇi para pakṣa pratiṣedha mātreṇa upasaṃhāre kriyamāṇe pariśeṣa lakṣaṇam bādhyate kasmāt iha pratiṣedha mātram ādau ucyate tena yathā hetu virodhāt paramāṇu adibhyaḥ na vyaktam utpadyate tathā hetu abhāvāt pradhānāt api na utpadyate iti śakyam kalpayitum atas tat vyavacchedaḥ api ca avītāt gamyate tathā sati kaḥ pariśeṣaḥ syāt sva rūpeṇa tu paricchinne dharmiṇi upasaṃhāraḥ yathāvat avakalpyate na ced paramāṇu ādibhyaḥ vyaktam utpadyate pariśeṣataḥ pradhānāt eva vyaktam utpadyate iti yathā uktebhyaḥ anvaya ādibhyaḥ iti uktam bhavati tasmāt prāk vīta prayogaḥ iti siddham sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anumānāt ati indriyāṇām arthānām samadhigamaḥ iti 
[I,198,i]	āha na kāraṇa antarataḥ anupalabhyamānānām agrahaṇāt yadi sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anumānāt sarvam parokṣam adhigamyate iti abhyupagamyate prāptam idam yeṣām api arthānām kāraṇa antarataḥ anupalabdhiḥ teṣām api tasmāt eva grahaṇam tat yathā ati dūrāt sāmīpyāt indriya ghātāt manaḥ anavasthānāt saukṣmyāt vyavadhānāt abhibhavāt samāna abhihārāt ca 
[I,198,ii]	tatra ati dūrāt tāvat tat yathā proḍḍīnasya śakuneḥ atisāmīpyāt añjana prabhṛtīnām indriya ghātāt śabda ādīnām manaḥ anavasthānāt śakaṭa ādīnām saukṣmyāt truṭi ādīnām vyavadhānāt hiraṇya ādīnām abhibhavāt sūrya prakāśāt graha ādīnām samāna abhihārāt aneka pradīpa prabhāṇām caśabdāt aiśvarya yogāt deva ādīnām na ca arhati bhavitum dharma sāmānya anupapatteḥ tasmāt ayuktam sarvam atīndriyam anumān a grāhyam iti 
[I,200,i]	ucyate śakyam tāvat kāraṇa antarataḥ anupalabhyamānam kiṃcid sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anumānāt adhigantum tat yathā samīpa avasthitasya śakuneḥ ayatnena cakṣuṣā grahaṇam yathā yathā tu viprakarṣam pratipadyate praṇidhāya cakṣuḥ gṛhyate tāvat yāvat krameṇa adarśanam upasaṃprāptaḥ tatra deśa viprakarṣe pracīyamāne adarśanam upacīyamānam avagamya atyanta adarśanam api paścāt tad hetukam anumīyate tathā na ati samīpa avasthitasya dravyasya asphuṭam ākāram avadhārya paścāt yathā yathā ārāt upasaṃpadyate tathā tathā pratipadyamāna darśana śaktayaḥ anumātāraḥ kṛṣṇa sāra añjana prabhṛtīnām agrahaṇam ati sāmīpyāt anumīyate tathā giri sarit samudra samīpa vartinam śravaṇa pratighātinam prāk śabdam upalabhya paścāt tasmin eva deśe śabdam agṛhṇānāḥ śravaṇa upaghātam anumimate 
[I,200,ii_I,200,iii]	tasmāt api ca asiddham parokṣam āpta āgamāt sādhyam tasmāt api ca asiddham iti anena āgama viṣaye sāmānyatodṛṣṭasya anavatāram ācaṣṭe parokṣam iti viṣayam prati nirdiśati āpta āgamāt sādhyam iti viṣayiṇam āha etat uktam bhavati tasmāt api sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anumānāt yat na siddhyati pratyakṣa grāhyam api svayam adṛṣṭam kāraṇa antara pratibaddha viṣaya bhāvam atyanta parokṣam vā svarga apavarga devatā ādi dharma sāmānya rahitam tad āpta āgamāt sādhyam 
[I,202,i]	sarva vāda siddhi prasaṅgāt aprāmāṇyam iti ced syāt etat yadi tarhi āgamaḥ pramāṇīkriyate tena pratiśāstram ye abhiyuktāḥ teṣām prāmāṇyam iti avaśyam abhyupagantavyam evam sati sarva ācārya prāmāṇyāt aneka vikalpa vicitrā tarka vṛttiḥ iti apariniścita tvāt bhrāntiḥ prasajyeta tathā ca sati jijñāsūnām apavarga prāpti vighātaḥ syāt tasmāt bhiṣajā iva bhavatā para upadeśaḥ prayuktaḥ na asmān ayam prīṇāti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt āpta lakṣaṇasya anavadhārita tvāt vyapagata rāga ādi doṣāṇām asandigdha matīnām atīndriya artha dṛśvanām īśvara mahā ṛṣīṇām āpta tvam ācakṣmahe na sarveṣām yadi ca anyaḥ api evaṃdharmaḥ asti bhavatu pramāṇam kiṃca anyat sva viṣaye ca tad prāmāṇyasya adoṣavat tvāt yasya khalu api yaḥ viṣayaḥ tasya tasmin viṣaye vacaḥ antareṇa api sādhanam pramāṇam iti avaśyam abhyupagantavyam itarathā pratiśāstram ācāra sthiti niyamānām adṛṣṭa arthānām apratipattiḥ syāt etena akhila liṅgāt āgamaḥ artha antaram yasmāt mahatā abhidhānena yuktiḥ anviṣyate tasmāt yukti apekṣāt liṅgāt āgamaḥ artha antaram iti 
[I,203,i_I,203,ii]	āha na anvaya vyatirekābhyām adhigama hetutvāt yathā kṛtaka tva ādi dharmaḥ anitya tva ādau viṣaye dṛṣṭaḥ tad abhāve ca adṛṣṭaḥ iti anitye arthe niścayam ādadhāti evam śabdaḥ api sva arthe tad jātīye na dṛṣṭaḥ pratipatti hetuḥ bhavati tasmāt anumānāt abhinnaḥ eva ayam iti ucyate candra ādiṣu idānīm asādhāraṇa viṣayeṣu kā pratipattiḥ syāt iti 
[I,204,i_I,204,iii]	āha avayava apekṣa tvāt candra śabdaḥ hi anekeṣu vacaneṣu vartate jāti dravya guṇa kriyāsu ca tathā ḍittha ādi śabdaḥ tasmāt evaṃjātīyakānām api ca anumānāt abhedaḥ ucyate svarga ādīnām tarhi katham anumāna tvam iti āha āpta vacaḥ avisaṃvāda sāmarthyāt yathā hairaṇyaka prabhṛtīnām āptānām vākyam avyabhicāri evam īśvara mahā ṛṣayaḥ api ca āptāḥ tasmāt eṣām api vākyam avyabhicāri iti śakyam atra api sāmānya viṣaya tvam kalpayitum evam anumānam eva āgamaḥ iti 
[I,205,i]	ucyate yat uktam anvaya vyatirekābhyām adhigama hetu tvāt śabdaḥ anumānam iti atra brūmaḥ na apratijñānāt na hi vayam vyavahāra anupātinām vṛkṣa ādīnām āgama tvam ācakṣmahe kim tarhi svarga ādīnām atyanta parokṣa viṣayāṇām tasmāt apratijñānāt anupālambhaḥ ayam iti upetya vā vaktrapekṣa tvāt athavā upetyā api sarva śabdānām āgama tvam anumānāt artha antara bhāvam brūmaḥ tathā hi kṛtaka tvāt iti liṅgam caṇḍāla kāpālikaiḥ api prayujyamānam sāhacarya apekṣam niścayam ādadhāti na vaktṛ viśeṣam apekṣate vaktṛ viśeṣa apekṣaḥ tu śabdaḥ tasmāt na liṅgam kim ca anyat viparyayāt na hi liṅgam deśa antare viparyeti śabdasya tu dṛṣṭaḥ viparyayaḥ saḥ eva hi śabdaḥ deśa antare kāla antare tu sva artham na pratyāyayati artha antaram ca praśaṃsati 
[I,206,i]	sambandha anupalabdheḥ iti ced syāt etat sambandha antaram deśa antare anupalakṣitam tasmāt śabda artha viparyayaḥ iti etad anupapannam liṅga vaidharmyāt na hi pratyakṣa abhimatasya liṅginaḥ upalabdhau gavā ādeḥ liṅgam na upalabhyate śabdaḥ tu upalabhyamānaḥ gavā ādau na upalabhyate tasmāt na liṅgam kiṃca anyat deśa niyamāt na hi liṅgasya deśa niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ asti tu śabdasya deśa niyamaḥ tat yathā śavatiḥ gati karmā kāmbojeṣu eva bhāṣyate raṃhatiḥ prācyeṣu tathā dātiḥ lavana arthaḥ dātram udīcyeṣu na anyatra tasmāt na śabdaḥ liṅgam kiṃca anyat iṣṭataḥ viniyogāt svābhāvikam liṅgam na hi dhūma ugneḥ apakṛṣya śakyate apsu vāyau ākāśe anyatra vā niveśayitum śabdaḥ tu yatra vaktuḥ abhiprāyaḥ tatra tatra viniveśyate yatha vṛddhi ādayaḥ śabdāḥ sva artha abhyuccaya ādiṣu prasiddhāḥ ādaikṣu viniveśyante tasmāt na te liṅgam 
[I,207,i^1]	sarva abhidhāna śakti tvāt śabdasya adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam sarva abhidhāna śaktiḥ śabdaḥ sarva abhidheya śaktiḥ ca arthaḥ tayoḥ puruṣa vyāpāreṇa śakti avavacchedaḥ kriyate katham ayam eva śabdaḥ asya arthasya pratyāyakaḥ bhavatu ayam eva ca arthaḥ anena śabdena abhidhīyatām etāvati puruṣa vyāpāraḥ tasmāt śabdasya svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ vaktṛ apekṣayā vyajyate iti etat api anyupapannam kasmāt sutarām anumānāt artha antara tva prasaṃgāt evam api kalpayitvā anumānāt sutarām śabdasya artha antara tvam āpadyate kasmāt na hi yathā vakrapekṣayā sarva arthasya sataḥ śabdasya śakti avacchedaḥ tathā sarva artham liṅgam vaktṛ apekṣayā artha antarāt avacchidyate yathā ca ekaḥ śabdaḥ jagati evam uditaḥ puruṣa viniyoga apekṣaḥ sarvam artham abhidhātum samarthaḥ tathā ekam liṅgam kayācid yuktyā sarva artha pratyāyana samartham 
[I,207,i^2]	tasmāt na śabdaḥ liṅgam yat punar etat uktam candra ādīnām avayava apekṣam sāmānyam abhyupagamyate tat ayuktam asādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāve śabda prasiddhaḥ arthaḥ iti vyāghātaḥ kim ca anyat jāti ādi sādhya tvāt jāti guṇa dravya kriyāṇām ca para sparataḥ artha antara tvam samudāyaḥ ca sādhyaḥ tasmāt ayuktam eṣām tad apekṣayā sāmānya viṣaya tvam yat api uktam āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt svarga ādi śabdānām anumāna tvam iti atra brūmaḥ etat api anupapannam kasmāt pramāṇa viṣaya tvāt satyam asti eṣām sāmānya parikalpanā sā tu pramāṇa viṣayā na tu prameya viṣayā prameyam tu sāmānyam anumānam asya iti ayam abhyupagamaḥ vaḥ tat ca asādhāraṇa tvāt svarga ādīnām pratiṣiddham tasmāt tyajyatām iyam āśaṅkā anumānam eva āgamaḥ iti 
[I,208,i^1]	anyaḥ punar anumāna āgamaya uḥ abheda pratijñaḥ idam āha svarga ādayaḥ śabdāḥ na pramāṇam kasmāt pramāṇa antareṇa tad artha anupalabdheḥ yasya hi śabdasya arthaḥ pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā na upalabhyate sa na pramāṇam itaraḥ tu pramāṇam tat yathā nadyāḥ tīre pakvam āmra vanam pathi guḍa śakaṭam viparyastam iti na ca svarga ādi śabdānām arthaḥ pramāṇa antareṇa upalabhyate tasmāt yathā vibhuḥ ātmā sarvatra sukha ādi sambhavāt iti evamādayaḥ bauddham prati dharmya siddha tva ādayaḥ yathārthāḥ tathā veda śabdāḥ api prāyeṇa iti etat tu na yukta rūpam kasmāt anyāyena sarva śabda apavādāt 
[I,208,i^2_I,210,i]	kā hi atra yuktiḥ yat asmad ādibhiḥ anupalabhyamāna artham pramāṇa bhūtānām api vākyam ayathārtham syāt saveṇa ca avaśyam kaścid āptaḥ tasya ca vākyam adṛṣṭa artham iti abhyupagantavyam atas ayam tava atra api samānaḥ prasaṃgaḥ na ca pramāṇam sva artha siddhaye pramāṇa antaram apekṣate tatra yadi śabdasya pramāṇa antara apekṣam yathārtha tvam āśrīyate tena na kevalam svarga ādayaḥ kim tarhi śabdāḥ eva apramāṇam iti prāptam anumānasya ca pramāṇa antara nirapekṣasya gamaka tva abhyupagamāt āgamasya tatas artha antara tvam sutarām prasajyate tasmāt yukta āgama virodhinaḥ evaṃvidhāḥ nāstika vādāḥ śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ dūrāt apohyāḥ iti sthitam etat anumānāt asiddham vastu yat tat āpta āgamāt sādhyam iti evam asya trividhasya pramāṇasya aindriyikam kāraṇa antarataḥ anupalabhyamānam ca prameyam vyākhyātam etasmāt tu yat anyat tat asat iti pratyavagantavyam 
[I,212,i]	āha yadi evam pradhānasya asattva prasaṅgaḥ anupalabdau kāraṇa antara tva anupalabdheḥ tat hi pratyakṣa aviṣaya tve sati atidūra ādibhiḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇaiḥ na upalabhyate tat na tāvat ati dūrāt sāmīpyāt vyavadhānāt ca asya agrahaṇam kasmāt vibhu tvāt na indriya ghātāt avikala indriyaiḥ agrahaṇāt na manaḥ anavasthānāt avasthita manobhiḥ agrahaṇāt na saukṣmyāt śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām sattva prasaṅgāt na abhibhavāt asambhavāt na samāna abhihārāt eka tvāt tasmāt kāraṇa antara abhāvataḥ anupalabhyamānasya asattvam icchataḥ pradhānasya api śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām api sattva prasaṅgaḥ atha etat neṣyate kāraṇa antaram tarhi anupalabdhau vaktavyam iti 
[I,213,i_I,214,i]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam anupalabdhau kāraṇa antara anupapatteḥ pradhānasya asattva prasaṅgaḥ iti atra astu saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ na abhāvāt yat tu uktam śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām api sattva prasaṅgaḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt sādhana upapatteḥ asti hi pradhānasya saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhau sādhanam na śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām kim tat ucyate kāryataḥ tad upalabdhiḥ pradhānasya hi kāryataḥ upalabdhiḥ iti etat upariṣṭāt pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ na tu śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām kāryam asti tasmāt viṣamaḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ āha evam api pratijñā antara ānarthakyam ekena kṛta tvāt saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ iti ukte gamyate etat na abhāvāt iti tasmāt tat vacanam anarthakam iti 
[I,214,ii]	ucyate na vītāvīta parigraha artha tvāt evam siddhe yat pratijñā dvayam karoti tat jñāpayati ācāryaḥ vīta avītābhyām abhipreta artha siddhiḥ prāk ca saukṣmya atiśayāt tad anupalabdhiḥ iti ācakṣāṇaḥ pratipādayati purastāt vītaḥ prayoktavyavaḥ iti ekasmin ca viṣaye dvau prayuṃjānaḥ samuccayena siddhim dyotayati kim siddham bhavati yat uktam tantra antarīyaiḥ na pṛthak pratipatti hetū vīta a ītau iti tat iṣṭam evam saṃgṛhītam bhavati tatra vītasya pratijñā saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ tasya ca avītasya prasaṅgi dharma antara nivṛtti rūpeṇa na abhāvāt hetuḥ ubhaya yogī katham yasya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabhyamānasya kāryaḥ tad upalabdhiḥ tasya saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā indriyāṇi yadi punar asya abhāvāt anupalabdhi ssyāt kāryataḥ anupalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ asti ca iyam kāryataḥ upalabdhiḥ tasmāt na abhāvāt na ced abhāvāt pariśeṣataḥ saukṣmyāt tad anupalabdhiḥ iti 
[I,216,i_I,217,i]	āha kim punar tat kāryam yat bhavān pradhānasya astitve liṅgam ācaṣṭaḥ iti ucyate mahat ādi tat ca kāryam prakṛti virūpam sarūpam ca tat hi mahat ahaṃkāra indriya viśeṣā viśeṣa lakṣaṇam kāryam pradhānena visadṛśam sadṛśam ca iti upariṣṭāt pravedayiṣyāmaḥ āha prastāva abhāvāt ayuktam etat kim punar adhikṛtya idam ucyate prakṛti virūpam sarūpam ca mahat ādi kāryam iti ucyate vyakta avyakta jña vijñānāt mokṣaḥ avāpyate iti etat prakṛtam etāni ca paraspara vaidharmya sādharmya pratipattim antareṇa na śakyāni vijñātum iti evam artham idam prastūyate tasmāt na akasmikaḥ vairūpya sārūpya upanyāse iti 
[II,1,i_II,1,iv]	āha āstām tāvat vairūpya sārūpya cintā kāryam idam eva tāvat mahat ādi parīkṣiṣyāmahe kim prāk utpatteḥ asti na asti iti kutas saṃśayaḥ iti ced syāt matam asaṅgatā artham prakaraṇa antaram upakṣipyate bhavatā na ca avidyamāna sambandhasya saṃśayasya prakaraṇa antare abhidhīyamānasya nirṇītim sādhvīm ācāryāḥ manyante avakāśa asambhavāt iti ucyate asti saṃśaya avakāśaḥ kasmāt ācārya vipratipatteḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryam asat iti ācāryāḥ kaṇā dākṣa pāda prabhṛtayaḥ manyante sat asat iti bauddhāḥ na eva san āsat iti anye tasmāt upapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ tatra idānīm bhavataḥ kā pratipattiḥ iti ucyate 
[II,1,v]	na avidyamānasya mahat ādeḥ vikārasya pradhānāt āvirbhāvaḥ iti pratijānīmahe kasmāt sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra abhyupagamāt na hi naḥ kāraṇāt artha antara bhūtam kāryam utpadyate iti abhyupagamaḥ kim tarhi viśva ātmakānām sattva rajaḥ tamasām apagata viśeṣā viśeṣāḥ sat mātra lakṣaṇa upacayāḥ pratinivṛtta pariṇāma vyāpārāḥ parama vibhāgam upasaṃprāptāḥ sūkṣmāḥ śaktayaḥ tāsām adhikāra sāmarthyāt upajāta pariṇāma vyāpārāṇām sat mātra anukrameṇa pracayam upasaṃpadyamānānām sanniveśa viśeṣa mātram vyaktam etasyām kalpanāyām asataḥ utpattau kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ iti etena eva bāhyānām tantu ādi kāryāṇām paṭa ādīnām sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra tvāt asataḥ utpattiḥ pratiṣiddhā boddhavyā 
[II,2,i_II,3,i]	āha avidyamānam etat kasmāt asiddhe na artha antara siddheḥ yadi hi sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra tvam kāryasya siddham syāt atas etat yujyate vaktum tad abhyupagamāt asat utpatteḥ aprasaṅgaḥ iti tattva siddham dravya antara bhūtasya avayavinaḥ niṣpatti pratijñānāt tasmāt kāka viṣāṇāt śaśa viṣāṇa siddhi vat ayuktam sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra abhyupagamāt sad kārya siddhiḥ iti itas ca asat kāryam agrahaṇāt iha śrotra ādīnām viṣaya bhūtasya tad sannidhānāt avaśyam grahaṇena bhavitavyam yadi ca prāk utpatteḥ satkāryam syāt tat api śrotra ādi sannidhānāt gṛhyeta na tu gṛhyate tasmāt asat kāryam 
[II,3,ii^1]	anupalabdhi kāraṇa sadbhāvāt iti ced tatra etat syāt asti prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya anupalabdhi kāraṇam tasmāt asya sataḥ api agrahaṇam bhavati uttara kālam tad vigamāt grahaṇam iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt anupalabdhi asambhavāt tat hi pratyakṣa aviṣaya tve sati atidūra ādibhiḥ anupalabdhi kāraṇaiḥ na upalabhyate na ca eṣām tatra sambhavaḥ tasmāt asat etat kāraṇa antara anabhidhānāt na ca ati dūra ādi vyatiriktam anupalabdhau kāraṇa antaram adhīdhve yatas asya agrahaṇam syāt atas ca asat eva kim ca anyat kāraṇa anupalabdhi prasaṅgāt anupalabdhi kāraṇa sadbhāvāt kāryasya agrahaṇam icchataḥ kāraṇa agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ kasmāt abhinna deśa tvāt eka indriya grāhya tvāt sthūla tvāt ca 
[II,3,ii^2]	tat tu a niṣṭam tasmāt ayuktam anupalabdhi kāraṇa sadbhāvāt sataḥ kāryasya agrahaṇam iti pramāṇa antara nivṛtti prasaṅgāt ayuktam iti ced syāt etat yadi tarhi pratyakṣa viṣayam eva asti tatas anyatra asti iti etat upagamyate tena atīndriya viṣayasya anumānasya nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt na anupalabdheḥ asatkāryam iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt kriyā guṇa vyapadeśa asambhavāt yat hi pratyakṣataḥ na upalabhyate tat kriyayā asti iti saṃsūcyate yathā harmya avasthitānām tṛṇānām udvahanāt vāyuḥ guṇena yathā mālatī latā gandhena vyapadeśena vā kārya ādinā yathā indriyāṇi na tu prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya kriyā guṇa vyapadeśa sambhavaḥ tasmāt asat kāryam 
[II,4,i]	itas ca asat kāryam kartṛ prayāsa sāphalyāt iha prāc vyāpāra upakramāt kartāraḥ tasmāt phalam upalipsamānāḥ kārya viśeṣa niyata sāmārthyam sādhanam upādāya vyāpriyante tat ced prāk api vyāpārāt syāt tad arthasya parispandasya ānarthakyam prāptam aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt kartṛ prayāsa sāphalyāt asat kāryam pariṇāma ādi upapatteḥ na doṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam kāraṇasya pariṇāma vyūha saṃśleṣa vyakti pracaya kṣaṇān dharmān yasmāt kartṛ ādīni kurvanti na anarthakāni syuḥ sattvam ca kāryasya na nirupyate kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ syāt iti ucyate na śakyam evam kalpayitum kasmāt mārga antara anupapatteḥ pariṇāmaḥ hi nāma avasthitasya dravyasya dharma antara nivṛttiḥ dharma antara pravṛttiḥ ca tatra sataḥ dharma antarasya nirodha abhyupagamāt asataḥ ca utpatti pratijñānāt na idam artha antaram ārabhyate evam vyūha ādayaḥ api upasaṃhartavyāḥ tasmāt pariṇāma ādibhiḥ abhibhavāt kartṛ ādīnām arthavat tvāt asat kāryam tathā ca uktam jahaddharma antaram pūrvam upādatte yadā param tattvāt apracyutaḥ dharmaḥ pariṇāmaḥ saḥ ucyate 
[II,6,i_II,6,ii]	kutas ca na satkāryam ārambha uparamayoḥ ādi antā viśeṣa prasaṃgāt yadi satkāryam syāt tena yaḥ kriyā arthaḥ sādhanānām ādau parispandaḥ saḥ ante api syāt vā yaḥ ante virāmaḥ saḥ ādau api syāt kasmāt sat aviśeṣāt na tu tat asti tasmāt asat kāryam itas ca asat kāryam utpatti dharmasya ādi antayoḥ aviśeṣa prasaṅgāt yadi satkāryam syāt tena yathā niṣpannasya utpatti dharmeṇa abhisambandhaḥ tathā ādau api syāt yathā eva ādau abhisambandhaḥ tathā ante api syāt dṛṣṭaḥ tu abhisambandhaḥ nābhi sambandhaḥ ca ādi antayoḥ tasmāt asat kāryam 
[II,6,iii_II,7,i]	itas ca asat kāryam janma sat śabdayoḥ virodhāt iha janma śabdaḥ prāc abhūtasya arthasya bhāva kramam āha sat śabdaḥ tu kriyā antara hetu tvam āha yadi sataḥ janma syāt aikārthyam anayoḥ syāt na tu etat asti tasmāt ayuktam sat jāyate iti ucyate yat uktam dravya antara bhūtasya avayavinaḥ niṣpatti pratijñānāt na sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra tvāt satkāryam iti atra brūmaha tad asiddhiḥ bhedena agrahaṇāt yadi tantu ādibhyaḥ dravya antara bhūtasya avayavinaḥ niṣpattiḥ syāt tena yathā tantu kalāpe paṭaḥ tatra eva vā paṭa antaram āhitam bhedena upalabhyate tathā eva upalabhyeta na tu upalabhyate tasmāt na dravya antaram 
[II,7,ii_II,7,iii]	samavāyāt agrahaṇam iti ced syāt etat saṃyoginoḥ dravyayoḥ satya ādhāra ādheya bhāve bhedena grahaṇam bhavati samavāya lakṣaṇā tu prāptiḥ tantu paṭayoḥ tasmāt na asti bhedena grahaṇam iti tat ca anupapannam kasmāt asiddha tvāt siddhe satyartha antara bhāve avayavinaḥ tad prāptau ca samavāye sarvam etat syāt tattva siddham ubhayam tasmāt ayuktam etat kiṃca anyat dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt mahā parimāṇam dravyam anyatra ahitam samavāyāt bhedena na upalabhyate iti etasmin arthe paryanuyuktasya kaḥ te dṛṣṭāntaḥ na ca asti anudāhṛtaḥ vādaḥ 
[II,8,i_II,8,iii]	vyāpte na grahaṇam iti ced syāt matam akārya kāraṇa bhūtam dravyam sati api sambandhe na dravya antaram vyaśnutaḥ iti atas bhedena gṛhyate tantu paṭayoḥ tu kārya kāraṇa bhūta tvāt vyāptiḥ tasmāt na asti bhedena grahaṇam iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt sādhya tvāt satyartha antara bhāve avaya vi dravya antara vat kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ samavāyaḥ ca atas iyam vyāptiḥ syāt sā ca aprasiddhāḥ iti atas na samyak etat vema ādi vat iti ced syāt etat yathā satyartha antara bhāve vema ādayaḥ avayavinaḥ kāraṇam evam tantavaḥ api 
[II,8,iv]	etad anupapannam kasmāt anabhyupagamāt karaṇam vema ādayaḥ paṭasya na kāraṇam iti ayam abhyupagamaḥ naḥ tasmāt viṣamaḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ kim ca anyat tadvat avyāpti prasaṅgāt vema ādi vat arthāntaram paṭāt tantavaḥ iti evam bruvataḥ tadvat avyāpti prasaṅgaḥ kim ca anyat sparśa kriyā mūrti guru tva antaravataḥ tadvati pratighātāt iti iha sparśa antaravati sparśa antara vat pratīghātaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā ghaṭasya aśmani sparśa antaravān ca te paṭaḥ tantubhyaḥ iti atas asya tat vyāpi tvam ayuktam evam ca kriyā ādayaḥ vaktavyāḥ tasmāt yuktam etat bhedānām grahaṇāt na avayavī dravya antaram iti 
[II,9,i^1]	itas ca na avayavī dravya antaram kṛtsna eka deśa vṛtti anupapatteḥ sa hi avayaveṣu vartamānaḥ kṛtsneṣu vā vartate pratyavayavam vā kim ca atas tat na tāvat kṛtsneṣu vartate kasmāt eka deśa grahaṇe grahaṇa abhāva prasaṅgāt yat anekeṣu vartate tasya kṛtsnā ādhāra grahaṇe sati grahaṇam dṛṣṭam tat yathā dvi tva ādīnām evam ca sati viṣāṇa ādi grahaṇe go grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ kim ca avayavān avasathā prasaṅgāt sa hi avayavān vyāpnuvan tat dvi atirekeṇa avayava antara abhāvāt kena vyāpnuyāt avayava antara abhyupagame ca anavasthā prasaṃgaḥ kṛtsna eka deśa vṛtti prasaṅgaḥ ca samānaḥ 
[II,9,i^2]	tasmāt na sarveṣu parisamāpyate na pratyekam aneka tva prasaṅgāt aneka ādhāra parisamāptam hi anekam rūpa ādi dṛṣṭam iti kiṃca anyat śāstra hāneḥ pratyavayavam parisamāptaḥ avayavī iti etat icchataḥ mūrtimatā avayavena samāna deśaḥ syāt tatas ca yat śāstram mūrtimatām asamāna deśa tvam iti tasya vyāghātaḥ avayava parimāṇam ca prāpnoti na mahat tva ādi parisamāpta tvāt eka dravyam ca prāpnoti tatas ca yat śāstram dravyam aneka dravyam adravyam vā tasya hāniḥ etāvatā ca asya vṛttiḥ bhavantī bhavet sarvathā ca doṣaḥ tasmāt na avayavī dravya antaram 
[II,10,i]	artha antara avasthāne artha antara utpatti vināśa darśanāt anyatvam iti ced syāt etat vidyamāneṣu tantuṣu paṭaḥ na bhavati saṃyoga lakṣaṇasya kāraṇa antarasya anutpatteḥ saṃyoga uttara kālam tu bhavati kāraṇa sāmagryāḥ vidhamāneṣu eva ca tantuṣu vināśam upayāti vibhāgāt artha antara avasthāne ca artha antara utpatti vināśau dṛṣṭau tat yathā himavat avasthāne dava agneḥ tasmāt artha antaram paṭaḥ tantubhyaḥ iti 
[II,10,ii_II,10,iii]	etat api ayuktam kasmāt sādhya tvāt sādhyam tāvat etat kim atra artha antaram utpadyate vinaśyati vā āhosvit tantuṣu eva samavasthāna viśeṣa apekṣasya paṭa abhidhānasya pravṛti nivṛttī senā vana vat bhavataḥ tasmāt etat api na avayavinaḥ dravya antara bhāve liṅgam tad puruṣa bahu vrīhi dvandva samāsa upapatteḥ anyaḥ iti ced syāt matam iha artha antara tve sati tatpuruṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ rāja puruṣaḥ iti bahuvrīhiḥ ca citraguḥ śabalaguḥ dvandvaḥ ca plakṣa nyagrodhau iti asti ca iha api tatpuruṣaḥ tantūnām paṭaḥ bahuvrīhiḥ ca dṛḍha tantuḥ śukla tantuḥ dvandvaḥ ca tantu paṭau iti tasmāt ca avayavi artha antaram 
[II,12,i_II,12,ii]	etat ca ayuktam kasmāt anekāntāt ananya tve api hi tatpuruṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā senā gajaḥ kānana vṛkṣaḥ iti bahuvrīhiḥ ca vīra puruṣāḥ matta gajā senā iti dvandvaḥ tu yadi syāt satyam eva artha antaram avayavī syāt na tu kaścid paṭa avasthāyām evam prayuṅkte tantu paṭau ānaya iti tasmāt manoratha mātram etat etena samākhyā sāmarthya bhedāḥ prayuktāḥ te ca api ca anarthāna tve sati senā ādiṣu dṛṣṭāḥ tasmāt na avayavī dravya antaram dravya antara bhūtasya avayavinaḥ niṣpatti pratijñānāt na sanniveśa viśeṣa mātra tvāt satkāryam iti etat ayuktam yat punar etat uktam anupalabdheḥ asatkāryam iti atra brūmaḥ etat api ayuktam kasmāt saṃśaya kāraṇa tvāt sa ca sat viṣaya anupalabdhiḥ iti etasmāt eva hetoḥ sāṃśayikāḥ vayam tām eva tu niścaya artham avalambamānaḥ na yukti mārgam anuyāti 
[II,13,i]	yat punar etat uktam kāraṇa antara anabhidhānāt iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt abhiprāyānavabodhāt yaḥ hi yathā kuṇḍe badarāṇi artha antara bhūtāni āhitāni tathā kāraṇe kāryam asti iti etat ācaṣṭe tam pratyayam upālambhaḥ syāt vayantu aneka śakta dharmiṇaḥ sahakāri śakti antara anugṛhītasya pūrvasyāḥ śakteḥ tirobhāvam uttarasyāḥ ca āvirbhāvam upādadhānāḥ kāraṇam eva kāryam iti anumanyāmahe tayoḥ tu śaktyoḥ yuga pada grahaṇam itaretara pratibandha hetu tvāt vastrasya āyāma vistāra vat kūrma aṅgam iva draṣṭavyam yathā vastrasya upasaṃhāra pratibandhāt āyāma vistārau na grahaṇa viṣaya tām pratipadyete sattām vā na jihītaḥ kūrmasya iva aṅgāni tatha tantu ādīnām api bhāvānām kāraṇa abhimatā kārya abhimatā ca avasthā krameṇa vā sthiraḥ ca bhavat tad nimittaḥ tad grahaṇa agrahaṇa vikalpaḥ 
[II,13,ii^1]	etena kāraṇa grahaṇam pratyuktam yat api uktam pramāṇa antara nivṛtti prasaṅgāt iti satyam etat yat tu uktam kriyā guṇa vyapadeśa asambhavāt anumāna abhāvaḥ iti tad anupapannam kasmāt pṛthaktvā anabhyupagamāt kārya kāraṇa pṛthaktva vādinaḥ tad kriyā guṇānām pṛthaktvam anumātum yuktam iti atas tantu avasthāne paṭa kriyā guṇa grahaṇāt anumāna abhāvaḥ iti ayam upālambhaḥ sa avakāśaḥ syāt asmākantu kāraṇa mātrasya eva saṃghātāt ākāra antara parigrahāt vā kriyā guṇānām pracitiḥ vyakti viśeṣaḥ bhavati iti bruvata ām adoṣaḥ vyapadeśaḥ tu kārya kāraṇa paryāyaḥ saḥ ayuktaḥ kasmāt anekāntāt dravya guṇa tva karma tva ādīnām kriyā guṇa kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ atha ca satyam iṣyate atha liṅga paryāyaḥ na tarhi vayam paryanuyojyā vyapadeśa abhāvāt asat kāryam iti kim kāraṇam prakaraṇāt 
[II,13,ii^2]	vipratipattau hi satyām liṅgataḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya samadhigamam kariṣyāmaḥ iti prakṛtam eva etat anaikāntika tvam ca samānam niṣpatti anantaram dravyasya astitva abhyupagamāt aguṇavataḥ dravyasya guṇa ārambhaḥ karma guṇāḥ aguṇāḥ iti vacanāt utpanna mātram dravyam niṣkriyam nirguṇam avatiṣṭhate iti vaḥ pakṣaḥ na ca asya tathābhūtasya liṅgam asti atha ca astitvam bhavadbhiḥ abhyupagamyate siddheḥ grahaṇāt sadbhāvaḥ iti ced na sarva vivāda siddhi prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭānta viruddham artham pratijñāya pratiṣidhyamānena siddha buddhi viṣaya tā smartavyā iti etasyām kalpanāyām sarva vivāda siddhi prasaṃgaḥ syāt kim ca anyat pratipakṣe samāna tvāt asmad pakṣe api tarhi bhagavat pañcaśikhā ādīnām pratyakṣa tvāt sat kāryam abhyupagantavyam tasmāt na kriyā guṇa vyapadeśa asambhavāt asat kāryam 
[II,15,i_II,15,ii^1]	yat punar etat uktam kartṛ prayāsa sāphalyāt asatkāryam iti atra brūmaḥ etat api ayuktam kasmāt asat akaraṇāt yadi ubhaya pakṣa prasiddhasya asataḥ kriyāyogaḥ syāt atas etat yujyate vaktum kārye sati kartuḥ prayāsaḥ anarthakaḥ iti tattva sataḥ karaṇam anupapannam tasmāt ayuktam etat hetu abhidhānāt asiddhiḥ iti ced syāt etat yathā niṣpanna tvāt madhu ādīnām dhāraṇa samarthaḥ ghaṭaḥ na kriyate iti ayam apadiṣṭaḥ hetuḥ asmābhiḥ evam ittham kāryasya asataḥ kāraṇam na upapannam iti na uktam bhavatā tasmāt asiddhiḥ iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt sati asati vā sambandhe doṣa prasaṅgāt tat hi kriyamāṇam sati vā sambandhe kārakaiḥ kriyate asati vā sambandhaḥ ca asya bhavan pravṛtti kāle vā kāraṇānām syāt niṣpatti kāle vā 
[II,15,ii^2]	kim ca atas tat na tāvat pravṛtti kāle sambandhaḥ yuktaḥ kasmāt adravya tvāt pravṛtti kāle kartṛ ādīnām kriyā guṇa vyapadeśa abhāvāt avastu bhūtam śaśa viṣāṇa sthānīyam vaḥ kāryam na ca asti tathābhūtasya vastu bhūtena sambandhaḥ atha niṣpatti kāle abhisambadhyate yat uktam sataḥ niṣpanna tvāt kriyā anutpattiḥ iti tasya vyāghātaḥ atha matam asati api sambandhe niṣpattiḥ bhavati iti tena kāraka vyāpāra vaiyarthya prasaṃgaḥ prāk api ca kāraka upādānāt kārya niṣpatti prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam ca asattvāt na asti sambandhaḥ kārakaiḥ sattva saṃgibhiḥ asambandhasya ca utpattim icchataḥ na vyavasthitiḥ iti 
[II,16,i_II,16,iv]	āha nanu ca madhyame kāle kartṛ ādibhiḥ kāryam kriyate kaḥ punar asau madhyamaḥ kālaḥ iti āha ārambhāya prasṛtāḥ yasmin kāle bhavanti karttāraḥ kāryasya aniṣpādāttam madhyamam kālam icchanti iti yadā hetavaḥ pravṛtta ārambhāḥ bhavanti uddiśya kāryam na ca tāvat naimittikasya ātma lābhaḥ saṃvartate sa madhyamaḥ kālaḥ tasmin kriyate kārakaiḥ kāryam iti 
[II,16,v]	ucyate na avasthā antara anupatteḥ prāk niṣpatteḥ asattā niṣpannasya sattā iti avasthā dvayam sat asat rūpā ca avasthā na asti yaḥ madhyamaḥ syāt atas na yuktam etat iti kiṃca anyat pūrva doṣa aparihārāt uddiśya kāryam tasya ātmanaḥ lābha ātmakena saha sambandhaḥ iti atra api ayam paryanuyogaḥ na eva nivartate iti tasmāt citram api vākyam prasārya na kiṃcid parihṛtam bhavatā tasmāt yuktam etat satyasati vā sambandhe doṣa prasaṃgāt asat na kriyate iti 
[II,18,i_II,18,iii]	yasya punar satkāryam tasya doṣaḥ na asti kasmāt upādāna grahaṇāt upādānam iti kāraṇam tantu ādi ācakṣmahe tat hi tasya kārakaiḥ gṛhyate abhisambadhyate iti arthaḥ tasmāt ca na artha antaram kāryam iti atas kāraṇena abhisambaddhānām kārakāṇām kāryeṇa eva sambandhaḥ bhavati iti adoṣaḥ āha nanu ca yasya api satkāryam tasya upādānāt artha antaram tat kāryam syāt kasmāt kārya arthiḥ upādānāt yat yad artham upādīyate tat tasmāt artha antara yathā vema ādibhyaḥ paṭaḥ tantavaḥ ca paṭa ādibhiḥ upādīyante tasmāt tebhyaḥ api artha antaram paṭaḥ iti etena sattvam prayuktam yat yad artham upādīyate tat tasmin asat yathā vema ādiṣu paṭaḥ iti 
[II,19,i_II,19,ii]	ucyate na avayavi pratiṣedhāt pratiṣiddhaḥ tāvat avayavī dravya antara bhūtaḥ tasmāt anupapanna artham etat kim ca anyat sarva sambhava abhāvāt upādāna sāmānyāt vema ādi vat artha antaram paṭaḥ tantubhyaḥ iti brūvataḥ artha antara tva sāmānyāt tantu vat sarvasmāt kāraṇāt kāryasya sambhavaḥ syāt na tu evam asti tasmāt sarva sambhava abhāvāt asamyak etat kiṃca anyat jāti bheda prasaṃgāt artha antara ārambha prasaṅgāt ca upādāna sāmānyāt vema ādi vat artha antaram paṭaḥ tantubhyaḥ iti brūvataḥ yathā vema ādibhyaḥ bhinna jātīyaḥ bhinna deśaḥ ca tathā tantubhyaḥ paṭaḥ syāt yathā ca avasthite paṭe vema ādayaḥ paṭa antaram kurvanti tathā hi avasthite paṭe tantavaḥ api paṭa antaram ārabheran na ca etat iṣṭam na tarhi upādāna sāmānyāt vema ādi vat tantubhyaḥ paṭasya artha antara tvam 
[II,20,i_II,20,ii]	yat punar etat uktam yat yad artham upādīyate na tat tatra asti iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt ādhāra ādheya bhāva anabhyupagamāt asakṛt uktam asmābhiḥ na tantuṣu paṭaḥ nāma kaścid asti kim tarhi tantavaḥ eva paṭaḥ tat tu sat mārga vidveṣāt bhavatā na gṛhyate kim ca anyat anekāntāt upetya vā brūmaḥ katham tāvat tilāḥ taila artham upādīyante bhavati ca atra tailam mṛdvīkā rasa artham upādīyate bhavati ca asyām rasaḥ godhukca payaḥ artham gām ādatte bhavati ca tasyām kṣīram śāli kalāpaḥ ca taṇḍula artham upādīyate santi ca atra taṇḍulāḥ iti anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ āha āvaraṇa upalabdheḥ ayuktam tila ādiṣu āvaraṇam pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate tad pratibandhāt taila ādīnām agrahaṇam vyāpāraḥ ca kartuḥ tad vigama arthaḥ na tu kāryasya āvaraṇam asti tasmāt viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
[II,21,i^1]	ucyate na mārga antara tvāt yadi atra asti tatra tad artham upādīyate iti pūrvam bhavatā atisṛṣṭam idānīm tu avagama vigama artham sataḥ api upādānam iti brūvataḥ mārga antara gamanam pūrvavāda tyāgaḥ anaikāntikasya ca aparihāraḥ iti yat punar etat uktam pariṇāma ādi upapatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti tathā tat astu yat tu uktam mārga antara anupapatteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ etat api ayuktam kasmāt pariṇāma dharma an avabodhāt sataḥ dharma antarasya nirodham asataḥ ca utpattim pariṇāmam abhidadhataḥ vyakta mayam upālambhaḥ syāt na tu anayā anusṛtyā pratiṣṭhāmahe kim tarhi sādhana anugṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ dharma antarasya āvirbhāvaḥ pūrvasya ca tirobhāvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ na ca āvirbhāva tirobhāvau utpatti nirodhau vyūha saṃśleṣa vyakti pracayāḥ tu kim asataḥ dharmāḥ uta svatas asantaḥ iti vicāryam 
[II,21,i^2]	kim ca atas yadi tāvat asataḥ dharmāḥ yathā kasya iti vācyam atha svayam asantaḥ paścāt bhavanti tat api ayuktam kasmāt anartha antara tvāt satyartha antara bhāve prāc asantaḥ paścāt upalabhyamānāḥ satkārya vādam nirākuryuḥ sa ca eṣām artha antara bhāvaḥ na prasiddhaḥ tasmāt kim atra upapannam grahaṇa agrahaṇa vikalpe ca uktaḥ parihāraḥ kim ca anyat dravya antara utpatti vyāghātāt upetya vā eṣām utpattim brūmaḥ yadi hi pariṇāma vyūha saṃśleṣa vyakti pracaya mātram kāryam iṣyate yat uktam dravyāṇi dravya antaram ārabhantaḥ iti tasya vyāghātaḥ kasmāt na hi ete bhāvāḥ dravya antaram tasmāt dinakara kiraṇa pratāpa mūrchitasya iva dāva agni upasarpaṇa doṣonutāpāya eva bhavataḥ pratipattiḥ 
[II,22,i^1]	etena ārambha uparama utpatti aviśeṣa prasaṅgaḥ janma sat śabdaḥ pratyuktaḥ katham ātma bhūtam hi tantūnām paṭa ākhyam vyūha sthānīyam sanniveśa viśeṣam yadā kārakāṇi svena svena vyāpāreṇa āviṣkurvanti tadā kriyate utpadyate jāyate iti evamādiḥ lokasya vyavahāraḥ pravartate yadā tu kārakāṇi śakti antarāvirbhāvāt saṃsthāna antareṇa autsukya varti tām avasthām upasaṃharanti tadā prāk upalabdham saṃsthānam vināśa śabda vācya tām pratipadyate paramārthataḥ tu na kasyacid utpādaḥ asti na vināśaḥ yat punar etat uktam janma śabdaḥ prāc abhūtasya arthasya bhāva upakramamāha iti tad api icchā mātram kasmāt vivādāt sat asat viṣayam janma iti vivāde anuṣakte janma śabdaḥ prāc abhūtasya sadbhāvam ācaṣṭaḥ iti brūvataḥ anukta samam 
[II,22,i^2]	puruṣa ādau adṛṣṭa tvāt asiddhiḥ iti ced syāt etat yadi tarhi kriyate utpadyate jāyate iti eṣorthaḥ sat viṣayaḥ kalpyate pradhāna puruṣayoḥ api tad prasaṃgaḥ sat asat aviśeṣāt iti atas ca vivāda avastham eva etat prakaraṇam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt saṃsthāna viṣaya tvāt yadā bhāvaḥ svatas anartha antara bhūtam saṃsthānam bhajate tadā ete śabdāḥ pravartante iti uktam dṛṣṭam ca loke tat yathā muṣṭi granthi kuṇḍalāni karoti janayati utpādayati abhivyakta ātmasu ca mūla udaka ādiṣu bhavati utpannam jātam iti ubhaya pakṣa prasiddhe tu śaśaviṣāṇa ādau na ete śabdāḥ pravartante tasmāt bhavataḥ eva aniṣṭa prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam ca yadi asattvam ghaṭa ādīnām utpattau hetuḥ iṣyate śaśa śṛṅge api tulya tvāt utpattiḥ te prasajyate 
[II,23,i_II,24,ii^1]	iti siddham satkāryam itas ca satkāryam śakti asya śakya karaṇāt śakyam idam asya śaktaḥ ca ayam asya iti ayam niyamaḥ satām dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā cakṣuṣaḥ rūpasya āsti ca ayam paṭasya vema ādīnām ca niyamaḥ tasmāt ca satkāryam sahakāri vat tat niyamaḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā apaḥ bīja aṅkurasya utpattau samarthāḥ bhavanti na kāṣṭhāt agneḥ vā ubhayam ca tat tāsu ca vidyate bījāt apām vicchinna tvāt yathā ca sūryaḥ sūryakāntāt agnim utpādayitum samarthaḥ na candrakāntāt ca pānīyam ubhayam tat tatra na vidyate tathā ca tattva ādīnām paṭasya eva śakti niyamaḥ syāt na ca paṭasya tantuṣu sattvam syāt iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt sādhya tvāt 
[II,24,ii^2_II,25,i]	aṃkura ādayaḥ api kāryam ap ādīnām atas sādhyam kim aṅkuraḥ asti atha na asti eva tathā sūryakānte agniḥ tad artham eva ca ayam vivādaḥ anuṣaktaḥ yat tu uktam apām vicchinnavān na tāsu aṅkuraḥ asti iti tatra api yāsām apām bīja anupraveśa daṅkura bhāvena vipariṇāmaḥ tābhyaḥ tasya ananya tvam sādhyam atas na kiṃcid etat kim ca anyat rūpa vyavasthānāt ca tat yathā vijñāna utpatti hetutve sati na rūpam dṛṣṭam iti na idānīm tad sāmānyāt rūpam api arūpam bhavati evam paṭa kāraṇa tvāt vema ādayaḥ na paṭaḥ iti na idānīm tantava upya paṭaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat śaktasya śakya karaṇāt satkāryam kāraṇa bhāvāt ca satkāryam 
[II,25,ii^1]	iha asati kārye kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na asti tat yathā vandhyāyāḥ asti ca iha kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tantu paṭayoḥ tasmāt satkāryam kāraṇa antarāt kārya utpatti darśanāt anyatra tad buddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam prāk kāraṇa antarāt kārya antarasya asataḥ utpattim upalabhya paścāt kāraṇa antare kāraṇa buddhiḥ bhavati iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt anabhyupagamāt asataḥ kāryasya utpattiḥ eva na siddhā śaśa viṣāṇa ādiṣu asiddha tvāt kutas punar tad nimitta ākāra buddhiḥ kāraṇa bhāvāt iti ced syāt etat asattva aviśeṣe api paṭasya kāraṇam samavāyi asamavāyi nimitta lakṣaṇam asti tasmāt paṭaḥ ucyate na śaśa viṣāṇasya iti etat ca ayuktam kutas hetu abhāvāt asattva aviśeṣe api paṭasya kāraṇam asti na śaśa viṣāṇasya iti atra hetuḥ anuktaḥ 
[II,25,ii^2]	puruṣa vat iti ced syāt etat yathā tulya tve sattve paṭasya kāraṇam asti na puruṣasya evam asattve paṭasya saṃsthānam na śaśa viṣāṇasya iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt ukta tvāt saṃsthānam kāryam paṭasya saṃsthānam na puruṣasya iti uktam prāk saṃsthāna vat tad viśeṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā sattva aviśeṣe paṭaḥ saṃsthānam na puruṣaḥ evam asattva aviśeṣe paṭaḥ kāryam na śaśaviṣāṇam iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvāt sāmānyasya hi viśeṣa parigrahaḥ saṃsthānam na tu ayam asti cetanā śaktau vikalpaḥ tasmāt na puruṣaḥ saṃsthānam asataḥ tu nirātmaka tvāt viśeṣaḥ durupapādaḥ tad upapattau vā sattva prasaṃgaḥ iti āha ca nirātmaka tvāt asatām sarveṣām aviśiṣṭa tā viśeṣaṇam ced bhinnam te sattvam abhyupagamyatām 
[II,26,i_II,28,i]	tasmāt yuktam etat kāraṇa bhāvāt ca satkāryam evam tāvat vaiśeṣika matena asat kārya vādaḥ na vimarda sahaḥ bauddha pakṣe tu bhūyān doṣaḥ katham tarhi dravya antaram paṭaḥ na iṣyate tantuṣu eva tathā stheṣu paṭaḥ ityādi buddhayaḥ iti evamādinā nyāyena avayavi pratiṣedhāt saṃyogaḥ api na saṃyogibhyaḥ teṣām artha antaram iṣṭaḥ tatra etāvatī parikalpanā syāt yat uta tantu saṃyogaḥ vā paṭaḥ saṃyoga kāraṇam vā dravya antaram ubhayam ca teṣām na artha antaram atha utpatti vināśau kasya api iti māyākāra ceṣṭitam tat api citrataraḥ ayam upanyāsaḥ kāṇādānām tu dravya antara uttpati vināśa abhyupagamāt na tārkika sadṛśaḥ vicāraḥ tasmāt pāramarṣaḥ eva pakṣaḥ jyāyān yathā ca asat kāryam na saṃbhavati tathā caśabdāt sadasat kāryam api paraspara virodhāt na eva sanna asat iti eke etat api anupapannam kasmāt sattve hetu abhidhānāt niścitaḥ prāk utpatteḥ kāryasya sadbhāvaḥ 
[II,33,i_II,33,ii]	prakṛtam idānīm vakṣyāmaḥ kim ca prakṛtam mahat ādi tat ca kāryam prakṛti virūpam sarūpam ca iti vacanāt vairūpyam āha prāk sārūpya grahaṇam sukha pratipatti hetu tvāt adhigata sārūpyasya hi sukham vairūpyasya pratipattiḥ bhavati iti prāc sārūpya grahaṇam kartavyam yathā tantra antarīyāṇām sat anityam dravya vat kāryam kāraṇam sāmānya viśeṣa vat iti dravya guṇa karmaṇā ām aviśeṣa sāmānyam uktvā dravyāṇi dravya antaram ārabhante guṇāḥ ca guṇa antaram iti evamādiḥ viśeṣaḥ abhidhīyate 
[II,33,iii_II,34,i]	ucyate tad anupapattiḥ aviśeṣāt yathā eva adhigata sārūpyasya laghīyasī vairūpya pratipattiḥ evam adhigata vairūpyasya laghīyasī sārūpya pratipattiḥ kasmāt paraspara apekṣa tvāt vairūpya apekṣam hi sārūpyam sārūpya apekṣam ca vairūpyam iti āha evam api vairūpyasya prāc abhidhāne prayojana vacanam dvayoḥ aviśeṣe anyatarasya prāc abhidhāne niyama hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ iti 
[II,34,ii]	ucyate na vairūpyasya prakaraṇa anaṅga bhāvāt vicchinnam hi vairūpyam atas tad pūrvam abhidhāya prakaraṇa aṅgam sārūpyam sukham abhidhātum iti evam artham ācāryeṇa evam kriyate katham sārūpyasya prakaraṇa aṅga tvam iti ced traiguṇya abhidhāna dvāreṇa guṇa lakṣaṇa upadeśāt tad siddhau ca aviveki a ādīnām vyakta siddheḥ kāraṇa guṇa ātmaka tvāt ca kāryasya pradhāne traiguṇya ādi pratipatteḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva āsan dehāt ca pradhāna astitva prasiddhi apadeśāt tad siddhau ca bhogyasya bhoktṛ apekṣa tvāt puruṣa siddheḥ adhigata bhoktṛ bhogyasya tad saṃyogasya ca sukha pratipādya tvāt tādarthyāt ca tattva bhūta bhāva sargāṇām tasmāt yuktam etat prakaraṇa aṅga tvāt sārūpyam paścāt nirdiśyate tad asambandhāt itarat prāk iti 
[II,35,i_II,35,iii]	āha yadi tarhi bhavān prāc vairūpya abhidhānam nyāyyam manyate tat vaktavyam kim punar idam vairūpyam iti ucyate hetu mada nityam avyāpi sa kriyam anekam āśritam liṅgam sa avayavam paratantram vyaktam viparītam avyaktam tatra hetuḥ kāraṇam iti anarthāntaram tat asya asti iti hetumat nityam dhruvam na nityam anityam vyāpnoti iti vyāpi na vyāpī avyāpi asarva gatam iti arthaḥ saha kriyayā sa kriyam anekam bhinnam āśritam ādheyam liṅgam tad lakṣaṇa upapannam avayūyante iti avayavāḥ pṛthak upalabhyante iti arthaḥ saha avayavaiḥ sa avayavam paratantram anya adhīnam ete hetumat a ādayaḥ paratantra antāḥ nirapavādāḥ vyaktasya asādhāraṇā pradhāna puruṣābhyām dharmāḥ 
[II,36,i_II,36,iii]	āha hetum aditi aviśeṣaḥ sarvatra sadbhāvāt vyakta avyakta puruṣāṇām hi sarveṣām hetuḥ asti iti aviśeṣaḥ eva ayam paṭhitavyaḥ ucyate na kāraka parigrahāt yadi api vyakta avyakta puruṣāṇām aviśiṣṭam hetumat tvam tathā api viśiṣṭasya kārakasya hetoḥ parigraham kariṣyāmaḥ sa ca vyaktasya eva na anyasya iti na ayam aviśeṣaḥ bhaviṣyati āha tad anupapattiḥ viśeṣa anupādānāt hetuḥ iti sāmānya śabdaḥ ayam sāmānya śabdāḥ ca na artha prakaraṇa śabda antara abhisambandham antareṇa viśeṣe avatiṣṭhante iti viśeṣaḥ upādeyaḥ syāt sa tu na upādīyate tasmāt te aviśeṣāḥ eva iti 
[II,36,iv]	ucyate na sarva sambhavinaḥ abhidhānasya prakarṣa artha tvāt iha yaḥ sarva saṃbhavī dharmaḥ eka viṣayaḥ upādīyate tasmāt prakarṣaḥ vijñāyate tat yathā bhoktā māṇavakaḥ iti ukte sarveṣām bhoktṛ tvasya saṃbhavāt evam vijñāyate prakarṣeṇa ayam bhoktā iti evam iha api sarva sambhavi iti āha ācāryaḥ vyaktam hetumat iti tena vayam asmāt prakarṣam vijñāsyāmaḥ kaḥ ca prakarṣaḥ kāraka jñāpakayoḥ ubhayoḥ api sambhave kārakasya eva grahaṇam anitya śabda sambandhāt vā athavā ayam ācāryaḥ hetumat iti uktvā anityam iti paṭhati śabda antara abhisambandhāt yaḥ anitya sahacaraḥ hetuḥ tasya iha grahaṇam gamyate kaḥ ca anitya sahacaraḥ hetuḥ kārakaḥ 
[II,37,i_II,37,ii]	āha evam api anupapannam etat kasmāt ubhayatra tad saṃbhavāt utpādya vyaṅgyayoḥ hi vināśam paṭa ādiṣu dṛṣṭa tvāt avyabhicārāt tantra antarīyāḥ manyante tasya vā parihāraḥ vaktavyaḥ na vā vaktavyaḥ viśeṣe sthitiḥ asti iti ucyate na ekānta vāda prasaṅgāt sarveṇa hi vādinā avaśyam kiṃcid nityam abhyupagantavyam antatas vināśe api na kaścid arthaḥ śabda buddhibhyām na vyajyate tathā sati ekānta vādaḥ ayam syāt sa ca yuktimadbhiḥ na iṣyate tathā ca saṃskṛtam api evam kalpyamāne vināśi syāt tasmāt utpādyavyaṅgyayoḥ vināśam bruvataḥ ati sāhasam 
[II,38,i_II,38,ii]	āha anitya tva anupapattiḥ satkārya vāda abhyupagamāt yathā eva hi na asataḥ utpattiḥ asti evam sataḥ api vināśena na bhavitavyam atha sataḥ api vināśaḥ abhyupagamyate tena pralaya kāle vinaṣṭānām tattva ādīnām praścāda satām utpattiḥ satkārya vādam nirākuryāt tasmāt anityam vyaktam iti ayuktam ucyate na vyakti apagama pratijñānāt sadā vayam sataḥ avināśam ācakṣāṇāḥ satkārya vādam pratyācakṣīmahi kāraṇānām tu yaḥ parasparam saṃsargāt saṃsthāna viśeṣa parigrahaḥ tasya virodhi śakti antarāvirbhavāt vyaktiḥ tirodhīyate iti etat vināśa śabdena vivakṣitam tathā ca vārṣa gaṇāḥ paṭhanti tat etat trailokyam vyakteḥ apaiti na sattvāt apetam api asti vināśa pratiṣedhāt asaṃsargāt ca asya saukṣmyam saukṣmyāt ca anupalabdhiḥ tasmāt vyakti apagamaḥ vināśaḥ sa tu dvividhaḥ ā sarga pralayāt tattvānām kiñcid kāla antara avasthānāt itareṣām iti 
[II,39,i]	āha ayuktam etat kasmāt vipratipatteḥ sarvam eva kṣaṇikam buddhi bodhyam ākāśa nirodha varjitam iti śākya putrīyāḥ pratipannāḥ teṣām pratiṣedhaḥ vaktavyaḥ vā na vaktavyam dvividham anityam iti ucyate na hetu anupagamāt pratikṣaṇam ucchidyate trailokyam iti atra liṅgam abhiyuktāḥ api na upalabhāmahe tasmāt na etat asmākam buddhau avatiṣṭhate iti 
[II,39,ii_II,40,i]	āha ante kṣaya darśanāt iha yasya ante kṣayaḥ tasya kṣaṇika tvam dṛṣṭam tat yathā pradīpa jvālā buddhi śabdānām asti ca ante kṣayaḥ saṃskārāṇām tasmāt kṣaṇikā ucyate tad anupapattiḥ sādhya tvāt iha tu siddhena atideśaḥ bhavati tat yathā gavā gavayasya na tu pradīpa jvālā buddhi śabdānām kṣaṇika tvam prasiddham atas na kiñcid etat 
[II,40,ii^1]	āha na etat aprasiddham kasmāt vṛddhi adarśanāt yadi hi avinaṣṭāyām jvālāyām indhana antarāle jvālā antaram utpadyeta vṛddhiḥ api syāt na tu dṛśyate tasmāt anavasthitā pradīpa jvālā kiñca āśraya abhāvāt yad āśrayā jvālā utpattiḥ tad utpadyamānā eva asau niruṇaddhi iti na yuktam asyāḥ vinā āśrayeṇa avasthātum upayukta indhanāyāḥ api avasthāna prasaṅgāt kiñca āvaraṇa upari pātena prabhā bheda prasaṅgāt jvālānām avasthānam icchate upariṣṭāt āvaraṇa upanipātāt prabhāyāḥ tantoḥ iva dvaidhīkaraṇam syāt aniṣṭañca etat tasmāt na dīpe jvālānām avasthitiḥ asti iti etena śabdaḥ api pratyuktaḥ katham
