[II,40,ii^2]	tasya api yadi vināśaḥ na syāt druta pavana ambu dhārā abhighātāt pratikṣaṇam apūrva śabda āvirbhāvāt pūrva śabda vināśāt ca vṛddhiḥ syāt adṛṣṭā ca asau kiñca pratyakṣataḥ upalabdheḥ pāṇi upaghāta jaḥ hi śabdaḥ utpatteḥ ūrdhvam na bhavati iti pratyakṣa siddham abhivyaktiḥ iti ced na niyama adarśanāt śabdānām vācya vaktṛ bheda bhinnānām kāraṇa niyamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na ca etat asti samāna indriya grāhyāṇām kiñca pṛthak śruteḥ abhivyakti kāraṇa deśāt ca pṛthak śrūyate śabdaḥ na ca etat abhivyaṅgyānām ghaṭa ādīnām dṛṣṭam iti kṣaṇika buddheḥ tu prāk eva uktāḥ nāśa hetavaḥ tatra yat uktam sādhya tvāt pradīpa jvālā buddhi śabda ādīnām kṣaṇika tvasya na saṃskārāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ iti etat ayuktam 
[II,41,i^1]	ucyate yat uktam vṛddhi adarśanāt iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt viśeṣa pratipatteḥ kṣaṇikam iti ukta parimāṇaḥ ayam kāla nirdeśaḥ āśrīyate vṛddhi abhāva ādibhyaḥ ca kadācid vināśa mātram pratīyate sa tu vināśaḥ ekakṣaṇam avasthitānām jvālānām bhavati na punar kṣaṇa dvayam iti etat apramāṇakam ājñā mātrañca gṛhīta śikṣākaḥ kaḥ pratipattum utsaheta yat tu uktam āvaraṇa upanipātāt prabhā bheda prasaṅgaḥ iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt ubhayathā anupapatteḥ kim tāvat yasya dvaidhībhāvaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tad akṣaṇikam āhosvit yasya na dṛṣṭaḥ tat kṣaṇikam iti kiñcātas tat yadi tāvat evam abhyupagamyate yasya dvaidhībhāvaḥ tat akṣaṇikam iti tanta urakṣaṇika tva prasaṅgaḥ atha matam yasya dvaidhīkaraṇam na dṛṣṭam tat kṣaṇikam iti yathā kim atra udāharaṇam kutas yasmāt na hi anudāhṛtaḥ vādaḥ 
[II,41,i^2]	etena śabda vṛddhiḥ pratyuktā yat punar etat uktam pāṇi upaghāta ja śabdān avasthānāt iti tatra bhavatā eva uktam vyaṅgya tvāt iti yat tu uktam niyama darśanāt na vyaṅgyaḥ śabdaḥ iti tat ayuktam anekāntāt yathā śukla kṛṣṇau niyamataḥ śukla kṛṣṇa śabdābhyām pratyāyyete na ca tau tayoḥ na vyaṅgyau evam śabdasya api vakti avādi niyamaḥ syāt na ca avyaṅgyaḥ syāt yat api uktam vyaṅgya vyañjakayoḥ deśa bhedānupapatteḥ na vyaṅgyaḥ śabdaḥ iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt cakṣuḥ vat tad siddheḥ tat yathā cakṣuṣaḥ rūpasya ca deśa bhede api vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvaḥ evam śabdasya api syāt tasmāt na śabdaḥ api kṣaṇikaḥ buddheḥ tu sva adhikāraḥ eva kṣaṇika tva hetu nirākaraṇam vakṣyāmaḥ tatra yat uktam ante kṣaya darśanāt pradīpa jvālā buddhi śabda vat kṣaṇikāḥ saṃskārāḥ iti etat ayuktam iti 
[II,43,i_II,43,ii]	āha itas tarhi pradīpa ādīnām anyeṣām ca bhāvānām kṣaṇika tvam kutas anavasthāna hetu abhāvāt naṣṭaḥ ced arthaḥ abhyupagamyate nanu prāptam idam utpanna mātrasya asya vināśa vighnaḥ na asti iti kauṭasthyam sarva bhāvānām prāptam iti ucyate na kāraṇa upapatteḥ adhikāraḥ hi sarva bhūtānām saṃskāra vaśāt utpattiḥ tad avasthānam eva teṣām alam sthitaye sati vinaśvara tve saṃskāra upayoge tu sthiti apabhraṃśaḥ iti atas asti kiñcid kālam avasthānam bhāvānām na ca kauṭasthya prasaṅgaḥ kiñca anyat santati vināśa prasaṅgāt naṃṣṭuḥ ced utpatti samanantaram vināśaḥ iṣyate santatiḥ api ante kṣaya darśanāt naṃṣṭrī tasyāḥ api tathā eva vināśaḥ prāptaḥ tatas ca taḍit vilasita vat kṣaṇa dṛṣṭa naṣṭasya trailokyasya abhāve saṃsāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt ayuktam naṃṣṭuḥ utpatti sama kālam eva vināśaḥ iti 
[II,44,i]	kāraṇa avasthānāt na doṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam asti kāraṇam pūrva utpannaḥ bhāvaḥ uttarasya utpattau sa ca api uttarasya iti evam santateḥ anucchedaḥ virodhi bhāva antara saṃsargāt tu ubhayatas tathā utpatteḥ bhraṃśaḥ iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt pūrva hetu tyāgāt prāk uktam yena naṃṣṭavyam asau mantra auṣadha prayogaiḥ api kṣaṇāt ūrddhvam na avatiṣṭhate sāmpratam tu naṃṣṭrī santatiḥ kāraṇa vaśāt eva tiṣṭhati iti saḥ ayam pūrva hetu tyāgaḥ 
[II,45,i]	vināśa hetu abhāvāt kṣaṇika tvam iti ced syāt etat na asti bhāvānām vināśa hetoḥ upalambhaḥ iti atas svābhāvikaḥ pradhvaṃsaḥ tasmāt utpatti sama kālam asau kena vāryate idam api ayuktam kasmāt anabhyupagamāt kaḥ hi etat avamaṃsyati ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ kim tarhi prāk eva uktam artha vaśāt bhāvānām sthitiḥ tad ava virodhi dravya antara sambandhena ādhyātmika ādinā bhavati iti 
[II,45,ii]	vināśasya vināśa prasaṅgāt ayuktam iti ced yadi tarhi abhāvaḥ api hetumān parikalpyate prāptam asya api ghaṭa vat vināśi tvam aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ iti etat ayuktam kasmāt vyakti apagama pratijñānāt bhāva vināśinam prati satyam eva ayam upālambhaḥ syāt vyakti apagamaḥ tu naḥ vināśaḥ sa tu hetumat tvena katham virotsyate iti tasmāt na vināśa hetu abhāvāt kṣaṇikam saṃskṛtam iti 
[II,45,iii_II,46,i]	itas ca na kṣaṇikam kasmāt agrahaṇa prasaṅgāt iha asataḥ agrahaṇam dṛṣṭam tat yathā dvitīyasya śirasaḥ kṣaṇāt ūrdhvam ca te ghaṭa ādayaḥ na bhavanti tasmāt teṣām api agrahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tad sadṛśa utpatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt etat utpatti sama kālam nirodhe api ghaṭasya anyasya tādṛśasya utpattiḥ bhavati tad nirodhe anyasya iti evam avicchedena grahaṇam bhavati jvālā nadī srotaḥ anusandhāna vat iti etat api ayuktam kutas kāraṇa abhāvāt syāt etat evam yadi tadānīm sadṛśa utpattau kāraṇam syāt na tu tat asti prāk eva nirodhāt tasmāt asat etat 
[II,46,ii]	pūrva utpannasya kāraṇa bhāvāt tad siddhiḥ iti ced na upādānāt tad niṣpatti prasiddheḥ iha upādānāt mṛd piṇḍaka saṃjñakāt loke ghaṭa niṣpattiḥ prasiddhā na ca tadā animasti mṛd piṇḍaḥ kiñca kramanupalabdheḥ iha śibikā ādīnām anukrameṇa ghaṭotpattiḥ upalabhyate na ca anukramaḥ asti kiñca kāraka sāmagrya abhavāt iha kumbhakāra daṇḍa cakra sūtra upalasāmagryāt ghaṭa niṣpattiḥ prasiddhā na ca asti eṣām tatra sambhavaḥ kiñca tad utpādya antara utpādyasya aniṣpatteḥ iha ghaṭāt ghaṭe nirvṛttiḥ na prasiddhā loke na ca aprasiddhaḥ asti dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
[II,47,i]	buddhi śabda vat iti ced syāt etat yathā buddhiḥ buddhi antaram sadṛśam sūte śabdaḥ ca śabda antaram evam ghaṭāt ghaṭa niṣpattiḥ bhavati iti etat api asat kasmāt siddham hi buddheḥ buddhi antaram śabdāt ca śabda antaram jāyate iti etat api asmākam prasiddham tasmāt pralāpa mātram etat tatra yat uktam sadṛśa utpatteḥ saḥ ayam iti grahaṇam avicchinnam kṣaṇika tve api bhāvānām iti etat ayuktam kiñca anyat kārya utpatti kāle kāraṇa nivṛtteḥ yadā na kāraṇam asti na tadā kāryam utpadyate dvayoḥ ghaṭayoḥ yugapad upalabdhi prasaṅgāt yadā tu kāryam utpadyate tadā kāraṇam niruddham iti nirbījaḥ pradurbhāvaḥ prāpnoti aniṣṭam ca etat satata utpatti prasaṃgāt 
[II,48,i]	anutpanne hetu sāmarthyāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt tad anutpanne kārye kāraṇena prayojanam utpanne tad vyāpārānarthakyāt asti ca anutpanne kārye kāraṇam atas na nirbījaḥ prādurbhāvaḥ iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt abhāve api tad utpatti prasaṅgāt aṃga tāvat aṇuśas vibhajyatām agnau vā kṣipyantām tantavaḥ tadā api prasiddha vināśānām abhūvan iti śakyam upadeṣṭum yadi tebhyaḥ paṭe utpadyate tasmāt bhrāntiḥ iyam 
[II,48,ii]	yugapad kārya kāraṇayoḥ utpatti nirodhau tulānata unnata vat iti ced syāt etat yathā nāma unnāmau tulā antaryā yaugapadyena bhavataḥ evam utpatti vināśau kārya kāraṇayoḥ iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva adarśanāt kim idam udake nimajjadbhiḥ phenam avalambyate tulyā tasya hi ekasya avanatiḥ avasthā tat dvitīyasya unnataye hetuḥ bhavati bhavataḥ kāraṇa vināśaḥ kārya utpattiḥ ca yaugapadyena bhavataḥ na ca tayoḥ hetumat bhāvaḥ śakyaḥ kalpayitum tasmāt ayuktam etat 
[II,49,i]	viśeṣa grahaṇāt kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi utpanna mātra uparatiḥ na asti bhāvānām kiṃka yutaḥ śarīra ādīnām prāṇa apāna śrama rūpa ādi kṛtaḥ abja aśma prabhṛtīnām ca śīta uṣṇa sparśa kṛtaḥ bhedaḥ ghaṇṭā ādīnām ca aśabdakānām paścāt śabdavatām grahaṇam tasmāt aniṣiddhaḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt ukta tvāt uktam atra uttaram kāraṇa abhāve anutpatti prasaṅgāt iti kiñca saṃsthāna antara anupaladheḥ na hi atra pūrva saṃśāna viparītam saṃsthāna antaram gṛhṇīmahe tasmāt aviśiṣṭāḥ te iti evam avagamyatām viśeṣa grahaṇantvavastu antara anugrahe śakti antarāvirbhāvāt uktam ca vyakteḥ apagamaḥ abhīṣṭaḥ pūrva saṃsthāna hānitaḥ tad abhāvāt asidhaḥ asya viśe 
[II,52,i_II,52,iii]	sattvam laghu prakāśakam iṣṭam upaṣṭambhakam calam ca rajaḥ guru varaṇakam eva tamaḥ eva śabdaḥ pratyekam pariśama āpyate sattvam laghu prakāṣakam eva iṣṭam yat kiṃcid kārya karaṇe laghu prakāśam ca tat sattva rūpam iti pratyavagantavyam tatra kāryasya tāvat udgama hetuḥ dharmaḥ laghu tvam karaṇasya vṛtti paṭu tva hetuḥ prakāśaḥ tu pṛthivī dharmasya cchāyā lakṣaṇasya tamasaḥ tiraskāreṇa dravya antara prakāśanam karaṇasya api grahaṇam saṅkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāya viṣayeṣu yathāsvam pravartamānam 
[II,52,iv]	upaṣṭambhakam calam eva rajaḥ yaḥ kaścid upastambhaḥ cala tā ca upalabhyate tat rajaḥ rūpam iti avagantavyam tatra upastambhaḥ prayatnaḥ calatā kriyā sā ca dvividhā pariṇāma lakṣaṇā praspanda lakṣaṇā ca tatra pariṇāma lakṣaṇayā saha kāri bhāva antara anugṛhītasya dharmiṇaḥ pūrva dharmāt pracyutiḥ praspanda lakṣaṇā prāṇa ādayaḥ karmendriya vṛttayaḥ ca vacana ādyāḥ bāhyānām dravyāṇām utpatana nipatana bhramaṇa ādīni 
[II,53,i]	guru varaṇakam eva tamaḥ yat kiṃcid gauravam varaṇam ca upalabhyate tat tamaḥ rūpam iti pratyavagantavyam tatra guru tvam kāryasya adhas gamana hetuḥ dharmaḥ karaṇasya vṛtti mandatā varaṇam api kārya gatam ca dravya antara tirodhānam karaṇa gatā ca aśuddhiḥ prakāśa pratidvandvibhūtā iti eṣa sattva ādīnām avyatikareṇa svabhāva upalambhaḥ yatas eṣām nānātvam avasīyate 
[II,53,ii]	yat punar etat uktam strī kṣatra megheṣu svabhāva vyatikara upalambhāt ekaḥ guṇaḥ trirūpaḥ sarve vā sarva rūpā rūpa antarasya vā sataḥ utpattiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na guṇa bhūtasya bhaktitaḥ upakārāt pradhāna rūpa upapatteḥ iha guṇa bhūtasya bhaktitaḥ pradhāna upakāri tve sati bhaktitaḥ tad rūpa upapattiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā kṣīra ādeḥ tat hi mukha ādiṣu dṛṣṭa pratilabdha pravṛttiḥ pittasya svena rūpeṇa aṅga bhāvam gacchan tasya upakārāt tiktam saṃpadyate na ca tathā sat eva sattvam api straiṇa guṇa bhūtam sapatnī rajasaḥ svena rūpeṇa aṅga bhāvam gacchan tasya upakārāt duḥkham saṃpadyate tamasaḥ mohaḥ evam kṣātram rajaḥ ārya dāra lakṣaṇasya sattvasya dasyu lakṣaṇasya ca tamasaḥ evam medhyam tamaḥ kārṣike sattvasya proṣita dayitāyāḥ ca rajasaḥ tasmāt na asti guṇānām svābhāva vyatikaraḥ kim ca anyat aguṇa bhūtānām svabhāva grahaṇāt yadā ca ete aṅga bhāvam apagacchantaḥ madhyasthāḥ tulya saṃskārāḥ ca pratipadyante tadā sva rūpeṇa eva tasmāt asaṃkīrṇam guṇa rūpam 
[II,54,i_II,54,ii]	āha na sandehāt ubhayathā hi rūpa antara grahaṇam kṣīra ādiṣu dṛṣṭam tādrūpyāt taiḥ ca vipariṇatānām guṇa bhāvāt ca yathā uktam tatra katham idam ekāntena niścīyante guṇa bhāvāt sattva ādīnām rūpa antara grahaṇam na punar tādrūpyāt eva iti ucyate grahaṇa vikalpa upalambhāt yadi straiṇam sattvam tādrūpyāt eva sapatnyā tena gṛhyate tena bhartuḥ api tathā grahaṇa prasaṃgaḥ madhyasthānām tulya saṃskārāṇām ca aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt bhāktaḥ ayam guṇa vikalpa upalambhaḥ kim ca anyat uttara kālam svarūpa grahaṇāt nivṛtta anuśayābhiḥ ca eka artha tām upagatābhiḥ sapatnībhiḥ svena eva rūpeṇa straiṇasya sattvasya grahaṇam upalabhyate sva gṛha sam avasthitaiḥ ca ārya dāraiḥ kṣatriyāṇām niṣpanna śasyaiḥ ca kṛṣīvalaiḥ meghānām tasmāt bhāktaḥ ayam grahaṇa vikalpa upalambhaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat anyaḥ anya janana vṛttayaḥ guṇāḥ na ca saṃkīrṇa svabhāvāḥ iti 
[II,55,i_II,56,i]	yat punar etat uktam anyonya mithuna tva anupapattiḥ sattvasya itara virodhāt iti atra brūmaḥ asti ca ayam virodhaḥ guṇānām pradīpa vat ca arthataḥ vṛttiḥ kim utpadyate iti vākya śeṣaḥ tat yathā varti jyotiḥ tailānām paraspara virodhe api pradīpa karaṇa eka kārya sādhana bhāva upagatānām vṛttaye ekatra saṃmūrchitāḥ sahabhāvaḥ prakṛṣṭam api kālam anubhavanti evam sattva rajaḥ tamasām sati virodhe mahat ādi eka kārya sādhana bhāva upagatānām vṛttaye ekatra mūrchitāḥ saha bhavanti iti yukti abhāvāt asiddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam kā punar atra yuktiḥ yena virodhinām eka kārya tā bhavati iti 
[II,56,ii_II,57,i]	ucyate guṇa pradhāna bhāvāt guṇa bhūtaḥ hi pratiyogī pradhāna bhūtena tad upakaraka tvāt na virudhyate iti saṃsargeṇa varttitum utsahate tulya balayoḥ tu dvayoḥ satyam eva saha avasthānasya na asti sambandhaḥ tathā ca bhagavān vārṣagaṇyaḥ paṭhati rūpa atiśayāḥ vṛtti atiśayāḥ ca virudhyante sāmānyāni tu atiśayaiḥ saha vartante tat yathā jala agnī pacanīyasvedanīyeṣu kāryeṣu chāyā ātapau ca sūkṣma rūprakāśane śīta uṣṇe ca prajā avasthitau evam tat siddhaḥ pradīpa vat sattva rajaḥ tamasām virodhe api sahabhāvaḥ āha yat uktam laghu ādi bhāva svabhāva bhedāt guṇa nānā tvam iti atra brūmaḥ bhinnāḥ lakṣaṇa bhedāḥ ced mithas sattva ādayaḥ guṇāḥ tarhi lakṣaṇa yukta tvāt ṣaḍguṇāḥ prāpnuvanti te 
[II,57,ii]	yadi laghu ādi lakṣaṇa bhedāt sattva ādīnām nānātvam mithas abhyupagamyate tena laghu tva prakāśa tvayoḥ api bhedaḥ asti guṇa dvaya prasaṃgaḥ evam upastambha calatābhyām gaurava varaṇābhyām ca dvayam dvayam iti ṣaḍguṇāḥ prāpnuvanti atha matam laghu tva prakāśayoḥ abhedaḥ iti pṛthak anabhidhānam prāptam tad bhede vā grahaṇa bhedam anicchataḥ prāptaḥ laghu tva ādi bhede api guṇa abhedaḥ tathā ca ekaḥ guṇaḥ iti prāptam yat punar etat uktam guṇa bhūtasya bhaktitaḥ upakārāt pradhāna rūpa āpattiḥ iti aṅga bhāvam vrajat sattvam duḥkham sampadyate yadi vairūpyasya upasaṃhārāt pūrva doṣā nivartanam 
[II,57,iii_II,57,v]	yadi hi rajasaḥ aṅga bhāvam upagacchat sattvam upakārāt tad rūpam bhavati tena pratijñātasya rūpa antarasya upasaṃhārāt trairūpyam guṇānām ekaikasya prāptam rūpa antarasya vā sataḥ utpattiḥ tasmāt pūrva doṣa aparihārāt pratijñā mātram eva ayam samādhiḥ yat api uktam aguṇa bhūtānām svabhāva grahaṇāt iti aṅga bhāva anapekṣam tu grahaṇam na asti ṛṣeḥ api parama ṛṣeḥ api guṇānām kāryam eva pratyakṣam na śakti mātreṇa avasthānam asaṃvedya tvāt tatra cāṅā aṅgi bhāva gamanam anivāryam tasmāt doṣam anicchatāḥ guṇāḥ parityājyāḥ na asti vā su dūram api gatvā tad saṃkara doṣa parihāraḥ 
[II,58,i^1]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam lakṣaṇa bhedāt guṇa nānā tva vādinaḥ lakṣaṇa dvaya yogāt ekaikasya guṇa ṣaṭtva prasaṃgaḥ iti tat na kasmāt dvayoḥ guṇa pradhāna bhāva anupapatteḥ iha artha antarasya artha antareṇa guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ bhavati yathā strī kṣatra megheṣu vyākhyātam na ca laghu tva prakāśayoḥ upastambha calanayoḥ gaurava varaṇayoḥ ca mithau guṇa pradhāna bhāvaḥ asti tad anartha antaram dharmāḥ te iti na asti ṣaṭtva prasaṃgaḥ iti kim ca aprasiddha tvāt na hi etat kvacid prasiddham yathā yāvantaḥ dharmāḥ tāvantaḥ dharmiṇaḥ iti na ca aprasiddhena vyavahāraḥ kiṃca pṛthaktvā ekānta prasaṅgāt lakṣaṇa bhedāt nānātva pratijñasya sarva arthānām sva sāmānya lakṣaṇa yogāt svataḥ artha antaram iti pṛthaktvā ekānta prasaṃgaḥ atha etat aniṣṭam na tarhi vaktavyam lakṣaṇa bhedāt guṇānām ṣaṭtvam iti 
[II,58,i^2]	yat punar etat uktam aṅga bhūtasya pradhāna rūpa āpatteḥ pūrva doṣa anivṛttiḥ iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt bhakti abhidhānāt asakṛt adhītam asmābhiḥ bhāktaḥ ayam guṇānām grahaṇa vikalpaḥ iti na ca bhaktiḥ parama arthaḥ iti asthāne yatnaḥ yat punar etat uktam aguṇa bhūtānām sattva ādīnām ṛṣeḥ api aviṣaya tvam iti satyam etat yat tu uktam kāryasya viṣaya bhūta tvāt aṅga aṅgibhāva gamanam guṇānām sakala satkāryam apekṣate tathā strī kṣatra meghāḥ prakṛta asteṣu aṅga bhāvam agacchate iti vijñāyate iti sāmānya śabdānām hi prakaraṇāt viśeṣe avasthānam bhavati tat yathā bhojana kāle saindhavam ānayā iti ukte lavaṇe saṃpratipattiḥ na aśu ādiṣu tasmāt prakaraṇam anapekṣya mahati tantre doṣa abhidhānam bāla vākya sthānīyam evam guṇa lakṣaṇa upadeśāt siddham traiguṇyam 
[II,64,i_II,64,iv]	āha aviveki ādiḥ idānīm gaṇaḥ katham pratipattavyaḥ iti ucyate aviveki ādiḥ siddhaḥ traiguṇyāt yat triguṇam tat aviveki viṣayaḥ sāmānyam acetanam prasava dharmī iti katham avagamyate iti ced tad viparyaya abhāvāt yasmāt guṇa viparyayaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ tatra viṣaya tvam acetana tvam prasava dharmi tvam ca na bhavati iti purastāt pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt pariśeṣataḥ vyakte eteṣām dharmāṇām avirodhaḥ 
[II,64,v_II,65,ii]	āha tathā pradhānam iti prāk uktam bhavatā tat idānīm katham pratipattavyam pradhānam api triguṇa ādi yuktam iti ucyate kāraṇa guṇa ātmaka tvāt kāryasya avyaktam api siddham iha kāraṇa guṇa ātmakam kāryam dṛṣṭam paṭa ādi vyakte ca traiguṇya ādi upalabhyate tasmāt kāraṇam api asya tathā ajātīyakam iti śakyam anumātum siddhānta mātra upadarśanam etat ācāryaḥ karoti nyāyam tu yathā ukteṣu pradeśeṣu upapādayiṣyāmaḥ 
[II,67,i_II,67,ii]	āha kārya dharmasya kāraṇa upalabdhau hetumadādi prasaṃgaḥ aviśeṣāt yadi kārye dṛṣṭasya dharmasya kāraṇe sadbhāvaḥ abhyupagamyate prāptau hetumat ādīnām api dharmāṇām kārya dṛṣṭa tvāt pradhāne prasaṃgaḥ atha kārya upalabdhau tulyāyām hetumat a ādayaḥ neṣyante na tarhi itareṣām api kāraṇa avasthitiḥ asti iti ucyate na sva rūpa virodhi tve tad apavāda vijñānāt kāraṇa guṇa ātmaka tvāt kāryasya iti anena liṅgena hetumat a ādayaḥ api kāraṇe prasajyante teṣām tu kārya kāraṇa rūpa virodhi tvāt apavādaḥ vijñāyate katham yadi tāvat hetumada ādayaḥ vyakte dṛṣṭa tvāt pradhāne vyañjante kṛtaka tvāt kāryam eva tat na kāraṇam iti prāptam anitya tvāt ca svayam ucchidyamānam ananugrāhakam avyāpi tvā ādibhiḥ ca ananta vikāra utpādana śakti hīnam ahetu mada ādayaḥ pradhāne abhyupagamāt vyakteḥ api prāpyante tādṛśāḥ kāraṇā sambhavāt kāryam eva tat na bhavati iti prāptam aviveki ādayaḥ tu ubhayatra api bhavantaḥ na itaretara svarūpa virodhinaḥ tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhyupagamāt hetumada ādi apavādaḥ itareṣām ca kāraṇa sadbhāvaḥ siddhaḥ 
[II,68,i_II,68,ii]	yat uktam kāraṇa guṇa ātmaka tvāt kāryasya avyaktam api siddham iti tat ayuktam kasmāt vyakta avyaktayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva aprasiddheḥ siddhe hi vyakta avyaktayoḥ kāraṇa tve etat evam syāt tattva siddham tasmāt ayuktam etat viśeṣān abhidhānāt ubhaya sāmyam iti ced syāt matam yathā bhavān āha vyakta avyaktayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ aprasiddhaḥ evam vayam vakṣyāmaḥ tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva aprasiddhiḥ api asiddhā na ca kvacid viśeṣaḥ asti ubhaya sāmyam bhaviṣyati iti tat ca ayuktam kasmāt sadbhāva asiddheḥ satyam anabhidhīyamāne viśeṣe syāt ubhaya sāmyam avyaktasya tu sadbhāvaḥ eva asiddhaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat api iti 
[II,69,i]	kāryasya kāraṇa pūrvaka tvāt vyaktasya ca kārya tvāt avyakta sadbhāve pratipattiḥ iti ced syāt etat kāryam kāraṇa pūrvakam dṛṣṭam ghaṭa ādi kāryam ced avyaktam pramita tvāt tasmāt idam api kāraṇa pūrvakam bhavitum arhati yat ca tasya kāraṇam tat avyaktam iti tat ca anupapannam kasmāt anekāntāt iha ākasmikī ca kāryasya utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā indradhanuṣaḥ asataḥ ca bhrānti mātrāt tat yathā māyā svapna indrajāla mṛga tṛṣṇikā alāta cakra gandharvanagarāṇām sataḥ ca kāraṇāt tat yathā mṛd ādibhyaḥ ghaṭa ādīnām kāryam ced avyaktam atas saṃśayaḥ kim indradhanuḥ vadakasmāt asya prādurbhāvaḥ atha māyā ādi vat asataḥ atha kāraṇāt sataḥ ghaṭa vat iti 
[II,69,ii_II,70,i]	ucyate na akasmikam asat pūrvam vyaktam kasmāt bhedānām parimāṇāt yat parimitam tasya sataḥ utpattiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā mūla aṅkura parṇa nāla daṇḍa vusa tuṣa śūka puṣpa kṣīra taṇḍula kaṇānām parimitāḥ mahat ahaṃkāra indriya tanmātra mahābhūta lakṣaṇa bhedāḥ tasmāt sat kāraṇa pūrvakāḥ yat eṣām kāraṇam tat avyaktam 
[II,70,ii_II,70,iii]	āha kasmāt asti avyaktam asat bhedānām api parimāṇa darśanāt anekāntaḥ iti ced syāt matam asti hi māyā svapna indrajāla anuvidhāyinām api bhedānām parimāṇam iti tasmāt anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt na hi teṣām niyamaḥ asti etāvadbhiḥ eva utpattavyam na anyaiḥ iti mahat ādayaḥ tu pralaya kāle tirobhūtāḥ tāvantaḥ eva utpadyante 
[II,71,i_II,71,ii]	āha parimāṇa an avasthānam kāla dvaya anupalabdheḥ satyam sāmprate kāle mahat ādayaḥ yukta parimāṇāḥ pratyakṣa anumāna upalabdheḥ atīta anāgatayoḥ tu kālayoḥ na asti prasiddhiḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat ucyate na viparyaye pramāṇa anupalabdheḥ idānīm etāvantaḥ bhedāḥ iti etat śakyam anumātum atīta anāgatayoḥ tu kālayoḥ na asti prasiddhiḥ tasmāt na bheda anavasthā prasaṃgaḥ 
[II,71,iii]	āha bheda abhedān avasthānāt mahat ādīnām ye bhedāḥ deva manuṣyatiryañcaḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ ca teṣām aśakyam parimāṇam paricchettum sāmānye antar bhāvāt ayuktam iti ced syāt matam asti śarīrāṇām mahābhūta sāmānyam ghaṭa ādīnām ca pṛthivī sāmānyam tad parimāṇāt ete api parimitāḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt abhāvāt na hi vaḥ sāmānyam dravyāt artha antara bhūtam asti sārūpya mātre sāmānya parikalpanāt 
[II,72,i]	ucyate na tattva antara anupapatteḥ tattva bhedena parimitāḥ bhedāḥ iti etat vivakṣitam yathoktam asmābhiḥ uktam ca yadi asti tattva antaram ucyatām yat punar etat uktam sāmānyasya artha antara bhūtasya bhavat pakṣe anupapattiḥ iti satyam etat tathāvidhena api tu tena saṃvyavahāraḥ na pratiṣidhyate iti vakṣyāmaḥ tasmāt siddham bhedānām parimāṇāt asti avyaktam 
[II,72,ii_II,73,i]	kim ca anyat samanvayāt iha yena bhedānām samanupagatiḥ tasya sattvam dṛṣṭam tat yathā mṛdā ghaṭa ādīnām asti ca iyam sukha duḥkha mohaiḥ śabda ādīnām samanugatiḥ tasmāt te api santi ye ca sukha ādayaḥ astamita viśeṣāḥ tat avyaktam tasmāt asti avyaktam āha na asiddha tvāt sukha ādibhiḥ śabda ādayaḥ anugamyante iti etat aprasiddham kena kāraṇena pratipattavyam iti 
[II,73,ii_II,73,iii]	ucyate tad buddhi nimitta tvāt iha śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām sannidhāne sva saṃskāra viśeṣa yogāt sukha duḥkha moha ākārāḥ prāṇinām buddhayaḥ utpadyante yat ca yādṛśīm buddhim utpādayati tat tena anvitam tat yathā candana ādibhiḥ śakala ādayaḥ tasmāt na asiddhiḥ samanvayasya iti āha asiddhaḥ eva ayam samanvayaḥ kasmāt vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti darśanāt na hi ayam niyamaḥ kāraṇa sadṛśam eva kāryam utpadyate kim tarhi vilakṣaṇam agni dhūma śabda ādi katham na hi agniḥ tṛṇa ādi svabhāvakaḥ agni svabhāvakaḥ vā dhūmaḥ na ca bherī daṇḍa ādi svabhāvaḥ śabdaḥ tasmāt sukha ādi anugatāḥ śabda ādayaḥ iti icchā mātram 
[II,74,i]	viśeṣita tvāt sukha ādi svarūpāḥ śabda ādayaḥ tad sannidhāne sukha ādi ākāra pratyaya utpattiḥ iti etat āditas eva asmābhiḥ viśeṣitam tasmāt na bhinna jātīyāḥ te iti yat tu khalu idam ucyate agni ādīnām vilakṣaṇānām utpatti darśanāt pradhāna bhedānām atad jātīya prasaṃgaḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt abhiprāyānavabodhāt na eva brūmaḥ yaḥ yasya vikāraḥ sa tad jātīyakaḥ iti kim tarhi yaḥ yad jātīyakaḥ sa tasya vikāraḥ iti tasmāt ayuktam etat kiṃca anyat udāharaṇa aprasiddheḥ na ca etat udāharaṇam prasiddham agni ādayaḥ sva kāraṇa jātim na anuvidadhatīta kasmāt bala vīrya anuvidhānāt tat yathā agneḥ dhūmasya ca tvac candana nalikā ādi snigdha tā anuvṛtteḥ taikṣṇya ādi anuvṛtteḥ ca bherī vikāraḥ śabdaḥ na tu yathā bherī rūpam avasthitam pradīpena iva tu daṇḍa abhighātena vyajyate iti sādhyam etat na ca ekaikaḥ rūpa ādīnām dravya ākāraḥ samudāya dharma tvāt tasmāt na bherī vikāraḥ śabdaḥ tatra yat uktam vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti darśanāt asiddhaḥ anvayaḥ iti etat ayuktam tasmāt yuktam etat samanvayāt asti avyaktam iti 
[II,75,i_II,75,ii]	kim ca anyat śaktitaḥ pravṛtteḥ ca iha yāvatī kācid loke pravṛttiḥ upalabhyate sā sarvā śaktitas tat yathā kumbhakārasya daṇḍa ādi sādhana vinyāsa lakṣaṇāyāḥ ca śakteḥ sannidhānāt ghaṭa karaṇe pravṛttiḥ asti vyaktasya ca iyam kāryatvāt tad bhāve pravṛttiḥ iti atas tasya api śaktyā bhavitavyam yā asau śaktiḥ tat avyaktam tasmāt asti avyaktam iti 
[II,75,iii]	āha prāc pravṛtteḥ śakti abhāvaḥ pravṛtti anupalabdheḥ yadi śakti pūrvikā pravṛttiḥ iti manyadhvam tena yāvat pravṛttiḥ na upalabhyate tāvat śaktiḥ na asti iti etat āpannam kasmāt satyām śaktyām kārya abhāve sva rūpa abhāva prasaṃgāt yadi khalu api vidyamānā śaktiḥ kenacid prabandhena kāryam na utpādayet śaktitara śaktā iti etat āpannam tasmāt saha kāri bhāva antara sannidhānāt pravrutti samakalām eva arthānām śaktayaḥ utpadyante tāḥ ca tāvat eva pradhvaṃsante 
[II,75,iv]	tatra yat uktam prāc pravṛtteḥ śakti darśanāt vyaktasya api niṣpādikā śaktiḥ asti iti etat ayuktam kim ca anyat bheda abheda kalpanā anupapatteḥ iha pradhānam eva vā śaktiḥ syāt pradhānāt vā bhinnā kim ca atas tat yadi tāvat pradhānam eva śaktiḥ tena kārye bhedāt śakti bhedaḥ avasīyate iti śakti bhedāt pradhāna nānā tva prasaṃgaḥ pradhāna eka tvāt vā tad avyatiriktānām śaktīnām eka tva prasaṃgaḥ tatas ca kārya nānā tva abhāvaḥ atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti pradhānāt artha antara bhāvaḥ śaktīnām abhyupagamyate tena bhinnānām śaktīnām pravṛttitaḥ siddhau pradhāna siddhiḥ na asti iti etat āpannam kim ca anyat svarūpa abhidhānam ca pradhānasya śakti mātrāt api artha antara tvam abhyupagamya rūpam īdṛś pradhānam sva avasthāyām iti tat ca aśakyam abhidhātum tasmāt bheda abheda kalpanā anupapatteḥ akalpanīyā śaktiḥ iti 
[II,77,i^1]	ucyate yat uktam prāc pravṛtteḥ śakti abhāvaḥ pravṛtti anupalabdheḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na aprasiddha tvāt kāraṇam śaktiḥ kāryam pravṛttiḥ na ca kārya anupalabdhau kārya abhāvaḥ iti etat loke prasiddham yat punaruktam kārya niṣpattau śakteḥ svarūpa hānam iti atra brūmaḥ na pradīpa dṛṣṭāntāt yat yathā pradīpasya ghaṭa ādi prakāśana śaktiḥ asti atha ca kuḍya ādi āvaraṇa sāmarthyāt na ghaṭa ādīn prakāśayitum śaknoti na ca śakyate vaktum pradīpasya prakāśana śaktiḥ aśaktā iti evam anyeṣām api bhāvānām prāc prarutteḥ api śaktiḥ syāt na ca apravṛtti darśanāt asyāḥ svarūpa hānam syāt 
[II,77,i^2]	yat tu uktam saha kāri bhāva antara sannidhānāt pravṛtti sama kālam eva arthānām śakti prādurbhāvaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ tad aprasiddhiḥ śakti apekṣa tvāt iha sarvaḥ kartā sva gatām śaktim apekṣya tad yogya tayā saha kāri bhāva antaram upādatte sā ced prāc pravṛtteḥ na syāt sādhanānām viṣaya svabhāva anavadhāraṇāt anupādāna prasaṃgaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt prāc pravṛtteḥ śaktiḥ yat punar etat uktam tāvat eva pradhvaṃsam iti atra brūmaḥ na kārya niṣṭhā darśanāt yadi pravṛtti sama kālam eva pradhvaṃsaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na kārya niṣṭhādarśanat yadi pravṛtti sama kālam eva pradhvaṃsaḥ syāt kārya niṣṭhā eva na syāt 
[II,77,i^3]	tad nimitta tvāt kāryasya asti tu asau tasmāt na pravṛtti sama kālam eva śati pradhvaṃsaḥ sadṛśa sandhāna utpatyā kārya niṣṭhā iti ced na vināśa sama kāla utpatti asambhavāt atha api syāt ekasyām śaktau kṣaṇa sādhyam aṃśam avasāya vinaṣṭāyām anyat tat sadṛśam śakti antaram utpadyate tasmin vinaṣṭe anyat iti evam śakti santānāt kārya niṣṭhā bhavati iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt vināśa kāla utpatti asambhavāt kaḥ hi atra hetuḥ yena vināśa sama kālam anyat śakti rūpam kāryam avasīyayati na punar prāktanam eva avasthitam iti kim ca anyat kauṭasthya doṣa parihārāt 
[II,77,i^4]	kṣaṇa uttara kāla avasthāne ca bhāvānām yaḥ doṣaḥ upāttar kauṭasthya prasaṃgaḥ iti tasya parihāraḥ uktaḥ tasmāt na asti śaktīnām pravṛtti kāle vināśaḥ pravṛtti uttara kālam api na asti kasmāt punar pravṛtti darśanāt śakti antara utpattau pravṛti uttara kālam api iti ced na hetu abhāvāt kaḥ hi atra nirbandhaḥ tasyām vinaṣṭāyām anyā pravṛtti antara hetuḥ bhavati na eva punar sā eva iti kṛtārtha tva ādi ced na anabhyupagamāt na hi eka ghaṭa arthā śaktiḥ abhyupagamyate tatra yena eva hetunā ekam ghaṭam avasāya na vinaśyati tena eva yāvanti kartavyāni iti tasmāt triṣu kāleṣu śaktayaḥ avatiṣṭhante 
[II,79,i^1]	yat punar etat uktam bheda abheda kalpanā anupapattiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ astu pradhānāt abhinnā śaktiḥ na tasya nānātvam śakti ekatvam vā prasajyate kasmāt saṃkhyā vyavahārasya buddhi apekṣa tvāt buddhi nimittasya ca asatkāreṇa pradhāna śakti svabhāvāt iha ayam saṃkhyā vyavahāraḥ buddhi apekṣaḥ katham yat abhinnām buddhim utpādayati tat ekam pradhāna avasthāyām ca śaktayaḥ astamita viśeṣa tvāt abhinnām buddhim utpādayanti tasmāt ekam tad pravṛtti kāle viśeṣa a agrahaṇe bhedam pratipadyate deva śaktiḥ manuṣya śaktiḥ ityādi 
[II,79,i^2]	tasmāt na āsām eka tvam atas na bheda abheda kalpanā anupapattiḥ iti vyakte darśanāt śaktīnām avyakte pratipattiḥ iti ced syāt etat vyakte śakti pravṛttī dṛṣṭe na ca avyakte kvacid anyatas vyaktam eva etasmāt hetoḥ siddhi ati na avyaktam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt sāmānyatodṛṣṭa antāt siddheḥ yathā eva hi devadatta ādhārayā kriyayā tasya deśa antara prāptim upalabhya atyanta adṛṣṭam jyotiṣām deśa antara prāpteḥ gamanam anumīyate evam pravṛtteḥ śakti niyamita tvāt vyaktasya ca pravṛtti bhūta tvāt avaśyam atyanta adṛṣṭā śaktiḥ abhyupagantavyā iti siddham śaktitaḥ pravṛtteḥ asti avyaktam 
[II,80,i_II,80,ii]	kim ca anyat kāraṇa kārya vibhāgāt kāraṇam ca kāryam ca kāraṇa kārye tayoḥ vibhāgaḥ kārya kāraṇa vibhāgaḥ idam kāraṇam idam kāryam iti buddhyā dvidhā avasthāpanam vibhāgaḥ yaḥ sa kāraṇa kārya vibhāgaḥ tad avasthita bhāva pūrvakam dṛṣṭam tat yathā śayana āsana ratha caraṇa ādiḥ asti ca ayam vyaktasya kāraṇa kārya vibhāgaḥ tasmāt idam api avasthita bhā pūrvakam yaḥ asau avasthitaḥ bhāvaḥ tat avyaktam 
[II,81,i_II,81,iii]	āha tad anupalabdheḥ ayuktam na hi śayana ādīnām kāraṇa kārya vibhāgaḥ kaścid upalabhyate tasmāt ayuktam etat ucyate na kārya kāraṇayoḥ upakāra kopa kārya paryāya tvāt kāraṇam kāryam iti nirvatya nirvartaka bhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ kim tarhi upakāra kopa kārya bhāvaḥ sa ca asti śayana ādīnām vyaktasya ca atas na pramāda abhidhāna netat āha kaḥ punar vyaktasya parasya parasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti 
[II,82,i_II,82,ii]	ucyate guṇānām tāvat sattva rajaḥ tamasām prakāśa pravṛtti niyama lakṣaṇaiḥ dharmaiḥ itaretara upakāreṇa yathā pravṛttiḥ bhavati tatha prīti aprīti viṣāda ātmakāḥ iti etasmin sūtre vyākhyātam tathā śabda ādīnām pṛthivī ādiṣu paraspara artham eka ādhāra tvam śrotra ādīnām itaretara arjana rakṣaṇa saṃskārāḥ karaṇasya kāryāt sthāna sādhana prakhyāpana ādi kāryasya karaṇāt vṛtti kṣata bhaṃga saṃrohaṇa saṃśoṣaṇa paripālanāni pṛthivī ādīnām vṛtti saṃgrahaṇa panthi vyūha avakāśa dānaiḥ gava ādi bhāvaḥ daiva mānuṣa tiraḥ ca am yathaṛtu vidhāna ijyā poṣaṇa abhyavahāra saṃvyavahāraiḥ itaretara adhyayanam varṇānām svadharma pravṛtti viṣaya bhāvaḥ anyaḥ ca lokāt yathāsaṃbhavam draṣṭavyaḥ āha tad anupapattiḥ krama yaugapadyā sambhavāt 
[II,82,iii^1]	yaḥ ayam guṇānām prakāśa pravṛtti niyamaiḥ itaretara upakāraḥ abhyupagamyate sa khalu krameṇa vā syāt yugapad vā kim ca atas tat na tāvat krameṇa saṃbhavati kasmāt ekasya nirapekṣasya pravṛttau itarayoḥ api tad prasaṃgāt yadi tāvat sattvam pūrvam guṇa antara nirapekṣam sva śaktitaḥ eva prakāśate tayoḥ upakārakam iti āśrīyate tena yathā sattvam evam itarau api upakāra nirapekṣau sva kāryam kariṣyate iti upakāra ānarthakyam atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti atas yaugapadyam āśrīyate tat api anupapannam kasmāt saha bhūtānām anupakāraka tvāt go viṣāṇa vat kim ca anyat sat asat vikalpa anupapatteḥ iha sattvam prakāśamānam rajaḥ tamasoḥ vidyamānam vā prakāśam āviṣkuryāt avidyamānam vā 
[II,82,iii^2]	kim ca atas tat yadi tāvat vidyamānam abhivyanakti tena sarveṣām eka svābhāvyāt guṇa tva prasaṃgaḥ kiṃca sattva vat ca itarayoḥ svātaṃtri aprasaṃgaḥ yathā sattvasya prakā śaktiḥ asti iti atas tat guṇa antara nirapekṣam prakāśate tadvat itara avapītyadoṣaḥ atha vā avidyamānā prakāśa śaktiḥ sattva smbandhāt rajaḥ tamasoḥ upajāyate tena yat uktam prāc pravṛtteḥ eva tiṣṭhante śaktayaḥ iti tat hīnam tatas ca satkārya vāda vyāghātaḥ kim ca ayam anekāntāt na hi ayam ekāntaḥ paraspara upakāriṇām avasthita bhāva pūrvakatvam iti tathā hi sattva ādayaḥ paraspara upakāriṇaḥ na ca avasthita bhāva pūrvakāḥ tena yat uktam kāraṇa kārya vibhāgāt bhedānām avyaktam asti etat ayuktam 
[II,84,i^1]	ucyate yat uktam upakāra abhāvaḥ krama yaugapadyā sambhavāt iti astu yugapad upakāraḥ yat tu uktam saha bhūtānām anupakāraka tvam go viṣāṇa ādi vat iti atra brūmaḥ na anyathā anupapatteḥ na hi go viṣāṇayoḥ saha bhūta tvāt aukāra anupapattiḥ kim tarhi eka kārya abhāvāt yeṣām tu kāryam ekam sahabhāve tu teṣām upakāraḥ na pratiṣidhyate tat yathā pṛthivī ādīnām dhṛti saṃgraha śakti vyūha avakāśa dānaiḥ śarīra sthitayoḥ akrama bhāvinoḥ api khura viṣāṇayoḥ na asti paraspara upakāraḥ tasmāt na sahabhāva asahabhāvau upakārānupakāra hetū kim ca dṛṣṭa tvāt 
[II,84,i^2]	dṛṣṭaḥ khalu vegena ūrdhva gamane vāyoḥ ara ghaṭṭa ādīnām yugapad upakāraḥ na kaścid doṣaḥ tathā guṇānām api syāt saṃyoga nimittaḥ iti ced sādhyam kimartha antara bhūtam uta prāpti mātram saṃyogaḥ iti yat punar etat uktam sat asat vikalpānupapatteḥ iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt paṅgu andha vat tad upakāre doṣa an upapatteḥ tat yathā paṅgu andhayoḥ itaretara sambandhāt na vidyamānayoḥ dṛggati śaktyoḥ anyonya ātmani vyaktiḥ na ca avidyamānayoḥ atha ca eka kārya siddhiḥ yathā ca pṛthivī ādīnām paraspara upakāri tvam śaktayoḥ abhivyajyate na para śaktyā evam guṇānām api iti 
[II,84,i^3]	yat punar etat uktam anekāntāt iti tat ayuktam kasmāt śāstra anavabodhāt iha asmākam kārya kāraṇayoḥ artha anabhyupagamāt guṇānām avasthā antaram eva avasthā antara anapekṣam kārya kāraṇa śabda vācya tām labhate tatra ye tāvat pradhāna avasthā anubhāvinaḥ guṇāḥ teṣām śakti mātra rūpa tvāt anirdeśya prakāśa ādi svabhāvānām na asti tad nibandhane upakāraḥ yadā vaiṣamyam āpadyante tadā anivārita prakāśa ādi rūpāḥ tad nimittam upakāram pratipadyante tasmāt vyaktānām upakāra abhyupagamāt avasthita bhāva pūrvaka tvam na virudhyate iti śāstram anavagamya evam ucyate anaikāntikaḥ ayam hetuḥ 
[II,84,i^4]	pradhāna avasthāyām upakāra anabhyupagamāt uttara kālam api tad prasaṃgaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi guṇānām ādye prakope sva sāmarthyāt eva pūrvasmāt pracyutiḥ tena uttara kālam api tadvat eva bhaviṣyati atha pradhāna avasthāyām api ca upakāraḥ na tarhi na anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt agni vat sva śakti nimitta tvāt tat yathā sūkṣmaḥ agniḥ sūkṣmam prakāśam svayam eva karoti ghaṭa ādi prakāśane tu taila vartti ādi apekṣate tadvat guṇānām ādyaḥ prakopaḥ sva śaktitaḥ mahat ādi apekṣaḥ tu upakārataḥ tasmāt yuktam etat kāraṇa kārya vibhāgāt asti avyaktam iti 
[II,87,i_II,87,iv]	kim ca anyat avibhāgāt vaiśvarūpyasya iha yat viśva rūpam tasya avibhāgaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā salila ādīnām jala bhūmī viśva rūpāḥ ca mahat ādayaḥ tasmāt eṣām api avibhāgena bhavitavyam yaḥ asau avibhāgaḥ tat avyaktam tasmāt asti avyaktam āha kim punar tat vaiśvarūpyam kaḥ vā viśvarūpaḥ iti ucyate vaiśvarūpyam iti viśiṣṭam avasthānam ācakṣmahe astamita viśeṣa tvam avibhāgaḥ iti viśeṣasya sāmānya pūrvaka tvāt iti yaḥ arthaḥ tat uktam bhavati avibhāgāt vaiśvarūpyasya iti evam etaiḥ pañcabhiḥ vītaiḥ vyaktasya kāraṇam asti avyaktam iti siddham 
[II,87,v^1]	āha vipratiṣedha prasaṃgaḥ kāraṇa antara pratiṣedha āvacanāt yathā bhavān āha pradhānam jagat utpatti samartham kāraṇam asti evam tantra antarīyāḥ paramāṇu puruṣa īśvara karma daiva svabhāva kāla yadṛcchā bhāvān kāraṇa tvena abhidadhati teṣām ca pratiṣedhaḥ na ucyate iti atas vipratiṣedhaḥ prāpnoti kim pradhānam eva kāraṇam āhosvit etāni eva vā ubhayam iti anvaya darśanāt tad anupapattiḥ iti ced syāt matam pradhāna anvayaḥ eva pṛthivī ādiṣu sukha ādi lakṣaṇaḥ upalabhyate yat ca yena anvitam tasya asau vikāraḥ iti yuktam etat prāc apadiṣṭam tasmāt pradhāna vikāraḥ eva vyaktam iti tat ca anupapannam 
[II,87,v^2]	kasmāt aneka anvaya saṃbhavāt paramāṇu anvayaḥ api hi vyaktaḥ upalabhyate rūpa ādi sattvāt puruṣa anvayaḥ karaṇasya saṃvedaka tvāt īśvara anvayaḥ śakti viśeṣa yuktānām upalabdheḥ karma dā eva anvayaḥ jagat vaicitrya upalambhāt svabhāva anvayaḥ dravya antara saṃsarge api bhāvānām tasmāt apracyuteḥ kāla anvayaḥ yuga ādi anuvidhānāt yadṛcchā anvayaḥ niyama abhāvāt abhāva anvayaḥ gavā ādīnām paraspara ātma sva darśanāditara itarāṇi prayuktāni kāraṇa antara pūrvaka tve api khalu vyaktasya śaktyāḥ parimāṇa ādayaḥ pūrvam eva kalpayitum tasmāt ayuktam anvaya ādibhyaḥ kāraṇam asti avyaktam iti 
[II,89,i^1]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam paramāṇūnām apratiṣedhāt vipratiṣedha prasaṃgaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ tad anupapattiḥ astitva anabhyupagamāt astitve hi paramāṇūnām abhyupagamyamāne sati satyam evam syāt iyam āśaṃkā kim paramāṇu pūrvakam idam viśvam atha pradhāna pūrvakam iti na tu teṣām sadbhāvaḥ niścitaḥ tasmāt ayuktam etat yat tu khalu idam ucyate pṛthivī ādiṣu rūpa ādi upalambhāt anvaya darśanāt aṇūnām sadbhāvaḥ pradhāna vat eva kalpayitavyaḥ iti etat api ca anupapannam kasmāt anyathā api tad upapatteḥ 
[II,89,i^2]	tanmātra pūrvaka tve api hi pṛthivī ādīnām kalpyamāne rūpa ādi sattvāt atas na yuktam etat sukha ādīnām ātma guṇa tvena abhyupagamāt pradhāne api tad prasaṃgaḥ iti ced atha api syāt yathā tanmātrāṇām rūpa ādimat tvam kalpyate tad pūrvaka tvam ca pṛthivī ādīnām dṛśyam api teṣu rūpa ādi sattva liṅgena paramāṇubhyaḥ niṣkṛṣyate evam asmābhiḥ sukha ādīnām ātma guṇa tva abhyupagamāt tad buddhi nimitta tve pṛthivī ādīnām pradhāna pūrva tva ākṣepaḥ kariṣyate iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt ātma guṇa tva tiṣedhāt tasmāt ca viparyāsāt iti atra sukha ādīnām ātma guṇa tva pratiṣedham kariṣyāmaḥ tasmāt asamyak etat 
[II,90,i_II,90,ii^1]	āha yadi punar tanmātrāṇām eva parama aṇu tvam abhyupagamyate kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ syāt ucyate na śakyam evam bhavitum kim kāraṇam vṛddhimatyaḥ tanmātra lakṣaṇāḥ prakṛtayaḥ asmābhiḥ abhyupagamyante kasmāt sva kāryāt hi prathīyasī prakṛtiḥ bhavati iti ca naḥ samayaḥ mahānti ca pṛthivī ādīni mahābhūtāni tasmāt teṣām tad atirikta tayā pṛthivyāḥ bhavitavyam paricchinna deśāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt na tanmātra abhyupagamāt teṣām abhyupagamaḥ upetya vā tad asambhavaḥ kṛtaka tvāt astu vā paramāṇūnām sadbhāvaḥ tathā api tebhyaḥ jagat utpatteḥ asambhavam brūmaḥ kim kāraṇam kṛtaka tvāt 
[II,90,ii^2]	akṛtakena hi jagat kāraṇena yuktam bhavitum kṛtakāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt sati api sadbhāve na teṣām jagat kāraṇam iṣyate iti ucyate tasya eva kāraṇa tva prasaṃgāt yat hi tad paramāṇūnām kāraṇam tat eva jagat kāraṇa tvena yuktam kalpayitum syāt na tad niṣādi matāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kṛtaka tva asiddheḥ ayuktam iti ced syāt matam yadi paramāṇūnām kṛtaka tvam prasiddham atas etat yujyate vaktum amuṣmāt hetoḥ akāraṇam paramāṇavaḥ iti tattva siddham tasmāt na kiṃcid etat ucyate paricchinna deśa tvāt iha yat paricchinna deśaḥ tad kṛtakam dṛṣṭam 
[II,90,ii^3]	tat yathā ghaṭaḥ paricchinna deśaḥ ca tasmāt paramāṇavaḥ kṛtakāḥ kim ca anyat rūpa ādimat tvāt iha yat rūpa ādimat tatkṛtakam dṛṣṭam tat yathā ghaṭāḥ rūpa ādimantaḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kim ca anyat auṣṇya yogāt yadā auṣṇya yuktam tat kṛtakam tat yathā pradīpaḥ tadvantaḥ ca āgneyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca vegavat tvāt iha yat vegavat tat kṛtakam tat yathā iṣuḥ vegavān tadvantaḥ vāyavīyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca sneha drava tva yogāt iha yat sneha drava tva yuktam tat kṛtakam 
[II,90,ii^4]	yathā kedāra ādiṣu āpaḥ ittham ca āpyāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca ādheya tvāt iha yat anyasmin ādhīyate tat kṛtakam tat yathā ṭhaghavam ādhīyante ca paramāṇavaḥ pṛthivyām tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca artha antara ādhāra tvāt iha yad artha antarasya ādhāra tvam pratipadyate tat kṛtakam tat yathā ghaṭaḥ artha antarasya ca dvi aṇuka ādeḥ ādhāra tvam aṇavaḥ pratipadyante tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca prāpti vyavadhānāt iha yayoḥ madhye antarā dravyam avasthitam prāpteḥ vyavadhāyakam bhavati tau kṛtakau tat yathā dvi aṅgulī 
[II,90,ii^5]	tathā ca aṇū dvau antarāṇu antaram avasthitam yaḥ yaḥ prāpteḥ vyavadhāyakam tau kṛtakau tasmāt tau api kṛtakau kiṃca dravya antara ārambhaka tvāt iha yat dravya antara ārambhakam tat kṛtakam vaḥ tat yathā tantuḥ dravya ārambhakāḥ ca paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt kṛtakāḥ kiṃca pratyakṣa tvāt iha yat pratyakṣam tat kṛtakam dṛṣṭam tat yathā ghaṭaḥ pratyakṣāḥ ca yoginām paramāṇavaḥ tad kṛtakāḥ atas eva kṛtaka tvam iti ced syāt matam yatas eva yoginām pratyakṣāḥ paramāṇavaḥ tatas eva kṛtakāḥ kim kāraṇam asmad ādi pratyakṣam ghaṭa ādi hi kṛtakam dṛṣṭam iti kṛtvā 
[II,90,ii^6]	etat api anupapannam kasmāt śarīra kṛtaka tva prasaṅgāt śarīram api hi yoginām pratyakṣam kāmam tat api akṛta kamaḥ tu atha na etat eva tarhi na akṛtakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ pradhāna ādiṣu prasaṃgaḥ iti ced na anabhyupagamāt śrī kapila brāhmaṇaiḥ api pradhāna puruṣau apratyakṣau iti naḥ śāstram tasmāt yat kiṃcid etat sattā ādi vat iti ced syāt matam yathā sattā guṇa tva rūpa tva ādīnām sati pratyakṣa tve akṛtaka tvam evam paramāṇūnām bhaviṣyati iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt sādhya tvāt paramāṇu akṛtaka tva vat sattā ādīnām sadbhāvaḥ asiddhaḥ 
[II,90,ii^7]	tasmāt śaśa viṣāṇāt puruṣa viṣāṇa siddhi vat agrāhyam etat saukṣmyāt aṇūnām kṛtaka tva aprasaṃgaḥ iti ced syāt matam na hi paramāṇubhyaḥ sūkṣmataram anyat bhāva antaram asti yat eṣām ārambhakam syāt parā khalu eṣā kāṣṭhā saukṣmyasya yat paramāṇavaḥ tasmāt eṣām kṛtaka tvam anupapannam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt pāka jeṣu ati prasaṃgāt saukṣmyāt akṛtaka tva prasaṃgaḥ te api paramāṇavaḥ sūkṣmāḥ yat tu khalu ati saukṣmyāt pradhāna puruṣa yoḥ akṛtaka tvam dṛṣṭam tat sati vibhu tve na ca yathā pradhāna puruṣau evam aṇavaḥ api viśvam vyaśnuvate 
[II,90,ii^8_II,94,i]	tasmāt sati saukṣmye pāka ja vat eṣām kṛtaka tvam anivāryam yeṣām tu kārya dravyam pacyate iti pakṣaḥ teṣām ayam anupālambhaḥ iti atas paramāṇu samavetam karma udāhāryam tat hi sūkṣmam atīndriyam kṛtakam ca iti siddham kṛtakāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kṛtaka tvāt caiṣām a nitya tāpi anapātini iti kṛtvā antarāla pralaya mahā pralayeṣu pradhvaṃsāt paramāṇūnām kāraṇa abhāvāt kāryā bhāvaḥ iti sva śāstra siddhāt anumānāt jagat ucchitti doṣa prasaṃgaḥ tathā bhoginām upacitasya sva karmaṇaḥ anupabhogāt kṛtasya vipraṇāśaḥ aniṣṭam ca etat tasmāt na jagat kāraṇam paramāṇavaḥ yā api khalu iyam āśaṃkā puruṣāt jagat utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati iti sā api ayuktā kasmāt pratiṣedhāt tasmāt ca viparyāsāt iti atra puruṣasya akartṛ tvam upapādayiṣyāmaḥ caitanya aviśeṣāt īśvarasya api saḥ eva vidhiḥ kāraṇa tva pratiṣedhe boddhavyaḥ 
[II,94,ii]	āha asti evam īśvaraḥ iti pāśupata vaiśeṣikāḥ kasmāt kārya viśeṣasya atiśaya buddhi pūrvaka tvāt iha kārya viśeṣaḥ prāsāda vimāna ādiḥ atiśaya buddhi pūrvakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ asti ca ayam mahābhūta indriya bhuvana vinyāsa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ tasmāt anena api atiśaya buddhi pūrvakeṇa bhavitavyam yat pūrvakaḥ ayam saḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt asti īśvaraḥ iti kim ca anyat cetanā cetanayoḥ abhisambandhasya cetana kṛta tvāt iha cetanā cetanayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ cetana kṛtaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā go śakaṭayoḥ asti ca ayam cetanā cetanayoḥ śarīra śarīriṇoḥ abhisambandhaḥ tasmāt anena api cetana kṛtena bhavitavyam yad kṛtaḥ ayam saḥ īśvaraḥ tasmāt asti īśvaraḥ kāraṇam 
[II,95,i^1]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam kārya viśeṣasya atiśaya buddhi pūrvaka tvāt īśvara sadbhāva siddhiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na sādhya tvāt asmad ādi buddhi pūrvikāḥ prāsāda ādayaḥ atiśaya buddhi pūrvikāḥ vā iti sādhyam etat tasmāt anuttaram kiṃca prāc pradhāna pravṛtteḥ buddhi asambhavāt kāraṇa antara pratiṣedhāt pradhānāt ayam buddhi pūrvakam kārya viśeṣam kurvīta prāk ca pradhāna vipariṇāmāt buddhiḥ eva na asti iti upapannam etat śaktimat tvāt svatas iti ced syāt punar etat sarva śakti pracitaḥ īśvaraḥ tasya prāk api pradhāna vipariṇāmātsvataḥ eva icchā yogāt buddhi sadbhāvaḥ na pratiṣidhyate iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt dṛṣṭānta abhāvāt buddhiḥ svatas eva iti atra paryanuyukta kaḥ te dṛṣṭāntaḥ tasmāt asat etat 
[II,95,i^2]	śakti viśeṣāt adoṣaḥ iti ced atha api syāt na anyeṣām buddhimatām īśvara tulyā śaktiḥ atas eṣām pradhānāt śarīra vyūha sama kālam ātma ādi sannikarṣāt vā buddhayaḥ utpadyante iti īśvarasya tu svatas iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt sarva vāda siddhi prasaṃgāt dṛṣṭānta viruddham artham ādāya pratibadhyamānena śakti viśeṣaḥ smartavyaḥ iti etasyām kalpanāyām sarva vāda siddhi prasaṃgaḥ syāt tasmāt graha mātram etat evam svatas īśvarasya buddhi sambhavaḥ na ced bhavet yuktam ucyate prāc pradhāna pravṛtteḥ buddhi asambhavāt na buddhimat pūrvakaḥ ayam kārya viśeṣaḥ kiṃca phala anupapatteḥ dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam vā phalam uddiśya buddhimantaḥ kārya viśeṣān prāsāda vimāna ādīn ārabhamāṇāḥ dṛśyante anupahataḥ ca ayam aiśvaryāt kim ca prayojaka anupapatteḥ 
[II,95,i^3]	kim ca anekāntāt na ca sarvaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ vṛkṣa ādīnām tad vyatirekeṇa utpatteḥ sarvasya īśvara buddhi pūrvaka tva abhyupagame dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ na ca asti anudāhṛtaḥ vādaḥ tasmāt anekāt na buddhimat pūrvakam vyaktam kim ca duḥkha uttara tvāt buddhi pūrvakaḥ ced asya kārya viśeṣaḥ syāt kartuḥ duḥkha uttara vidhāne prayojanam na asti śaktimān ca ayam iti sukha uttaram eva vidadhyāt duḥkha uttaraḥ ca ayam tasmāt na buddhi pūrvakaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ kiṃca duḥkha upāya tvāt buddhi pūrvakaḥ ced ayam kārya viśeṣaḥ syāt dharma artha kāma mokṣa prāptayaḥ sukha upāyāḥ syuḥ duḥkha upāyāḥ ca tasmāt abuddhi pūrvakaḥ 
[II,95,i^4]	dharma adharma nimitta tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi api īśvara pūrvakaḥ ayam kārya viśeṣaḥ tathā api ādisarge sukha uttarāṇām asmad utpannānām prāṇinām dharma adharma parigrahāt hīna madhyama utkṛṣṭa vayaḥ jāti svabhāva ādi yogaḥ bhavati tatas ca na aparādhaḥ ayam īśvarasya iti etat api ayuktam kasmāt adharma utpatti hetu abhāvāt īśvaraḥ ced dharma adharmayoḥ utpattau īṣṭe dharmam eva prāṇinām sukha hetu tvāt utpādayet na adharmam prayojana abhāvāt atha matam svābhāvikī dharma adharmayoḥ sva kāraṇāt utpattiḥ yat uktam sarvam īśvara buddhi pūrvakam vyaktam iti tu tasya vyāghātaḥ tasmāt īśvaraḥ na kāraṇam yat punar etat uktam cetanā cetanayoḥ abhisambandhasya cetana kṛta tvāt īśvarasya sadbhāvaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kasmāt sādhya tvāt yaḥ ayam cetanā cetanayoḥ go śakaṭayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ sa kena cetanena kṛtaḥ 
[II,95,i^5]	yadi caitreṇa tasya kārya kāraṇa saṃghāta tvāt ācetanyam atha caitra śabda vācyasya piṇḍasya upadraṣṭā kṣetrajñaḥ tad kṛtaḥ iṣyate tat ayuktam sādhya tvāt na hi puruṣa kartṛ tvam asmat pakṣe prasiddham ubhaya pakṣa prasiddhena vyavahāraḥ kim ca anyat anavasthā prasaṃgāt cetanā cetanayoḥ abhisambandhasya cetana kṛta tvam bruvataḥ prāptam īśvara kārya kāraṇayoḥ abhisambandhasya cetana kṛta tvam tathā ca anavasthā prasaṃgaḥ atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti svābhāvikaḥ īśvarasya kārya kāraṇayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ iṣyate na tarhi aikāntikaḥ hetuḥ tayoḥ ācetanyādadoṣaḥ iti ced syāt punar etat īśvarasya yat kārya kāraṇam tat api cetanam īśvaraḥ api tasmāt sambandhena pratyudāharaṇam upapadyate iti etat ayuktam kasmāt asambandha prasaṃgāt 
[II,95,i^6]	caitanyā viśeṣāt ātmanaḥ ātma antareṇa abhisambandhaḥ na asti evam īśvara kārya kāraṇayoḥ api na syāt aniṣṭam ca etat kim ca aviparyaya prasaṃgāt ubhaya caitanya pratijñasya yathā īśvarasya karaṇam buddhi ādayaḥ evam īśvaraḥ api buddhi ādīnām karaṇam syāt kasmāt aviśeṣāt atha etat aniṣṭam na tarhi ubhayoḥ caitanyam kārya kāraṇa vattā anabhyupagamāt adoṣaḥ iti ced vyāpī niravayavaḥ ananta śaktiḥ sūkṣmebhyaḥ sūkṣmatamaḥ mahadbhyaḥ mahat tamaḥ adhikaraṇa dharma anādiḥ iti evam ananta lakṣaṇam īśvara padārtha tad vidaḥ vyācakṣate tasya kutas kārya kāraṇam avalambya idam ādhyāropitam iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt anumāna virodhāt ittham ced īśvaraḥ yat idam anumānam kārya viśeṣasya atiśaya buddhi pūrvaka tvāt ca cetanā cetanayoḥ abhisambandhasya cetana kṛta tvāt iti tat vyāhanyate 
[II,95,i^7]	kasmāt na hi etāvat īdṛśa arthena saha etat dṛṣṭam iti upetya vā mūrti parigraha vyāghātāt yadi ekāntena evaṃrūpaḥ īśvaraḥ kṣiti ādi mūrti parigrahaḥ vyāhanyeta kim ca anyat śruteḥ śrutiḥ api ca asya mūrtim ācaṣṭe kṛttivāsāḥ pinākahastaḥ vitata dhanvā nīlaśikhaṇḍī ityādi tad abhyupagamāt sva pakṣa hāniḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi tarhi śruti vacanāt mūrtimān īśvaraḥ parigṛhyate tena siddham asya astitvam kasmāt na hi asataḥ mūrtimat tvam upapadyate iti kṛtvā etat api ayuktam abhiprāyānavabodhāt na hi ekāntena vayam bhagavataḥ śakti viśeṣam pratyācakṣmahe māhātmya śarīra ādi parigrahāt yathā tu bhavatā ucyate pradhāna puruṣa vyatiriktaḥ tayoḥ prayoktā na asti iti ayam asmad abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt etasya bādhakam 
[II,95,i^8]	atas na pradhāna puruṣayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ anya kṛtaḥ kim ca anyat aśakya tvāt kurvāṇaḥ khalu api ayam abhisambandham śarīra mātreṇa vā śarīriṇaḥ kuryāt śarīra kāraṇena vā kim ca atas tat na tāvat śarīra mātreṇa karoti kasmāt anapekṣasya śarīra utpattau nimitta abhāvāt na śarīra kāraṇena vibhu tvāt paricchinnayoḥ go śakaṭayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ anya kṛtaḥ vibhū ca pradhāna puruṣau kim ca pārārthyāt go śakaṭayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ para arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na tu pradhāna puruṣayoḥ abhisambandhaḥ para arthaḥ iti īśvara arthaḥ iti ced na ukta tvāt dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa arthaḥ īśvarasya anupapannaḥ iti ādau eva uktam etat evam tāvat pāśupatānām īśvara parigrahe doṣaḥ 
[II,101,i^1]	vaiśeṣikāṇām ca ayam doṣaḥ kim ca dravya ādi padārtha antara bhāva abhāva parikalpanā anupapattiḥ ca taiḥ īśvaraḥ dravya guṇa karma sāmānya viśeṣa samavāya bhūtaḥ vā parikalpyamānaḥ parikalpyate padārtha antara bhūtaḥ vā kim ca atas tat na tāvat dravya ādi bhūtaḥ kasmāt dvividham hi dravyam aneka dravyam adravyam ca tatra na aneka dravyam īśvaraḥ kṛtaka tva ādi doṣa prasaṃgāt na adravyam parisaṃkhyānāt pṛthivī ādīni manaḥ paryantāni nava eva dravyāṇi vaḥ siddhāntaḥ iti karaṇasya parisamāpti artha tvāt kim ca guṇa karma nirdeśāt sati ca asya dravya tve vaiśeṣika guṇa nirdeśaḥ ācāryeṇa kṛtaḥ syāt kāraṇa antara prayoga samarthasya ca karma nirdiṣṭam syāt na tu tathā tasmāt na dravya guṇa ādayaḥ āśraya paratantrāḥ hi guṇa ādayaḥ para arthāḥ evam na dravya ādi bhūtaḥ na api padārtha antara bhūtaḥ padārtha tve hi sati dravya ādi vat lakṣaṇam uktam abhaviṣyat ācāryeṇa tu na uktam tasmā sūtra kāra mate na asti īśvaraḥ liṅgāt iti ced syāt matam saṃjñā karma tvam asmad viśiṣṭānām liṅgam 
[II,101,i^2]	pratyakṣa pūrvaka tvāt vā saṃjñā karmaṇaḥ iti etasmāt liṅgāt īśvara parigrahaḥ ācāryasya siddhaḥ iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt abhipreta asiddheḥ satyam anena liṅgena asmad ādibhyaḥ viśiṣṭa śakteḥ kasyacid eva māhātmya śarīrasya anyasya vā pratipattiḥ syāt saṃjñā mātram tu yathā bhavadbhiḥ sarva kāraṇānām sṛṣṭi upasaṃhāra pravṛtti hetuḥ ekaḥ svatantraḥ iṣyate tathā ca asmāt liṅgāt pratipattiḥ kim ca anyat prāc anupadeśe akauśala prasaṃgāt īśvara paratantre ced aṇūnām pravṛtti nivṛttī syātām tam eva prāk upadiśet dharma vat pradhāna padārthasya vā prāk anupadeśāt akuśalaḥ sūtrakāraḥ iti etat āpadyate na ca etat iṣṭam ubhayam kim ca anyat asaṃkīrtanāt śāstra pradeśe ca ayam īśvaraḥ na kasmiṃścid api ācāryeṇa saṃkīrtitaḥ na ca asya vadhvāḥ iva śvaśura nāma saṃkīrtane doṣa upapattiḥ syāt doṣa saṃvibhāga artham idam ācāryasya aniṣṭam adhyāropyate na tu matam asya etat evam kāṇādānām īśvaraḥ asti iti pāśupata upajñam etat tasmāt īśvaraḥ api akāraṇam 
[II,103,i^1]	karma aṇubhiḥ vyākhyātam katham yathā kṛtaka tvāt na jagat kāraṇam aṇavaḥ evam karma api na śarīra nimittam tasmāt tat api akāraṇam itaretara nimitta tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā antareṇa śarīram karma na utpadyamānam dṛṣṭam evam antareṇa karma śarīrasya api kāraṇa antaram aśakyam kalpayitum iti paraspara nimitta tvāt na asya parivartasya pūrva koṭiḥ prajñāyate tasmāt na asti anayoḥ kāraṇa antaram iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt anavasthānām avasthāna pūrvakatva darśanāt tat yathā śukra śoṇitāt śarīram śarīrāt śukra śoṇitam iti asya parivartasya pūrva koṭiḥ adṛṣṭā pratijñāyate ca ayonija tvam īśvara śarīrāṇām ādisarge ca tathā ca bīja aṅkura ādayaḥ aṅkura ādibhyaḥ bījam iti anavasthā bhāti ca atra ādisarge paramāṇu mātrāt api bīja prādurbhāvaḥ tathā śarīra karmaṇoḥ anavasthā idānīm api ca ādisarge ca adhikāra mātra vaśāt śarīra utpattiḥ syāt sādhāraṇa vigraha tva prasaṃgaḥ iti ced syāt etat yadi adhikāra nimittā śarīra utpattiḥ ādi sarge abhyupagamyate prāptam ekena śarīreṇa sarva puruṣāṇām abhisambandhaḥ niyama hetu abhāvāt 
[II,103,i^2]	tatas ca śarīra antara ānarthakyam tena eva sarveṣām upabhoga sāmarthyāt iti etad anupapannam kasmāt pratyakṣa virodhāt satyam etat anumānataḥ pratyakṣataḥ tu śarīrāṇi prati puruṣam tasmāt na ayam prasaṃgaḥ apavarga niyama prasaṃgaḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi adhikāra mātra vaśāt śarīra utpattiḥ parama ṛṣeḥ eva apavarga sādhanam śarīrāt utpadyeta iti ucyate na tasya eva kim tarhi sarveṣām guṇānām prādhānyāt tad nimittāni śarīrāṇi ādi sarge sāṃsiddhikāni utpadyante tatra yasya sattva pradhānam kārya karaṇam sa parama ṛṣiḥ yasya sattvam rajaḥ bahulam sa māhātmya śarīraḥ evam guṇa samparkāt guṇa pradhāna apradhāna bhāvena yāvat sthāvara śarīra prādurbhāvaḥ iti atas na asti guṇānām śarīra viniyoga pakṣapātaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat kṛtaka tvāt na karma jagat kāraṇam iti etena ca evam vyākhyām tat api hi karmaṇām eva prāpta paripākāṇām abhidhānam artha antaram eva iti ced sādhyam tasmāt api akalpanīyam iti 
[II,105,i]	yat api uktam kālāt jagat utpattiḥ bhaviṣyati iti tad anupapannam kasmāt kāraṇa parispandasya eva tad abhidhāna sanniveśāt na hi naḥ kālaḥ nāma kaścid asti kim tarhi kriyamāṇa kriyāṇām eva āditya gati go doha ghaṭā stanita ādīnām viśiṣṭa avadhi sarūpa pratyaya nimitta tvat parāpara ādi liṅga sadbhāvāt pratipattiḥ iti ced na akṛtakeṣu tad anupapatteḥ yat eva kṛtakam tatra eva parama param iti ādiḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa yadi kriyā vyatirikta nimittaḥ syāt aviśeṣān nitya anityeṣu syāt kvacid sāmarthāt apāka javat adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā agni saṃyogaḥ pākaja hetuḥ tathā ca aviśeṣe api pṛthivyām eva pākaja utpatti nimittam bhavati na ākāśa ādiṣu evam kālaḥ api parāpara ādi hetuḥ atha ca anityeṣu eva syāt na nityeṣu iti tat ca ayuktam kasmāt viśeṣa upapatteḥ rūpa ādi vikriyā hetuḥ agniḥ tad yuktam yat asau tadvati dravye pāka jānādadyāt tadvati ākāśa ādau kālaḥ tu sambandha mātra upakārī na vikriyā hetuḥ tasmāt asat etat evam yadi kriyābhyaḥ anyaḥ kālaḥ iṣyate kāraṇa parispandasya jagat kāraṇa tvam atha anyat sādhyam 
[II,106,i_II,106,ii]	yadṛcchā api na kāraṇam karma vat kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt kārya kāraṇa bhūtam hi idam vyaktam iti prāc vyākhyātam sa ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prekṣā pūrva kṛtānām śayana ādīnām upalabdhau yādṛt chikeṣu ca anupalabdhau na tasyāḥ liṅgam iti śakyam vaktum abhāvaḥ api akāraṇam parimāṇa ādi darśanāt na hi tatas utpannānām parimāṇam upapadyate iti atas na api anvayaḥ sa ātmaka nirātmakayoḥ atyanta jāti bhedāt 
[II,107,i_II,107,ii]	na api śaktiḥ tad abhāvāt na upakāraḥ anavasthānāt na vibhāgaḥ nirātmaka tvāt tasmāt na paramāṇu puruṣa īśvara karma daiva kāla svabhāva yadṛcchā bhāvebhyaḥ vyaktam utpadyate na ced ebhyaḥ pariśeṣataḥ pradhānasya eva astitva liṅgam idam tasmāt yuktam etat bhedānām parimāṇa ādibhyaḥ kāraṇam asti avyaktam iti 
[II,112,i_II,112,ii]	āha evam api asya vyakta hetu tvam anupapannam eka tvāt bahūnām kārya ārambhaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tantu ādīnām ekam pradhānam tasmāt na tad ārambha śakti yuktam iti ucyate yadi api guṇānām pradhāna lakṣaṇam avasthā antaram abhinna buddhi nimitta tvāt ekam api kārya kāle kiṃcid vaiṣamya upajanita vyapadeśya rūpābhiḥ itaretara upakāriṇībhiḥ śaktibhiḥ smudāya tvam āpadyate tasmāt idānīm pravartate triguṇataḥ samudayāt ca
[II,112,iii]	pravartate iti anena utpattim ācaṣṭe triguṇataḥ iti avyapadeśya rūpāṇām pradhāna apradhāna bhāvena guṇa śaktīnām vaiṣamyāt vyapadeśya rūpa antaram āha yatra etat śakyate vaktum trayaḥ sattva ādayaḥ iti tad avasthānam kārya ārambhakam iti samudayāt iti anena paraspara apekṣāṇām ārambha śaktim avadyotayati etat uktam bhavati kārya kāle guṇāḥ parityakta pūrva avasthā bhedam pratilabhya paraspara upakāreṇa saṃhanyate saṃhatāḥ ca vyaktam utpādayanti tasmāt na avasthā antarasya abhinna buddhi nimitta tvāt pradhāna eka tva doṣaḥ guṇa bhedāt na ekasya kārya ārambhaḥ iti 
[II,113,i_II,113,iv]	āha niṣkriya tvāt tarhi prakṛteḥ kārya ārambhaḥ anupapannaḥ kriyā tva anabhyupagame vā vyakta vaidharmya virodhaḥ iti ucyate na kriyā vaidharmya bhedāt dvividhā hi kriyā praspanda lakṣaṇā pariṇāma lakṣaṇā ca tatra praspandaḥ pradhānasya saukṣmyāt pratiṣidhyate pariṇāmataḥ tu tat kāryam ārabhate iti 
[II,114,i_II,114,v]	āha nanu ca pariṇāmaḥ api saukṣmyāt pradhānasya na upapadyate kasmāt na hi saukṣmyāt sūkṣmasya ākāśa ādeḥ vipariṇāmaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti ucyate saṃskārasya saukṣmye api pariṇāmaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tasmāt yuktaḥ sūkṣma pariṇāmi iti āha kaḥ punar ayam pariṇāmaḥ nāma ucyate jahaddharma antaram pūrvam ādatte yadā param tattvāt apracyutaḥ dharmī pariṇāmaḥ saḥ ucyate iti 
[II,114,vi_II,114,viii]	yadā śakti antara anugrahāt pūrva dharmān tirobhāvya svarūpāt apracyutaḥ dharmī dharma antareṇa āvirbhavati tad avasthānam asmākam pariṇāmaḥ iti ucyate āha na etat abhidhāna mātram dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa pratipadyāmahe tasmāt yathā kim iti vaktavyam ucyate yathā pālāśam palāśāt apracyuta nimitta antarasya ātapa ādeḥ anugrahāt śyāmatām tirobhāvya pīta tām vrajati tathā idam draṣṭavyam 
[II,115,i_II,115,ii]	āha na anyathā utpatteḥ apratiṣedhāt katham punar etavagamyate pālāśam svarūpāt apracyutam dharma antarasya parityāgam upādānam ca karoti na punar anyathā ca anyathā ca upapadyate iti ucyate kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiṣedhāt prāk eva kṣaṇa bhaṅga nirdiṣṭam vinaṣṭānām bhāvānām punar utpattau na asti kāraṇam tad abhāve ca utpattiḥ ayuktā iti 
[II,115,iii_II,116,i]	āha dharma dharmiṇoḥ ananya tva abhyupagamāt dharma utpatti vināśe dharmī utpatti vināśa prasaṃgaḥ na hi vaḥ dharmebhyaḥ anyaḥ dharmī tatra yadi dharmasya nivṛttiḥ abhyupagamyate dharmiṇaḥ api nivṛttiḥ ananya tvāt prāptā dharma utpattau tad utpattiḥ tatra yat uktam dharma utpatti virodhe dharmī svarūpa avasthānam iti etat ayuktam ucyate na sena ādi vat vyavasthāna upapatteḥ tat yathā senā aṅgebhyaḥ ananya tvam senāyāḥ na ca senā aṅgānām vināśe senā vināśaḥ tat yathā na anyaḥ paṭaḥ bauddhānām saṃyoga avayavi pratiṣedhāt na ca paṭa vināśe tantu vināśaḥ tatra yat uktam dharmi vināśe dharma vināśaḥ iti etat ayuktam 
[II,116,ii]	āha evam api ayuktam tat kasmāt sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ dharmi svarūpa parikalpana anupapatteḥ iha rūpa ādi sāmānyam vā dharmi rūpa tvena parikalpyamānam parikalpyeta rūpa ādi viśeṣaḥ vā kim ca atas tatra tāvat rūpa ādi sāmānyam dharmi svarūpam iti śakyam kalpayitum kasmāt asambhavāt yadi tāvat pṛthivī sāmānyam ghaṭa ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ tena pṛthivī api tanmātra apekṣayā viśeṣaḥ yāvat pradhānam iti na asti sāmānyam tad abhāvāt dharmi svarūpa abhāvaḥ atha viśeṣāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ teṣām viśeṣa antareṇa saha avasthānāt dharmi svarūpa anavasthānāt tatas ca yat uktam svarūpāt apracyutaḥ dharmī dharma antaram vijahāti dharma antaram upādatte iti tat vyāhanyate iti 
[II,117,i]	ucyate yat uktam rūpa ādi sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ dharmi svarūpa parikalpanā anupapattiḥ iti astu sāmānyam yat tu uktam sāmānyam sāmānya antara apekṣam viśeṣa tvam iti na pratyaya nivṛttau sāmānya abhāva avasthiteḥ tatas ca dharmi svarūpa siddheḥ yāvat pṛthivī ityayam pratyayaḥ na nivartate sāmānyam ghaṭa ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ dravya tvam ca asau dharma antara parivarteṣu tad ākāra pratyaya utpattitaḥ svarūpa avasthāna siddheḥ dharmā ghaṭa ādayaḥ yadā tu pṛthivī pratyaya nivṛttiḥ tadā tanmātrāṇām sāmānya bhāvaḥ dravya tvam ca viśeṣaḥ dharmaḥ iti yāvat pradhānam tasya tu sāmānya antara anupapatteḥ kauṭasthyam eva yatra sarva viśeṣa abhāvaḥ tad pradhānam yadi tu pṛthivī ādīnām nityam avyāvṛtam sati kauṭasthyam eṣām prāptam tasmāt na dharmi svarūpa abhāvaḥ śakteḥ vā sāmānya bhāva abhyupagamāt athavā sukha duḥkha moha śaktayaḥ eva iha mahat ādinā viśeṣa antena liṅgena pariṇāmam pratipadyante tāsām ca satatam sāmānya pratyaya nimitta tvāt svarūpāt apracyute tat dravya tvam liṅgasya dharma tvam aprasiddheḥ ayuktam iti ced na ukta tvāt prāk uktam etat sukha ādi pūrvakam viśvam iti 
[II,118,i_II,118,iii]	āha evam api vaiśvarūpya anupapattiḥ kāraṇa viśeṣāt yadi sukha ādi śaktayaḥ eva pariṇāminyaḥ yat idam brahma ādi sthāvara antam vaiśvarūpyam tat na upapadyate kasmāt na hi abhinnam kāryam utpadyate iti ucyate śaktitaḥ ca pariṇāmini bhavati tena vaiśvarūpyam katham salila vat prati pratiguṇa āśraya viśeṣāt 
[II,118,iv]	yathā antarikṣā viśiṣṭasya ambhasaḥ pracyutiḥ āśrayeṇa gobhujaṅgama uṣṭra ādīnām viśeṣāt kṣīra mūtra viṣa ādi vaiśvarūpyam ca upapadyate tathā guṇa śaktayaḥ viśiṣṭāḥ paraspara āśraya viśeṣāt brahma ādi stamba antam jātyākṛti vāc buddhi svabhāva āhāra vihāra rūpam vaiśvarūpyam pratipadyante tasmāt siddham etat prakṛtiḥ eva sarva bhāvanām prasavitrī na ca kaścid doṣaḥ iti 
[II,122,i]	āha samadhigatam pradhānam puruṣaḥ idānīm kārya kāraṇa vyatiriktaḥ asti iti etat pratipādyam kutas saṃśayaḥ iti ced anupalabhyamānasya ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iti uktam kim ca anyat ācārya vipratipatteḥ vijñāna skandha vyatiriktaḥ na asti kaścid arthaḥ iti śākya putrīyāḥ pratipannāḥ kasmāt sarva pramāṇa anupalabdheḥ iha yat asti tad pratyakṣa ādinā pramāṇena upalabhyate tat yathā rūpa ādi tatas ca tāvat ayam ātmā na pratyakṣataḥ upalabhyate kasmāt aśabda ādi lakṣaṇāt na antar pratyakṣataḥ kasmāt triguṇa ādi viparītasya tad aviṣaya tvāt na pūrvavat śeṣavadbhyām kārya kāraṇa anupapatteḥ na ca sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt dharma sāmānya abhāvāt na āpta vacanāt anabhyupagamāt na hi bauddhānām śruti smṛti purāṇa itihāsāḥ pramāṇam yaḥ ca eṣām āgamaḥ saḥ evam āha
[II,122,ii_II,122,iii]	ātmā eva hi ātmanaḥ na asti viparītena kalpyate na eva iha sattvam ātmā asti dharmāḥ tu ete sa hetukāḥ dvādaśa eva tava aṅgāni skandha āyatana dhātavaḥ vicintya sarvāṇi etāni pudgalaḥ na upalabhyate śūnyam ādhyātmikam viddhi śūnyam paśya bahis gatam na dṛśyate saḥ api kaścid yaḥ bhāvayati śūnyatām punar api āha asti karma asti vipākaḥ kārakaḥ tu na upalabhyate yaḥ imān svān dharmān ākṣipati anyān ca prati sandadhāti anyatra dharma saṃketāt tasmāt sarva pramāṇa anupalabdheḥ na asti ātmā iti 
[II,123,i_II,124,ii]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam pratyakṣataḥ pūrvavat śeṣavadbhyām ca ātmanaḥ na upalabdhiḥ iti satyam etat yat tu uktam sāmānyatodṛṣṭāt anupalabdhiḥ ātma sāmānya anupapatteḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt saṃghāta para artha tvāt iha saṃghātāḥ para arthāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tat yathā śayana āsana ratha caraṇa ādayaḥ asti ca ayam śarīra lakṣaṇaḥ saṃghātaḥ tasmāt anena api para arthena bhavitavyam yaḥ asau paraḥ sa puruṣaḥ tasmāt asti puruṣaḥ āha saṃghāta para artha tva upalabdheḥ śayana ādayaḥ hi sati api parārtha tve saṃghāta arthāḥ yadi ca taiḥ ati deśaḥ kārya kāraṇa saṃghātasya kriyate prāptam asya tadvat saṃghāta artha tvam evam puruṣa viparīta artha siddhi prasaṃgaḥ atha etat aniṣṭam na tarhi cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ para arthāḥ 
[II,124,iii]	ucyate na śakyam etat āpādayitum kasmāt asaṃhata tva siddhau vāda pravṛtteḥ siddhe satya saṃhata tve puruṣasya ayam vādaḥ pravṛttaḥ tasmāt na pārārthyam anena bādhyate katham avagamyate iti ced pratyakṣataḥ anupalabdheḥ sati hi saṃghāta tve devadatta ādi vat ayam puruṣaḥ pratyakṣatas eva upalabhyeta tathā ca sati saṃśaya abhāvāt pravṛttiḥ eva asya vādasya na syāt tasmāt ayuktam saṃhata arthāḥ śayana ādi vat cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ 
[II,125,i_II,125,ii]	āha paraspara upakāri tvāt pāra arthya siddhiḥ iha kṣetra udaka sūrya ādayaḥ śasya ādīnām upakārakāḥ tathā kārya kāraṇa tvāt saṃghātaḥ ca yathā uktam tasmāt ayuktam eteṣām pāratantryam iti ucyate na śayana ādi vat tatas anyena arthavat tvāt tat yathā śayana ādi aṅgānām sati paraspara upakāri tve tatas anyena arthavat tvāt tad abhāve ca artha ānarthakyam evam cakṣuḥ ādīnām sati paraspara upakāri tve tatas anyena arthavat tvam bhavitum arhati tad abhāve ca artha ānarthakyam iti 
[II,125,iii]	āha śayana ādīnām devadatta artha tvāt tasya ca bhedāḥ bahis bhāvāt paraspara artha tva prasaṃgaḥ evam śayana ādayaḥ devadatta arthāḥ kārya kāraṇa saṃghātaḥ ca devadatta śabda vācyaḥ tatra bhedānām eva bheda artha tvāt puruṣa artha siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānta abhāvaḥ vā atha matam śayana ādayaḥ na devadatta arthāḥ kim tarhi kṣetrajña arthāḥ tathā sati sādhya samaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti 
[II,126,i]	ucyate na prasiddhi anurodhāt satyam kārya kāraṇa saṃghātasya pārārthyam bhoktṛ tvam na upapadyate loke tu devadatta artha tvam śayana ādīnām prasiddham atas tad anugacchantaḥ vayam api evam brūmaḥ kasmāt prasiddheḥ prasiddhena hi aprasiddham tad dharma tām āpadyate bhavadbhiḥ api uktam yasya hi pratikṣaṇam anyathātvam na asti tasya bāhya pratyayayoḥ bhedaḥ paścāt viśeṣa grahaṇe na asti tat yathā bhūmeḥ apacyamānāyāḥ pāka jānām na ca bhūmeḥ pratikṣaṇam anyathātvam na asti akṣaṇika tva prasaṃgāt saukṣmyāt duradhigamaḥ bhedaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ prayuktaḥ tasmāt siddham saṃghāta para artha tvāt asti puruṣaḥ 
[II,126,ii_II,127,iii]	itas ca triguṇa ādi viparyayāt triguṇam aviveki viṣayaḥ sāmānyam acetanam prasava dharmi ca bāhya ādhyātmikam tathā pradhānam tatra yadi etāvat etat syāt kim apekṣya vyakta avyaktayoḥ traiguṇyāt iti kim ca anyat adhiṣṭhānāt iha ākasmikyām pradhāna pravṛttau artha vaśaḥ sanniveśa niyamaḥ na syāt śrotra ādi pṛthivī ādīnām deva mānuṣa tiryakṣu hita yoga arthaḥ ca apratiṣedha arthaḥ ca saḥ tasmāt asti tad vyatiriktaḥ yat adhiṣṭhitānām guṇān ām ayam citra rūpaḥ vipariṇāmaḥ 
[II,127,iv]	kartṛ tva prasaṃgāt adhiṣṭhāna anupapattiḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi guṇānām puruṣa adhiṣṭhitānām pravṛttiḥ abhyupagamyate kartṛ tvam asya prāptam atha akartā na tarhi asti adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt arthe tad upacārāt yathāpuruṣa arthaḥ siddhyati tathā guṇāḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvena vyūhyante iti atas tad pāratantryāt eṣām adhiṣṭhita tvam upapadyate puruṣasya ca adhiṣṭhitṛ tvam atas na asya kartṛ tva prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat adhiṣṭhānāt puruṣaḥ 
[II,128,i_II,129,iii]	kiñca anyat puruṣaḥ asti bhoktṛ bhāvāt iha sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tvāt acetanam vyaktam avyaktam ca tasmāt asya paraspareṇa bhogaḥ na upapadyate iti avaśyam bhoktrā bhavitavyam yaḥ asau bhoktā sa puruṣaḥ āha kaḥ punar ayam bhogaḥ nāma ucyate bhogaḥ upalabdhi sadbhāvāt vijñānam eva hi viṣaya upalabdhi samartham iti atas tāvat mātram eva astu kim puruṣeṇa parikalpitena iti ucyate kim punar idam vijñānam nāma iti 
[II,129,iv]	āha cittam manaḥ vijñānam iti tat ca ṣaḍvidham jñānam cakṣuḥ vijñānam śrotra vijñānam ghrāṇa vijñānam jihvā vijñānam kāya vijñānam manaḥ vijñānam iti tatra rūpam pratītya cakṣuḥ ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam evam śrotra śabda ghrāṇa gandha jihvā rasa manaḥ dharmāḥ cittam utpādayanti tasya dharmāḥ vedanā saṃjñā sparśaḥ manaḥ saṃskāraḥ evamādayaḥ tasmāt vijñāna skandhasya eva upabhoga sāmarthāt na asti ātmā iti 
[II,129,v^1]	ucyate na acetana vikārasya cetanā anupatteḥ tat tu khalu idam iṣyate rūpam pratītya cakṣuḥ ca utpadyate cakṣuḥ vijñānam ityādi tena acetana vikāra tvāt tat acetanam ghaṭa ādi vat iti āpannam tasmāt manaḥ dharmaḥ cetanā iti manoratha mātram etat vilakṣaṇa kārya utpatti darśanāt tad siddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam na ayam niyamaḥ yat uta yat jātīyam kāraṇam tat jātīyakena kāryeṇa bhavitavyam kim tarhi vilakṣaṇa kārya utpattiḥ iti bhāvānām upalabhyate tat yathā śṛṅgāt śaraḥ jāyate golomā vilomabhyaḥ dūrvā vatsatarān muka yaḥ candrakānta indu saṃyogāt salilam sūryakānta gomaya arka samparkāt sudhā udaka samparkādaraṇī nirmathanāt ca agniḥ evam acetanebhyaḥ rūpa ādibhyaḥ cetanam utpadyate iti etat ca ayuktam cetana acetana utpatti niyama vat tat niyamāt 
[II,129,v^2]	yathā sati etasmin vilakṣaṇa kārya prādurbhāve bhavataḥ cetanāt cittānna acetanam ghaṭa ādi utpadyate iti niyamaḥ tathā sati etasmin vilakṣaṇa kārya prādurbhāve na acetanebhyaḥ rūpa ādibhyaḥ cetanam cittam utpadyate iti ayam niyamaḥ naḥ tasmāt eṣām dṛṣṭānām sati bahu tve māyākāra nagara vinyāsa vat ayathārtha jñāna viṣaya tvāt asādhīyaḥ tvam pradīpa vat tat vyavasthā iti ced syāt etat yathā acetanebhyaḥ sattva ādibhyaḥ avyavasāyakam ghaṭa ādi utpadyate iti na idānīm vyavasāyakaḥ mahān na utpadyate evam rūpa ādibhyaḥ acetanam ghaṭa ādi utpadyate iti na idānīm cetanam cittam na utpadyate iti etat api anupapannam kasmāt śakti bhedāt prakāśa svābhāvyāt vyavasāya ātmakam sattvam tat yuktam yadi tat prānyāt vyavasāya ātmakaḥ mahān utpadyate tamaḥ prādhānyāt vyavasāyakāḥ ghaṭa ādayaḥ bhavataḥ tu eka ākārāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ tasmāt āyam asamaḥ samādhiḥ iti 
[II,131,i_II,131,iii]	āha kim vyavasāya caitanyayoḥ kaścid rūpa bhedaḥ asti na vā iti ucyate kim tarhi traiguṇyāt sati pratyaya rūpa tve saṃvedyā buddhiḥ yathā tu vyavasāya rūpam tathā caitanya rūpam iti tathā ca vārṣa gaṇāḥ paṭhanti buddhi vṛtti āviṣṭaḥ hi pratyaya tvena anuvartamānām anuyāti puruṣaḥ iti āha ca artha ākāraḥ iva ābhāti yathā buddhiḥ tathā pumān ābhāsamānaḥ buddhyā ataḥ boddhā maṇi vat ucyate yathā yathā manaḥ vṛttiḥ puruṣaḥ asti tathā tathā buddhi rūpam avāpnoti cetana tvāt parāśrayam 
[II,132,i]	āha rūpa abhedāt puruṣa antaḥkaraṇayoḥ anyatara parikalpanā narthakyam yadi tarhi yathā vyavasāya rūpam tathā caitanya rūpam evam sati vyavasāya mātram parikalpanīyam caitanya mātram vā kasmāt na hi ekānta kāriṇoḥ yugapad kalpane sāmarthyam asti rūpa antara abhidhānam vā atha vyavasāya caitanyayoḥ padārthānām antaram eva iti nityataḥ viśeṣyate tarhi vaktavyam idam amuṣya eva rūpam na amuṣya iti 
[II,132,ii_II,133,iv]	ucyate yaḥ evam āha rūpa abhedāt artha abhedaḥ iti sa tāvat idam praṣṭavyaḥ atha kim bhavataḥ kim vijñāna viṣayayoḥ ākāra hedaḥ asti uta na asti iti na iti āha kasmāt ākāra antare sati viṣaya pariccheda anupapatteḥ na hi viṣayasya vijñāna pratyavabhāsam antareṇa śakyam svarūpam paricchettum tatra yat anya ākāraḥ gauranyākāram go vijñānam syāt tena yathā anyākāreṇa aśva vijñān ena anya ākārasya goḥ a paricchedaḥ evam anya ākāreṇa go vijñān ena anya ākārasya go paricchedaḥ syāt tasmāt na asti viṣaya vijñānayoḥ ākāra bhedaḥ iti ucyate tayoḥ idānīm viṣaya viṣaya vijñānayoḥ kim ubhaya tvamutābhedaḥ iti āha kasmāt jñāpya jñāpaka bhāvāt iti ucyate jñāna vijñeyayoḥ yadvat rūpā bhede api bhinna tā grāhya grāhaka bhāvena tathā eva ātma prakāśayoḥ 
[II,133,v]	yathā eva tarhi bhavataḥ sati api ākāra bhede jñāna vijñeyayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāva parikalpanāt bhedaḥ evam puruṣa antaḥkaraṇayoḥ api iti grāhya grāhaka bhāva asiddheḥ ayuktam iti ced syāt etat yathā gotadvijñānayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ niścitaḥ na evam puruṣa antaḥkaraṇayoḥ tasmāt vaiṣamyam iti etad anupapannam kasmāt mārga antara gamanāt prāk uktam yeṣām ākāra bhedaḥ na asti teṣām ekatvam idānīm tu rūpa abhede api grāhya grāhaka bhāvāt evam bruvataḥ mārga antaram jñāna mātra abhyupagamādaśākyīyam iti ced syāt matam jñānam eva antara asat viṣaya bhūta anurañjitam viṣaya viṣayi rūpeṇa pratyavabhāsate na tu kiṃcid bāhyam kiṃcid grāhya rūpa āpannam asti tasmāt jñāna vijñeyayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhedāt bhedaḥ iti aśākyīyam etat iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt siddhānta bhedāt yeṣām bāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ asti tad pakṣe ayam doṣaḥ itareṣām tu jñāna mātrasya viṣaya viṣayi bhāvam pratiṣetsyāmaḥ iti 
[II,135,i]	āha evam api viṣayān avasthā prasaṃgaḥ viṣayiṇaḥ viṣaya tva pratijñānāt yadi viṣayiṇaḥ api adhyavasāyasya viṣaya bhāvaḥ pratijñāyate tena puruṣasya api viṣayiṇaḥ anyaḥ viṣayi iti prāptam tasya api anyaḥ iti anavasthāḥ atha mā bhūt ayam doṣaḥ iti puruṣaḥ niścaya rūpa tvāt na viṣayaḥ na tarhi adhyavasāyāt api niścetuḥ artha antaram kalpayitavyam iti 
[II,135,ii_II,135,iii]	ucyate cetanā tvāt puruṣe tad anupapattiḥ indriyāṇi tāvat grahaṇa mātra rūpa tvāt apratyayāni iti pratyaya vat antaḥ tāvat karaṇam parikalpyate anaḥkaraṇam api upātta viṣaya indriya vṛtti upanipātāt tad rūpa āpattau api satyām acetana tvāt svayam upalabdhum asamartham eva viṣayam iti atas bhoktāram cetanam puruṣam apekṣate puruṣasya tu cetana tvāt draṣṭṛ antaram aśakyam kalpayitum tasmāt na anavasthā prasaṃgaḥ āha puruṣasya adhyavasāya kartṛ tva prasaṃgaḥ caitanyāt yadi acetanā buddhiḥ tena tasyāḥ adhyavasāyaḥ vṛttiḥ ghaṭa ādi vat na prāpnoti atas puruṣasya adhyavasāyaḥ prāptaḥ tatas ca buddhi abhāvaḥ iti 
[II,136,i]	ucyate na kaivalyāt apratibandha prasaṃgāt anāmiśra rūpam puruṣa tattvam iti etad upariṣṭāt vakṣyāmaḥ sa yadi vyavasāya ātmakaḥ syāt apratibandhena diś niścaya ādiṣu supta matta mūrcchitānām ca vyavasāyaḥ syāt dṛṣṭaḥ tu evam avasthasya vyavasāya pratibandhaḥ tasmāt na puruṣasya vyavasāya ha yasya punar antaḥkaraṇam vyavasāyakam tasya evam doṣaḥ na asti kasmāt traiguṇyāt sattva ādi saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ hi buddhiḥ karaṇa antara pratiṣedhāt tatra yadā adhyavasāya lakṣaṇam sattvam guṇa abhāvāt pradhāna bhūtena tamasā tiraskṛta śakti bhavati tadā adhyavasāya pratibandhaḥ 
[II,136,ii_II,137,i]	āha katham punar etat gamyate sarvam idam acetanam iti ucyate prakṛti vikāra bhūta tvāt iha yat prakṛti vikāra bhūtam tat acetanam tat yathā tantu paṭa ādayaḥ prakṛti vikāra bhūtam tasmāt acetanam ākāśe darśanāt na ekāntaḥ iti ced na asiddha tvāt na hi ākāśasya ātma pakṣe prakṛti vikāra tva abhāvaḥ siddhaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat prakṛti vikāra bhūta tvāt acetanam sarvam atas eva ca cetanasya aprakṛti vikāra bhūta tvam paraspara vaidharmyāt tasmāt na anyasya parama arthasya bhoktṛ tvam ācetanyāt upapadyate na ced sūktam bhoktṛ bhāvāt asti puruṣaḥ kaivalya artham pravṛtteḥ ca 
[II,137,ii]	iha pravṛttimatām nimittam antareṇa nivṛttiḥ na upapadyate pradhānam api ca pravṛttimat vyakta darśanāt tasmāt yasya kaivalyam pradhāna pravṛtti hetuḥ sa puruṣaḥ pradhāna anabhyupagamāt ubhaya aprasiddhiḥ iti ced syāt etat pradhānam cetanavat asmākam aprasiddham yāvat tasya kaivalya artham pravṛttiḥ bhavatā puruṣa astitve liṅgam apadiśyate tat idam asiddham pradipādyate iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt pūrvam tad pratipādanāt prāc pradhānam apratipādya evam ācakṣāṇaḥ satyam evam paryanuyoga arhaḥ syāt sādhitam tu pradhānam parimāṇa ādibhiḥ iti atas na kiṃcid etat 
[II,138,i^1]	sarva ācārya vipratipatteḥ puruṣa artha siddhiḥ iti ced syāt matam yadi puruṣasya sattvam eva syāt tena tam pratyācāryāṇām na dharma vivādaḥ syāt asti ca asau tathā hi keṣāṃcid nirguṇaḥ keṣāṃcid paravān atas sarveṣām vibhuḥ parimitaḥ anyeṣām tathā ekaḥ na ekaḥ iti tasmāt bhrānti mātram puruṣa kalpanā iti etad anupapannam kasmāt sarva padārtha abhāva prasaṃgāt rūpa ādiṣu api vipratipatteḥ keṣāṃcid kṣaṇikāḥ keṣāṃcid kāla antara avasthāyinaḥ tathā āśritāḥ svatantrāḥ ityādi tathā śrota ādīni bhautikāni āhaṃkārikāṇi pauruṣāṇi iti vipratipattiḥ evam sarva padārtha abhāvaḥ syāt 
[II,138,i^2]	tasmāt asti puruṣaḥ tatra yuktam sarva pramāṇa anupalabdheḥ na asti puruṣaḥ iti etat ayuktam yat api uktam śūnyakam ādhyātmikam paśya iti tasya paścāt pratiṣedham vakṣyāmaḥ yat punar etat uktam asti karma asti vipākaḥ kārakaḥ tu na upalabhyate iti satyam etat na hi puruṣa skandhānām nikṣepe pratisaṃdhāne anyatra vā kārakaḥ iti naḥ pakṣaḥ tasmāt śreyaḥ arthibhiḥ sarva āgama tarka viruddhām nairātmya vāda parikalpanā bhrāntim asamañjasām apohya puruṣa sattva parijñānāt eva janana maraṇa ādi sarva upadrava pratipakṣa bhūtam param a m ṛtam dhruvam sthānam avāptavyam iti 
[II,142,i]	āha gṛhṇīmahe tāvat asti ayam ātmā iti idānīm anekaḥ atha ekaḥ iti vicāryam kutas saṃśayaḥ iti ced sambandhinām ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iha kasyacid anekasya anekena sambandhaḥ upalabhyate tat yathā śrotra ādinā śarīrasya kasyacid ekasya anekena tat yathā ākāśasya ghaṭa ādinā ayam api ca ātmā kārya kāraṇa sambandhī iti atas saṃśayaḥ kim śrotra ādi vat anekaḥ ākāśa vat ekaḥ vā iti kim ca anyat ācārya vipratipatteḥ aupaniṣadāḥ khalu ekaḥ ātmā iti pratipannāḥ kāṇāda akṣa pāda arhata prabhṛtayaḥ punar ekaḥ iti yathā ca eka aneka tvam pratyātmanaḥ vipratipattiḥ evam sākṣi tva audāsīt yat raṣṭṛ tva ākartṛ tveṣu tasmāt vaktavyam katham ete dharmāḥ puruṣe avatiṣṭhante iti 
[II,142,ii_II,143,i^1]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam sambandhi tvāt ātma padārthe sandehaḥ kim anekaḥ atha ekaḥ iti atra brūmaḥ bahavaḥ puruṣāḥ iti pratijñā kasmāt janma maraṇa karaṇānām pratiniyamāt janma iti mahat ādeḥ sūkṣma śarīra āśritasya liṅgasya yathāsaṃskāram bāhyena śarīreṇa sambandhaḥ maraṇam iti pūrva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phala bhoga parisamāpteḥ sāmpratasya ca phala bhogasya pratyupasthāne liṅgasya pūrva śarīra tyāgaḥ karaṇam trayodaśavidham iti vakṣyati janma ca maraṇam ca karaṇāni ca janma maraṇa karaṇāni teṣām prati puruṣam niyamaḥ etasmāt liṅgāt ātmanaḥ bahu tvam avasīyate etat uktam bhavati janma lakṣaṇam ca maraṇa lakṣaṇam ca kārya kāraṇasya avasthā antaram paraspara virodhinī tamaḥ prakāśa vat 
[II,143,i^2]	tatra yadi ekaḥ ātmā syāt tena yathā ekam dravyam tamaḥ prakāśau eka pradeśa upanipātinau na śaknoti anubhavitum asambhavāt evam ayam janma maraṇe api na śaknuyāt upabhoktum asti ca ayam kenacid kārya karaṇena janma upabhogaḥ kenacid maraṇa upabhogaḥ tena manyāmahe nānā ātmānaḥ yeṣām virodhi dharma upabhoga sāmarthyam iti tathā karaṇānām prakāśa atiśayaḥ viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇa aśuddhi atiśayaḥ ca aṣṭāviṃśatidhā śaktiḥ tayoḥ paraspara virodhāt ekena ātmanā yugapad upabhogaḥ na upapadyate na hi śakyam ekena ātmanā prakāśa atiśayaḥ viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇaḥ aśuddhi atiśayaḥ ca aśakti lakṣaṇaḥ virodhi tvāt yugapad upabhoktum asti ca ayam karaṇa nimittaḥ prati puruṣam niyamaḥ tena manyāmahe nānā ātmānaḥ iti 
[II,144,i_II,145,i]	kim ca anyat ayugapad pravṛtteḥ ca puruṣa bahu tvam siddham kasmāt ayugapad pravṛtteḥ pradhānasya itiśeṣaḥ yasya pravṛttiḥ upapadyate kasya pravṛttiḥ upapadyate pradhānasya katham iti ucyate yadi ekaḥ ātmā syāt tena eka puruṣa adhikāra nibaddham pradhānam śaktaḥ ca asau yugapad anekāni śarīrāṇi upabhoktum iti atas yāvadbhiḥ śarīraiḥ apacitāsu kāla mātrāsvasmin bhava parivarte bhavitavyam sarveṣām utpattim prati yugapad pravarteta dṛṣṭā tu pradhānasya ayugapad śarīra bhāvena pravṛttiḥ tasmāt ayugapad pravṛtteḥ ca nānā ātmānaḥ iti 
[II,145,ii]	anye punar āhuḥ bahiṣkaraṇām eva ayugapad pravṛtteḥ katham yadi ekaḥ ātmā syāt tena tad saṃskāra upanibaddhāni eva sarvāṇi karaṇāni iti atas pratipaṇḍitam avasthitaiḥ karaṇaiḥ yugapad viṣayān gṛhṇīyāt bādhirya ādi upaghāte vā sati piṇḍa antara sambandhinā karaṇena asya śabda ādi karaṇam apratiṣiddham syāt na tu tathā bhavati tasmāt karaṇānām ayugapad pravṛtteḥ nānā ātmānaḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt pūrveṇa aviśeṣāt karaṇānām pratiniyamāt iti anena ayam upasaṃgṛhītaḥ arthaḥ tasmāt yathā uktam eva astu 
[II,146,i_II,146,ii]	kim ca anyat triguṇa ādi viparyayāt ca eva iha triguṇam aviveki viṣayaḥ sāmānyam acetanam prasava dharmī iti ete dharmāḥ pratipiṇḍam upalabhyante yathā ca ete tathā tad pratiyoginaḥ nairguṇya ādayaḥ puruṣa dharmāḥ tatra yathā eva guṇa svabhāva viparīta svabhāvasya upalambhāt ekasmāt piṇḍāt eka puruṣa siddhiḥ evam pratipiṇḍam guṇa svabhāva viparīta svabhāvasya upalambhāt puruṣa nānā tvam avaseyam tasmāt avasthitam etat nānā ātmānaḥ iti 
[II,148,i_II,148,iv]	āha siddham ātmanaḥ nānātvam sākṣi tva kaivalyam ādhyasthya t raṣṭṛ tva ākartṛ tvānām idānīm kasmāt hetoḥ pratipattiḥ iti ucyate tasmāt ca viparyāyāt siddham sākṣi tvam asya puruṣasya kaivalyam mādhyasthyam draṣṭṛ tvam akartṛ bhāvaḥ ca tasmāt iti anena hetu sāmānyam ācaṣṭe caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇe viparyāsāt iti sāmānyena hetum upāttam viśeṣe avasthāpayati siddham sākṣi tvam asya puruṣasya iti evamādinā sādhya dharma nirdeśam karoti tatra sākṣi tvam iti anena guṇānām pravṛttāvaḥ tvātantryam khyāpayati pradhānasya tad artha nibandhana tvāt pravṛtteḥ adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam katham iti 
[II,149,i^1]	ucyate yathā hi kriyā sākṣiṇi kasmiṃścid avasthite kartā tad icchā anuvidhāyī kāryam nirvartayati na svatantraḥ evam pradhānam api pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ yathā puruṣasya arthaḥ sidhyati tathā mahat ahaṅkāra tanmātra indriya bhūta deva manuṣya tiryak sthāvara bhāvena vyūhate na yadṛcchātaḥ tasmāt puruṣaḥ tad artha paratantra tvāt pradhāna pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ sākṣī kaivalyam iti anena saṃsarga dharma tvam ātmanaḥ nivartayati na yathā sattva ādīnām paraspareṇa prakāśa ādi dharma apekṣāṇām saṃsargaḥ evam puruṣasya taiḥ bhavati mādhyasthyam iti anena atiśaya nihrāsa anupapatteḥ puruṣasya guṇaiḥ saha bādha anugraha anupapattim sva kārya pravṛttau ca apakṣapātam darśayati draṣṭṛ tvam iti anena udāsīnasya kārya kāraṇa piṇḍa vyūha sama kālam caitanya śakti sadbhāvāt sukha duḥkha moha svabhāvānām guṇa ceṣṭā nām anivṛtta arthānām sannidhāna mātrāt upalabdhi mātram pratijānāti 
[II,149,i^2]	akartṛ bhāvaḥ ca iti anena saptavidhama kartṛ tvam āśrayati na hi ayam viṣayeṣu bāhya antaḥkaraṇa sānnidhye adhyavasāyam kurute na ca sattva ādīnām prakāśa pravṛtti niyama lakṣaṇaiḥ dharmaiḥ itaretara upakāreṇa pravartamānānām svena caitanya lakṣaṇena dharmeṇa aṅga bhāvam pratipadyate na api aṅgi bhāvam evam saha guṇaiḥ kāryam na kurute strī kumāra vat sthita prayogam na kurute ratha śakaṭayantra preraka vat na sva ātmanaḥ mṛd piṇḍa vat na paratas kumbhakāra vat na api adeśāt māyā kāra vat na ubhayatas mātṛ pitṛ vat tat evam anena sūtreṇa ācāryaḥ puruṣasya adhiṣṭhātṛ tvam nairguṇyam audāsīnyam bhoktṛ tvam akartṛ tvam ca sādhya tām āpādya triguṇayā ādi viparyayam sādhana tvena upanyati taiḥ pañcabhiḥ triguṇa ādi viparītaiḥ karmabhiḥ pañcānām eṣām yathāsaṃbhavam pravṛttiḥ avagantavyā 
[II,150,i_II,150,ii]	yasmāt ayam sukha ādibhyaḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ tasmāt ayam tad kriyā sākṣī tatra nairguṇyāt sākṣi tvam āha tad asiddheḥ nairguṇya asiddheḥ yadi asya sukha ādi dharma tvam ātmanaḥ prasiddham syāt atas etat yujjate vaktum tattva siddham tasmāt ayuktam etat viśeṣān abhidhānāt itarāt siddhiḥ api iti ced syāt matam ātma guṇāḥ sukha ādayaḥ na śabda guṇāḥ iti atra api bhavatā viśeṣaḥ na abhidhīyate tasmāt etat api asiddham etat api ayuktam kasmāt ahaṃkāreṇa eka vākya tve bhinna adhikaraṇa tvam syāt dṛṣṭam tu sukhitaḥ aham duḥkhitaḥ aham iti tasmāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ śabda ādi ātma bhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[II,151,i_II,151,ii]	ucyate na gaura ādiṣu anekāntāt tat yathā gauraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ aham iti śarīra dharmeḥ ātmanaḥ bhinna adhikaraṇa tvam ahaṅkāreṇa evam sukha duḥkhayoḥ api syāt na ca ātma guṇa tvam syāt iti āha pṛthak upalabdheḥ ayuktam yadi api gaura ādīnām avibhaktam ahaṃkāreṇa grahaṇam tathā api pṛthak ayam prāc etān ātmanaḥ gṛhītvā paścāt avibhaktān gṛhṇan śaktnoti vyavasthāpayitum uṣyā ete na punar amuṣya iti na tu evam sukha duḥkhayoḥ pṛthak upalabdhiḥ tasmāt asat etat iti
