[II,151,iii]	ucyate na evam utpadyate kasmāt mārga antara gamanāt ahaṃkāreṇa avibhakta grahaṇāt ātma guṇa tvam iti prāc apadiṣṭam idānīm tu sati api tasmin pṛthak grahaṇāt abhāvam bruvataḥ mārga antara gamanam anaikāntikasya ca aparihāraḥ kim ca anyat saṃśaya avyatirekāt yatas eva gaura ādayaḥ pṛthak upalabhyante na sukha ādayaḥ eva saṃśayaḥ na ca yatas eva saṃśayaḥ tatas eva nirṇayaḥ yuktaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat gaura ādi vat ahaṅkāreṇa api abhinna grahaṇāt śabda ādi ātma bhūtāḥ sukha ādayaḥ kim ca anyat svabhāva anavadhāraṇāt anupādāna prasaṃgāt sukha ādi ātmakāḥ śabda ādayaḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā agniḥ pāka ja nimittam upādīyate atha ca eṣām pārthiva tvam evam śabda ādayaḥ api sukha ādi nimitta tvena upādīyeran atha ca eṣām ātma guṇa tvam eva syāt iti tat api anupapannam kasmāt sāmānādhikaraṇya darśanāt yathā nimittasya agneḥ na pāka jaiḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam pakvaḥ agniḥ pacyate agniḥ iti evam śabda ādīnām nimitta tvāt na sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt sukha śabdaḥ duḥkhaḥ iti dṛṣṭam tu tasmāt na teṣām nimitta arthena upādānam iti 
[II,153,i_II,153,ii]	āha evam api sukha ādīnām śabda ādi ātma bhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ kasmāt vipratipatteḥ yathā hi śabdāḥ śabda ātmakāḥ eti sarvaiḥ śabda rūpeṇa gṛhyante evam sukha ātmakaḥ ayam iti sarvaiḥ tad rūpeṇa gṛhyate dṛṣṭā tu vipratipattiḥ tasmāt ātma guṇāḥ iti ucyate na saṃskāra viśeṣa nimitta tvāt tat yathā pitta ādi sāmarthān mādhurya ādiṣu vipratipattiḥ na ca eṣām a śabda ādi guṇa tva saṃskāra viśeṣa yogāt sukha ādiṣu vipratipattiḥ na ca eṣām a śabda ādi guṇa tvam iti kim ca anyat nimitta tve api tad prasaṃgāt nimitta vādinaḥ api etat samānam na hi nimitta naimittikayoḥ vipratipattiḥ asti tat yathā pradīpa prakāśayoḥ tatas ca vipratipatteḥ nimitta tvam api śabda ādīnām akalpanīyam syāt yaḥ ca dvayoḥ doṣaḥ na tam ekaḥ ca udyate iti ātma guṇākāṃkṣi tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam nimitta pradhāna tvāt anya paripāka vaśena sukha duḥkhena utpādayati ātmanaḥ tad maya tve tu nirāka aṃkṣa tvāt pradhānasya vyavasthā bhedaḥ na yuktaḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt ukta tvāt tad maya tve api guṇa bhāvāt mādhurya ādiṣu vipratipattiḥ iti ādau eva uktam etat tasmāt tad maya tve prādhānyam iti ca aniścita abhidhānam etat 
[II,154,i_II,154,ii^1]	āha evam api ayuktam etat kasmāt atīta anāgateṣu api tu dṛṣṭeḥ tasmāt sukha ādīnām śabda ādi ātma bhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ iti ucyate na smṛti nimitta tvāt buddheḥ ayam atīta anāgateṣu api śabda ādiṣu smārta sukha duḥkha yogaḥ bhavati tad saṃparkāt tu puruṣeṇa tathā anubhūyate puruṣa guṇa tve tu pāka ja vat nimittāt utpannānām sukha ādīnām viśeṣa bhāvāt tīvra manda tā anupapattiḥ syāt tasmāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ śabda ādi ātma bhāvaḥ na yuktaḥ kiṃca anyat anirmokṣa prasaṃgāt dravyasya guṇaiḥ aviprayogāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ ātma guṇa tve satya ātmanaḥ tābhyām anirmokṣa prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt tayoḥ ātma guṇa tvam ayuktam iti śyāma ādi vat tat vinivṛttiḥ iti ced syāt matam yathā śyāma guṇa tve sati aṇoḥ agni sambandhāt tad vinivṛttiḥ śabda ādi guṇa tve ca ākāśasya aśabdakasya avasthānam evam ātmanaḥ api etat ayuktam kasmāt 
[II,154,ii^2]	viśeṣa upādāna prasaṃgāt sādhya tvāt ca yathā hi aṇuḥ śyāma tām parityajya rūpa viśeṣam eva rakta lakṣaṇam upādatte na rūpavat tām tyajati evam ātmā api bāhya nimitta sāmarthyāt sukha antaram duḥkhāt duḥkha antaram upādadīta na te atyantam jahyāt tathā ākāśam śabda lakṣaṇam kasyāṃcid avasthā āyāma śabdakam bhavati iti asmān prati sādhyaḥ ayam arthaḥ bherī ādi śabdāḥ tu tad guṇaḥ eva iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt sukha duḥkhayoḥ śabda ādi ātma bhāvaḥ ayuktaḥ evam anāmiśra rūpaḥ ātmā tatas ca icchā dveṣa prayatna dharma jñāna saṃskārāṇām aneka svabhāvānām paraspara virodhinām ca tad guṇa tvam anupapannam tasmāt yuktam etat nirguṇaḥ ātmā nairguṇyāt ca sākṣi mātraḥ iti kevalaḥ vivikta tvāt 
[II,156,i_II,156,iii]	tasmāt ayam guṇebhyaḥ pṛthak bhūtaḥ tasmāt kevalaḥ na taiḥ saha saṃsargeṇa vartate āha kaḥ punar asya ātmanaḥ guṇebhyaḥ pṛthagbhāvaḥ abhipretaḥ iti ucyate tad upakāra nirapekṣāṇām sattva ādīnām sva kārya sāmarthya pṛthagbhāvaḥ na hi sattva ādayaḥ prakāśa ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ itaretara upakāreṇa vartamānāḥ puruṣa kṛtam upakāram apekṣante prakāśa ādi dharma sannidhāna mātrāt eva tu pravartante tathā ca vārṣa gaṇāḥ paṭhanti pradhāna pravṛttiḥ apratyayā puruṣeṇa aparigṛhyamāṇa ādi sarge vartante iti yasmāt guṇāḥ tad upakāra nirapekṣāḥ pravartante tasmāt asau api tad saṃsarga na anubhavati dṛṣṭā tu loke api eka kārya tva apṛthak pṛthak bhāva parikalpanā tat yathā ime bhrātaraḥ pṛthak eṣām na ekam kāryam na pṛthak ime yeṣām ekam iti 
[II,157,i]	madhyasthaḥ viṣayi tvāt yasmāt ayam puruṣaḥ viṣayī tasmāt madhya sthaḥ kim kāraṇam viṣayāṇām hi atulya bala tvāt nyūna atiśaya upapatteḥ ca paraspareṇa bādha anugrahau utpannau viṣayī ca ayam tasmāt na asti nyūna tā ādi upapattiḥ tatas cetana abhāvaḥ na ca āmiśra rūpa tvāt saṅga dveṣau guṇa viṣayau atas madhyasthaḥ 
[II,157,ii_II,157,iv]	draṣṭṛ tvam caitanyāt prakṛti vikāra bhūta tvāt sattva ādibhyaḥ caitanyam apoddhṛtya puruṣe vyavasthāpanīyam na ca acetanānām draṣṭṛ tvam upapadyate iti atas puruṣaḥ eva caitanyāt dṛṣṭā na anyat tattva antaram akartṛ bhāvaḥ aprasava dharmi tvāt prasava arthaḥ dharmaḥ prasava dharmaḥ saḥ asya asti iti prasava dharmī kaḥ punar asau prasava arthaḥ dharmaḥ iti 
[II,157,v^1]	ucyate praspandana pariṇāmau niṣkriya tvāt akartā iti yāvat tad idam aprasava dharmi tvāt akartā iti katham asya niṣkriya tvam iti ced caitanyāt acetanānām hi kṣīra ādīnām kriyāvat tvam upalabdham cetanasya na kasyacid iti ataḥ niṣkriyaḥ puruṣaḥ kiṃca anāmiśra rūpa tvāt anāmiśra rūpam hi kriyā ādimad kṣīra ādi anāmiśra rūpaḥ ca ayam tasmāt niṣkriyaḥ vibhu tvāt iti ced syāt etat yathā vibhu tve sati pradhānasya sa kriya tvam evam puruṣasya iti vibhu tve sa kriyatvena bhavitavyam iti tat ca na evam kasmāt dharma dvaya sahitasya sāhacarya upalabdheḥ tad vibhu tvam ācetanya aneka rūpa tva sahitam kriyāvati dṛṣṭam na kevalam na tu tathā puruṣe tasmāt viṣamam etat evam niṣkriyaḥ puruṣaḥ niṣkriya tvāt ca pradhānāt kārya kāraṇam na kurute kasmāt kriyāvataḥ kumbhakārasya mṛd piṇḍāt kārya niṣpatti sāmarthya darśanāt syāt etat utpāditasya anyena sthitim kurute dhātrī kumāra vat 
[II,157,v^2_II,158,i]	sthitasya vā prayogam ratha śakaṭayantra preraka vat iti etat api anupapannam pūrvasmāt eva hetoḥ atha api syāt svatas puruṣaḥ kārya karaṇam kurutaḥ iti tat api ayuktam cetanā cetanayoḥ atyanta bhedāt prakṛti vikāra bhāva anupapatteḥ atha matam ubhayatas iti tat api na eva saṃbhavati ubhaya doṣa prasaṃgāt syāt punar etat avyapadiśya yonim puruṣaḥ abhidhyāna mātreṇa kārya karaṇam kurute iti asat etat kasmāt anutpattau abhidhyāna anupapatteḥ īśvara kāraṇa pratiṣedhe abhihitam prāk pradhāna vipariṇāmāt buddhim atas buddhiḥ na asti na ca buddhim antareṇa abhidhyānam upapadyate tad vṛtti bhūta tvāt tathā buddhimat pūrvaka sṛṣṭi pratiṣedhaḥ kṛtaḥ saḥ iha api yojyaḥ adhyavasāya kartṛ tvam ca prāk pratiṣiddham evam saptavidhena akartṛ tvena akartā puruṣaḥ uktam ca na adhyavasāyam kurute puruṣaḥ na evam sthitim prayogam vā na sva ātmanaḥ na paratas na vyapadeśāt na ca ubhayatas tat yuktam etat tasmāt ca viparyāsāt siddham sākṣi tvam asya puruṣasya kaivalyam mādhyasthyam draṣṭṛ tvam akartṛ bhāvaḥ ca iti 
[II,163,i_II,163,iii]	yatas cetanā śakti sambandhāt puruṣaḥ eva draṣṭā na anyat tattva antaram guṇāḥ ca kartāraḥ na puruṣaḥ tasmāt tad saṃyogāt acetanam cetanāvat iva liṅgam guṇa kartṛ tve ca tathā kartā iva bhavati udāsīnaḥ puruṣa samparkāt hi grahaṇa dhāraṇa vijñāna vacanoha apoha kriyā yathā anyāya abhiniveśānām karaṇa dharmāṇām pratyaya rūpāṇām iva upalabdheḥ cetanā śakteḥ ca adhyavasāya vṛttim anurudhyamānāyāḥ tad bhāva sanniveśinām sattva ādīnām vyāpāravatām abhisambandhāt vyāpāra āviṣṭāyāḥ iva upalabdhiḥ yatas tatra ayam aneka kāla pravṛtta mithyā pratyaya abhyāsa vāsana apekṣaḥ bhava bīja hetuḥ jñāna viśeṣaḥ prāṇabhṛtām avabhāsate śrotram upalabhyate tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇam ityādi tathā puruṣaḥ karmaṇām kartā puruṣaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ iti tasmāt karaṇasya grahaṇa rūpa tā puruṣasya ca kartṛ rūpa tā sambandhi antara samparkāt anya gatā anyatra upalabhyamānā bhaktyā adhyavasātavyā na paramārthataḥ uktam ca
[II,163,iv_II,164,i]	cetanā adhiṣṭhātā buddhiḥ cetanā iva vibhāvyate kartṛṣu avasthitaḥ ca ātmā bhoktā kartā iva lakṣyate āha saṃyogāt para rūpa tā āpattau atiprasaṃgaḥ aviśeṣāt yadi cetana saṃyogāt buddhi ādīnām pratyaya vat upacāraḥ vyāpi tvā ādasya ghaṭa ādibhiḥ api saṃyogaḥ na pratiṣidhyate iti atas prāptaḥ teṣām api pratyaya vat upacāraḥ atha saṃyoga aviśeṣāt karaṇānām eva pratyaya vat upacāraḥ na ghaṭa ādīnām viśeṣaḥ tarhi vaktavyaḥ iti 
[II,164,ii_II,165,i]	ucyate tad aprasaṃgaḥ śakti apekṣa tvāt sphaṭika ādi vat yathā upadhāna saṃyoga viśeṣe satya ākāśa sphaṭikayoḥ sphāṭikam eva upadhana sarūpam pratyavabhāsate śaktitaḥ na ākāśam evam puruṣa saṃyoga aviśeṣe buddhi ghaṭayoḥ śaktitas buddhiḥ eva cetanā rūpāpan eva upalabhyate na ghaṭaḥ āha puruṣasya vikārya tva prasaṃgaḥ rūpa antara upādanāt yadi tarhi karaṇa sambandhāt puruṣaḥ kartṛ tva upacāram viṣaya sarūpa tām ca pratipadyate prāptam asya api sphaṭika vat rūpa antara upādānāt vikārya tvam atha na asya viṣaya rūpa āpattiḥ na tarhi karaṇa svarūpaḥ puruṣaḥ iti 
[II,165,ii]	ucyate na bhaktitaḥ abhyupagamāt buddhiḥ upātta viṣaya indriya vṛtti upanipātāt tādrūpyam pratipadyate buddhi rūpam tu sannidhāna mātrāt śakti viśeṣa yogāt phala bhoktṛ tvāt ca rājani bhṛtya jaya parājaya upacāra vatpuruṣaḥ upacaryate na tu asau buddhi saṃparkāt tad rūpaḥ bhavati atas eva asya satyām cetanā śaktau vyavasāya kartṛ tvam pratiṣidhyate mā bhūt viṣaya rūpa āpattau satyām aneka svabhāva tva ādi kārya tva prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt viṣaya samparkāt api avikāryaḥ puruṣaḥ na hi asya nitya tvāt kiṃcid anugrahāya na apaghātāya āha ca muṣṭiḥ yathā vikīrṇaḥ sūcī agre sarṣapa ādīnām tiṣṭhanti na sūkṣma bhāvāt tadvat dvandvāni sarvajñe 
[II,165,iii_II,165,iv]	iti cetanā śakti yogāt tu draṣṭṛ tvam asya svābhāvikam evam ced yayuktam varṣa ātapābhyām kim vyomnaḥ carmaṇi asti tayoḥ phalam carma upamaḥ ced saḥ anityaḥ kha tulyaḥ ced asat samaḥ iti tat ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt avikārya rūpasya ākāśasya sannidhāna mātrāt megha payaḥ rajaḥ dhūma prabhṛtibhiḥ abhinna deśa tvāt atyanta śuddhasya api malinam iva rūpam upalakṣyate na ca vikārya tvam evam anātmanaḥ api syāt tat yuktam etat puruṣa saṃyogāt karaṇasya pratyaya upacāraḥ puruṣasya ca guṇa saṃyogāt kartṛ tva upacāraḥ iti 
[II,167,i^1]	āha ayuktam etat kasmāt saṃyoga anupapatteḥ puruṣasya hi guṇānām ca saṃyogaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ anyatara karma jaḥ vā parikalpyate yathā sthāṇu śyenayoḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ yathā meṣayoḥ saṃyoga jaḥ vā dvi aṅgula ākāśayoḥ svābhāvikaḥ vā yathā agni uṣṇayoḥ śakti nimittaḥ vā yathā cakṣu rūpayoḥ yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ vā yathā matsya udakayoḥ iti tat na tāvat anyatara karma jaḥ ubhya karma jaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ eṣām upapadyate kasmāt vibhu tvāt na svābhāvikaḥ anirmokṣa prasaṃgāt yathā agneḥ svābhāvikāt auṣṇyāt mokṣaḥ na bhavati evam ātmanaḥ svābhāvika tvāt guṇa saṃyogāt anirmokṣa prasaṃgaḥ syāt śakti nimittaḥ ca kim anirmokṣa prasaṃgāt eva sa na bhavati iti anuvartate sva svāmi śakti nimitte hi saṃyoge parikalpyamāne śaktyoḥ satata avasthānāt anirmokṣaḥ eva prasajyeta yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ śakti mātra rūpa tvāt asaṃvedyaḥ atas tat asiddhiḥ 
[II,167,i^2]	kiṃca prayojana antara anupapatteḥ pravṛtti anuguṇam hi yogyam iti ucyate tasyāḥ eva tu pravṛtte puruṣa artham apohya nimitta antaram śakyam kalpayitum ākasmika tve ca niyama dvaita anupapattiḥ tasmāt ayuktam puruṣasya guṇānām ca yogya tā lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ na yādṛcchikaḥ mokṣa kāraṇa niyama anupapatteḥ saṃyoga kāraṇa pratidvandvam kaivalya kāraṇam yadi ca yādṛcchikaḥ guṇa puruṣa saṃyogaḥ syāt tasya ajñānāt nivṛttiḥ na asti iti tad arthasya abhyutthānasya anarthakyam prāptam viśeṣa anupapatteḥ ca kāraṇa antaram kalpayitum atas etat api ayuktam iti na vaiṣayikaḥ anirmokṣa prasaṃgāt satatam eva hi puruṣasya viṣayi tvam avyāvṛttam guṇānām ca viṣaya tvam iti anirmokṣa prasaṃgaḥ eva syāt etāvān ca saṃyogaḥ parikalpyamānaḥ parikalpyeta sarvathā ca na upapadyate tasmāt tad saṃyoga āditya yuktam abhidhātum iti 
[II,169,i]	ucyate saṃyoga anitya tvāt iha ca aupakārika parikalpa nāda doṣaḥ iha anekavidhaḥ saṃyogaḥ tat yathā prāpti pūrvikā prāptiḥ yathā udāhṛtam anyatara jaḥ ubhaya karma jaḥ saṃyogaḥ ityādi yatra asau na saṃbhavati tatra sannidhi mātra sāmānyāt bhaktyā kalpyate tat yathā ākāśasya gavā ādibhiḥ pradeśaiḥ iti ced na abhāvāt te api hi niravayava tvāt ākāśasya bhaktyā kalpyante mā bhūt kṛtaka tva anitya tva doṣa prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt pradeśa upacārāt kāryam api upacaritam anyaḥ tu śāstrīyaḥ saṃyogaḥ artha nimittaḥ tatra aneka saṃyoga upapatteḥ iha puruṣa antaḥkaraṇayoḥ abhinna deśa tvāt sannidhi mātra sāmānyāt bhāktam saṃyogam parikalpya evam ucyate iti adoṣaḥ 
[II,171,i_II,171,iii]	āha vijñātam saṃyoga dvayam ayam tu anyaḥ artha nimittaḥ śāstrīyaḥ saṃyogaḥ bhavatā paribhāṣyate tatra vaktavyam kimarthaḥ asau iti ucyate puruṣasya darśana arthaḥ dṛṣṭiḥ darśanam artha śabdaḥ nimitta vacanaḥ darśanam arthaḥ asya asau darśana arthaḥ darśana nimittaḥ darśana hetuḥ darśana kāraṇaḥ iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati sannidhāna aviśeṣe sati ātmanaḥ ākāśa ādeḥ ca yasmāt dṛś chakti yuktaḥ puruṣaḥ tasmāt kārya kāraṇa tām āpannena pradhānena saha bhoktṛ tvena saṃbadhyate na ācaitanyāt ākāśa ādayaḥ iti athavā artha śabdaḥ phala vacanaḥ yathā tṛpti arthā bhuji kriyā tṛptyau satyām nivartate prāpti arthāḥ gami kriyā prāptau satyām evam puruṣasya pradhānena darśana arthaḥ saṃyogaḥ darśane sati nivartate tathā ca vakṣyati dṛṣṭā mayā itiyupekṣakaḥ ekaḥ dṛṣṭā aham iti uparata eka iti 
[II,172,i_II,172,iv]	āha evam api śabda ādi upalabdhi sama kālam eva nivṛtti prasaṃgaḥ kim kāraṇam tasyām api avasthāyām śakyam vaktum dṛṣṭā prakṛtiḥ iti ucyate yadi api etat evam tathā api yathā puruṣasya darśana arthaḥ saṃyogaḥ kaivalya arthaḥ tathā pradhānasya kaivalyam iti viveka paricchinnam sattva ādibhiḥ asaṃsarga dharmi tvam ātmanaḥ saḥ arthaḥ asya saḥ ayam kaivalya arthaḥ sati api hi darśana aviśeṣe pradhānam puruṣasya kaivalya artham pravartate yadā asya buddhiḥ tamasaḥ aṅgi tvā ādye guṇāḥ kārya rūpa āpannāḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādayaḥ ādhyātmikā bāhyāḥ ca gavā ādayaḥ kāraṇa rūpa āpannāḥ ca ālocana kriyā saṃkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāya lakṣaṇāḥ saḥ aham iti aviśiṣṭa pratyaya upasaṃhāram karoti tadā pravartate eva yadā tu anye guṇāḥ prakṛti bhūtāḥ vikāra bhūtāḥ kārya bhūtāḥ kāraṇa bhūtāḥ acetanāḥ para arthāḥ anyaḥ aham na prakṛtiḥ na vikṛtiḥ na kāryam na kāraṇam na acetanaḥ sva arthaḥ iti bhinna pratyaya upasaṃhāram karoti tadā nivartate saḥ ayam puruṣasya dṛś chakti nimittaḥ pradhānasya ca kaivalya avadhi paricchinnaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ sati api pāribhāṣika tve paṅgu andhavat ubhayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ
[II,172,v]	etat uktam bhavati prāk api kārya kāraṇa sambandhāt puruṣe ca etu anyam avasthitam tat yathā agneḥ dahanam paraśoḥ chedanam asati dāhye chedye na vyajyate tad sannidhāna sama kālam eva tu vyajyate iti atas pradhānam apekṣate tathā pradhānam api antareṇa puruṣa upakāram svakādasarmartham aniṣpanna kārya samam cetitam anartha kama syāt iti atas puruṣam apekṣate tatra ubhayoḥ itaretara apekṣā tam saṃyogam adhikāra bandham āhuḥ ācāryāḥ paṅgu andha dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu na antarīyaka mātra pradarśana artham yathā paṅgurna antareṇa andham dṛś chaktyā viśiṣṭena arthena arthavān bhavati andhaḥ ca na antareṇa paṅgum viśiṣṭena arthena evam pradhānam na antareṇa puruṣam kṛtam api kāryam draṣṭum śaktam anavadhikam ca pravartamānam viśeṣa abhāvāt na eva nivartate tathā puruṣaḥ sati api cetana tve na antareṇa pradhānam upalabhya abhāvāt upalabdhā bhavet iti pradhānam apekṣate tasmāt itara itara apekṣayā saṃyoga tve kalpyamāne yat uktam vinā sargeṇa bandhaḥ hi puruṣasya na yujyate sargaḥ tasya eva mokṣa artham aho sāṃkhyasya sūkta tā 
[II,173,i_II,175,ii]	iti tat ayuktam kasmāt na hi asau vinā sargeṇa na yujyate iti āha ca dṛśya darśana bhāvena prakṛteḥ puruṣasya ca apekṣā śāstra tattva jñaiḥ bandhaḥ iti abhidhīyate evam vinā api sargeṇa yasmāt baddhaḥ pumān guṇaiḥ tasmāt viphala tām yātu manoratha manorathaḥ iti siddhaḥ saṃyogaḥ tad kṛtaḥ sargaḥ pradhāna puruṣayoḥ hi bhoktṛ bhogya bhāva apekṣa nimittaḥ ayam tattva sargaḥ mahat ādiḥ bhāva sargaḥ ca dharma ādiḥ bhūta sargaḥ ca brāhma ādiḥ pravartate sā ca apekṣā puruṣa ānantyāt na nivartate iti atas arthavatīnām hi prakṛtīnām tad aparisamāpteḥ na nivṛtiḥ asti 
[II,177,i^1]	evam kāraṇa antara pratiṣedhāt prakṛteḥ puruṣa arthaḥ ayam vyakta bhāvena vipariṇāmaḥ iti sthitam tatra idānīm vipratipattiḥ ācāryāṇām kecid āhuḥ pradhānāt anirdeśya svarūpam tattva antaram utpadyate tatas mahān iti patañjali pañca adhikaraṇa vārṣa gaṇānām tu pradhānāt mahān utpadyate iti tad anyeṣām purāṇa itihāsa praṇetṝṇām mahataḥ ahaṃkāraḥ vidyate iti pakṣaḥ mahataḥ asmi pratyaya kartṛ tva abhyupagamāt ahaṃkārāt pañca tanmātrāṇi iti sarve mahataḥ ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ sṛjyante pañca tanmātrāṇi ahaṃkāraḥ ca iti vindhya vāsi matam tathā ahaṃkārāt indriyāṇi iti sarve bhautikāni indriyāṇi iti pañca adhikaraṇa matam eka rūpāṇi tanmātrāṇi iti anye eka uttarāṇi iti vārṣagaṇyaḥ indriyāṇi saṃskāra viśeṣa yogāt parigṛhīta rūpāṇi iti kecid paricchinna parimāṇāni iti apare 
[II,177,i^2]	vibhūni iti vindhya vāsi matam adhikaraṇam api kecid trayodaśavidham āhuḥ ekādaśakam iti vindhya vāsī tathā anyeṣām mahati sarva artha upalbdhiḥ manasi vindhya vāsinaḥ saṃkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāya nānātvam anyeṣām eka tvam vindhya vāsinaḥ tathā karaṇam nirlikhita svarūpam śūnya grāma nadī kalpam prākṛta vaikṛtikāni tu jñānāni preraka aṅga saṃgṛhītāni pradhānāt āgacchanti ca iti pañca adhikaraṇaḥ na tu tathā iti anye kāraṇānām mahatī svabhāva ativṛttiḥ pradhānāt su alpā ca svatas iti vārṣagaṇyaḥ sarvā svatas iti patañjaliḥ sarvā paratas iti pañca adhikaraṇaḥ buddhiḥ kṣaṇikā iti ca kāla antara avasthāyinī iti apare evam aneka niścayeṣu ācāryeṣu ye tāvat pradhāna mahatoḥ antarāle tattva antaram icchanti tad pratikṣepāya ācāryaḥ sva matam upanyasyati 
[II,178,i_II,178,iii]	prakṛteḥ mahān prakṛteḥ mahān utpadyate mahān buddhiḥ matiḥ brahma āpūrtiḥ khyātiḥ īśvaraḥ vikharaḥ iti paryāyāḥ sa tu deśa mahat tvāt kāla mahat tvāt ca mahān sarva utpādyebhyaḥ mahā parimāṇa yukta tvāt mahān anyasya tu pakṣe na eva ahaṃkāraḥ vidyate iti pratiṣedha vivakṣayā idam āha tatas ahaṅkāraḥ tasmāt mahataḥ ahaṃkāraḥ utpadyate 
[II,178,iv_II,179,i]	yaḥ punar āha mahataḥ ṣaṣ aviśeṣāḥ sṛjyante pañca tanmātrāṇi ahaṃkāraḥ ca iti tad nirāsa artham āha tasmāt gaṇaḥ ca ṣoḍaśakaḥ tasmāt ahaṃkārāt ṣoḍaśakaḥ gaṇaḥ utpadyate pañca tanmātrāṇi ekādaśa indriyāṇi ca anena eva ca bhautika indriya vādī pratikṣiptaḥ boddhavyaḥ tasmāt api ṣoḍaśakāt pañcabhyaḥ pañca bhūtāni 
[II,179,ii]	tasmāt api ṣoḍaśakāt gaṇāt yaḥ pañcakaḥ gaṇaḥ tatas pañca mahābhūtāni utpadyante pūrva pada lopena atra mahābhūtāni iti vaktavye bhūtāni iti ucyate bhūta saṃjñā hi tanmātrāṇām na pṛthivī ādīnām atra tu sāṃkhya ācāryāṇām avipratipattiḥ bhūta kauṭasthya vādinaḥ tu mīmāṃsakāḥ ārhatāḥ ca tad pratikṣepeṇa idam ucyate iti 
[II,181,i_II,181,iv^1]	āha uktam pradhānāt buddhiḥ utpadyate iti tatra vaktavyam kiṃlakṣaṇā punar buddhiḥ iti ucyate adhyavasāyaḥ buddhiḥ kaḥ ayamadhyavasāyaḥ gauḥ eva ayam puruṣaḥ eva ayam iti yaḥ pratyayaḥ niścayaḥ artha grahaṇam saḥ adhyavasāyaḥ atra kṣaṇika vādi āha yadi artha grahaṇam buddhiḥ anityā kasmāt hetu apekṣaṇāt artha grahaṇam hi indriyā ādi viṣaya sannidhānam āvaraṇa ādi abhāvam ca apekṣate na ca nityasya kāraṇa apekṣā upapadyate tasmāt anityā buddhiḥ abhivyakteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt etat na indriya sannidhāna ādibhiḥ artha grahaṇam janyate kim tarhi abhivyajyate iti tat ca na evam dvidhā doṣāt sā hi abhivyaktiḥ svarūpa lābhaḥ vā syāt grahaṇa pratibandha vyudāsaḥ vā kim ca atas tat yadi tāvat svarūpa lābhaḥ kriyate artha grahaṇam iti prāptam artha grahaṇa pratibandhasya andhakārasya vyudāsaḥ tat api ayuktam vipratiṣedhāt grahaṇam ca syāt tad pratibandhaḥ ca iti vipratiṣiddham kiṃca bhedāt vyaṅgyam hi ghaṭa ādi candra arka oṣadhi maṇi ratna pradīpa bhedāt na bhidyate asti buddhīnām artha bhedāt bhedaḥ vṛtti bhedāt adoṣaḥ mṛdvat iti ced syāt matam yathā mṛd dravyasya ghaṭa ādi saṃsthāna vṛtti bhede api abhedaḥ evam buddheḥ iti tat api ayuktam ananya tvāt yadā buddhiḥ anyāḥ vṛttibhyaḥ prāptaḥ tad bhede buddhi bhedaḥ 
[II,181,iv^2]	kiṃca dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ sādhyam ca etat kim tat eva mṛd dravyam ghaṭa ādi vṛtti bhedam anubhavati āhosvit pratyaya antara vaśāt anyat ca anyat ca utpadyate iti avayava bhedāt ca upetya vā anuvṛttim brūmaḥ na hi tat ekam mṛd dravyam kim tarhi bahavaḥ mṛd paramāṇavaḥ aneka deśa avacchinna vṛttayaḥ iti kim ca anyat nivṛtti vibhakti grahaṇāt tat hi mṛd dravyam saṃsthānam apekṣya api gṛhyate na tu artha grahaṇam anapekṣya buddheḥ grahaṇam asti tasmāt viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ parimāṇāt adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam sattva ādīnām aṅga aṅgi bhāva niyamāt tena tena artha grahaṇa ātmanā vipariṇāmaḥ vṛttiḥ iti etat ca ayuktam ubhaya kalpane doṣa prasaṃgāt yadi dharma antara upādāna parityāgau vyakta vyaktī datta uttaraḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ atha nāśa utpādau tena dharma dharmiṇoḥ ananya tvāt dharmāṇām nāśa utpādāt buddheḥ api nāśa utpāda prasaṃgaḥ tad anabhyupagame vā anya tvam iti doṣaḥ āha ca naṣṭa utpannam ananya tvāt anityam nityam eva vā naṣṭa utpanna avinaṣṭānām nityam taḥ na asti ca ekadā 
[II,182,i]	yat api uktam sattva ādīnām aṅga aṅgi bhāva niyamāt iti tat ayuktam atas eva anitya tva siddheḥ tulyānām guṇa pradhāna bhāva anupapatteḥ sattva ādīnān aṅga aṅgibhāva abhyupagamāt vṛddhi kṣayau abhyupagantavyau tatas ca buddhiḥ anityā iti prāptam tebhyaḥ ananya tvāt atha matam tad avasthā api asau nityā iti na tarhi satva ādi ātma bhūtā buddhiḥ iti prāptam tatas ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ avivekaḥ iti asya virodhaḥ tasmāt anityāḥ buddhiḥ iti 
[II,184,i^1]	ucyate yat tāvat uktam hetu apekṣaṇāt anityā buddhiḥ iti tat ayuktam kasmāt siddha sādhanāt kasya atra vipratipattiḥ anityā vā buddhiḥ syāt nityā vā iti kim tarhi hetu mada nityam vyaktam iti vacanāt anitya eva tasmāt iṣṭam eva etat saṅgṛhītam atas eva kṣaṇika tvam iti ced atha api syāt hetu apekṣā hi saṃskṛta tvam saṃskṛtam tu kṣaṇikam tat yathā pradīpaḥ iti tasmāt anitye sati api viśeṣān abhidhāne kṣaṇika tvam eva anena hetunā buddheḥ pratipādyate iti kasmāt uttara vacana virodha prasaṃgāt evam api yat uttaram kṣaṇika tva prasiddhi artham ucyate pratyartha grahaṇa anyatvāt anitya ityādi tasya ānarthakyam tasmāt pūrva uttara viruddha tvāt sakalam eva idam prakaraṇam na adhyayanam na pratyākhyānam arhati 
[II,184,i^2]	pareṣām tu abhiniṣṭā buddhiḥ atra iti asaṃgata artha uttara apavāda doṣam anapekṣyā api pratyekam api etat asādhanam vṛtti viṣaya tvāt sva kāraṇa pariniṣpannāyāḥ hi buddheḥ vyāpāraḥ artha grahaṇa saṃjñakaḥ indriya ādi sannidhāna apekṣaḥ na buddhiḥ tat ananya tvāt prasaṃga nivṛttiḥ iti ced atha matam vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ ananya tvāt ittham api kalpayitvā ayam prasaṃgaḥ na nivartate tathā ca uktam svālakṣaṇyam vṛttiḥ trayasya iti tat api abādhakam kasmāt upacārāt satyam ananyā vṛtti vṛtti matoḥ bhedena agrahaṇāt tathā api uparata vyāpārasya api para śu ādeḥ vṛttimataḥ svarūpa na uparama ti iti bhedam upacarya vyavahāraḥ nānā kārya viṣayaḥ pravartate atas eva anya tvam api syāt iti tat ayuktam ekāntāt 
[II,184,i^3]	tat yathā senā paṅkti senā kuṇḍala ādi uparame na tad sanniveśinām uparamaḥ kārya bhedaḥ ca na ca anya tvam evam vṛtti tadvatoḥ api ca syāt tasmāt yuktam etat hetu apekṣaṇasya vṛtti viṣaya tvāt na buddheḥ anitya tvam iti etena vyakti vikalpaḥ prayuktaḥ saḥ api vṛtti viṣayaḥ iti kṛtvā tat api uktam indriya ādi bhede bhedāt iti tat api anena eva uktam vṛtti bhedaḥ atra na bhedaḥ iti kim ca anekāntāt yathā udaka ādi bhedāt pratibimba bhedaḥ na ca avyaṅgya tvam evam anyatra api syāt dravya antara utpatteḥ adoṣaḥ iti ced syāt matam udakasya ānana saṃyogāt dravya antaram eva pratibimba lakṣaṇam utpadyate na tu mukham bhidyate iti asat etat kasmāt ubhayoḥ kāraṇa tvena kalpanā anupapatteḥ na hi mukhaḥ nimittam śakyam vaktum viprakṛṣṭa tvāt na āsa ādayaḥ mukha apagame api upalabdhi prasaṃgāt pāka ja vat 
[II,184,i^4]	yat punar etat uktam vṛtti bhedāt adoṣaḥ mṛdvat iti tathā tat astu yat tu uktam ananya tvāt dṛṣṭānta asiddheḥ ca iti vṛtti ananya tvam idānīm eva pratyuktam kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiṣedhe ca uktam na pṛthivī ādīnām anyathā ca anyathā ca utpattiḥ yat punar etat uktam na ekam mṛd dravyam iti tatra buddhiḥ pramāṇam yat ekabuddhi nimittam tat ekam tatra yadi mṛdaḥ aneka tvena prayojanam buddhiḥ upalabhyate vayam iti yat punar etat uktam mṛd dravyasya saṃsthāna vyatirekeṇa svabhāvaḥ avadhāryate na tu buddheḥ artha grahaṇam antareṇa svarūpa grahaṇam iti tat ayuktam abhāvasya arūpa tvāt upetya vā yathā bāhya ādi avasthāsu vyākārā citta santatiḥ vidyate bīja mātrā vaḥ tathā dhīḥ iti gṛhyatām 
[II,185,i^1]	yathā bāhya artha ākāra vat citta santatiḥ atha ca supta mūrchita virodha samāpannānām artha rūpāt ṛte bīja mātrā asti iti upagamyate sā citi kā api vā avasthā iti vacanāt na ca gṛhyate tathā buddhiḥ api iti kasmāt na parikalpyate yat punar etat uktam yadi dharma antara upādāna parityāgau vyakta vyaktī datta uttaraḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ iti tat itaratra tulyam asmābhiḥ api tarhi asat kārya pratyākhyāne datta uttaraḥ eṣa pakṣaḥ vyaktitar na kriyate iti nāśa utpādau tu aniṣṭau eva iti na parihāram pratyādaraḥ kriyate yat api uktam naṣṭāt utpannāt ca anaṣṭam anutpannam ca anyat na asti iti tat ayuktam anabhyupagamāt nāśa utpādau kaḥ pratijānīte yam pratyetat arthavat syāt kim ca tvad pakṣa prāpteḥ bhavataḥ eva naṣṭa utpannebhyaḥ skandhebhyaḥ na anyā santatiḥ atha ca na asti doṣaḥ kayā api yuktayā syāt etat anyā eva asau iti tatas ca ekā santatiḥ iti hīnam yat api uktam guṇa vṛddhi kṣaye anitya tvam iti tad anupapannam kasmāt rūpa antara āpyāyanāt 
[II,185,i^2]	sattvam hi prakarṣam anubhavat rajaḥ tamasī ca nyūna tām dharma ādi rūpām buddheḥ āpyāyanti na artha antaram kurvanti no khalu api abhāvam evam rahaḥ tamaḥ vā prakarṣam anubhavat sattvam ca nyūna tā dharma ādi rūpam buddheḥ āpyāyanti na artha antaram kurvanti na abhāvam evam guṇa vṛddhi kṣaye api rūpa antara āpyāyanāt na asti kṣayaḥ buddheḥ tatra yat uktam hetu apekṣaṇāt anityāḥ buddhiḥ iti etat ayuktam yat punar etat uktam pratyakṣa grahaṇa anyatvāt pratikṣaṇam dīpa ādi taila dhārāsu śabda bhedāt ca kṣaṇikā iti atra brūmaḥ grahaṇa anya tve ca uktam vṛtti bhedaḥ na vṛttimat bhedaḥ kim ca anyat bhinna artha grahaṇa eka tvāt upetya vā brūmaḥ yadi pratyartham anyat anyat grahaṇam kalpyate vikalpa bādha samuccaya saṃśaya dvi tva atiśaya nivāraṇeṣu tathā kalmāṣam śabalam citram iti aneka artha rūpam ekam grahaṇam na syāt dṛṣṭam tat tasmāt na ayam kṣaṇika tve hetuḥ evam avasthitam idam adhyavasāyaḥ buddhiḥ na kṣaṇikā iti 
[II,188,i_II,189,iii^1]	buddheḥ tu triguṇa ātmaka tvāt tasya guṇasya prakarṣe tad tad rūpa antaram utpadyate iti āha kasya guṇasya prakarṣe buddheḥ kim lakṣaṇam rūpa antaram upajāyate iti ucyate dharmaḥ jñānam virāga aiśvaryam sāttvikam etat rūpam atra tu etat rūpam iti sati api dharma ādi bhede buddhiḥ iti abheda vivakṣā viṣayaḥ ekavacana nirdeśaḥ kriyate etat uktam bhavati yadā rajaḥ tamasī vaśam āpādya buddhi gatam sattvam utkṛṣṭam bhavati tadā dharmaḥ jñānam virāga aiśvaryam iti etat rūpam bhavati tatra śruti smṛti vihitānām karmaṇām anuṣṭhānāt buddhi avasthaḥ sattva avayavaḥ āśaya bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ iti ucyate sa tu dvividhaḥ brahma ādi sthāneṣu abhipreta śarīra indriya viṣaya upabhoga nirvartakaḥ jñāna ādi aṅga bhūtaḥ ca prathamaḥ agni hotra havana ādi kriyā anuṣṭhāna sādhanaḥ yama niyama sādhanaḥ itaraḥ tatra ahiṃsā satyam asteyam akalka tā brahmacaryam iti pañca yamāḥ akrodhaḥ guru śuśrūṣā śaucam āhāra lāghavam apramādaḥ iti pañca niyamāḥ 
[II,189,iii^2]	eteṣām avilopena anuṣṭhānāt yateḥ evaṃvidha uttaraṇe sattva dharmaḥ āśayatām pratipadyate yaḥ jñāna ādīnām rūpāṇām āpyāyanam karoti etat abhyudaya niḥśreyasayoḥ sopāna bhūtam prathamam parva yatra ayam avasthitaḥ yatiḥ itareṣām parvaṇām anuṣṭhāne yogyaḥ bhavati jñānam dvividham śabda ādi upalabdhi lakṣaṇam guṇa puruṣa antara upalabdhi lakṣaṇam ca tatra śabda ādi upalabdhi lakṣaṇam pratyakṣa anumāna āgama rūpam guṇa puruṣa antara upalabdhi lakṣaṇam ca dvividham apūrvam abhyāsa jam ca tayoḥ apūrvam ūhaḥ śabdaḥ adhyayanam iti siddhi kāṇḍa anupatitāni pramāṇāni abhyāsa jam punar vairāgya pūrva avajaya pṛṣṭha labdham śāntam amalam dhruvam sakala bhava abhava pratipakṣa bhūtam yat ācāryaḥ vakṣyati evam tattva abhyāsāt na asmi na me na aham iti apariśeṣam aviparyayāt viśuddham kevalam utpadyate jñānam iti 
[II,189,iv^1]	virāgaḥ tu rāga pratipakṣa bhūtaḥ jñāna abhyāsa upajanitaḥ buddheḥ prasādaḥ tasya tu yatamāna vyatireka eka indriya vaśīkāra lakṣaṇāḥ catasraḥ avasthāḥ bhavanti tatra indriyāṇām viṣaya abhilāṣa lakṣaṇa kaṣāya pācanam prati yaḥ prayatnaḥ utsāhaḥ sā yatamāna saṃjñā yatamānakaḥ hi ayam asmin parvaṇi avasthitaḥ yatiḥ bhavati yadā tu keṣāṃcid indriyāṇām paripakvam sā vyatireka saṃjñā vyatiricyante hi tadā yateḥ indriyāṇi paripakvāṇi aparipakvebhyaḥ viśiṣṭatarāṇi bhavanti iti arthaḥ viparipakva sarva indriyaḥ tu saṃkalpa mātra avasthita kaṣāyaḥ yadā bhavati tadā eka indriya saṃjñā nivṛtta sarva indriya viṣaya icchasya yateḥ ekam eva manaḥ lakṣaṇam indriyam tadā paripakvam bhavati saṃkalpa mātrā avasthitasya api paripākaḥ vaśīkāra saṃjñā 
[II,189,iv^2]	saṃkalpa mūla ucchinna viṣaya mṛga tṛṣṇaḥ hi ayam yatiḥ indriyāṇām antaḥkaraṇasya ca pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ īṣṭe ekāgre ekarāmaḥ avidyā parvaṇaḥ atikrāntaḥ parasya brahmaṇaḥ pratyanantaraḥ bhavati tat evam catur avastham vairāgyaparva vijñāya tad anuṣṭhānāya yatiḥ prayateta tasya upāyaḥ dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya pratyākhyāne yaḥ upadiṣṭaḥ yaḥ ca tuṣṭiṣu vakṣyamāṇaḥ tam ekīkṛtya uttarottarām tattva bhūmim vijñānasya viṣayīkurvan pūrvasyām tattva bhūmau madhyasthaḥ syāt aiśvaryam apratighāta lakṣaṇam yat punar aṣṭavidham aṇimā mahimā laghimā garimā prāptiḥ prākāmyam īśitvam vaśitvam yatra kāmāvasāyi tvam iti atra aṇimā mahimā laghimā garimā iti bhūta vaiśeṣikam buddheḥ tu prāpti ādi evam etat caturvidham mahataḥ sāttvikam rūpam iti 
[II,192,i_II,192,iii^1]	āha atha guṇa antara rūpam kim ucyate tāmasam asmāt viparyastam etat asmāt dharma ādeḥ sattva rūpa ādi viparyastam tāmasam tamaḥ prakarṣa upajanitam iti arthaḥ atra śāstra codita anuṣṭhānāt āśaya niṣpanna sattva avayavaḥ dharmaḥ iti uktam śāstra coditasya nityasya ca karmaṇaḥ anuṣṭhānāt buddhi avasthaḥ tamaḥ avayavaḥ āśayatām pratipannaḥ adharmaḥ sa ca api dvividhaḥ aniṣṭa śarīra indriya viṣaya upabhoga nirvartakaḥ khyātivārakaḥ ca yathā ca jñānam dvividham śabda ādi upalabdhi lakṣaṇam guṇa puruṣa antara upalabdhi lakṣaṇam ca evam ajñānam api viparyayeṇa vācyam yathā ca catur avastham vairāgyam tathā yatamāna ādikaḥ catur avasthaḥ rāgaḥ yathā ca aṣṭaguṇam aiśvarya maṇima ādi tathā aṣṭaguṇam anaiśvaryam evam etat tāmasam mahataḥ rūpam 
[II,192,iii^2]	yat ca etat adharma ādi nimitta bhūtam utkṛṣṭam tamaḥ rūpam tat rajasā saha avirodhāt ekatām iva āpannam aśuddhiḥ iti ācāryaiḥ paṭhyate sattva rūpam tu prakāśaḥ iti anayoḥ ca abhidhāna āt yaḥ pañca adhikaraṇa pakṣaḥ prākṛta vaikṛtānām jñānānām pradhāna vat śuṣka nadī sthānīya antaḥkaraṇe bāhye ca preraka jñāna aṃśaka kṛtaḥ upanipātaḥ tathā sāttvika sthiti ātmaka kṛtam apratyayasya avasthānam iti tat pratikṣiptam bhavati kim kāraṇam yasmāt aśuddhiḥ eva prakāśa malam atipravṛttam nivartayitum prakarṣa āpanna ani ābhūtā ca pravartayitum iti evam aṣṭa rūpā buddhiḥ vyākhyātā 
[II,196,i_II,196,iv]	yaḥ tu asau anantara muktaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ tam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ āha yadi evam tasmāt idam eva tāvat ucyatām kim asya ahaṅkārasya lakṣaṇam iti ucyate abhimānaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ kartuḥ sva ātma pratyavamarśa ātmakaḥ yaḥ ayam aham iti pratyayaḥ utpadyate sa khalu ahaṃkāraḥ mahataḥ tattva antaram kasmāt tasya sarva viṣaya adhyavasāya rūpa tvāt asya tu sva ātma pratyavamarśāt na tu artha antaram kasmāt prakṛti vikārayoḥ ananya tva abhyupagamāt na hi naḥ prakṛteḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ vikāraḥ iti prāk vistareṇa pratipāditam sa ca mūrti pratyayābhyām mahataḥ sthūlataraḥ kasmāt avibhāgāt vibhāga niṣpatteḥ kāla ādi vat triguṇasya ca mahataḥ vikāra tvāt asau api triguṇaḥ kasmāt prakṛti rūpasya vikāre dṛṣṭa tvāt tantu paṭa vat tad bhāva sanniviṣṭāḥ tu ye sattva ādayasya ācāryaiḥ vaikārika taijasa bhūta ādi śabdena ākhyāyante tathā ca śāstram āha etasmāt hi mahataḥ ātmanaḥ ime trayaḥ ātmānaḥ sṛjyante vaikārika taijasa bhūta ādayaḥ ahaṃkāra lakṣaṇāḥ aham iti eva eṣām sāmānya lakṣaṇam bhavati guṇa pravṛttau ca punar viśeṣa lakṣaṇam iti 
[II,197,i_II,197,iii]	āha kā punar guṇa pravṛttiḥ yasyām asmi pratyaya eka rūpasya ahaṅkārasya viśeṣa pratipattiḥ bhavati iti ucyate yaḥ ayam tasmāt dvividhaḥ pravartate sargaḥ dvividhaḥ indriya lakṣanaḥ tanmātra lakṣaṇaḥ ca sā guṇa vṛttiḥ iti ucyate kasmāt tad kāryatvāt guṇa pravṛtti kāryaḥ hi sargaḥ dṛśyate ca khalu loke kārya kāraṇam upacaryamāṇam tat yathā śālīn bhuṅktaḥ iti 
[II,198,i_II,198,iii]	āha prāk uktam ahaṃkārāt ṣoḍaśakaḥ gaṇaḥ utpadyate idānīm punar ucyate tasmāt dvividhaḥ pravartate sargaḥ tat idam pūrva uttara vyāghātāt ayuktam iti ucyate na sāmānyena vivakṣita tvāt abheda vivakṣāyām hi kṛtvā kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇam evam asmābhiḥ upadiṣṭam dvividhaḥ sargaḥ iti bheda vivakṣāyām punar aindriyaḥ ekādaśakaḥ tān mātraḥ pañcakaḥ ca eva 
[II,198,iv]	indriyāṇām ayam aindriyaḥ ekādaśa parimāṇam asya ekādaśakaḥ evam tanmātreṣu vaktavyam tanmātrāṇām śabda sparśa ādīn ām ayam tān mātraḥ sargaḥ pañcakaḥ ca pañca parimāṇam asya iti pañcakaḥ asya tu ṣoḍaśakasya vikārasya saṃjñā lakṣaṇa prayojanāni uttaratra vakṣyati eṣā guṇa pravṛttiḥ vyākhyātā yasyām asmi pratyayasya viśeṣa grahaṇam bhavati śabde aham sparśe aham rūpe aham rase aham gandhe aham iti 
[II,199,i]	āha ahaṅkāre sattva ādīnām saṃjñā antarā vacanam ānarthakyāt yat idam ahaṃkāre sattva ādīnām saṃjñā antaram ārabhyate vaikārikaḥ taijasaḥ bhūtādiḥ iti tat na vaktavyam kasmāt ānarthakyāt na hi tattva antara sanniveśinām sattva ādīnām saṃjñā antara abhidhāne kiṃcid prayojanam asti iti saṃjñā bhūyaḥ tvāt atha ayam nirbandhaḥ tattva antaram saṃjñā bhūyaḥ tvam prāpnoti prayojana abhidhānam vā viśiṣṭa yatnānām anākasmika tvāt athavā prayojanam vaktavyam evam artham ahaṅkāre saṃjñā antara abhidhānam iti kasmāt na hi viśiṣṭa yatnānām ākasmika tvam upapadyate iti 
[II,199,ii]	ucyate na kārya viśeṣa hetu tvāt mahat ādi lakṣaṇānām hi guṇānām aneka rūpaḥ tattva ārambhaḥ iti hi na saṃjñā antaram ārabhyate ahaṃkāraḥ tu sattva tamaḥ bahulayoḥ indriya tanmātra parvaṇoḥ prakṛtiḥ tad artham ācāryāṇām yatna viśeṣaḥ dharma ādi viśeṣa abhyupāmāt mahati prasaṃgaḥ iti ced na viśeṣita tvāt tattva antara ārambhaḥ iti viśeṣitam na tu dharma ādayaḥ tattva antaram atas na mahati prasaṃgaḥ viśeṣānabhidhānāt ayuktam iti ced syāt etat kaḥ punar atra viśeṣaḥ yena dharma ādi na tattva antaram tattva antaram tu śrotra ādi iti etat ca na evam kutas vṛtti mātre tad upacārāt vṛtti mātre hi mahataḥ dharma ādi upacāraḥ tathā ca tantra antare api uktam prakāśa vṛttiḥ dharmaḥ iti vṛtti niṣpāditaḥ tu saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ vṛttimataḥ tattva antaram iti anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ tasmāt yuktam etat kārya viśeṣa hetu tvam iti 
[II,202,i_II,202,vi]	āha yadi evam idam tarhi vaktavyamuṣya kārya viśeṣasya evam saṃjñakāt ahaṃkārāt pravṛttiḥ iti ucyate sāttvikaḥ ekādaśakaḥ pravartate vaikṛtāt ahaṅkārāt sargaḥ iti anuvartate ekādaśa indriyāṇi sattva bahulāni vaikṛtāt ahaṃkārāt pravartante niṣpadyante iti arthaḥ ekādaśa abhidhānāt eva ca indriya pratītiḥ pūrva sūtre tad sāmāna adhikaraṇyāt atas na punar indriya grahaṇam āha tanmātra sargaḥ punar kiṃguṇaḥ kasmāt ca ahaṅkārāt pravartate iti ucyate bhūtādeḥ tānmātraḥ sa tāmasaḥ bhūtādeḥ bhūta ādi saṃjña kāt tamaḥ pradhānāt tān mātraḥ sargaḥ tān mātraḥ tu tamaḥ bahulaḥ bhūta ādi saṃjñakāt ahaṅkārāt pravartate tatra punar tanmātra grahaṇāt saṃkhyā śasyate iti na ucyate 
[II,203,i]	āha prakṛti viśeṣa nirdeśa ānarthakyam prāk uktam sattva ādīnām ahaṅkāra avasthitānām vaikārika ādyāḥ saṃjñāḥ ucyante tat yadi sattvam vaikārika śabdena ucyate vaikārikāṇi ca aindriyaḥ ekādaśakaḥ sargaḥ pravartate iti ukte gamyate etat sāttvikaḥ asau bhūtādeḥ tān mātraḥ iti ukte gamyate etat tāmasaḥ iti kasmāt na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat sattvāt tamaḥ bahulaḥ sargaḥ syāt tamasaḥ ca sattva bahulaḥ iti 
[II,203,ii_II,204,i]	ucyate na aprasiddha tva jñāpanāt yasya eva arthasya jñāpana artham evam iha kriyate katham gamyate sattvam vaikārika śabdena ucyate tamaḥ bhūta ādi śabdena rajaḥ taijasa śabdena aprasiddha arthā hi tāntrikī paribhāṣā iyam anirṇītā na gamyate iti āha taijasa saṃjñā narthakyam iti ucyate na taijasāt ubhayam 
[II,204,ii^1]	ubhayatra tad sāmarthyāt syāt etat evam yat yasya kārya sāmarthyam eva na syāt asmāt tu taijasāt ubhayam api etat tanmātra indriya saṃjñakam pravartate iti anuvartate katham yadā hi vaikārikaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ indriya bhāvena pravartate tadā niṣkriya tvāt taijasam pravartaka tvena akāṃkṣati bhūta ādi bhedaka tvena kasmāt tena eva tad bhedāt tat yathā agninā agnau prakṣiptaḥ agniḥ eva bhavati āpaḥ vā apsu prakṣiptāḥ āpaḥ eva bhavanti evam sattvam eva sattve tu bhedam janayati guṇa antara saṃsargam apekṣate 
[II,204,ii^2]	bhūta ādi lakṣaṇasya tu tamasaḥ saṃsargāt bhidyamānam taijasena ca rajasā kriyā ātmakena anugṛhītam ekādaśa indriya bhāvam apekṣate tathā bhūta ādi lakṣaṇam tamaḥ ahaṅkārāt tanmātra bhāvena pravartamānam pravṛtti artham taijasamākāṃkṣati vaikārikam bheda tvena kasmāt tena eva tasya bhedāt iti yojyam śāsram ca evam āha tat etasmin vaikārike strakṣyamāṇaḥ eṣa bhūtādiḥ taijasena upaṣṭabdhaḥ evam vaikārikam abhidhāvati tathā eva tasmin bhūta ādau srakṣyamāṇe eṣa bhūtādiḥ taijasena uṣṭabdhaḥ etam bhūta ādim abhibhavati iti anena nyāyena taijasāt ubhaya niṣpattiḥ iti vyākhyātaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ 
[II,207,i_II,207,iii]	āha prāk apadiṣṭaḥ aindriyaḥ ekādaśakaḥ pravartate vaikṛtāt ahaṃkārāt iti tad sāmānya abhidhānāt na pratipadyāmahe tasmāt vaktavyam kāni indriyāṇi bhavataḥ abhipretāni ucyate dvividhāni indriyāṇi buddhīndriyāṇi karmendriyāṇi ca tatra buddhīndriyāṇi karṇa tvac cakṣū rasana nāsikā ākhyāni karṇau tvac cakṣuṣī ca rasanam ca nāsikā ca karṇa tvac cakṣū rasana nāsikāḥ ākhyānam ākhyā pratyāyanam iti arthaḥ etaiḥ śabdaiḥ ākhyāḥ yeṣām tāni imāni karṇa tvac cakṣū rasana nāsikā ākhyāni adhiṣṭhāna bhedāt dvi vacanena vigrahaḥ kriyate etāni buddhīndriyāṇi pratyavagantavyāni buddheḥ indriyāṇi buddhīndriyāṇi 
[II,207,iv_II,208,i]	kim punar etāni buddheḥ iti ucyate śabda ādi viṣaya pratipattau dvāram kasmāt abahis vṛtti tvāt antaḥkaraṇasya na asti bahis vṛttiḥ iti atas na alam etat sākṣāt śabda ādīn arthān pratipattum tasmāt śrotra ādi lakṣaṇam sākṣāt bāhya viṣaya prakāśana samartham kāraṇa antaram apekṣate tad praṇālikayā tasya viṣaya grahaṇam tasmāt yuktam uktam buddheḥ bāhya viṣaya pratipattau dvāra bhūta tvāt buddhīndriyāṇi iti 
[II,208,ii_II,208,iii]	āha karmendriyāṇi punar kāni iti vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāḥ karmendriyāṇi āhuḥ vāc ca pāṇī ca pādau pāyuḥ ca upasthaḥ ca vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāḥ etāni karmendriyāṇi āhuḥ ācakṣate karma arthāni indriyāṇi karmendriyāṇi kim punar karma vacana ādi vakṣyamāṇam etat vikurvat iti karmendriyāṇi 
[II,208,iv_II,209,ii]	āha katham etat upalabhyate adhiṣṭhānāt artha antara bhūtāni indriyāṇi na punar adhiṣṭhāna mātram iti ucyate adhiṣṭhānāt indriya pṛthaktvam śakti viśeṣa upalambhāt yathā śarīra asambhavinaḥ viṣaya vyavasāya lakṣaṇasya śakti viśeṣasya upalambhāt artha antaram buddhiḥ anumīyate evam adhiṣṭhāna asambhavinaḥ viṣaya grahaṇa lakṣaṇasya śakti viśeṣasya upalambhāt artha antaram indriyam iti āha na asambhava asiddheḥ adhiṣṭhāna mātrasya viṣaya grahaṇam na sambhavati artha antarasya ca sambhavati iti etat ubhayam api ca aprasiddham iti 
[II,209,iii_II,210,i]	ucyate na etat aprasiddham tulya jātīyeṣu tad anupapatteḥ yasmāt bhautikeṣu anyeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu viṣaya grahaṇa sāmarthyā sambhavaḥ āhaṃkāra vikāra vat tad sāmarthya apratiṣedhāt na indriyāṇām naḥ tad pratiṣedhaḥ anumātavyaḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt śakti bheda āpatteḥ vaikārikam sattvam āhaṅkārikam prakāśa rūpam tad śakti viśeṣāt indriyāṇi utpadyante bhūta ādi lakṣaṇasya tamasaḥ sāmarthyāt tanmātrāṇi parasya pṛthivī ādīnām eka rūpa tvāt tasmāt ayam asamaḥ samādhiḥ iti etena bhautika tvam pratyuktam āha katham avagamyate bahūni indriyāṇi na punar ekam eva indriyam manaḥ vat sarva artham aneka adhiṣṭhānam syāt iti 
[II,210,ii^1]	ucyate na yugapad pravṛtti apravṛtti prasaṃgāt yadi ekam eva indriyam manaḥ vat sarva artham aneka adhiṣṭhānam syāt eka viṣaya pratipattau vā sarva viṣaya pratipattiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tu grahaṇa bhedaḥ tasmāt na ekam indriyam iti bhautikaiḥ anugraha upaghāta darśanāt indriyāṇām bhautika tvam iti ced syāt matam iha bhautikānām ghaṭa ādīnām bhautikaiḥ mṛd daṇḍa cakra sūtra udaka mudgara ādibhiḥ anugraha upaghātaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yadi ca bhautikāni indriyāṇi na syuḥ na eṣām bhautikaiḥ añjana ādibhiḥ anugrahaḥ kriyate upaghātaḥ ca rajaḥ prabhṛtibhiḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt anekāntāt tat yathā bhautikaiḥ vadana ādibhiḥ antaḥkaraṇasya grahaṇa dhāraṇa smṛti lakṣaṇaḥ anugrahaḥ kriyate upaghātaḥ ca upala ādibhiḥ 
[II,210,ii^2]	na ca asya bhautika tvam evam indriyasya api syāt vaiśeṣika guṇa vyañjaka tvāt vikāra pratītiḥ iti ced atha matam pṛthivī ādi vaiśeṣikaḥ gandhaḥ ghrāṇena abhivyajyate audakaḥ rase rasanena ca āgneyam rūpam vīkṣaṇena vāyavīyaḥ sparśaḥ tvacā ākāśīyaḥ śabdaḥ śrotreṇa yena ca yasya vaiśeṣika guṇa abhivyaktiḥ tasya tat vikāra tvam dṛṣṭam tat yathā pradīpasya rūpa abhivyañjaka tve sati taijasa tvam iti etat ca anupapannam kasmāt aniṣṭa prasaṃgāt vaiśeṣika guṇa vyañjakānām tad vikāram icchataḥ prāptam apām gandha abhivyakti hetu tvāt pārthivat tvam atha etat aniṣṭam na tarhi aikāntikaḥ hetuḥ iti tatra yat uktam vaiśeṣika guṇa abhivyañjaka tvāt bhautikāni indriyāṇi iti etat ayuktam 
[II,213,i_II,213,iii]	āha ekādaśa indriyāṇi ahaṅkārāt utpadyante iti prāc apadiṣṭam idānīm buddhīndriya karmendriyāṇi daśa apadiśyante tat idam padārtha nyūnam iti ucyate syāt etat evam yadi etāvat indriya parva syāt kim tarhi iti saṅkalpakam atra manaḥ atra indriya parvaṇi manaḥ bhavadbhiḥ pratyavagantavyam tatra saṃkalpakam iti lakṣaṇam ācakṣmahe saṃkalpaḥ abhilāṣaḥ icchā tṛṣṇā ityādi anarthāntaram saṃkalpayati iti saṃkalpakam etat manasaḥ lakṣaṇam 
[II,213,iv]	tasmāt asya pratyakṣataḥ anupalabhyamānasya astitvam avasīyate kasmāt vyasta samastānām indriya antarāṇām tad asambhavāt apohya hi manaḥ saṃkalpam vyastānām indriya antarāṇām bhavān parikalpayet samastānām vā kim ca atas tat na tāvat vyasthānām indriyāṇām saṃkalpaḥ bhavati kim kāraṇam aniyata viṣaya tvāt niyataḥ hi śrotra ādīnām śabda ādiḥ viṣayaḥ aniyata viṣayaḥ ca saṃkalpaḥ kiṃca tri kāla viṣaya tvāt vartamāna viṣayā śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ tri kāla viṣayaḥ ca saṃkalpaḥ tasmāt na vyastānām na api samastānām badhira ādiṣu tad abhāva prasaṃgāt yadi samasta indriya vṛttiḥ saṃkalpaḥ syāt prāṇa ādi vat iti ced syāt matam yathā samasta indriya vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādiḥ na ca anyatara vaikalye tad abhāvaḥ evam samasta indriya vṛttiḥ saṃkalpaḥ syāt na ca anyatara vaikalye tad abhāvaḥ syāt iti etat ca anupapannam viśeṣita tvāt nirviṣayā prāṇa ādi vṛttiḥ śabda ādi viṣayaḥ tu saṃkalpaḥ iti viśeṣitam tasmāt vyasta samastānām indriyāṇām saṃkalpa anupapatteḥ manasaḥ liṅgam etat astitve iti siddham 
[II,214,i_II,215,ii]	āha tat avadhāraṇīyam indriya dvaividhyāt dvi prakārāṇi hi indriyāṇi purastāt upadiṣṭāni tatra manaḥ api avadhāraṇīyam kim buddhīndriyam atha karmendriyam iti ucyate tat ca indriyam ubhayathā samākhyātam hi arthe caḥ paṭhitaḥ tat hīndriyam ubhayathā iti arthaḥ manaḥ na kevalam buddhīndriyam api tu karmendriyam api 
[II,215,iii_II,215,v]	niyama hetu abhāvāt ayuktam iti ced syāt punar etat kaḥ atra niyama hetuḥ yat indriya tva aviśeṣe manasaḥ eva ubhaya pracāra tvam abhyupagamyate na anyeṣām iti ucyate antar tri kāla viṣayam tasmāt ubhaya pracāram tat tri kāla viṣaya tvāt iha yasya antar triṣu ca kāleṣu karaṇasya vṛttiḥ tad ubhaya pracāram tat yathā buddhiḥ sākṣāt viṣayān abhisandhānāt atīta anāgata vartamāna viṣaya tvāt ca manaḥ antar trikāla viṣayam tasmāt ubhaya pracāram tat iti siddham 
[II,218,i]	samadhigatam karaṇa parva tasya idānīm vyasta samasta vṛttayaḥ vaktavyāḥ sati ca ubhaya abhidhāne vyasta vṛttiḥ eva tāvat ucyate na samasta vṛttiḥ kim kāraṇam prakaraṇa śeṣa bhūta tvāt śrotra ādīnām hi sadbhāva prakaraṇam idam anukrāntam sa ca eṣām sadbhāvaḥ śakti viśeṣa upālambhāt iti uktam idānīm asau śakti viśeṣaḥ asmākam vyasta vṛttiḥ iti ucyate tasmāt tat anukramaṇam kariṣyāmaḥ 
[II,218,ii_II,218,iv]	āha yadi evam tasmāt ucyatām tasya karaṇasya kasmin arthe vṛttiḥ kim lakṣaṇam vā iti ucyate yat uktam tasya kasmin arthe vṛttiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ rūpa ādiṣu pañcānām ālocana mātram iṣyate vṛttiḥ rūpa ādiṣu śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandheṣu sva bheda bhinneṣu pañcānām śrotra tvac cakṣuḥ jihvā ghrāṇānām śravaṇa sparśana darśana rasana ghrāṇa lakṣaṇaḥ vyāpāraḥ vṛttiḥ iti ucyate tatra karaṇa nirdeśe śrotra indriyasya prāc pāṭhāt tad viṣaya nirdeśa ati laṃghane prayojanam na asti iti kṛtvā śabda ādiṣu pañcānām iti eva paṭhitavyam prāktanaḥ tu pramāda pāṭhaḥ 
[II,219,i_II,219,ii]	yat punar etat uktam kiṃlakṣaṇa iti atra brūmaḥ ālocana mātram iṣyate ālocanam grahaṇam iti anarthāntaram mātra śabdaḥ viśeṣa nivṛtti arthaḥ tat yathā bhaikṣa mātram asmin grāme labhyate iti ukte na anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti jñāyate chandraḥ mātram adhīte māṇavakaḥ iti ukte na anyat adhītaḥ iti evam ālocana mātram indriyāṇām iṣyate vṛttiḥ iti ukte na anyaḥ viśeṣaḥ iti gamyate tena kim siddham bhavati yat uktam anyaiḥ ācāryaiḥ sāmānya jñānam indriyāṇām viśeṣa jñānam buddheḥ iti tat pratiṣiddham bhavati āha kaḥ punar asmin darśane doṣaḥ yatas etat pratiṣidyate iti 
[II,219,iii_II,221,i]	ucyate sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ itaretara apekṣa tve sati ekasmin avirodhāt anyatara parikalpanā narthakyam yadi khalu indriyasya sāmānya jñānam na syāt tena viśeṣa apekṣam sāmānyam sāmānya apekṣaḥ ca viśeṣaḥ iti yatra sāmānya jñānam tatra viśeṣa jñānam api na pratiṣidhyate iti ubhayam api indriyasya syāt tatas ca antaḥkaraṇa parikalpanā narthakyam viśeṣavataḥ vā antaḥkaraṇasya kaḥ sāmānyena virodhaḥ iti ubhayasya api tatra sambhavāt indriya ānarthakyam tasmāt apratyayam indriyam iti indriyasya ced pratyayaḥ syāt yathā pratyayavataḥ antaḥkaraṇasya aniyata viṣaya tvam evam asya api syāt na tu tat asti tasmāt apratyayam indriyam iti kiṃca kāla ativṛtti prasaṃgāt indriyasya ced pratyayaḥ syāt yathā pratyayavataḥ antaḥkaraṇasya tri kāla viṣaya tvam evam asya api syāt na tu tat asti tasmāt apratyayam indriyam iti kim ca anyat smṛtyadarśanāt indriyasya ced pratyayaḥ syāt yathā pratyayavataḥ antaḥkaraṇasya ādi rūpa upapattiḥ evam atra api syāt na tu tat asti tasmāt apratyayam indriyam siddham iti āha bhavatu tāvat apratyayam indriyam tat tu grahaṇa rūpam na tu prakāśakam pradīpa vat iti atra kaḥ hetuḥ iti 
[II,221,ii]	ucyate na kāraṇa antara prasaṃgāt yadi pradīpa vat indriyam prakāśakam syāt tena yathā tad prakāśiteṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu artheṣu karaṇa antara mārgaṇam evam atra api syāt na ca etat iṣṭam atas na pradīpa vat indriyam prakāśakam iti antaḥkaraṇa sadbhāvāt ayuktam iti ced syāt matam asti kāraṇa antaram buddhi lakṣaṇam yat indriyeṇa pradīpa vat prakāśitam artham gṛhṇāti tasmāt para vāda anuvādaḥ ayam kriyate na pratiṣedhaḥ iti tat ca na evam kasmāt pradīpa indriyayoḥ anyatara anupādāna prasaṃgāt indriyam api prakāśakam pradīpaḥ api tatra anyatarasya anupādānam prasaktam kasmāt na hi eka artha kāriṇaḥ yugapad karaṇe sāmarthyam asti iti kim ca anyat antaḥkaraṇa hāneḥ indriyeṇa pradīpa vat prakāśitān bāhyān arthān sākṣāt antaḥkaraṇam gṛhṇāti iti vadataḥ antaḥkaraṇam eva hīyate tasmāt ayuktam antaḥkaraṇasya sāmarthyam puruṣasya iti ced na karaṇa anarthakya prasaṃgāt sākṣāt viṣaya grahaṇa samartham puruṣam icchataḥ karaṇa ānarthakyam prasajyate tasmāt yuktam etat grāhakam indriyam na tu pradīpa vat prakāśakam iti 
[II,222,i_II,222,ii]	āha bhavatu tāvat grahaṇa mātram indriya vṛttiḥ apratyayā grahaṇa pratyaya prakāśa abhedaḥ ucyate viṣaya samparkāt tāt rūpya āpattiḥ indriya vṛtti grahaṇam tathā viṣaya indriya vṛtti anukāreṇa niścayaḥ gauḥ ayam śuklaḥ dhāvati iti evamādiḥ pratyayaḥ tathā viṣaya samparka āgame śrotra ādi vṛtteḥ tādrūpya āgamaḥ vartamāna kāla tā grahaṇasya anubhavāt tu saṃskāra ādhānam tad pūrvikā ca smṛtiḥ iti tri kāla viṣayā pratyayasya iti ayam anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ bāhyaḥ tu prakāśaḥ na viṣaya rūpa āpannaḥ saṃskārāt tu ghaṭa ādīnām vyavadhāna rūpam pārthivam chāyā lakṣaṇam vyañjaka tvāya kalpate cakṣuṣaḥ anugrahāya ubhayoḥ vā cakṣuḥ viṣayayoḥ iti apare tasmāt upapannam etat prakāśakam pradīpa ādi grāhakam śrotra ādi vyavasāyakam antaḥkaraṇam iti 
[II,223,i^1]	atha karmendriyāṇām kā vṛttiḥ iti ucyate naiyāyikāḥ tu evam āhuḥ ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvakcśrotrāṇi indriyāṇi bhūtebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ iti anena sva viṣaya upalabdhi lakṣaṇam hi indriyāṇām bhūta prakṛti tve sati nirvahati na anyathā tāni punar indriya kāraṇāni pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vāyuḥ ākāśam iti bhūtāni ebhyaḥ pañcabhyaḥ yathāsaṃkhyam ghrāṇa rasana cakṣuḥ tvakcśrotrāṇi pañca indriyāṇi bhavanti bhūta prakṛti tvam iti bhūta svabhāvam vyākhyāyamānam pañcasu api sambhavati bhūta kāraṇa tvam tu anyeṣu caturṣu tathā eva śrotre tu kathaṃcid karṇa śaṣkulī avacchinna nabhaḥ bhāga abhiprāyeṇa vyavahārataḥ samarthanīyam 
[II,223,i^2_II,224,ii]	evam bhautikāni indriyāṇi sva sva viṣayam adhigantum utsahante iti tad lakṣaṇa tvam eṣām sidhyati iti atas bhūtebhyaḥ iti uktam etat tu sāṃkhya ācāryāṇām na iṣṭam evam hi sāṃkhya vṛddhāḥ āhuḥ āhaṅkārikāṇi indriyāṇi artham sādhayitum arhanti na anyathā tathā hi kārakam kāraka tvāt eva prāpya kāri bhavati bhautikāni ca indriyāṇi katham prāpya kārīṇi duravartini viṣaye bhaveyuḥ āhaṃkārikāṇām tu teṣām vyāpaka tvāt viṣaya ākāra pariṇāma ātmikā vṛttiḥ vṛttimataḥ ananyā satī sambhavati eva iti su vacam prāpya kāri tvam api ca mahat aṇu guṇa grahaṇamāhaṅkāri tve teṣām kalpate na bhautika tve bhautika tve hi yat parimāṇam karaṇam tat parimāṇam grāhyam gṛhṇīyāt āha atha karmendriyāṇām kā vṛttiḥ iti ucyate vacana ādāna viharaṇa utsarga ānandāḥ ca pañcānām 
[II,224,iii]	vāc pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthānām tu vacana ādāna viharaṇa utsarga ānanda lakṣaṇāḥ yathākramam vṛttayaḥ pratyavagantavyāḥ tatra ucyate anena iti vacanam tasmāt yaḥ eva artha pratyāyana samarthaḥ varṇa samudāyaḥ pada vākyaśloka grantha lakṣaṇaḥ sa vāc indriyasya arthaḥ na anyaḥ ādīyate anena iti ādānam āṅabhividhi arthe prayujyate tatas ca yat eva prakṣālana parimārjana upasparśana adhyayana praharaṇa śilpa vyāyāma ādi kṛtsnam grahaṇam saḥ indriya arthāḥ na anyaḥ viśiṣṭam haraṇam viharaṇam atas ca yat eva sama viṣama nimna unnata caṅkramaṇa parivartana nāṭya vyāyāma ādiḥ saḥ indriya arthaḥ na anyaḥ evam utkṛṣṭaḥ sargaḥ utsargaḥ na anyaḥ atas ca yaḥ eva aśita pīta vipariṇāmasya samyak stra utaḥ mārga anusāriṇaḥ visargaḥ saḥ indriya arthaḥ na anyaḥ evam abhivyāpya ānandam ānandaḥ tatas ca yaḥ eva asādhāraṇa prīti nayana abhiniṣpatti lakṣaṇaḥ saḥ indriya arthaḥ na anyaḥ 
[II,227,i_II,227,ii]	āha prāc antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti nirdeśaḥ sarga krama anugamāt pūrvam buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām vṛtti nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ kim kāraṇam evam hi sarga kramaḥ anugataḥ bhavati krama bhede vā prayojanam vaktavyam iti ucyate na indriya vṛtti pūrvaka tvāt antaḥkaraṇasya hi indriya vṛtti pravartakaḥ pratyayaḥ tathā ca vakṣyati dṛṣṭe tathā api adṛṣṭe trayasya tad pūrvikā vṛttiḥ iti tasmāt sarga krameṇa vinā tat nirdeśaḥ prāc ācāryeṇa kriyate iti 
[II,227,iii]	āha tad asambhavaḥ śāstre prāc abhimāna abhidhānāt śāstram hi evam āha kā nu bhoḥ saṃjñā mātuḥ udare avasthitam kumāram pratyabhinirviśate iti asmi iti eṣā māhātmī saṃvid iti tathā kārya kāraṇa vyūha sama kālam māhātmya śarīraḥ asmi iti pratibuddhyate pravṛttāḥ ca eva hi avyaktāḥ bhavanti asmi iti asmitā mātrāḥ pramāṇam ca śāstram tasmāt prāc antaḥkaraṇa nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ 
[II,228,i_II,228,ii]	ucyate tad nimitta arthena vivakṣita tvāt satyam etat kārya kāraṇa vyūha niṣpatti sama kālam asmi iti eṣā māhātmī saṃvid pratyupadhīyate śabda ādi viṣayaḥ tu antaḥkaraṇa pratyayaḥ śrotra ādi nimittaḥ iti etat pūrva śabdena vivakṣitam na ca nimittam atikramya naimittika abhidhānam nyāyyam athavā na eva vayam idam praṣṭavyāḥ yathā prāc antaḥkaraṇa vṛtti nirdeśaḥ kartavyaḥ iti kim kāraṇam yasmāt svālakṣaṇyam vṛttiḥ trayasya
[II,228,iii]	sva lakṣaṇam eva svālakṣaṇyam sva arthe tad hita vṛttiḥ anya bhāvaḥ tu kāla śabda vyavāyāt iti yathā buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām hi saukṣmyāt na śakyam svarūpam abhidhātum iti atas vṛttiḥ eva lakṣaṇa bhāvena upadiśyate śrotra ādīnām api ca saukṣmyāt lakṣaṇam apadeṣṭum aśakyam iti vṛttiḥ eva ucyate na lakṣaṇam tat eva ca eṣā lakṣaṇam bhavati yat śabda ālocana samartham tat śrotram evam itareṣu api vaktavyam buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām ca lakṣaṇa madhyavasāya ādi uktam tat eva vṛtti tvena ācakṣāṇaḥ śrotra ādīnām eva ca abhidadhānam lakṣaṇam ca api ācakṣāṇaḥ vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ ananya tvam jñāpayati anyathā tu yathā adhyavasāya ādi lakṣaṇam evam rūpa ādiṣu pañcānām alocana mātram lakṣaṇam iti ucyate na tu vṛttiḥ iti śrotra ādi vat buddhi ādīnām api vyavasāya ādayaḥ vṛttiḥ iti ucyate na tu lakṣaṇam tasmāt anyathā nirdeśaḥ jñāpakam vṛtti vṛttim atoḥ anyatvasya iti vyākhyātā karaṇa vṛttiḥ 
[II,229,i_II,229,ii]	sā eṣā bhavati asāmānyā sā iti pūrva kṛtām vṛttim abhisambadhnāti eṣā iti sarva nāmnā pratyākṛṣṭām tām eva pratyakṣam prati nirdiśati bhavati iti vakṣyamāṇena dharma antareṇa āsyāḥ tadvat ta anubhāvitam khyāpayati asāmānya iti dharmam ācaṣṭe sāmānyā sādhāraṇā iti arthaḥ na sāmānyā sāmānyā pratikaraṇam niyata iti uktam bhavati yā hi iyam anukrāntā karaṇa parvaṇaḥ adhyavasaya ādikā vṛttiḥ iyam vyastānām karaṇānām pratisvam niyatā tatas ca eṣām buddhi ādīnām kārya viśeṣa nimitta bhāva saṃsūcitasya svarūpasya asaṃkaraḥ siddhaḥ 
[II,230,i_II,230,iii]	āha sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ itaretara apekṣa tvāt asāmānya abhidhānena sāmānyasya api abhidhānāt adhyavasāya ādikā karaṇānām asāmānyā vṛttiḥ iti ukte arthāt āpannam eṣām sāmānyā api vṛttiḥ asti iti tasmāt asau api vaktavyā iti ucyate sāmānya karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca sāmānyā ca asau karaṇa vṛttiḥ sāmānya karaṇa vṛttiḥ prāṇaḥ ca ādyaḥ yeṣām te prāṇa ādyāḥ prāṇa apāna samāna udāna vyānāḥ pañca samasta karaṇa vṛttiḥ pratyavagantavyā iti taiḥ sarvaiḥ sahitaḥ prāṇaḥ iti vedānteṣu api 
[II,231,i_II,231,iii]	āha ayuktam etat kasmāt dharmiṇaḥ dharmi antara vṛtti bhāva anupapatteḥ vṛttiḥ iti ayam śabdaḥ vyāpāram ācaṣṭe na ca dharma antaram dharma antarasya vyāpāraḥ bhavitum arhati iti ucyate na kārye kāraṇa upacārāt satyam etat dharmī dharmi antarasya vṛtti tvena aśakyaḥ parikalpayitum kim tu sāmānya karaṇa vṛttyā preryamāṇaḥ vāyuḥ tad pravaṇa tvāt tat kāryatām pratipadyate tatra prāṇa ādi kārye vāyau prāṇa upacāram kṛtvā evam ucyate prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca tad preraṇā siddheḥ ayuktam iti ced syāt etat katham etat avagamyate artha antara preritasya vāyoḥ iyam kriyā bhavati na punar svatantrasya iti 
[II,231,iv]	ucyate na svatas tad vyatirikta tva anupapatteḥ iha iyam akasmāt bhinnā kriyāvāyoḥ svatas vā syāt karaṇa vṛtti vyatirikta tvāt vā kim ca atas tatra tāvat svatas upapadyate kasmāt sarvatra prasaṃgāt svābhāvike hi vāyoḥ diś saṃcāre abhyupagamyamāne sarvatra tad saṃbhavaḥ syāt tatas ca tiryak pāta ādi vṛttiḥ hanyeta na ca anyatas kasmāt adarśanāt na hi pṛthivī ādīnām vāyu preraṇa sāmarthyam kvacid upalabdham bhastrā ādiṣu dṛṣṭam iti ced na anya nimitta tvāt atra api caitra vyāpāraḥ upalabhyate iti avaśyam anyat nimittam upalabhyate iti abhyupagantavyam ātmā iti ced na kriyā pratiṣedhāt upapāditam etat pūrvam ātmā niṣkriyaḥ iti na ca niṣkriyasya preraṇam upapadyate na ca nirnimittā svabhāva bhedānām anākasmika tvāt tasmāt yat tad nimittam sā samasta karaṇa vṛttiḥ 
[II,232,i_II,233,i]	sa ca ayam vāyuḥ ekaḥ eva sthāna saṃcāra viśeṣāt nānā ākhyaḥ bhavati yathā ekaḥ devadattaḥ pācakaḥ lāvakaḥ iti kvacid tat ayuktam kasmāt yugapad paraspara atiśaya virodhāt pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt uttaraḥ uttaraḥ vāyuḥ balīyān iti hi abhyupagamaḥ tat etat ekasya ekasmin kāle na upapadyate tasmāt upapannam prāṇa ādyāḥ vāyavaḥ pañca kim punar eṣām prāṇa ādīnām lakṣaṇam iti 
[II,233,ii]	ucyate dvividhāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ antar vṛttayaḥ bahis vṛttayaḥ ca tatra mukha nāsikābhyām pragamanāt praṇateḥ ca prāṇaḥ yaḥ ayam mukha nāsikābhyām sañcarati saḥ antar vṛttiḥ vāyuḥ prāṇaḥ iti abhidhīyate yā kācid praṇatiḥ nāma bhūteṣu tat yathā praṇatā iyam senā praṇataḥ ayam vṛkṣaḥ praṇataḥ ayam dharme praṇataḥ ayam arthe praṇataḥ ayam kāme praṇataḥ ayam vidyāyām tad viparīteṣu vā bāhya prāṇa vṛttiḥ eṣā prāṇi viṣayaḥ eva eṣā bhavati sa khalu ayam atra abhivyaktaḥ bhavati tat yathā mahatā vā duḥkhena abhiplutasya mahatā vā bandhunā viyuktasya sahitasya vā saurabheyasya nipāna avatīrṇasya vā mahiṣasya avagateḥ 
[II,233,iii]	apakramaṇāt ca āpānaḥ yaḥ ayam rasam dhātūn śukram mūtram purīṣam vāta ārtava garbhān ca ākarṣan adhas gacchan ayam antar vṛttiḥ vāyuḥ apānaḥ iti abhidhīyate yat ca api kiṃcid apakramaṇam nāma bhūteṣu tat yathā apakrāntaḥ ayam dharma ādibhyaḥ tad viparītebhyaḥ vā iti bāhyā khalva pāna vṛttiḥ eṣā apāna viṣayaḥ eva eṣa bhavati balavattaraḥ ca ayam prāṇa udvāyoḥ kasmāt eṣā hi etam prāṇam ūrdhvam vartamānam arvāk eva san iyacchati arvāk eva sat niruṇaddhi eṣaḥ atra abhivyaktaḥ bhavati tat yathā upakūpam upaśvabhram vā parivartamānasya a śatapadīm laṅghayataḥ 
[II,234,i]	hṛdi avasthānāt saha bhāvāt ca samānaḥ yaḥ tu ayam prāṇa apānayoḥ madhye hṛdi avatiṣṭhate sa samānaḥ vāyuḥ antar vṛttiḥ yaḥ ca api kaścid saha bhāvaḥ nāma bhūteṣu dvandva ārāma tā tat yathā saha dāsye saha yakṣye saha tapaḥ cariṣyāmi saha bhāryā putraiḥ bandhubhiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ ca vartiṣya bāhyā samāna vṛttiḥ eṣā samāna viṣayaḥ eva eṣa bhavati iti balavattaraḥ khalu ayam prāṇa apānābhyām eṣa hi etau prāṇa apānau ūrdhvam arvāk ca vartamānau madhye eva san iyacchati madhye eva sat niruṇaddhi sa ca eṣau atra abhivyaktaḥ bhavati tat yathā srutasārasya vā sārameyasya anaḍuhaḥ voḍha bhārasya dharma abhitaptāyāḥ vai eḍakāyāḥ ardha ardha kāyam śakaśaka iti prāṇānte sarva prāṇinām prāṇa apānau utsṛjya ūrdhvam adhas ca mukta yoktrau hayau iva viṣamam saṃcārayan śarīram sa parāsyati 
[II,235,i]	mūrdha ārohaṇa dātma utkarṣaṇāt ca udānaḥ yaḥ tu ayam prāṇa apāna samānānām sthānāni atikramya rasam dhātūn ca ādāya mūrdhānam ārohati tatas ca pratihataḥ nivṛttaḥ sthāna karaṇa anupradāna viśeṣāt varṇa pada vākya śloka grantha lakṣaṇasya śabdasya abhivyakti nimittam bhavati ayam antar vṛttiḥ vāyuḥ udānaḥ iti ucyate yaḥ ca api kaścid ātma utkarṣaḥ nāma bhūteṣu tat yathā hīnāt asmi śreyān sadṛśena vā sadṛśaḥ sadṛśāt asmi śreyān śreyasā vā sadṛśaḥ śreyasaḥ vā śreyān etasmin tathā rūpa abhimānaḥ vā prāpta vidyaḥ tu tat yathā bahu antara viśeṣāt alpa antara viśeṣaḥ asmi aguṇavataḥ vā guṇavān asmi iti bāhya udāna vṛttiḥ eṣā udāna viṣayaḥ eva eṣa bhavati balavattaraḥ khalu ayam pūrvabhyaḥ katham eṣa hi etān prāṇa ādīn ūrdhvam avāk madhye ca vartamānān ūrdhvam eva unnayati ūrdhvam eva utkarṣati sa ca eṣaḥ atra abhivyaktaḥ bhavati śīta udakena vā paryukṣitasya prāsamasim vikośam ca udyatam abhipaśyataḥ 
[II,235,ii]	śarīra vyāpteḥ atyanta avinā bhāvāt ca vyānaḥ yaḥ tu ayam āloma nakhāt śarīram vyāpya rasa ādīnām dhātūnām pṛthivī ādinām vyūham marmaṇām ca praspandanam prāṇa ādīnām ca sthitim karoti saḥ antar vṛttiḥ vyānaḥ yaḥ ca api kaścid atyantauvinābhāvaḥ nāma bhūteṣu tat yathā pativratā bhartāram mṛtam api anugacchati bhava antare api ayam eva bhartā syāt tathā dharma ādibhiḥ tad viparītaiḥ ca iti bāhyaḥ vyāna viṣayaḥ eva eṣa prabhavati balavattamaḥ ca ayam sarvebhyaḥ katham anena hi vyāpte śarīra daṇḍake tad vaśīkṛtānām prāṇa ādīnām samā sthitiḥ bhavati saḥ eṣaḥ anta kāle prāṇabhṛta ām avinā abhāvena vartamānaḥ abhivyajyate tat yathā hā tarhi pādau haimau śītībhūtau gulphe jaṅghe urū kaṭiḥ udaram uraḥ kaṇṭhe asya khuraghuraḥ vartate hū iti avaiṣaḥ bāhyaḥ vyānaḥ iti evam ete prāṇa ādyāḥ sthāna kārya viśeṣa sūcitāḥ pañca vāyavaḥ vyākhyātāḥ teṣām prerikā sāmānya karaṇa vṛttiḥ 
[II,236,i_II,237,i]	eṣā ca tantra antareṣu prayatnaḥ iti ucyate sa ca dharma ādi saṃskāra bhāvanā vaśāt anuparataḥ jīvanam āha ca vṛttiḥ antar samastānām karaṇānām pradīpa vat aprakāśā kriyā rūpā jīvanam kāya dhārikā sā yāvat aniruddhā tu hanti vāyum rajaḥ adhikā dharma ādyanāvṛtti vaśāt tāvat jīvati mānavaḥ atra ca sāmānya karaṇa vṛtti grahaṇa sāmarthyāt prāṇa ādyāḥ pañca vāyavaḥ buddhīndriyāṇi ṣaṣṭham karmendriyāṇi saptamam pūraṣṭamam pūriti ahaṃkāra avasthā saṃvidham adhikurute yasmāt āha tatra saṃvid ahaṃkāra gatam kāryam kāraṇam pūrayati yasmāt tasmāt pūriti uktā pratyavabhāsā aṣṭamam bhoktuḥ 
[II,237,ii_II,237,iv]	sā ca ahaṅkāra gatā saṃvid buddhi gatā eva puruṣeṇa upalabhyate yasmāt vakṣyati ete pradīpa kalpāḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇāḥ guṇa viśeṣāḥ kṛtsnam puruṣasya artham prakāśya buddhau prayacchanti sarva pratyupabhogam yasmāt puruṣasya sādhayati buddhiḥ tasmāt sā eva pūriti śāstram ca evam āha prāṇa apāna samāna udāna vyānāḥ pañca vāyavaḥ ṣaṣṭham manaḥ saptamī pūraṣṭamī vāc vāc grahaṇena karmendriya parvaṇaḥ grahaṇam manaḥ grahaṇena buddhīndriya parvaṇaḥ tat etad prāṇa aṣṭamam vaikārikam guṇa śarīrasya paridraṣṭuḥ kṣetrajñasya śarīram ādadānasya nityam stambha sthānīyam pratyaṅgam bhavati acchedyam abhedyam adāhyam avināśyam avikampyam anityāni punar bhautikāni bāhyāni kuśa mṛttikā sthānīyāni upacīyante ca iti 
[II,238,i]	āha kutas punar iyam prāṇa ādi vṛttiḥ pravartate iti ucyate sā karma yonibhyaḥ mahataḥ pracyutam hi rajaḥ vikṛtam aṇḍa sthānīyāḥ pañca karma yonayaḥ bhavanti dhṛtiḥ śraddhā sukhāḥ vividiṣā avividiṣā iti āha ca pracyutaḥ mahataḥ yaḥ tu na prāptaḥ jñāna lakṣaṇam vyāpāraḥ jñāna yoni tvāt sā yoniḥ kukkuṭa aṇḍa vat 
[II,238,ii^1]	tāsām lakṣaṇa viṣaya sa tattva guṇa samanvayāḥ bhavanti tatra lakṣaṇam tāvat vyavasāyāt apracyavanam dhṛtiḥ phalam anabhisandhāya śāstra ukteṣu kāryeṣu avaśya kartavya tā bīja bhāvaḥ śraddhā dṛṣṭa ānuśravika phala abhilāṣa dvārakaḥ hi buddheḥ ābhogaḥ sukhā vettum icchā vividiṣā tad nivṛttiḥ avividiṣā tatra yadā ayam jantuḥ śubha aśubheṣu kāryeṣu vṛtti anusārī jijñāsu ḥ ajijñāsuḥ vā śarīram parityajati tām eva karma yonim upapadyate tasyām upapannaḥ tām eva bhāvayati etat tāvat lakṣanasa tattvam āha ca vāci karmaṇi saṃkalpe pratijñām yaḥ na rakṣati tad niṣṭhaḥ tad pratijñaḥ ca dhṛteḥ etat hi lakṣaṇam anasūyā brahmacaryam yajanam yājanam tapaḥ dānam parigrahaḥ śaucam śraddhāyām lakṣaṇam smṛtam sukha arthī yaḥ tu seveta vidyām karma tapāṃsi vā prāyaścitta paraḥ nityam sukhāyām sa tu vartate dvi tva eka tva pṛthaktvam nityam cetanam acetanam sūkṣmam satkāryam asat kārya vividiṣitavyam vividiṣāyāḥ viṣa pīta supta matta vat avividiṣā dhyāyinām sadā yoniḥ kārya karaṇa kṣaya karī prākṛtikā gatiḥ samākhyātā 
[II,239,i_II,239,ii]	viṣaya sa tattvam punar sarva viṣayiṇī dhṛtiḥ āśrama viṣayiṇī śraddhā dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣayiṇī sukhā vyakta viṣayiṇī vividiṣā avyakta viṣayiṇī avividiṣā guṇa samanvayaḥ tu rajaḥ tamaḥ bahulā dhṛtiḥ sattva rajaḥ bahulā śraddhā sattva tamaḥ bahulā sukhā rajaḥ bahulā vividiṣā tamaḥ bahulā vividiṣāḥ iti uktam ca lakṣaṇa viṣaya sa tattvam traiguṇya samanvayam ca pañcānām yonīnām yaḥ vidyāt yati vṛṣabham tam tu aham manye iti uktāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ yonayaḥ ca 
[II,240,i^1]	etat dvayam adhigamya samyak mārga anugamanam kuryāt rajaḥ tamaḥ dharma ādi sādhana bhāva vinivṛttitaḥ tu atra prāṇānām antar vṛttiḥ anupādhika tvāt anivartyā bahis vṛttiḥ tu mārgāḥ mārga viṣaya tayā prayoktavyā katham iti ucyate prāṇa viṣayā tāvat praṇatiḥ dharma ādi viṣayaḥ eva aparoddhavyā tatas hi asya sattva vṛddhiḥ sattva vṛddheḥ ca uttarottara buddhi rūpa adhigamaḥ apāna viṣayaḥ tu apakramaṇam dharma ādi viṣayaḥ eva aparoddhavyam evam hi asya khyāti viṣaya ākārasya tamasaḥ nirhrāsaḥ tatas ca uttarottara buddhi rūpa adhigamaḥ tathā samāna viṣayam sāhacarya sattva dharma anuguṇam kuryāt yasmāt śāstram āha sattva ārāmaḥ sattva mithunaḥ ca sadā syāt iti ātma utkarṣa tu udāna viṣayam 
[II,240,i^2]	avidyā parvaṇaḥ antyam rūpam vivarjya tad pratipakṣaiḥ nivartayet atyanta avinābhāvam ca vyāna viṣayam jñāna viṣayaḥ eva bhāvayet yonīnām catasṛṇām dharma tā bīja tām eva ādadyāt avividiṣām api aniṣṭa phala hetuṣu bhāvayet saḥ ayam dharma ādiṣu pravaṇaḥ tad pratipakṣa apakrāntaḥ sattva ārāmaḥ vinivṛtta abhimānaḥ jñāna niṣṭhaḥ sa viśuddha yoniḥ acireṇa parama brahma upapadyate iti āha ca bāhyām prāṇa vivṛttim samyak mārge budhaḥ pratiṣṭhāpya vinivṛtta vikhara kaluṣaḥ dhruvam amṛtam sthānam abhyeti pañcānām yonīnām dharma ādi nimitta tām ca saṃsthāpya paripakvam iti adhastāt na punar tad bhāvitaḥ gacchet iti vyākhyātā vyasta samastā karaṇānām vṛttiḥ 
[II,244,i_II,244,iii]	āha yā iyam ekaikasmin rūpa ādau arthe karaṇa catuṣṭayasya vṛttiḥ sā kim yugapad āhosvit krameṇa iti kutas saṃśayaḥ iti ced ubhayathā dṛṣṭa tvāt iha eka artha viṣayāṇām yugapad api vṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā candra maṇḍale cakṣuṣām manasaḥ vā kramaśas ca tat yathā ghaṭe madhu udaka payasām eka artha viṣayam ca karaṇa catuṣṭayam atas naḥ saṃśayaḥ kim cakṣuḥ manaḥ vat yuga padasya vṛttiḥ āhosvit madhu ādi vat krameṇa iti ucyate yathādarśanam api tāvat ucyatām kim atra yuktam bhavān manyate sa ced sapyak upadekṣyasi kaḥ nirbandhaḥ tat eva pratipadyāmahe iti yat yavam tasmāt idam asmad darśanam yugapad catuṣṭayasya tu vṛttiḥ
[II,244,iv]	tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ yugapad ā iva iti arthaḥ buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām hi buddhīndriyāṇām ca samāna deśa tvam tatra na śakyate etat vaktum sati śakti sadbhāve viṣaya sambandhe ca kasyacid tatra vṛttiḥ kasyacid na iti kim ca anyat megha stanita ādiṣu krama anupalabdheḥ yadi hi krameṇa śrotra ādīnām antaḥkaraṇasya ca bāhye arthe vṛttiḥ syāt api tarhi megha stanita kṛṣṇa sarpa ālocana ādiṣu api upalabhyate kramaḥ na tu upalabhyate tasmāt yugapad eva bāhye arthe catuṣṭaya vṛttiḥ iti 
[II,245,i_II,245,iii]	ucyate yat uktam śrotra ādīnām antaḥkaraṇasya ca abhinna kālam vṛttiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ ayuktam etat kim kāraṇam yasmāt asmākam kramaśas ca tasya nirdiṣṭā tasya iti catuṣṭayam api sambadhyate caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ kramaśas eva iti arthaḥ kramaśas eva hi bāhya antaḥkaraṇa vṛttyoḥ eka artha nipātaḥ yat tu uktam samāna deśānām śakti sambandha sadbhāve vṛtti abhāva anupapattiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vat etat syāt tat yathā cakṣuḥ tvacoḥ samāna deśa tve śakti viṣaya sambandha upapattau rajaḥ dhūma ātapa ādi gataḥ sparśaḥ eva upalabhyate na rūpam evam iha api syāt tasmāt dṛṣṭe tathā api adṛṣṭe
[II,245,iv]	kramaśas eva catuṣṭayasya vṛttiḥ adṛṣṭa grahaṇena punar atra atīna āgata vyavahita viṣaya grahaṇam tatra atītam dvividham dṛṣṭa viṣaya dṛṣṭa viṣayam ca atra api dṛṣṭa viṣayam pratyabhijñānam iti abhipretam adṛṣṭa viṣayam smṛtiḥ sā tu liṅga āgamābhyām akasmāt vā bhavati tathā ca vṛṣa gaṇa vīreṇa api uktam bhavati anāgata vyavahita viṣaya jñānam tu liṅga gāgamābhyām āha ca viṣaya indriya saṃyogāt pratyakṣa jñānam ucyate tat eva atīndriyam jātam punarbhāvanayā smṛtiḥ tat eva bhāvanā apekṣa jñānam kāla antare punar tatra eva sa indriyam jātam pratyabhijñānam ucyate 
[II,246,i_II,246,iii]	tatra duṣṭe kramaḥ prati na asti sandehaḥ yat punar etat uktam dṛṣṭe megha stanita kṛṣṭa sarpa ālocana ādau krama anupalabdheḥ yugapad catuṣṭayasya vṛttiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ etat api ayuktam kim kāraṇam yasmāt trayasya tad pūrvikā vṛttiḥ na tāvat buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām sākṣāt bāhya artha grahaṇa sāmarthyam asti antaḥkaraṇa anupapatti prasaṃgāt śrotra ādi vaiyarthya prasaṃgāt dvāri dvāra bhāva vyāghāta prasaṅgāt ca tasmāt pūrvam śrotra ādīnām artha sambandhaḥ asti megha stanita ādau api avaśyam etat abhyupagantavyam paścāt tu tad vṛtti upanipātāt antaḥkaraṇasya iti asti kramaḥ atra api tatra yat uktam megha stanita ādiṣu kramān anugate yugapad catuṣṭayasya vṛttiḥ iti etat ayuktam 
[II,248,i]	anyaiḥ tu anyathā anvayaḥ darśitaḥ tat yathā catuṣṭayasya manaḥ ahaṃkāra buddhīnām antaḥkaraṇānām bāhyena ekena karaṇena śrotreṇa vā cakṣuṣā vā saha catuṣṭayasya iti arthaḥ asya dṛṣṭe vartamāne yugapad vṛttiḥ pūrva ācāryaiḥ nirdiṣṭā ācāryeṇa tu krameṇa iti arthaḥ adṛṣṭe atīta ādau api kramaśas ca krameṇa eva yatas trayasya antaḥkaraṇasya tad pūrvikā bāhya indriya pūrvikā vṛttiḥ yadā yathā anubhavaḥ tathā saṃskāraḥ yathā ca saṃskāraḥ tathā smṛtiḥ iti evam vṛttiḥ bāhya indriya pūrvikā iti 
[II,250,i_II,251,i]	āha kim punar eṣām karaṇānām sva viṣaya niyamena vṛttiḥ bhavati āhosvit vyatikareṇa iti ucyate nanu ca prāk eva rūpa ādiṣu pañcānām ālocana mātram iṣyate vṛttiḥ iti ca uktvā ācāryeṇa ante apadiṣṭam sā eṣā bhavati asāmānyā iti tatra evam gate bhavataḥ saṃśayaḥ kutas iti ucyate satyam eva etat tathā api jāyate saṃśayaḥ kutas karaṇa antareṇa sva viṣaya upalabdhau karaṇa antara autsukya darśanāt iha karaṇa antareṇa cakṣuṣā āmra dāḍima ādi rūpa upalabdhau satyām karaṇa antarasya jihvā lakṣaṇasya autsukyam pravṛttiḥ ca upalabdhā tat yadi sva viṣaya niyatāni indriyāni na eṣām karaṇa antara viṣaya upalambhāt tad sāha caryā apekṣaḥ sva viṣaya grahaṇa bhāvaḥ syāt asti ca tasmāt upapannaḥ saṃśayaḥ tatra idānīm bhavataḥ pratipattiḥ iti ucyate atra api na asti indriyāṇām sva viṣaya grahaṇa vyatikaraḥ kim tarhi svām svām pratipadyante paraspara ākūta hetukīm vṛttim puruṣa arthaḥ eva hetuḥ na kenacid kāryate karaṇam 
[II,251,ii]	yasya karaṇasya yā vṛttiḥ apadiṣṭā tat yathā śrotrasya śabda grahaṇam cakṣuṣaḥ rūpa grahaṇam ityādi tām eva pratipadyante sva viṣaya jidhṛ kṣaya avalambante iti arthaḥ parasparasya ākūtam paraspara ākūtam ākūtam abhiprāyaḥ abhisandhiḥ iti arthaḥ paraspara ākūtam hetuḥ pratipatteḥ asyāḥ sā iyam paraspara ākūta hetukī paraspara ākūtam pratipatteḥ kāraṇam iti kṛtvā tāt śabdyam labhate tat yathā dadhi trapusam jvaraḥ etat uktam bhavati yadā cakṣuṣā āmra dāḍima ādi rūpam upalabdham bhavati tadā rasanā indriyam upātta viṣayasya cakṣuṣaḥ vṛttim saṃvedya sva viṣaya jighṛkṣayā autsukta vat vikāram āpadyate rasanasya vṛtim saṃvedya pādau viharaṇam ārabhete hastau ādānam tāvat yāvat asau viṣayaḥ rasanā indriya yogya tām nītaḥ tatas rasanam sva viṣaye pravartate evam itareṣu api vaktavyam 
[II,252,i]	āha yadi evam tena tarhi indriya antara vṛtti saṃvedane akṣa pratyayavatu aprasaṃgaḥ yadi tarhi indriya antareṇa indriya antarasya vṛttiḥ saṃvedyate prāptam asya pratyayavat tvam atha apratyayam indriyam paraspara ākūta saṃvedanam tarhi na vācyam iti kim ca paraspara dvāri dvāra bhāva prasaṃgaḥ ca indriya antaram ced indriya antarasya vṛttim saṃvedya sva artham ākāṃkṣet prāptam asya dvāri tvam itarasya ca dvāra tvam tat ayuktam indriyāṇām paraspara ākūta saṃvedanam iti 
[II,252,ii]	ucyate na upacārāt prāk eva upadiṣṭam asmābhiḥ apratyayam indriyam iti kim tarhi sva viṣayasya paṭoḥ sahacāriṇam artham indriya antara viṣaya tām āpannam saṃspṛśya svabhāvataḥ indriya antaram sva viṣayam prati sā akāṃkṣam bhavati tad sannidhau vikriyā darśanāt tatra saṃvedanam upacarya evam ucyate iti adoṣaḥ kim ca anyat bhautika avayava pratyaya vivṛtti vat tad vivṛtteḥ yathā buddheḥ prasādam anantaram bhautikānām avayavānām mukha nayana ādīnām prasādaḥ bhavati na ca eṣām pratyayavat tvam evam iha api syāt na ca pratyayavat tvam etena dvāri dvāra bhāvaḥ pratyuktaḥ 
[II,253,i]	manaḥ adhiṣṭhāna sāmarthyāt vā athavā paraspara viṣayam ākūtam paraspara ākūtam yathā jala viṣayaḥ puruṣaḥ jalapuruṣaḥ ākūtam icchā saṃkalpaḥ manaḥ iti arthaḥ sa hetuḥ asyāḥ sā iyam paraspara ākūta hetukī tām etat uktam bhavati yathā kiṃcid indriyam viṣaye pravṛttam bhavati tadā tad dvāreṇa samastam artham upalabhya tad sahacāriṇam artha antaram ākāṃkṣat indriya antaram vṛttyā pratitiṣṭhate tena akāṃkṣāvatāḥ manasā adhiṣṭhitām indriyam vikriyām āpadyate tathā ca tantra antare api uktam yasya yasya indriyasya viṣayam manaḥ dhyāyati abhisampatti arthena tasya tasya autsukyam pravṛttiḥ ca bhavati iti etat uktam svām svām pratipadyante paraspara ākūta hetukīm vṛttiḥ iti 
[II,253,ii_II,254,i^1]	kim indriyam manaḥ vṛttyā adhiṣṭhāya sva viṣaye pravartayati yathā paraśu ādīn caitraḥ iti na iti ucyate kim tarhi sva viṣaya saṃkalpa anugṛhītasya manasaḥ saṃsparśāt svayam eva indriyam sva viṣayam pratipadyate kasmāt prayoga śakti asiddheḥ na hi yathā caitrasya paraśu ādi prayoga śaktiḥ siddhāḥ evam manasaḥ indriya prayoga śaktiḥ tasmāt ayuktam indriyasya manaḥ prerakam iti rajaḥ iti ced syāt matam rajasaḥ hi indriyā antara prayoga sāmarthyam vidyate tasmāt ayuktam uktam prayoga śakti asiddheḥ na indriyāṇām manaḥ prayojakam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt aviśeṣāt indriya antare api hi tarhi rajaḥ asti iti atas ātma bhūtena eva asya nimittena pravṛttiḥ apratiṣiddhā kim manasā parikalpitena iti 
[II,254,i^2]	kim ca anyat karaṇa antara anupapatteḥ caitraḥ hi paraśu a ādīnām prayogam karaṇa antareṇa karoti na tu manasaḥ karaṇa antaram asti iti asamānam pāṇi vat iti ced na caitravyāpāra apekṣa tvāt tat api hi caitravyāpāra apekṣam pravartate na svatas kiṃca tad vyatirekeṇa pravṛtti upalabdheḥ yasya hi prayojaka antara apekṣā pravṛttiḥ na tasya kadācid api svatantrasya bhavati asti tu saṃkalpa vyatirekeṇa megha stanita ādiṣu indriyasya pravṛttiḥ tasmāt na indriya antarasya manaḥ kārakam na ced kārakam yathā maulānām guṇānām evam iha api puruṣa arthaḥ evam hetuḥ na kena cit kāryate karaṇam iti siddham 
[II,257,i_II,257,ii]	āha karaṇam pratyācārya vipratipatteḥ tad avadhāraṇam karttavyam ācāryāṇām karaṇam prati vipratipattiḥ ekādaśavidham iti vārṣa gaṇāḥ daśavidham iti tāntrikāḥ pañca ādi karaṇa prabhṛtayaḥ dvādaśavidham iti patañjaliḥ tasmāt bhavataḥ katividham karaṇam abhipretam iti vaktavyam etat ucyate karaṇam trayodaśavidham tad āharaṇa dhāraṇa prakāśa karam 
[II,257,iii_II,258,i]	pañca karmendriyāṇi pañca buddhīndriyāṇi manaḥ ahaṅkāraḥ buddhiḥ ca iti etat sarvam puruṣa artha upayogi karaṇam kasmāt apuruṣa artha upayogi tve tattva antara anupapatti prasaṃgāt yadi yathā vārṣa gaṇāḥ āhuḥ liṅga mātre mahān asaṃvedyaḥ kārya kāraṇa rūpeṇa viśiṣṭa aviśiṣṭa lakṣaṇena tathā syāt tattva antaram tat na syāt anarthaka tvāt āha satyam pradhāna lakṣaṇānām guṇānām vaiṣamya mātra rūpa tve api tattva antaram asau bhaviṣyati iti kasmāt sāmyāt vaiṣamyam upākhya antaram iti 
[II,258,ii]	etat ca ayuktam kasmāt tattva anavasthā prasaṃgāt evam hi parikalpyamāne pradhāna mahatoḥ yat antarālam tat api ca kriyā rūpa tvāt akriyāvataḥ upākhya antaram iti tattva antara anavasthā prasaṃgaḥ abhyupagame vā mahataḥ tattva antarāṇām ca kriyā kāla virodhaḥ tasmāt tattva antara anupapattiḥ anavasthā vā trayodaśavidham karaṇam iti anyatara vat avaśyam abhyupagantavyam tatra ca asmad pratijñātam eva nirdoṣam lakṣyate tasmāt upapannam etat trayodaśavidham karaṇam iti 
[II,258,iii_II,259,i]	āha karaṇam iti kriyā kāraka sambandha garbhaḥ ayam nirdeśaḥ katham yena tat karaṇam iti tatra vaktavyam kā kriyā kim ca tat kriyate yat apekṣya buddhi ādīnām karaṇa tvam iti ucyate yat uktam kā kriyā iti atra brūmaḥ tad nirvartakam iha abhipretāt na daṇḍa ādi vat kim tarhi tad āharaṇa dhāraṇa prakāśa karam tatra āharaṇam karmendriyāṇi kurvanti viṣaya arjana samartha tvāt dhāraṇam buddhīndriyāṇi kurvanti viṣaya sannidhāne sati śrotra ādi vṛtteḥ tad rūpa āpatteḥ prakāśam antaḥkaraṇam karoti niścaya sāmarthyāt 
[II,259,ii_II,259,v]	aparaḥ āha āharaṇam karmendriyāṇi kurvanti dhāraṇam manaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ ca prakāśanam buddhīndriyāṇi buddhiḥ ca iti etat abhisandhāya buddhi ādīnām karaṇa tvam ucyate iti yat tu uktam kim kāryam iti ucyate kāryam ca tasya daśadhā daśadhā iti pañca viśeṣāḥ pañca aviśeṣāḥ tat api atas eva kārya śabdam labhate āhāryam dhāryam prakāśyam ca tat hi āhartavyam dhāraṇīyam prakāśayitavyam ca atas kāryam iti ucyate na nirvartya tvāt 
[II,262,i_II,262,iii]	etasmin trayodaśavidhe tu karaṇe trayodaśam katarat iti ucyate buddhiḥ ahaṃkāraḥ manaḥ ca tasmāt antaḥkaraṇam trividham kasmāt viṣayān abhisandhānāt śrotra ādi praṇālikayā ca viṣaya saṃpratipatteḥ aviśeṣa abhidhānāt buddhi ādi pratipattiḥ ayuktā iti ced syāt matam aviśeṣeṇa idam uktam ācāryeṇa antaḥkaraṇam trividham iti tatra katham idam avagamyate buddhi ahaṃkāra manasām grahaṇa abhipretam na punar anyeṣām iti ucyate na prathama saṃkhyā vyatikrama hetu anupapatteḥ buddhi ādi saṃkhyām hi vyatikramamāṇasya pratipattau na asti hetuḥ tasmāt teṣām eva grahaṇam yathā vasantāya kapiñjala an ālabhate iti śrotrasya antaḥkaraṇa tva prasaṃgāt ayuktam iti ced syāt etat buddhim ahaṃkāram ca uktvā tatas āha buddhīndriyāṇi karṇa tvac cakṣū rasana nāsikā ākhyāni iti tasmāt śrotram antaḥkaraṇam prasajyate iti etad anupapannam kasmāt manasaḥ pṛthak abhidhānāt atas eva idam ācāryeṇa apekṣya manasaḥ antaḥkaraṇa tvam pṛthak uktam tat ca indriyam ubhayathā samākhyātam antar tri kāla viṣayam iti tasmāt upapannam antaḥkaraṇam trividham buddhi ādīni 
[II,263,i_II,263,iv]	daśadhā bāhyam pañca buddhīndriyāṇi pañca karmendriyāṇi iti etat bāhyam daśa prakāram ācāryaiḥ ākhyāyate āha daśadhā bāhyam iti asya ānarthakyam pariśeṣa buddheḥ antaḥkaraṇam trividham iti ukte gamyate etad pariśeṣāt eva daśadhā bāhyam iti tasmāt tat grahaṇam anarthakam iti ucyate na viṣaya artha tvāt trayasya viṣaya ākhyam iti evam vakṣyāmi iti ācāryaḥ ārabhate akriyamāṇe tu asmin kintat trayasya viṣaya ākhyam iti na jñāyate 
[II,264,i_II,264,ii]	āha evam api viṣaya grahaṇāt siddheḥ bāhya grahaṇa pārthakam iti ucyate vaktavyam tāvat idam avaśyam viṣaya bhāva pratipatti artham tatra śeṣe vā yathānyāsam vā ucyamāne na kaścid viśeṣaḥ athavā na idam bāhya saṃjñā pratipatti artham ārabhyate kim tarhi niyama artham katham daśadhā bāhyam śabda ādi viṣaya grahaṇa bhūtam eva trayasya api viṣaya ākhyam yathā syāt mā bhūt antar prāṇa ādi bhūtam athavā daśadhā eva bāhyam bheda viṣayam bāhyam iti arthaḥ prāṇa ādi bhūtasya tu bhedaḥ na asti iti adoṣaḥ 
[II,264,iii_II,265,iii]	tat etat trayasya viṣaya ākhyam buddhi ahaṃkāra manaḥ lakṣaṇasya hi trayasya upātta viṣayā buddhīndriya karmendriya vṛttayaḥ samparkāt viṣaya rūpa pratyavabhāsa nimitta tām upagacchantyaḥ viṣaya ākhyatām labhante tathā manaḥ ahaṃkārau api buddheḥ buddhiḥ tu niścaya rūpa tvāt karaṇa antara nirapekṣā sarvam artham pravṛttau prati niścaya rūpeṇa adhyastam puruṣāya upasaṃharati tatra śabda ādi sannidhāne vṛttīnām tādrūpya āpatteḥ tad apagame ca tādrūpya apagamāt prāpya kāri sāmprata kālam bāhyam upātta viṣaya indriya vṛtti sannidhānāt tu tad ākāra saṃskāra ādhāna nimitta smṛti pratyaya vaśāt tri kālam ābhyantaram karaṇam 
[II,267,i_II,267,ii]	āha prāc śabda ādiṣu śrotra ādīnām ālocana mātram vṛttiḥ iti aviśeṣeṇa uktam tatra kim tathā eva pratipattavyam atha indriyāṇām viṣaya viśeṣaḥ asti iti atha ca uktam kāryam ca tasya daśadhā viśeṣa lakṣaṇam aviśeṣa lakṣaṇam ca tatra kena karaṇena kasya viṣayasya grahaṇam iti ucyate buddhīndriyāṇi teṣām pañca viśeṣa aviśeṣa viṣayāṇi 
[II,267,iii_II,268,i]	teṣām pūrva uktānām indriyāṇām yāni buddhīndriyāṇi pañca śrotra ādīni tāni viśeṣa aviśeṣa viṣayāṇi pratipattṛ bhedena tatra devānām yāni indriyāṇi tāni dharma utkarṣāt viśuddha ani aviśeṣān api gṛhṇanti prāk eva viśeṣāt yoginām ca saṃprāpta viśeṣāṇām asmad ādīnām tu viśeṣān eva tamasā parivṛta tvāt āha kim karmendriyāṇām api pratipattṛ bhedāt grahaṇa bhedaḥ bhavati 
[II,268,ii_II,268,v]	na iti ucyate kim tarhi sarveṣām eva vāc bhavati śabda viṣayā vāc indriyasya vāyu abhihateṣu vadana pradeśeṣu tālu ādiṣu dhvaneḥ varṇa pada vākya śloka grantha bhāvena vikāra āpādanam sarva prāṇinām aviśiṣṭam āha atha itarāni karmendriyāṇi katham iti ucyate śeṣāṇi api pañca viṣayāṇi 
[II,268,vi_II,269,ii]	pāṇi pāda pāyu upasthāḥ tu ādāna viharaṇa utsarga ānanda lakṣaṇaiḥ karmabhiḥ śabda sparśa rasa rūpa gandha samudāya rūpāḥ mūrtīḥ vikurvanti iti āha yadi pañca viṣayāṇi eva aviśeṣāṇi iti niyamaḥ abhyupagamyate tena eka karaṇeṣu ādāna ādi kriyā anupapatti prasaṃgaḥ iti ucyate na niyama pratiṣedha artha tvāt sva viṣaya niyamaḥ buddhīndriya vat karmendriyāṇām api mā vijñāyi iti atas niyama pratiṣedha artham idam ārabhyate tad artham eva ca api śabdam ācāryaḥ adhijage sambhāvana artham api ca pañca viṣayāṇi etāni prāk eva tu catur tri viṣayāṇi iti āha katham etat avagamyate viśeṣa aviśeṣa viṣayāṇi indriyāṇi na punar asat viṣayāṇi iti 
[II,269,iii^1]	ucyate viśeṣāṇām asattva asiddheḥ pratyakṣataḥ tāvat viśeṣāḥ upalabhyante tasmāt eṣām asattvam aśakyam pratijñātum atha api syāt sādhyam etat pratyakṣam eva etat anavadyam bāhya vastu viṣaya maya mṛga tṛṣṇikā ādi vijñāna vat pratyakṣa ābhāsam etat ca ayuktam kasmāt vikalpa anupapatteḥ sarvam abhūtam abhyupagantavyam yatra na asti kiṃcid bhūta arthena pratyakṣam yat api ekṣyetarat pratyakṣa ābhāsam syāt uktaḥ tu ayam vikalpaḥ tasmāt ayuktam jñāna mātram idam iti kim ca anyat viparīta darśana prasaṃgāt mṛgatṛṣṇikā svapna viṣayaiḥ asadbhiḥ satām asattvam icchataḥ tadvat eva viparīta darśana prasaṃgaḥ tathā hi gandharvanagara ādiṣu kadācid tam eva artham gām paśyati kaścid gajam paśyati kadācid patākām
