[II,269,iii^2]	svapne ca eka mūrti patitānām go puruṣa aśvarāsabha nadī vṛkṣa prabhṛtīnām darśanam smaraṇe viparyayeṇa dṛṣṭam tathā vātāyanena hasti yūtha praveśane vicchinnānām ca avayavānām punar sandhānam ākāśa gamanam anīśvarasya animittam rājya lābhaḥ iti tat itaratra api syāt na tu asti tasmāt ayuktam mṛgatṛṣṇikā svapna ādi vat asattvam bhāvānām artha kriyā ca na syāt yathā svapne snāta anulipta aśita pīta vastra ācchāditānām a phala tvam dṛṣṭam evam iha api syāt śukra visarga vat iti ced syāt etat yathā dvaya samāpti pūrvakaḥ śukra visargaḥ sa ca tad abhāve api svapne bhavati evam itarat syāt iti tat ayuktam rāga ādi nimitta tvāt tathā hi jāgrataḥ api tat dvaya samāpattim antareṇa bhavati 
[II,269,iii^3]	tasmāt manorañjana animittam tat preta vat iti ced syāt iyam mama sat buddhiḥ yathā pretānām asadbhiḥ pūya nadi ādibhiḥ artha kriyā nara kapālaiḥ ca bādhanam evam atra api syāt iti tat ayuktam asiddha tvāt na hi etat asat iti siddham kiṃca pratyakṣeṇa ca apratyakṣa bādhanāt iha pratyakṣam balīyaḥ iti apratyakṣasya tena pratyākhyānam upapadyate bhavantaḥ tu apratyakṣena pratyakṣam pratyācakṣate tasmāt ayuktam nara kalāpa ādi vat asatām artha kriyā iti svabhāva bhedāt tat asattvam iti ced syāt etat yadi paramārthataḥ naraka pālāḥ syuḥ teṣām api duḥkha sambandhaḥ syāt mūrtimat tva aviśeṣāt na tu teṣām bādhā asti tasmāt bhrāntiḥ asau iti etat ayuktam kasmāt 
[II,269,iii^4]	karma śakti vaicitryāt pratyakṣam eva tāvat karma nimittaḥ vāc buddhi svabhāva āhāra vihāra śakti bheda bhinnaḥ vicitraḥ saṃsāraḥ upalabhyate sa nipuṇam avekṣitum aśakyaḥ gambhīra tvāt kim punar apratyakṣa karmaṇām vipāka vaiśvarūpyam atarka gocaram asmad ādi buddhayaḥ paricchetsyanti tasmāt manoratha mātram etat dharma adharma anupapattiḥ ca syāt yathā svapne brahmahatyā surā pāna agamya gamana ādīnām aphala tvam evam itaratra api syāt asat aviśeṣāt middha upaghātāt tad viśeṣaḥ iti ced na aviśeṣāt asattve tulye kvacid upaghātaḥ kvacid na iti it chā mātram etat evam ced na asantaḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ na ced asantaḥ yuktam upadiṣṭam buddhīndriyāṇi teṣām pañca viśeṣa aviśeṣa viṣayāṇi iti 
[II,274,i_II,274,iii]	dvāri dvāra bhāvam eṣām idānīm vakṣyāmaḥ tatra bāhyam karaṇam dvāram antaḥkaraṇam dvāri iti āha karaṇā viśeṣāt ayuktam antaḥkaraṇasya hi indriyānām ca karaṇa tvam aviśiṣṭam tatra kaḥ hetuḥ antaḥkaraṇam dvāri dvārāṇi indriyāṇi iti ucyate sa antaḥkaraṇā buddhiḥ sarvam viṣayam avagāhate yasmāt tasmāt trividham karaṇam dvāri dvārāṇi śeṣāṇi 
[II,274,iv]	saha antaḥkaraṇena vartate yā sa antaḥkaraṇā buddhiḥ ahaṃkāram anobhyām sahitāḥ buddhiḥ iti arthaḥ atra ca antaḥkaraṇa grahaṇena eva buddheḥ grahaṇe siddhe bhūyas buddhi grahaṇam prādhānya khyāpana artham bhavati hi pradhānasya sāmānye antarbhūtasya api pṛthak upadeśaḥ tat yathā jagāma tam vana uddeśam vyāsaḥ saha mahā ṛṣibhiḥ 
[II,274,v]	iti mahā ṛṣi grahaṇe vyāsaḥ api antarbhūtaḥ prādhānyāt pṛthak ucyate evam sa antaḥkaraṇā buddhiḥ sarvam viṣayam avagāhate viśiṣṭān aviśiṣṭān ca śabda ādīn sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭa vyavahitān pramāṇa balena sva vṛtte viṣayīkaroti iti arthaḥ etat uktam bhavati aniyata viṣayaḥ dvārī niyata viṣayāṇi dvārāṇi tat yathā prāsādasya pūrva uttara dakṣiṇa paścimānām sva diś niyamaḥ na pūrvam uttaram dakṣiṇam paścimam vā kadācid bhavati tathā itarāṇi api dvārīṇi tatra aniyatāḥ sarva diś avasthitaiḥ dvāraiḥ pravartante evam iha api śrotra ādīni sva viṣaya niyatāni sa antaḥkaraṇā tu buddhiḥ sarvam viṣayam avagāhate yasmāt tasmāt aniyata viṣaya tvāt upapannamet trividham karaṇam dvāri dvārāṇi śeṣāṇi iti 
[II,276,i_II,276,ii]	ete pradīpa kalpāḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇāḥ guṇa viśeṣāḥ kṛtsnam puruṣasya artham prakāśya buddhau prayacchanti ete iti anena trayam abhisambadhnāti śrotra ādīnām anyatamam manaḥ ahaṃkāraḥ ca pradīpa kalpāḥ iti anena prakāśa sāmyam karaṇa parvaṇaḥ ācaṣṭe yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśakaḥ evam karaṇam api tad vyāpāre sati viṣaya āvirbhāva anupapatteḥ paraspara vilakṣaṇaḥ iti anena vyasta vṛttim pūrva uktām ākarṣati tayā hi eṣām vailakṣaṇyam anumīyate ālocana saṃkalpa abhimāna bhedāt guṇa viśeṣāḥ iti anena sattva ādīnām puruṣa vijñānam uddiśya tad bhāvena pariṇāmam khyāpayati kṛtsnam puruṣasya artham iti viśeṣa aviśeṣa lakṣaṇam kāryam āhārya dhārya prakāśya tayā yathāsambhavam prakāśya sva vṛtti anuguṇam kṛtvā viṣaya vyāpāreṇa anubhūya buddhau ādhatte atat viṣaya tām āpādayati iti arthaḥ kadācid tu buddhiḥ eva bāhya karaṇa saṃkalpa abhimāna gṛhītam sarvathā tu ayam śāstra arthaḥ yena vā tena karaṇena viṣayam upāttam buddhiḥ adhyavasyati tayā ca adhyavasāya rūpa āpannayā cetanāśaktiḥ anugṛhyate na karaṇa antarasya puruṣeṇa sama bandhaḥ asti tatas ca dvāriṇām bahu tvāt tad darśana viśeṣa svātantrya samuccaya antaḥkaraṇa puruṣa kartṛ tva doṣāṇām aprasaṃgaḥ 
[II,278,i_II,278,iii]	āha kaḥ punar atra hetuḥ yena dvāri tvā viśeṣe sati ahaṃkāra manasī buddhau viṣaya ādhānam kurutaḥ na punar anayoḥ sākṣāt puruṣeṇa sambandhaḥ iti ucyate sarva pratyupabhogam yasmāt puruṣasya sādhayati buddhiḥ ahaṃkāra manasoḥ hi na asti niścaya rūpa tā saṃkalpa abhimāna mātra rūpa tvāt aniścita viṣayayā ca karaṇa vṛttyā puruṣasya samandhaḥ anarthakaḥ syāt svayam vā niścetuḥ asya kartṛ tvam syāt tatas ca āmiśra niścaya kāraṇa tvāt ayam api āmiśra rūpaḥ syāt sarvam ca etat ukta uttaram niścaya rūpā hi buddhiḥ atas tad vṛtti upanipātī viṣayaḥ sannidhāna mātrāt puruṣeṇa saṃcetitaḥ na asya audāsīnyam bādhitum utsahate no khalu api ānarthakyam anuṣajyate etat uktam sarvam pratyupabhogam yasmāt puruṣasya sādhayati buddhiḥ iti 
[II,279,i_II,279,ii]	āha evam api śabda ādi lakṣaṇaḥ viṣayaḥ prakṛtaḥ sa ca buddhyā sarvaḥ pratipādyate tatra viṣaya antaram api asti pradhāna puruṣa antara lakṣaṇam tathā ca āhuḥ upabhogasya śabda ādi upalabdhiḥ ādiḥ guṇa puruṣa upalabdhiḥ antar tasmāt tad pratipatti artham karaṇa antaram vaktavyam iti ucyate na vaktavyam kim kāraṇam yasmāt sā eva ca viśinaṣṭi punar pradhāna puruṣa antaram sūkṣmam 
[II,279,iii]	yatas yasmāt kāraṇāt sā buddhiḥ eva hi kāṣṭha āpannena tamasā abhibhūta tvāt dharma ādīnām sattva dharmāṇām prakṛti bhūtān vikāra bhūtān paratantra anupakāryānupakāra kāna cetanān saṃsarga dharmiṇaḥ ca guṇān ātma tvena adhyavasya puruṣāya upaharati sa ca mithyājñāna abhyāsa vāsanā anurañjitam buddhi pratyayam anurudhyamānaḥ darśita viṣaya tvāt tathā eva pratipadyate yadā tu dharma ādi abhyāsāt tamaḥ rūpa āgame sati uttarottarāṇām sattva dharmāṇam utkarṣaḥ tadā vinivṛtta mithyā pratyayā vṛttiḥ na prakṛti vikāra bhūtaḥ svatantraḥ anupakāryaḥ anupakārakaḥ cetanaḥ asaṃsarga dharmā ca tatas viparītāḥ ca guṇāḥ iti śuddha adhyavasāyam karoti puruṣaḥ ca para upahṛta pravṛtti tvāt tathā eva pratipadyate tat etat guṇānām puruṣasya ca antaram dvayoḥ api niścaya svabhāva tvāt asmāt pūrva ukta dharma bhede api sati sūkṣmam gambhīram durjñeyam atas ca sūkṣmam yat buddhi mātram avalambya tad aviśiṣṭāyāḥ cetanāśakakteḥ grāhya grāhaka 
[II,282,i_II,282,iv]	vyākhyātam karaṇa parva kārya parva idānīm vaktavyam tasya ca purastāt uddeśaḥ kṛtaḥ kāryam ca tasya daśadhā pañca viśeṣāḥ iti sāmpratam tu nirdeśam kariṣyāmaḥ āha yadi evam tasmāt idam eva tāvat ucyatām ke viśeṣāḥ ke aviśeṣāḥ iti ucyate tanmātrāṇi aviśeṣāḥ yāni tanmātrāṇi pañca ahaṃkārāt utpadyante iti prāc apadiṣṭam te khalva viśeṣāḥ kāni punar tanmātrāṇi iti ucyate śabda tanmātram sparśa tanmātram rūpa tanmātram rasa tanmātram gandha tanmātram iti 
[II,282,v_II,283,iii]	katham punar tanmātrāṇi iti ucyate tulya jātīya viśeṣa anupapatteḥ anye śabda jāti abhede api sati viśeṣāḥ udātā anudātta svarita anunāsikā ādayaḥ tatra na santi tasmāt śabda tanmātram evam sparśa tanmātre mṛdu kaṭhina ādayaḥ evam rūpa tanmātre śukla kṛṣṇa ādayaḥ evam rasa tanmātre madhura amla ādayaḥ evam gandha tanmātre surabhi a ādayaḥ tasmāt tasya tasya guṇasya sāmānyam eva atra na viśeṣaḥ iti tanmātrāsu ete aviśeṣāḥ āha atha ke punar viśeṣāḥ iti ucyate yāni khalu tebhyaḥ bhūtāni pañca pañcabhyaḥ utpadyante ete smṛtāḥ viśeṣāḥ
[II,283,iv^1]	tatra śabda tanmātrāt ākāśam sparśa tanmātrāt vāyuḥ rūpa tanmātrāt tejaḥ rasa tanmātra āt āpaḥ gandha tanmātrāt pṛthivī tebhyaḥ bhūtāni iti etāvati vaktavye pañca pañcabhyaḥ iti grahaṇam sama saṃkhyā kataḥ tad utpatti jñāpana artham tena ekaikasmāt tanmātrāt ekaikasya viśeṣasya utpattiḥ siddhā tatas ca yat anyeṣām ācāryāṇām abhipretam eka lakṣaṇebhyaḥ tanmātrebhyaḥ paraspara anupraveśāt eka uttarāḥ viśeṣāḥ sṛjyante iti tat pratiṣiddham bhavati kintarhi antareṇa api tanmātra anupraveśam eka uttarebhyaḥ bhūtebhyaḥ eka uttarāṇām bhūta viśeṣāṇām utpattiḥ tatra śabda guṇāt śabda tanmātrāt ākāśam eka guṇam śabda sparśa guṇāt sparśa tanmātrāt dviguṇaḥ vāyuḥ śabda sparśa rūpa guṇāt rūpa tanmātrāt triguṇam tejaḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa guṇāt rasa tanmātrāt caturguṇāḥ āpaḥ śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhāt gandha tanmātrāt pañcaguṇā pṛthivī atra ca vāyoḥ śītaḥ sparśaḥ apām ca tejasaḥ uṣṇaḥ anuṣṇa aśītaḥ pṛthivyāḥ rūpam ca śuklam bhāsvaram ca tejasaḥ apām ca kṛṣṇam pṛthivyāḥ 
[II,283,iv^2]	rasaḥ madhuraḥ apām sādhāraṇaḥ pṛthivyāḥ gandhaḥ tu pārthivaḥ eva tad avayava anupraveśāt bhūta antareṣu upalabhyate iti ete pṛthivī ādīnām dharmāḥ anye ca paraspara anugrāhakāḥ ke punar te iti āha ākāraḥ gaurām raukṣyam varaṇam sthairyam eva ca sthiti bhedaḥ kṣamā kṛṣṇa chāyā sarva upabhogyate iti te pārthivāḥ dharmāḥ tad viśiṣṭāḥ tathā pare jala agni pavana ākāśa vyāpakāḥ tān nibodhata snehaḥ saukṣmyam prabhā śauklyam mārdavam gauravam ca yat śaityam rakṣā pavitra tvam santānaḥ ca audakāḥ guṇāḥ ūrdhva gam pāvakam dagdhṛ pācakam laghu bhāsvaram pradhvaṃsi oja svi tā jyotiḥ pūrvābhyām sa vilakṣaṇam tiryak gatiḥ pavitra tvam ākṣepaḥ nodanam balam raukṣyam acchāyatā śaityam vāyoḥ dharmāḥ pṛthagvidhāḥ sarvatas gatiḥ avyūhaḥ viṣkambhaḥ ca iti te trayaḥ ākāśa dharmāḥ vijñeyāḥ pūrva dharma virodhinaḥ saṃhatānām tu yat kāryam sāmānyam te gavā ādayaḥ itaretara dharmebhyaḥ viśeṣāt na atra saṃśayaḥ 
[II,285,i^1]	tatra ākāra ādi dharmaiḥ pṛthivyāḥ lokasya ca upakriyate bhūta antarāṇām ca tatra ākārāt tāvat gavā ādīnām ghaṭa ādīnām ca ākāra nirvṛttiḥ gauravāt eṣām avasthānam raukṣyāt apām saṃgrahaḥ vaiśadyam ca bhūtānām varaṇāt anabhipretānām chādanam sthairyāt vṛttiḥ prajānām bhūta antarāṇām ca sthiteḥ mātra ādi sannidhāna ādi anugrahaḥ bhedāt ghaṭa ādi niṣpattiḥ vyūhaḥ ca avayavānām kṣānteḥ upabhoga bhogya tā kṛṣṇa chāya tvāt rātri sampacchāya akārya prasiddhiḥ ca sarva upabhogya tvāt sarva bhūta anugrahaḥ evam sneha ādibhiḥ lokasya upakāraḥ kriyate bhūta antarāṇām ca snehāt rūpa saṃpad vāyu pratīkāraḥ agni śamanam saṃgrahaḥ ca pṛthivyāḥ saukṣmyāt anupraveśaḥ śauklyāt candrāt vinirvṛttiḥ mārdavāt snāna avagāhanam eka kriyā kaṭhinānām ca avanāmanam gauravāt santānāt ca bhūta anugraha artham srotaḥ tvam śaityāt uṣṇa pratīkāraḥ rakṣātaḥ prajāsu ghora śamanam pavitra tvāt dharma upacayaḥ śauca vidhiḥ alakṣya upaghātaḥ ca santānāt dravya saṃghātaḥ tathā ūrdhvagati ādibhiḥ dharma mātraiḥ tejasām lokasya ca upakriyate bhūta antarāṇām ca ūrdhva gateḥ pāka prakāśa siddhiḥ 
[II,285,i^2]	pāvaka tvāt dravya śaucam ca dāhaka tvāt kṣāra utpattiḥ śīta pratīkāraḥ nabhasaḥ ca uṣṇa tvam śabda niṣpatti artham pācaka tvāt svedya svedanam anna paktiḥ pṛthivī avayavānām kriyāyogya tā tathā bāhya antara pariṇāmaḥ rasa lohita māṃsa snāyu asthi majjā śukrāṇām lāghavāt dāhyā atikramaḥ bhāsvara tvāt dravya antara prakāśanam pradhvaṃsi tvāt dagdha pakvānām upabhogaḥ taijasaḥ prajā pālanam tathā tiryakpāta ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ vāyunā lokasya ca upakāraḥ kriyate bhūta antarāṇām ca tiryakpātāt dṛṣṭi vikṣepaḥ gandha saṃvahanam ca pavitra tvāt pūti dravya pavanam ākṣepanodanābhyām utkarṣaḥ prathamam dharma ambhasaḥ vyūhaḥ ca śarīre rasa ādīnām dhātūnām ca agneḥ ca upadhmānam abhidhātaḥ ca ākāśasya balāt samīkaraṇam sarveṣām raukṣyāt viśoṣaṇam acchāya tvāt ahorātra prasiddhiḥ śaityāt uṣṇa pratīkāraḥ tathā sarvatas gati a ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ nabhasā lokasya upakāraḥ kriyate bhūta antarāṇām ca sarvatas gateḥ samantāt tulya deśa śravaṇanām eka śruti tvam avyūha viṣkambhābhyām sarveṣām avakāśa tā dānam iti uktāḥ pṛthivī ādayaḥ ete viśeṣāḥ iti ucyante iti 
[II,287,i_II,287,iii]	āha katham punar ete viśeṣāḥ iti ucyante yasmāt śāntāḥ ghorāḥ ca mūḍhāḥ ca tatra śāntāḥ tāvat sva saṃskāra viśeṣa yogāt tad sannidhau prasāda ādi dharma utpatteḥ ghorāḥ tu śeṣa ādi dharma nimitta tvāt mūḍhāḥ ca varaṇa ādi dharma hetu tvāt tanmātrāṇi punar aśānta ghora mūḍhāni atas aviśeṣāḥ iti ucyante tat ete yathā vyākhyātāḥ aviśeṣāḥ viśeṣāḥ puruṣa artha siddhi artham bahudhā vyavatiṣṭhante kasmāt na hi eteṣām ekadhā avasthāne puruṣa arthaḥ siddhyati iti 
[II,290,i_II,291,i]	āha atisāmānya uktam idam iti atas na pratipadyāmahe tasmāt vaktavyam katham viśeṣaṇām avasthānam iti ucyate sūkṣmāḥ mātā pitṛ jāḥ saha prabhūtaiḥ tridhā viśeṣāḥ syuḥ tatra sūkṣmā nāma ceṣṭā āśritam prāṇa aṣṭakam saṃsarati mātṛ pitṛ jāḥ tu dvividhāḥ jarāyu jāḥ aṇḍa jāḥ ca teṣām kośa upahṛtāḥ kośāḥ loma rudhira māṃsa asthi snāyu śukra lakṣaṇaḥ tatra loma rudhira māṃsānām mātṛtaḥ sambhavaḥ asthi snāyu śukrāṇām pitṛtaḥ tatra eva aśita pīta adhyāsāḥ daṣṭau kośānapare vyācakṣate katham punar eṣām kośa tvam āveṣṭana sāmarthyāt yathā kośakāraḥ kośena āveṣṭitaḥ asvatantraḥ evam sūkṣmaśarīram sa prāṇam etaiḥ āveṣṭitam asvatantram tad tad karma upacinoti 
[II,291,ii]	prabhūtāḥ tu udbhid jāḥ sveda jāḥ ca tat etaiḥ trividhaiḥ daiva mānavatairyagyona lakṣaṇaḥ trividhaḥ bhūta sargaḥ ārabhyate tatra devānām caturvidham śarīram pradhāna anugrahāt yathā parama ṛṣeḥ viriñcasya ca tad siddhibhyaḥ yathā brahmaṇaḥ putrāṇām tad putra putrāṇām ca mātā pitṛtaḥ yathā aditeḥ kaśyapasya ca putrāṇām kevalāt vā yathā pitṛtaḥ mitrāvaruṇābhyām vaśiṣṭhasya manuṣyāṇām tu jarāyu jam dharma śakti viśeṣāt tu kasyacid anyathā api bhavati yathā droṇa kṛpa kṛpī dhṛṣṭadyumna ādīnām tiryagyonīnām api caturvidham
[II,291,iii_II,292,iii]	jarāyu jam gavā ādīnām aṇḍa jam ca eva pakṣiṇām tṛṇa ādeḥ ca udbhid jam kṣudra jantūnām sveda jam smṛtam evam trividhāḥ viśeṣāḥ vyākhyātāḥ tatra kecid niyatāḥ kecid aniyatāḥ iti āha ke punar atra niyatāḥ ke vā aniyatāḥ sūkṣmāḥ teṣām niyatāḥ mātā pitṛ jāḥ nivartante sūkṣmāḥ āsarga pralayāt nityāḥ mātṛ pitṛ jāḥ nivartante saha prabhūtaiḥ iti vartate kecid tu prabhūta grahaṇena bāhyānām eva viśeṣāṇām grahaṇam icchanti teṣām udbhid ja sveda jayoḥ agrahaṇam tasmāt ubhayathā prabhūtāḥ iti etat anavadyam āha sūkṣma abhidhānam aprasiddha tvāt mātā pitṛ jāḥ ca prabhūtāḥ ca iti atas yuktaḥ eṣām parigrahaḥ sūkṣmāḥ tu aprasiddhā tasmāt vaktavyam katham eṣām utpattiḥ astitvam vā iti 
[II,292,iv]	ucyate pūrva sarge prakṛteḥ upapannānām prāṇinām sattva dharma utkarṣāt antareṇa dvaya samāpattim manasā eva apatyam anyat vā yathā īpsitam prādurbabhūva priyam khalu api cakṣuṣā nirīkṣya kṛtārtham ātmānam manyate tasyām api kṣīṇāyām vāc siddhiḥ babhūva abhibhāṣya prāṇinaḥ yat icchanti tadāpādayanti tat adya api anuvartate yat śaṅkhī virutena apatyam bibharti priyam khalu api sambhāṣya mahatīm prītim anubhavati tasyām upakṣīṇāyām hasta siddhiḥ babhūva saṃspṛśya pāṇim īpsitam artham upapādayanti tat etat adya api anuvartate yat priyam cirāt ālokya pāṇau saṃspṛśya prītiḥ bhavati asyām upakṣīṇāyām āśleṣa siddhiḥ babhūva āliṅganena prāṇinaḥ īpsitam labhante tat etat adya api anuvartate yat priyam āliṅgya nirvṛttiḥ bhavati tasyām upakṣīṇāyām dvandva siddhiḥ ārabdhā strī puṃsau saṃdhṛṣya apatyam utpādayetām mama idam mama idam iti ca parigrahāḥ pravṛttāḥ etasmin eva avasare saṃsāraḥ varṇyate 
[II,293,i^1]	tatra ca ācāryāṇām vipratipattiḥ pañca adhikaraṇasya tāvat vaivartam śarīram mātā pitṛ saṃsarga kāle karaṇa āviṣṭam śukra śoṇitam anupraviśati tad anupraveśāt ca kalala ādi bhāvena vivardhate vyūḍha avayavam tu upalabdha pratyayam mātuḥ udarān nissṛtya yau dharma adharmau ṣaṣ siddhi upabhoga kāle kṛtau tad vaśāt avatiṣṭhate yāvat tad kṣayāt śarīra pātaḥ tāvat yadi dharma saṃskṛtam karaṇam tatas dyudeśam sūkṣma śarīreṇa prāpyate tad viparyayāt tu yātanā sthānam tiryagyonim vā miśrībhāvena mānuṣyam evamātivāhikam sūkṣma śarīram indriyāṇām dhāraṇa prāpaṇa samartham nityam bāhyena apāyinā pariveṣṭyate parityajyate ca 
[II,293,i^2]	patañjaleḥ tu sūkṣmaśarīram yat siddhi kāle pūrvam indriyāṇi bīja deśam nayati tatra tad kṛta āśaya vaśāt dyudeśam yātanā sthānam vā karaṇāni vā prāpayya nivartate tatra ca evam yukta āśayasya karma vaśāt anyat utpadyate yat indriyāṇi bīja deśam nayati tat api nivartate śarīra pāte ca anyat utpadyate evam anekāni śarīrāṇi vindhya vāsinaḥ tu vibhu tvāt indriyāṇām bīja deśe vṛttyā janma tad tyāgaḥ maraṇam tasmāt na asti sūkṣmaśarīram tasmāt nirviśeṣaḥ saṃsāraḥ iti pakṣaḥ eṣā sūkṣma śarīrasya utpattiḥ 
[II,296,i_II,296,ii]	āha evam aneka niścayeṣu ācāryeṣu bhavataḥ kā pratipattiḥ iti ucyate yat tāvat patañjaliḥ āha sūkṣmaśarīram vinivartate punar ca anyat utpadyate tat sūkṣmāḥ teṣām niyatāḥ iti vacanāt asmābhiḥ na abhyupagamyate tasmāt pūrva utpannam asaktam niyatam mahat ādi sūkṣma paryantam saṃsarati nirupabhogam bhāvaiḥ adhivāsitam liṅgam 
[II,296,iii^1]	tatra pūrva utpannam iti anena mahat ādeḥ sūkṣma paryantasya liṅgasya asarga pralayāt nitya tvam āha asaktam iti anena gūḍha sthira bīja anupraveśam ācaṣṭe na hi liṅgam kvacid vyāhanyate kim tarhi likṣā ādi bījam api āviśati badara golam api bhitvā praviśati niyatam iti anena prati puruṣa vyavasthām pratijānāti sādhāraṇaḥ hi mahān prakṛti tvāt iti vārṣa gaṇānām pakṣaḥ mahat ādi iti anena prāṇa aṣṭakam parigṛhṇāti pūrva ātmānaḥ prāṇa ādyāḥ ca pañca vāyavaḥ iti sūkṣma paryantam iti tattva antara pratiṣedham āha etāvat eva na atas anyat iti 
[II,296,iii^2]	saṃsarati iti gatim ācaṣṭe tatas ca avibhu tvāt bīja āveśa tyāgau prakhyātaḥ bhavataḥ nirupabhogam iti śarīra antarasya avakāśam karoti sūkṣmaśarīrasya hi upabhoga sāmarthye abhyupagamyamāne śarīra antarasya niravakāśa tvāt anutpatti prasaṃgaḥ syāt bhāvaiḥ adhivāsitam iti anena bhāva aṣṭaka parigraham dyotayati buddhi rūpaiḥ iha dharma ādibhiḥ adhivāsitam tad sāmarthyāt sarvatra apratihatam prāṇa aṣṭakam sūkṣma śarīre avasthāna gamana mātra phale vyavasthitam dyutiryak preteṣu saṃsarati iti tena eva ca artha siddhau śarīra antara parikalpanā narthakyam atas na bahūni śarīrāṇi 
[II,298,i]	yat punar etat uktam vibhu tvāt indriyāṇām sva ātmani avasthānam vṛtti lābhaḥ vṛtti nirodhaḥ ca saṃsāraḥ iti ayuktam etat kasmāt vibhu tva asiddheḥ na hi vibhu tvam indriyāṇām kaścid abhyupagacchati kim kāraṇam satata upalabdhi prasaṃgāt yugapad upalabdhi prasaṃgāt ca kārya karaṇa puruṣāṇām hi vibhu tve satata upalabdhi prasaṃgaḥ viṣayāṇām pratibandha abhāvāt prasajyate prātpyaviśeṣāt ca sarva viśeṣāṇām yugapad upalabdhi prasaṃgaḥ vyavahita viṣaya grahaṇam ca sarvatra sannidhānāt sannikṛṣṭa viprakṛṣṭayoḥ pratyakṣa anumāna āgamānām ca aviśeṣaḥ prasajyate vṛtti viśeṣāt tad viśeṣaḥ iti ced na hetu abhāvāt vibhūnām iha asti vṛtti viśeṣaḥ iti atra hetuḥ anuktaḥ tasmāt na karaṇānām vibhu tvam upapadyate tasmāt citram yathā āśrayam ṛte sthāṇu ādibhyaḥ vinā yathā cchāyā tadvat vinā viśeṣaiḥ na tiṣṭhati nirāśrayam liṅgam 
[II,298,ii_II,299,iii]	yathā hi citrasya kuḍyam ṛte avasthānam na asti sthāṇu puruṣa ādibhyaḥ vā vinā cchāyāyāḥ tadvat vinā viśeṣaiḥ na tiṣṭhati nirāśrayam liṅgam tasmāt upapannam etat sa viśeṣaḥ saṃsāraḥ āha yadi sa viśeṣaḥ saṃsāra bīja deśa gamane śarīram upalabhyeta na tu evam tasmāt ayuktam etat ucyate na viśeṣita tvāt sūkṣmam tat śarīram iti viśeṣitam tatas na asya ahetukam agrahaṇam iti āha sūkṣma śarīra yogāt pūrva īśvara tva prasaṃgaḥ tasmāt ayuktam tad nimittam asya agrahaṇam iti 
[II,300,i_II,300,ii]	ucyate na anekāntāt tat yathā kṣudra jantūnām sūkṣmaśarīram laghimā ca na ca eṣām īśvara tvam evam sarva prāṇinām syāt atha matam agṛhyamāṇena sambandhāt sthūlasya api śarīrasya agrahaṇam pretāñjana siddha mālya ādi vat tat api anupapannam anekāntāt tat yathā karaṇaiḥ agṛhyamāṇaiḥ śarīrasya sambandhaḥ na ca agrahaṇam piśāca ādibhiḥ vā tathā etat api syāt kiṃca antaḥkaraṇa anuvidhāne ca aiśvarya abhimānāt yasya ca adhyavasāya m anu vidadhati aṇima ādīni tasya aiśvaryam abhipretam na tu yasya svabhāva siddhāni anyathā tu pipīlikā ādīnām api ākāśa gamanāt aiśvaryam syāt āha na śarīra anupapatti prasaṃgāt sūkṣma śarīra utpattau tarhi caritārthayoḥ śarīra antara sāmarthyam virudhyate tasmāt ayuktam sa viśeṣaḥ saṃsāraḥ 
[II,300,iii^1]	ucyate na anabhyupagamāt na dharma adharma nimittam vaivartam śarīram kim tarhi ādhi kāri kam ityadoṣaḥ na ca aneka śarīra tvam abhyupagamyate tasmāt pakṣa antara upālambhaḥ ayam kim ca kṛtsnā āśaya pariṇāma apratijñānāt kṛtsnasya āśayasya pariṇāmam jānan evam upālabhyaḥ syāt eka deśaḥ tu naḥ vipariṇāmī tasmāt na kiṃcid etat nimittau aśeṣāt āśaya eka deśa abhivyaktiḥ ayuktā iti ced syāt matam iha nimittānām alpa bahu tva viśeṣāt āśaya abhivyakti viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tat yathā vāyu ādi krodha ādiṣu prāyaṇa kālaḥ ca ayam phala abhivyaktau nimittam aviśiṣṭaḥ ca asau tasmāt āśaya eka deśa pariṇāmaḥ anupapannaḥ iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt naimittika tvāt pūrva kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ phala bhoga parisamāptiḥ sāmpratasya ca phala upabhoga artha vipariṇāmaḥ prāyaṇasya nimittam 
[II,300,iii^2]	na tu prāyaṇaḥ vipariṇamasya iti kiṃca śarīra antara abhāvaḥ ca kṛtsnasya āśayasya abhivyaktim icchataḥ śarīra antara abhāvaḥ nimitta antara abhāvāt prāpnoti tatra kṛtena iti ced na kalala ādi avasthānāśe tad asambhavāt tatra kṛtābhyām hi bīja āveśaḥ karaṇasya niṣpāditaḥ yāvat kalala ādya sthāyām eva tat śarīram vinaṣṭam iti tatra kṛta āśayasya asambhavāt śarīra antara anupapatti prasaṃgaḥ kim ca sthāvarāṇām ca śarīra antara asambhavaḥ āśayasya sthāvara śarīra ārambhe caritārtha tvāt sthāvara śarīreṇa ca āśaya upādāna sambhavāt tasya saṃsāra abhāvaḥ prāptaḥ tasmāt upapannam etat puruṣa artham ādi sarga utpannam sūkṣmaśarīram saṃsarati yāvat ca sa puruṣa arthaḥ na parisamāpyate tāvat tiṣṭhate iti 
[II,304,i_II,304,ii]	āha yadi puruṣa arthāḥ liṅgasya utpattiḥ abhyupagamyate tad samanantaram eva anena puruṣa arthaḥ avasāyayitavyaḥ na punar deva mānuṣa tiryagbhāvena punar punar ājan javībhāvaḥ anuṣṭhātavyaḥ iti ucyate puruṣa artha hetukam idam nimitta naimittika prasaṅgena prakṛteḥ vibhu tva yogān naṭa vat vyavatiṣṭhate liṅgam 
[II,304,iii]	yadi api puruṣa artha siddhi artham liṅgam utpadyate tathā api sattva rajaḥ tamasām trayāṇām api prādhānyāt rajaḥ tamobhyām abhibhūte sattve tad preritam nimitta naimittika śarīra indriya viṣaya upabhoga nirvartakam śṛṇoti tat yathā agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ yama rājyam agniṣṭomena abhijayati iti tatra phala icchayā yonīḥ prāṇa ādīn ca sammukhīkṛtya kriyām ārabhate guṇa vṛtta vaicitryāt ca prayatnavān api manaḥ vāc dehaiḥ malinam api karma karoti tatas ca prakṛteḥ vibhu tva yogāt tena tena nimittena upasthāpitam deva manuṣya tiryak preta ādi śarīram eka svabhāvam api san aṭa vat vyavatiṣṭhate liṅgam ākṛti viśeṣa upādāna tyāga sāmyataḥ vibhu tvam guṇānām trayāṇām api sāmyāditaretara abhibhavaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tasmāt bhāva nimittaḥ saṃsāraḥ tad nimitta anupādānāt mokṣaḥ 
[II,306,i_II,306,v]	āha bhāvāḥ iti tatra bhavatā abhidhīyate na ca asya śabdasya artham pratipadyāmahe tasmāt vaktavyam idam ke punar amī bhāvāḥ iti ucyate dharma ādyāḥ bhāvāḥ dharmaḥ jñānam vairāgyam aiśvaryam adharmaḥ ajñānam avairāgyam anaiśvaryam iti ete bhāvāḥ tatra ācāryāṇām vipratipattiḥ pañca adhikaraṇasya tāvat dvividham jñānam prākṛtikam vaikṛtikam ca prākṛtikam trividham tattva sama kālam sāṃsiddhikam ābhiṣyandikam ca tatra tattva sama kālam saṃhataḥ ca mahān tattva ātmanā mahati pratyayaḥ bhavati utpanna kārya kāraṇasya tu sāṃsiddhikam ābhiṣyandikam ca bhavati sāṃsiddhikam yad saṃhata vyūha sama kālam niṣpadyate yathā parama ṛṣeḥ jñānam ābhiṣyandikam ca saṃsiddha kārya karaṇasya kāraṇa antareṇa utpadyate vaikṛtam tu dvividham sva vaikṛtam para vaikṛtam ca sva vaikṛtam tārakam para vaikṛtam siddhi antarāṇi āha ca tattva samam vaivartam tatra abhiṣyandikam dvitīyam syāt vaikṛtam atas tṛtīyam ṣāṭkauśikam etat ākhātam atra tu sattvaiḥ saha utpatti aviśeṣāt sāṃsiddhikam abhedena āha vaikṛtam api ca dvividham sva vaikṛtam tatra tārakam bhavati syāt saptavidham para vaikṛtam sva tāra ādi nirdiṣṭam iti yathā jñānam evam dharma ādayaḥ api iti 
[II,307,i^1]	vindhya vāsinaḥ tu na asti tattva samam sāṃsiddhikam ca kim tarhi siddhi rūpam eva tatra parama ṛṣeḥ api sarga saṃghāta vyūha uttara kālam eva jñānam niṣpadyate yasmāt guru mukha abhipratipatteḥ pratipatsyate iti api iti āha siddham nimittam naimittikasya anugraham kurute na apūrvam utpādayati iti nimitta naimittika bhāvāt ca evam upapadyate tatra parama ṛṣeḥ paṭurūhaḥ anyeṣām kliṣṭaḥ iti ayam viśeṣaḥ sarveṣām eva tu tāraka ādya viśiṣṭam ācāryaḥ āha trividhāḥ bhāvāḥ sāṃsiddhikāḥ prākṛtikāḥ vaikṛtikāḥ ca iti tatra sāṃsiddhika grahaṇāt tattva sama kālam pratyācaṣṭe na eva tat asti iti katham yadi hi tathā syāt tattva antara anutpatti saṃghātaḥ vyūhaḥ ca anarthakaḥ syāt mahati utpannam jñānam tatra eva upalabdham iti kaḥ saṃghāta arthaḥ tathā ca ṛṣeḥ ūhaḥ na upapadyate pratibandha abhāvāt na hi asya kārya kāraṇa vyūha sama kāla jñāna utpattau kaścid pratibandhaḥ asti aparivṛta khala tvāt yatas kāla antaram pratīkṣate tasmāt asya saha eva kārya kāraṇābhyām jñānam abhiniṣpadyate pradīpa prakāśāt iti ataḥ sāṃsiddhikam 
[II,307,i^2]	anyeṣām tu sattvasya apaṭu tvāt kāla antareṇa prakṛti abhiṣyandāt drāk iti bhavati kṛṣṇa sarpa darśana vat tad prākṛtam vaikṛtam tu dvividham pūrvavat yathā ca parama ṛṣeḥ jñānam sāṃsiddhikam evam māhātmya śarīrasya aiśvaryam bhṛgu ādīnām dharmaḥ sanaka ādīnām vairāgyam adharmaḥ yakṣa rakṣaḥ prabhṛtīnām anaiśvaryam ṣaṣ siddhi kṣaya kāla utpannānām manuṣyāṇām tiraścāñca rāgaḥ ajñānam parama ṛṣi varjyānām prākṛtāḥ tu tat yathā vairāgyam bhagavat āsureḥ tasya hi parama ṛṣi sambhāvanāt utpannaḥ dharmaḥ aśuddhim pratidvandvi bhāvāt apajagāma tasyām apahatāyām prakṛteḥ śuddhi srotaḥ pravṛttam yena anugṛhītaḥ duḥkha traya abhighātāt utpanna jijñāsaḥ pravrajitaḥ tathā maheśvara samparkān nandinaḥ aiśvaryam nahuṣasya agastya samparkāt dharmaḥ ityādi vaikṛtāḥ tu bhāvāḥ asmad ādīnām evam trividha bhāva parigrahāt tu a ācāryasya na sarvam svatas patañjali vat na sarvam paratas pañca adhikaraṇa vat kintarhi mahatī svabhāva ativṛttiḥ prakṛtitaḥ alpā svatas vikṛtitaḥ 
[II,309,i_II,309,iii]	evam sāṃsiddhikāḥ ca bhāvāḥ prākṛtikāḥ vaikṛtāḥ ca dharma ādyāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ karaṇa āśrayiṇaḥ yathā ca ete tathā kārya āśrayiṇaḥ ca kalala ādyāḥ trividhā eva iti kalala ādi grahaṇena śarīrāṇi āha teṣām ākṛti vaiśvarūpyam caturdaśavidhe saṃsāre trividham tatra sāṃsiddhikaḥ tāvat vaivarttānām graha nakṣatra tārā ādīnām jāti kṛtaḥ ca viśeṣaḥ haṃsānām śauklyam tittira mayūra ādīnām citracchada tvam iti prākṛtam yathāmāhātmyam śarīra abhimānāt tasya hi abhimānaḥ bhavati hanta aham putrān srakṣye ye me karma kariṣyanti ye mām param ca jñāsyanti sa yādṛś sargam abhidhyāyati tādṛś pradhānāt utpadyate tat yathā maheśvarasya rudra koṭi sṛṣṭau iti vaikṛtāḥ tu kalala ādyāḥ yathā bhiṣaj vede abhihitam kṣīram pītvā garbhiṇī gauram putram janayati iti ete bhāvāḥ vyākhyātāḥ eṣām vaiśvarūpyān liṅgasya gati viśeṣaḥ saṃsāraḥ bhavati iti 
[II,312,i_II,312,v]	āha kasya punarbhāvasya anuṣṭhānāt kaḥ gamana viśeṣaḥ liṅgasya niṣpadyate iti ucyate dharmeṇa gamanam ūrdhvam uktaḥ dharmaḥ tad anuṣṭhānāt aṣṭa vikalpāyām deva bhūmau utpattiḥ bhavati gamanam adhastāt bhavati adharmeṇa adharmaḥ api uktaḥ tad anuṣṭhāna apañca vikalpāyām tiryak bhūmau utpattiḥ bhavati 
[II,312,vi_II,313,iv]	āha eka bhūmi viśeṣa anupapattiḥ gati viśeṣāt yadi bhāvānām bhūmi viśeṣa nimitta tvam niyamyate tena ekasyām bhūmau hīna madhyama utkṛṣṭa tvam jāti ākṛti svabhāva anugraha upaghātānām na prāpnoti ucyate na tarhi anena bhūmi viśeṣaḥ niyamyate kim tarhi ūrdhva śabdaḥ utkṛṣṭa vacanaḥ dharmeṇa deveṣu mānaveṣu tiryakṣu ca ūrdhva gamanam utkṛṣṭam janma bhavati tathā adharmāt adhas gamanam apakṛṣṭam janma bhavati jñānena ca apavargaḥ caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ jñānena eva apavargaḥ na bhāva antareṇa iti yat uktam anyaiḥ ācāryaiḥ vairāgyāt puruṣa kaivalyam jñāna vairāgyābhyām ca iti tat pratiṣiddham bhavati āha yadi punar vairāgyāt puruṣa kaivalyam abhyupagamyate kaḥ evam sati doṣaḥ syāt 
[II,313,v_II,313,vii]	ucyate na śakyam evam pratipattum kasmāt saṃsāra nimitta apratipakṣa tvāt yadi rāga nimittaḥ pradhāna puruṣa saṃyogaḥ syāt prāptam idam tad pratipakṣeṇa vairāgyeṇa viyogaḥ bhaviṣyati iti na tu evam kutas saṃyoga kṛte kārya karaṇa sarge niṣpatteḥ kārya karaṇa vyūha uttara kālam hi rāgaḥ bhavati tasmāt na asau kārya karaṇa niṣpatteḥ nimittam iti śakyam āśrayitum yasya tu jñānāt mokṣaḥ iti pakṣaḥ tasya pratipakṣāt ajñānāt bandhaḥ iti prāptam asti na ca asau prāk api kārya karaṇa niṣpatteḥ tasmāt na vairāgyāt mokṣaḥ atas eva na jñāna vairāgyābhyām mokṣaḥ asti ubhaya nimitta asambhavāt tasmāt sūktam jñānena eva apavargaḥ viparyayāt iṣyate bandhaḥ jñāna viparyayaḥ ajñānam tasmāt bandhaḥ trividhaḥ bhavati prakṛti bandhaḥ dakṣiṇābandhaḥ vaikārika bandhaḥ ca iti 
[II,315,i_II,315,iv]	āha kasmāt bhāvāt prakṛti bandhaḥ bhavati ucyate vairāgyāt prakṛti layaḥ vairāgyāt aṣṭasu prakṛtiṣu layam gacchati asau ucyate prakṛti bandhaḥ iti āha yadi vairāgyāt prakṛti layaḥ prāptaḥ yat etat prakṛtau vairāgyamāñjasam anyā prakṛtiḥ triguṇā kāraṇa bhūtā kārya bhūtāḥ kārya kāraṇa bhūtā akārya kāraṇa bhūtā acetanā paratantrā ca iti anyaḥ puruṣaḥ nirguṇaḥ na kāryam na kāraṇam na kārya kāraṇam tad viparītaḥ cetanaḥ svatantraḥ ca iti tatas api prakṛtau layaḥ tatas ca anirmokṣa prasaṃgaḥ iti 
[II,315,v]	ucyate viparyayāt iti vartate tat iha abhisambhantsyāmaḥ tatas ca viparītam yat eva vairāgyam tuṣṭi kāṇḍa anupatitam prakṛti ādiṣu paratva abhimānaḥ tatas eva prakṛti layaḥ bhavati na anyasmāt athavā atrā api yat tat prakṛtau anya tva jñānam tatas eva mokṣaḥ na vairāgyāt kutas bhava bīja apratipakṣa tvāt iti hi uktam āmbhasikasya ca mokṣa prasaṃgāt tulyā hi asya nānātva saṃvid āsaṃga doṣa nivṛtteḥ na ca etat iṣṭam tasmāt yuktam etat vairāgyāt prakṛti layaḥ iti 
[II,316,i_II,316,iii]	āha atha dakṣiṇābandhaḥ kutas ucyate saṃsāraḥ bhavati rājasāt rāgāt yaḥ ayam dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya abhilāṣaḥ sa rāgaḥ tatra dṛṣṭa viṣaya rāgāt tad prāpti nirvartakam karma karoti tatas ca tatra upapadyate ānuśravika viṣaya abhilāṣāt agni hotra ādiṣu pravartate tatas ca svarga ādiṣu upapattiḥ bhavati asau dakṣiṇābandhaḥ dṛṣṭa ānuśravika viṣaya abhilāṣa dvāreṇa tad nirvartake karmaṇi pravartamānaḥ guṇa vṛtti vaicitryāt aniṣṭa phala nirvartakam api karma karoti evam mānuṣye gati antare yā upapattiḥ sarvā asau rāgāt 
[II,317,i_II,317,ii]	āha rāja saṃgrahaṇa ānarthakyam tad pūrvaka tvāt rāgasya rajaḥ nimittaḥ eva hi rāgaḥ tatra saṃsāraḥ rāgāt iti eva vaktavyam rājasa grahaṇam anarthakam iti ucyate na viṣaya viśeṣaṇa tvāt viṣaye yaḥ rāgaḥ sa saṃsāra hetuḥ iti asya arthasya jñāpana artham idam ucyate anyathā yaḥ yateḥ sāttvikaḥ yama niya ma dhyāna ādi anuṣṭhāna anurāgaḥ pravacana rāgaḥ vā saḥ api saṃsārāya syāt 
[II,317,iii_II,318,i]	aiśvaryāt avighātaḥ yat aṣṭaguṇam aiśvarya maṇima ādi prāk upadiṣṭam tasmāt sve sve viṣaye avighātaḥ utpadyate tad abhiratiḥ vaikārikaḥ bandhaḥ āha yadi tribhiḥ tribhiḥ nimittaiḥ vairāgya ādibhiḥ trividhaḥ bandhaḥ nirvartyate yat uktam ajñānāt bandhaḥ iti tat ayuktam bhāva antaram hi ajñānam atas phala antareṇa bhavitavyam iti 
[II,318,ii]	ucyate na mūla kāraṇa tvāt jñāna varjitānām hi bhāvānām yat phalam tatra ajñānam mūlam tad nimitta tvāt sarveṣām na hi jñāni vairāgya malam prakṛti layāya tathā itarāṇi para ma ṛṣya ādau adṛṣṭa tvāt vicitram kāryam ekasmāt kāraṇāt ayuktam iti vairāgya ādīni asādhāraṇāni pṛthak kalpyante sādhāraṇam tu ajñānam atas na kaścid doṣaḥ 
[II,318,iii_II,318,iv]	viparyayāt tad viparyāsaḥ anaiśvaryāt tu aṇima ādeḥ aṣṭavidhāt avighāta viparyayaḥ vighātaḥ bhavati tat evam etat aṣṭavidham dharma ādi vidhānam upādāya aṣṭavidham naimittikam upapadyate evam eṣa tattva sargaḥ bhāva sargaḥ ca vyākhyātaḥ etat ca vyaktasya rūpam pravṛttiḥ ca parikalpyate phalam idānīm vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,321,i_II,321,iii^1]	āha kim punar tat phalam iti ucyate yaḥ khalu eṣa pratyaya sargaḥ viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭi siddhi ākhyaḥ tat phalam iti vākya śeṣaḥ eṣaḥ iti vakṣyamāṇasya sammukhīkaraṇa artham ucyate pratyaya sargaḥ iti pratyayaḥ padārthaḥ lakṣaṇam iti paryāyāḥ pratyayānām sargaḥ pratyaya sargaḥ padārtha sargaḥ lakṣaṇa sargaḥ iti arthaḥ athavā pratyayaḥ buddhiḥ niścayaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ iti paryāyāḥ tasya sargaḥ ayam atas pratyaya sargaḥ pratyaya kāryam pratyaya vyāpāraḥ iti arthaḥ athavā pratyaya pūrvakaḥ sargaḥ pratyaya sargaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ iti uktaḥ katham evam hi śāstram mahat ādi viśeṣa antar sargaḥ buddhi pūrvaka tvāt utpanna kārya karaṇaḥ tu māhātmya śarīraḥ ekākinam ātmānam avekṣya abhidadhyau hantā aham putrān srakṣye ye me karma kariṣyanti ye mām param ca aparam ca jñāsyanti tasya abhidhyāyataḥ pañca mukhya srotasaḥ devāḥ prādurbabhūvuḥ teṣu utpanneṣu na tuṣṭim lebhe 
[II,321,iii^2]	tatas anye tiryaksrotasaḥ aṣṭāviṃśatiḥ prajajñe teṣu api asya matiḥ na eva tasthe atha apare nava ūrdhvasrotasaḥ devāḥ prādurbabhūvuḥ teṣu api utpanneṣu na eva kṛtārtham ātmānam mene tatas anye aṣṭau arvāk srotasaḥ utpeduḥ evam tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ abhidhyānāt utpannaḥ tasmāt pratyaya sargaḥ sa viparyaya ākhyaḥ aśakti ākhyaḥ tuṣṭi ākhyaḥ siddhi ākhyaḥ ca iti tatra aśreyasaḥ śreyaḥ tvena abhidhānam viparyayaḥ vaikalyāt asāmarthyam aśaktiḥ cikīrṣitāt ūnena nirvṛtiḥ tuṣṭiḥ yatheṣṭasya sādhanam siddhiḥ tat yathā dharma artha pravṛttaḥ agniṣṭoma ādīn parityajya saṃkaram kurvīta saḥ asya viparyayaḥ sādhana vaikalyāt asāmarthyam aśaktiḥ ādhāna mātra santoṣaḥ tuṣṭiḥ kṛtsnasya kriyā atiśeṣasya anuṣṭhānam siddhiḥ evam artha ādiṣu yojyam yaḥ ca ayam caturvidhaḥ phala viśeṣaḥ viparyaya ādiḥ ākhyātaḥ 
[II,323,i_II,323,ii]	guṇa vaiṣamya vimardāt tasya bhedāḥ tu pañcāśat guṇānām vaiṣamyam guṇa vaiṣamyam guṇa vaiṣamyam prādhānya guṇa bhāva yogaḥ iti arthaḥ guṇa vaiṣamyāt vimardaḥ guṇa vaiṣamya vimardaḥ pratyaya paryāyeṇa sattva rajaḥ tamasām itaretara bhāvaḥ tad nimittāḥ eṣām pratyayāṇām pañcāśat bhedāḥ bhavanti 
[II,325,i_II,325,ii^1]	katham iti ucyate pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ bhavanti tamaḥ mohaḥ mahāmohaḥ tāmisraḥ andhatāmisraḥ iti tatra aśreyasi pravṛttasya pratyaya avare śreyaḥ abhimāne ādyaḥ viparyayaḥ tamaḥ iti abhidhīyate bhautikeṣu ākāreṣu śiraḥ pāṇi ādiṣu ātma grahaḥ yaḥ ayam vyūḍha uraskaḥ sita daśanaḥ tāmra akṣaḥ pralamba bāhuḥ saḥ aham iti tathā śravaṇa sparśana rasana ghrāṇa vacana ādāna viharaṇa utsarga ānanda saṃkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāya lakṣaṇāsu karaṇa vṛttiṣu aham śrotā draṣṭā ca iti evamādiḥ ādya kāla pravṛttaḥ grahaḥ sarvasmāt avaraḥ mohaḥ iti ucyate katham punar ayam avaraḥ iti ucyate pūrvam śarīra indriya vyatiriktam upalabdhum icchan saukṣmyāt tad tat anadhigame bhūta ākāram abhūtam pramāṇam para parikalpitam vā anumanyeta svayam vā parikalpayet iti na mārgāt dūra apagatam etat 
[II,325,ii^2]	ayam tu pratyakṣa ādi gata utpatti sthiti vināśeṣu aneka rūpakeṣu kārya karaṇeṣu aham iti abhimanyate tasmāt pūrvasya āt avaraḥ bāhye tu viṣaye mama idam iti abhiniveśaḥ pūrvasmāt avaraḥ iti ucyate pūrvaḥ śarīriṇaḥ apratyakṣa tvāt karaṇa vṛtti aviśeṣāt vā ātma vṛtteḥ kārya karaṇe kuryāt ātma buddhim iti śakyam etat bhinna nimitta ākāra deśa svabhāva prayojana anugraha upaghāta utpatti sthiti vināśān ca mātṛ pitṛ putra bhrātṛ putra dāra gohirāya vasana ācchādana ādīn ayam akasmāt ātma tvena paśyati tasmāt pūrvasmāt avaraḥ 
[II,325,ii^3]	krodhaḥ caturthaḥ viparyayaḥ pūrvasmāt avaraḥ tāmisraḥ iti abhidhīyate katham punar ayam pūrvasmāt avaraḥ iti ucyate pūrvaḥ abhiniveśa pratiṣedham abhyanujānāti yadā asya bāhya dravya viyoge kaścid kuśala saṃsṛṣṭaḥ evam bravīti saṃsārasya buddhau avasthāpya vimṛśyatām yāvat ayam kālaḥ yadi kaścid priyeṇa aviyukta pūrvaḥ tasmāt āgama apāyiṣu bāhyeṣu dravyeṣu viduṣā na abhiniveśaḥ kāryaḥ iti tadā pratyāha satyam evam etat iti sannikṛṣṭaḥ tu viyoga kālaḥ iti na buddhiḥ avasthāpayitum śakyate krodha āviṣṭaḥ tu sva vikalpita grāha viparīta buddhiḥ aśakyaḥ daṇḍena apinivartayitum tasmāt pūrvasmāt avaraḥ maraṇa viṣādaḥ pañcamaḥ viparyayaḥ pūrvasmāt avaraḥ andhatāmistraḥ iti abhidhīyate katham punar ayam pūrvasmāt avaraḥ iti ucyate pūrvaḥ abhiniveśāt pratiṣidhyamānaḥ pratīkāram antatas jihvā akṣi nirīkṣataḥ na api tāvat ārabhate na tu brahma ādau stamba paryante saṃsāre sva nimitta niyatatama pātasya vināśasya kenacid pratīkāraḥ kṛtaḥ tasmāt aparihāryam maraṇam anuśocat pūru asmāt avaraḥ iti ete pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ bhavanti 
[II,325,iii_II,325,vi]	aśaktiḥ ca karaṇa vaikalyāt aṣṭāviṃśati bhedā bhavati iti anuvartate tatra bāhya karaṇa vaikalyam saha manasā ekādaśa prakāram saptadaśavidham buddhi vaikalyam ete aśakti bhedāḥ tuṣṭiḥ navadhā aṣṭadhā siddhiḥ evam caturvidhasya pratyaya sargasya guṇa vaiṣamya vimardena pañcāśat bhedāḥ bhavanti 
[II,329,i_II,329,v]	vistareṇa tu padārtha śata sahasram ānantyam vā lakṣaṇānām katham iti ucyate yasmāt bhedaḥ tamasaḥ aṣṭavidhaḥ ye ete pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ vyākhyātāḥ teṣu tamasaḥ aṣṭavidhaḥ bhedaḥ katham para vijñānam āśritya pravṛttasya aṣṭāsu prakṛtiṣu aparāsu para abhimāna grahāt mohasya ca kim aṣṭavidhaḥ bhedaḥ iti caśabdāt kārya karaṇa sāmarthye aṣṭavidhe aṇimāt au aham iti pratyayaḥ 
[II,329,vi_II,330,iv]	daśavidhaḥ mahāmohaḥ mātṛ pitṛ bhrātṛ svasṛpatnī putra duhitṛ guru mitra upakāri lakṣaṇe daśavidhe kuṭumbe yaḥ ayam mama iti abhiniveśaḥ dṛṣṭa ānuśravikeṣu vā śabda ādiṣu iti apare sa daśavidhaḥ mahāmohaḥ parisaṃkhyāyate tāmisraḥ aṣṭādaśadhā aṣṭavidhe kārya karaṇa sāmarthye daśavidhe ca kuṭumbe viṣayeṣu vā yaḥ pratihanyamānasya āveśaḥ tathā bhavati andhatāmisraḥ tathā iti sāmānya atideśa arthaḥ andhatāmisraḥ aṣṭādaśadhā eva iti katham asau api aṣṭavidhāt kārya karaṇa sāmarthyāt daśavidhāt ca kuṭumbāt pratyavasānasya viṣādaḥ 
[II,330,v]	evam ete pañca viparyaya bhedāḥ sva lakṣaṇataḥ viṣaya viśeṣāḥ lakṣitāḥ tatra api ca aṣṭāsu prakṛtiṣu sattva rajaḥ tamasām saṃhata vivikta pariṇata vyasta samastānām paratva abhimāna bhedāt ekaikā prakṛtiḥ pañcadaśa bhedā atas eva te aṣṭau pañcadaśa viṃśam śatam ca bhavanti yathā mokṣe pravṛttasya evam dharma kāmeṣu api ekaḥ padārthaḥ vistareṇa parisaṃkhyāyamānaḥ ananta bhedaḥ sampadyate nidarśana mātram etat ācāryeṇa kṛtam evam aśakti ādiṣu api lakṣaṇa antareṣu yojyam sā iyam avidyā pañca parvā sa prapañcā vyākhyātā tad anantara uddiṣṭān aśakti bhedān vakṣyāmaḥ 
[II,332,i_II,332,iii]	āha ativyāsa abhihitam idam iti na asmākam buddhau avatiṣṭhate tasmāt viparyaya uktam bheda abhidhānam parityajya vaktavyam katham aśaktiḥ aṣṭāviṃśati bheda iti ucyate ekādaśa indriya vadhāḥ saha buddhi vadhaiḥ aśaktiḥ uddiṣṭā indriyāṇām vadhāḥ indriya vadhāḥ sva saṃskāra viṣaya yogāt prakarṣa āpannena tamasā grahaṇa rūpasya sattvasya abhibhavāt sva viṣayeṣu apravṛttayaḥ tat yathā bādhiryam āndhyam aghra tvam mūka tā jaḍa tā ca yā unmāda kauṣṭhya kauṇyāni klaibya udāvarta paṅgutāḥ 
[II,332,iv_II,333,i]	tatra bādhiryam śrotrasya āndhyam cakṣuṣaḥ aghra tvam nāsikāyāḥ mūka tā vācaḥ jaḍatā rasanasya unmādaḥ manasaḥ kauṣṭhyam tvacaḥ kauṇyam pāṇeḥ klaibyam upasthasya udāvartaḥ pāyoḥ paṅgu tā pādayoḥ iti evam indriya vadhāḥ ekādaśa anye tu saptadaśa vadhāḥ buddheḥ viparyayāt tuṣṭi siddhīnām 
[II,333,ii_II,334,i]	tatra tuṣṭayaḥ prakṛti ādyāḥ vakṣyamāṇāḥ tāsām dvividhaḥ viparyayaḥ avyutpannasya yoga dharmeṇa tasyām bhūmau apravṛttiḥ vyutpannasya ca uttara bhūmi aparijñānāt pūrvasyām bhūmau akṣema rūpeṇa grahaṇam ātma vidaḥ vā sarvāsu bhūmiṣu teṣu yat pūrvam tad aśakti bhāva abhipretam yat madhyamam tadāpekṣikam katham tanmātra bhūmi avasthaḥ hi yogya smita ādi bhūmi anavajayāt tuṣṭaḥ mahābhūta atikramāt siddhaḥ tathā vijita asmitā rūpaḥ mahat ādi avasthā apekṣayā tuṣṭaḥ pūrva bhūmi apekṣayā siddhaḥ evam mahat avasthaḥ pradhāna apekṣayā pūrva apekṣayā ca pradhāna avasthaḥ puruṣa apekṣayā pūrva apekṣayā ca guṇa puruṣa antara jñaḥ tu siddhaḥ eva tasmāt avyutpannasya ambhaḥ prabhṛtiṣu navān ambhaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ buddhi vadhāḥ tāraka ādi viparyayeṇa aṣṭa avatāraka ādayaḥ eṣā khalva śaktiḥ aṣṭāviṃśati bhedā tuṣṭiḥ tu sannihita viṣaya santoṣāt cikīrṣitāt arthāt ūnena nivṛttiḥ sāmānyatas ekā eva pratyartham anantā śatena tuṣṭaḥ sahasreṇa iti śāstre tu bāhya ādhyātmikānām sukha duḥkha mohānām prāptiṣu apagameṣu vācā avyavasthya lakṣaṇāḥ upāya nava tvān nava tuṣṭayaḥ bhavanti 
[II,335,i_II,335,iii^1]	tāsām ādhyātmikyaḥ catasraḥ prakṛti upādāna kāla bhāgya ākhyāḥ ādhyātmikī iti śarīra śarīriṇoḥ viśeṣam upalipsamānena yoginā yat anātmani ātma buddhiḥ avasthāpyate sā khalu ādhyātmikī siddhiḥ tuṣṭiḥ santoṣaḥ kṣemaḥ iti arthaḥ tāsām prakṛti ākhyā yadā vīta avītaiḥ pradhānam adhigamya tat pūrvaka tvam ca mahat ādīnām vikārāṇām ānantyāt ca pradhāna ātmanaḥ kṛtsnasya mahat ādi bhāvena vipariṇāma asambhavāt eka deśasya aprakṛti vikāra bhūtasya bhoktṛ tvam akartṛ tvam ca adhyavasya saṅga dveṣa nivṛttim labhate sādyā tuṣṭiḥ ambhaḥ iti abhidhīyate kasmāt amitam hi pradhāna tattvam bhāti jagat bīja bhūta tvāt mahat ādi bhāva pariṇāmena nyūnasya eka deśasya ātmanaḥ eva āpūrāt tad vyatirekeṇa ca anyasya eka deśasya ubhaya dharmiṇaḥ bhoktṛ bhūtasya sadbhāvāt saṃprakṣālane api cāpa saṃhṛtam vaiśvarūpyasya anucchedāt tathā ca śāstram āha ambhaḥ iti guṇa liṅga sannicayam eva adhikurute guṇāḥ ca sattva rajaḥ tamāṃsi liṅgam ca mahat ādi atra sannihitam bhavati 
[II,335,iii^2]	tat idam pradhānam amitam bhāti amitam upalabhyate iti ambhaḥ sa khalu ayam yogī pradhāna lakṣaṇām bhūmim avajitya tat mahimnā ca tat aśūnyam dṛṣṭvā vyatiriktasya padārtha antarasya abhāvam manyamānaḥ tām eva bhūmim kaivalyam iti gṛhṇāti bhinne ca dehe prakṛtau layam gacchati tatas ca punar āvartate tasyām ca tuṣṭau anye sapta mahat ādikāraṇinaḥ avaruddhāḥ draṣṭavyāḥ tatra yathā prādhānikasya puruṣe na asti vijñānam evam itareṣām uttareṣu tattveṣu mahat kāraṇinaḥ pradhāne asmitā kāraṇinaḥ mahati tanmātra kāraṇinaḥ ahaṃkāre tad eka deśāḥ ca eṣām bhoktāraḥ pūrvavat atra api ca sattva ādīnām saṃhata vivikta pariṇata vyasta samastānām bhedāt avidyā avaccheda ānantyam avaseyam 
[II,337,i_II,337,ii]	āha tuṣṭi avidyayoḥ abhedaḥ lakṣaṇa eka tvāt aṣṭāsu prakṛtiṣu ātma buddhiḥ tuṣṭiḥ tat eva ca tamaḥ iti avidyā kāṇḍe nirdiṣṭam tasmāt padārtha saṃkaraḥ iti ucyate na pratyaya viśeṣāt tamaḥ pradhāna puruṣa upadeśe sati pratyaya nirdidha ārayiṣayā tayoḥ pradhānam eva jyāyaḥ na puruṣaḥ iti abhiniviśeta tuṣṭiḥ tu kim param iti āśritya pravṛttaḥ pradhāna jñāna mātre santoṣāt padārtha antaram vijñātum eva na ādriyate kim ca prahāṇa viśeṣāt nirūḍha mūlaḥ hi anātmani ātma grahaḥ jñāna uttara kāla bhāvanayā prahātavyaḥ tamaḥ bahula tvāttamaḥ iti abhidhīyate pelavaḥ tu sattva bahulaḥ darśana praṇayaḥ tuṣṭiḥ kiṃca tattva abhijayāt vijita bhūmikasya hi yoginaḥ tad māhātmya vaśīkṛta tvāt bhūmi antare pravṛttiḥ tuṣṭiḥ itarasya tu abhiniveśa mātram eva iti anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ tasmāt na padārtha saṃkaraḥ iti vyākhyātā prakṛti ākhyā tuṣṭiḥ 
[II,338,i]	yadā tu sati api prakṛti sāmarthye na anapekṣya yathāsvam upādānam bhāvānām utpattiḥ sambhavati prakṛti aviśeṣe sarva kālam utpatti prasaṃgāt prakṛti kṛtyam eva idam viśvam iti abhyupagacchataḥ tat aviśeṣāt goḥ puruṣāt utpatti prasaṃgaḥ puruṣasya vā mahiṣāt kim ca jāti abheda prasaṃgāt prakṛti kṛtyam idam viśvam iti abhyupagacchataḥ jāti bhedaḥ na syāt tad aviśeṣāt dṛṣṭam tu upādānāt jāti anuvidhānam bhāvānām tasmāt tat eva kāraṇa tvena parikalpayitum nyāyyam upādāna eka deśaḥ eva ca kārya kāraṇa vidha ātmā bhoktā iti etasmāt darśanāt saṅga dveṣa nivṛttim labhate sā dvitīyā tuṣṭiḥ salilam iti abhidhīyate katham punar etat salilam sati upādāne vikāraḥ līyate iti tathā ca kṛtvā śāsram āha salilam salilam iti vaikārika upanipātam eva adhikurute sati tasmin līyate jagat iti sa khalu ayam yogī pārthivān avajitya tat mahimnā jagat aśūnyam dṛṣṭvā padārtha antarasya abhāvam manyamānaḥ tām eva bhūmim kaivalyam iti gṛhṇāti bhinne ca dehe pṛthivī ādiṣu līyate tatas ca punar āvartate 
[II,339,i^1]	yadā ca sati upādāna sāmarthye na tāvatā eva bhāvānām prādurbhāvaḥ kim tarhi sannihita sādhanānām api kālam pratyapekṣā bhavati kāla viśeṣāt bījāt aṅkuraḥ jāyate aṅkurāt nālam nālāt kāṇḍam kāṇḍāt prasavaḥ ityādi anyathā tu upādānānām sannidhāna mātrāt kṣaṇena eva amīṣām avasthā viśeṣāṇām abhivyaktiḥ syāt kiṃca kāla viparyayeṇa utpatti prasaṃgāt na ca etat iṣṭam kim ca tad anabhidhānāt dṛśyante ca prāṇinām kāla anurūpāḥ svābhāva āhāra vihāra vyavasthāḥ tasmāt asau eva kāraṇam 
[II,339,i^2_II,339,ii]	tad eka deśaḥ ca aprakṛti vikāra bhūtaḥ bhoktā iti etasmāt darśanāt saṃga dveṣa nivṛttim labhate sā tṛtīyā tuṣṭiḥ oghaḥ iti abhidhīyate katham punar ayam kālaḥ oghaḥ iti ucyate salila ogha vat sarva abhyāvahanāt tat yathā salila oghaḥ tṛṇam kāṣṭham aśmānam prāṇinam vā sva mūrti saṃsṛṣṭam sarvam eva abhyāvahati evam ayam kālaḥ garbhāt bālyam bālyāt kaumāram kaumārāt yauvanam yauvanāt sthāviryam sthāviryāt maraṇam tathā bījāt mūlam mūlāt aṅkuram iti vahati tathā ca āha yām eva prathamām rātrim garbhe bhavati pūruṣaḥ saṃprasthitaḥ tām bhavati sa gacchan na nivartate tasmāt ogha sāmānyāt oghaḥ kālaḥ sa khalu ayam yogī kālam avajitya padārtha antara abhāvam manyamānaḥ tām eva bhūmim kaivalyam iti manyate dehabhede ca kālam anupraviśati tatas ca punar āvartate 
[II,340,i^1]	yadā tu sati api kāla sāmarthye bhāvānām utpattiḥ bhāgyān apekṣate kasmāt tad sannidhāne api aprādurbhāvāt sati api sādhana sāmarthye kāla viśeṣe ca kasyacid utpattiḥ bhavati kasyacid na iti tasmāt asti kāraṇa antaram yat apekṣya bhāvānām utpattiḥ anutpattiḥ ca kim ca abhyutthāna anupapatti prasaṃgāt kāla mātrāt phalam bhavati iti etat icchataḥ śāstra ukteṣu kriyā viśeṣeṣu abhiṣecana vrata upavāsa agnihotra ādiṣu abhyutthānam na syāt kasmāt ānarthakyāt asti ca tasmāt na kāla nimittā bhāvānām utpattiḥ kim ca tad anuvidhānāt dṛśyante khalu api prakṛti upādāna kāla aviśeṣe api bhāgya viśeṣāt phala viśeṣāḥ tasmāt tad saṃkāraḥ eva kāraṇam 
[II,340,i^2]	tad eka deśaḥ ca aprakṛti vikāra bhūtaḥ bhoktā iti etasmāt darśanāt saṃga dveṣa nivṛttim labhate sā caturthī tuṣṭiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ iti abhidhīyate katham punar vṛṣṭiḥ iti ucyate sarva sattva āpyāyanāt yathā hi śīrṇānām api tṛṇa latā ādīnām vṛṣṭim prāpya punar āpyāyanam bhavati evam eva sarveṣām prāṇinām bhāgya vipariṇāmāt punar āpyāyanam bhavati tasmāt vṛṣṭi sāmyāt bhāgya ākhyā tuṣṭiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ iti abhidhīyate śāstram api āha vṛṣṭiḥ vṛṣṭiḥ iti śriyaḥ eva upanipātam adhikurute sā hi vṛṣṭi vat sarvam āpyāyati iti sa khalu ayam yogī bhāgyāni avajitya tat mahimnā jagat aśūnyam dṛṣṭvā padārtha antarasya abhāvam manyamānaḥ tām eva bhūmim kaivalyam iti gṛhṇāti sa tasyām eva dehabhede līyate tatas ca punar āvartate iti 
[II,341,i_II,342,i]	āha kāla bhāgyayoḥ apratipattiḥ samākhyā parijñānāt prakṛti ātmakasya tāvat yoginaḥ aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ viṣayaḥ iti uktam purastāt upādāna ātmakasya ca pṛthivī ādīni mahābhūtāni kāla bhāgyayoḥ tu na tathā uktam tasmāt vaktavyam kasya tattvasya eṣā samākhyā iti ucyate na ukta tvāt prāk eva etat apadiṣṭam na kālaḥ nāma kaścid padārthaḥ asti kim tarhi kriyāsu kāla saṃjñā tāḥ ca karaṇa vṛttiḥ iti pratipāditam na ca anyā vṛttiḥ vṛttimataḥ tasmāt kāraṇa caitanya pratijñaḥ kāla ātmakaḥ iti bhāgya saṃjñā tu dharma adharmayoḥ tau ca buddhi dharmau iti prāc apadiṣṭam tasmāt bhāgya vādī buddhi caitanikaḥ iti 
[II,342,ii_II,342,iii]	āha na tuṣṭi antara tvāt prakṛti tvāt mahān pūrvam prakṛti ākhyāyām tuṣṭau avaruddhaḥ tasya idānīm tuṣṭi antara tvena parikalpanam na ati samañjasam iti ucyate mahān tarhi pūrva tuṣṭi viṣaya bhāvāt apakṛṣyate iti kārya karaṇa vṛtti kriyā rūpām vṛttimat dyotyām parikalpya tasyām kāla tvamayam āha mahataḥ ca rūpam dharma ādikam mahataḥ artha antaram bhāgyam iti bhāgyavān athavā bāhyaḥ eva ayam kālaḥ karma kāraṇam nirdiśyate tatra ca anye api sva mati parikalpita padārtha antarātma bhāva grahāḥ eva iti sāṅkhyāḥ pravādinaḥ pratikṣiptāḥ boddhavyāḥ iti 
[II,342,iv_II,343,i]	aparaḥ āha prakṛti caitanikaḥ pradhāna bhāvāśa ādi upādāna kāla bhāgya vādinaḥ mahat ahaṅkāra tanmātra vādinaḥ iti tat etat apasiddha tvāt ayuktam na hi mahat ahaṅkāra tanmātra lakṣaṇāḥ prakṛtayaḥ upādāna kāla bhāgya bhāvena prasiddhāḥ tasmāt idam api ayuktam evam etāḥ ādhyātmikyaḥ catasraḥ tuṣṭayaḥ bāhyāḥ viṣaya uparamāt pañca ca nava tuṣṭayaḥ abhihitāḥ 
[II,343,ii]	caśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ avyutpanna ātma vicārasya yoginaḥ viṣaya doṣa darśana mātrāt saṃga doṣa nivṛttiḥ bāhyā tuṣṭiḥ tatra yadā arjana doṣam avagacchati na tāvat sarvasya abhijātiḥ asti iti arthinā avaśyam viṣaya arjane vartitavyam teṣām asvābhāvika tvāt kvacid eva avasthitiḥ iti uktam prāk kim ca sa pratyanīka tvāt svābhāvikam avasthānam viṣayāṇām aparikalpya api yadā pratigraha ādibhiḥ arjanam pratyādriyate tat api ayuktam kutas sa pratyanīka tvāt evam api na asti kaścid apratyanīka viṣaya upārjanāya iti tad vighāte avaśyam prayatitavyam sa ca yadi pratiyatamānaḥ pratyanīki vighātam kuryāt para upaghātena ātma anugraha anuṣṭhānāt śāstra virodhaḥ yasmāt āha na tad parasya sandadhyāt pratikūlam yadātmanaḥ eṣa saṃkṣepataḥ dharmaḥ kāmāt anyaḥ pravartate 
[II,343,iii_II,344,i]	punar api āha prāṇinām upaghātena yaḥ arthaḥ samupajāyate saḥ anapekṣaiḥ prahātavyaḥ loka antara vighāta kṛt tasmāt saṃghāta mātra tvāt sattva ādīnām ghaṭa ādi vat ābrahmaṇaḥ parijñāya dehānām anavasthitim satyam sadbhiḥ ādīptam tṛṇa ulkā capalam sukham su dṛḍhaiḥ na nipātavyam duḥkhaiḥ deha antara udbhavaiḥ atha punar ayam pratyanīkaiḥ vihanyate tatas asya viṣaya abhāvaḥ sukha artham ca pravṛttasya bhūyiṣṭham duḥkham eva iti etasmāt darśanāt mādhyasthyam labhate sā pañcamī tuṣṭiḥ sutāram iti abhidhīyate katham punar sutāram iti ucyate sukham anena upāyena taranti viṣaya saṃkaṭam iti sutāram 
[II,345,i]	yadā tu yogī pūrva doṣa adhigame abhijātyāḥ vā yatna arjita viṣaya tve sati rakṣā doṣam upanyasyati katham bhoktṛ bhogya bhāva avyatirekāt sarva prāṇi sādhāraṇāḥ viṣayāḥ tasmāt teṣām rakṣā vidheyā tasyām ca pravartamānaḥ yadi param uparundhyāt tadā pūrva ukta doṣaḥ atha ātmānam viṣaya abhāvaḥ rātrindivam ca tad ekāgra manasaḥ sukha artham pravṛtasya bhūyiṣṭham duḥkham eva iti etasmāt darśanāt mādhyasthyam labhate sā ṣaṣṭhī tuṣṭiḥ supāram iti abhidhīyate katham punar supāram iti ucyate sukham anena pāram viṣaya arṇavasya prayānti iti 
[II,345,ii]	yadā tu sati pūrva doṣe sati vā grāma nagara nigama sanniveśa ādi upāya anuṣṭhānāt vā kṛta viṣaya rakṣaḥ yogī kṣaya doṣam upanyasyati katham yena dravyeṇa mohāt varantum icchanti dehinaḥ tat eva eṣām vināśi tvāt bhavati arati kāraṇam yatna upāttāḥ su guptāḥ ca viṣayāḥ viṣaya eṣiṇām paśyatām eva naśyanti budbudāḥ salile yathā na tat asti jagati asmin bhūtam sthāvara jaṅgamam pratyakṣataḥ anumānāt vā vināśaḥ yasya na īkṣyate tasmāt vināśiṣu āsaktānām putra dāra gṛha ādiṣu mama iti buddhim yatnena buddhimān vinivartayet 
[II,346,i_II,347,ii]	iti etasmāt darśanāt mādhyasthyam labhate sā saptamī tuṣṭiḥ sunetram iti ucyate katham punar sunetram iti ucyate sukham anena ātmānam kaivalya avasthām nayanti iti sunetram yadā tu satsu pūrva doṣeṣu prasaṅga doṣam upanyasyati katham prāpta viṣayāṇām indriyāṇām tad abhilāṣāt nivṛtiḥ tad sukham viṣaya jighṛkṣayā ca duḥkham prāptiḥ api eṣām anupaśāntaye tad upabhoga kauśalāya ca yasmāt āha yadā prabandhāt viṣayī viṣayān upasevate tadā asya itaḥ tu abhiprāyaḥ sutarām saṃpravartate atas api yena puruṣaḥ śamayet vaḍavānalam na indriyāṇi upabhogena viṣayebhyaḥ nivartayet tasmāt viṣaya samparkam asamartham nivartane indriyāṇām parijñāya nirāsaṅga matiḥ caret iti etasmāt darśanāt mādhyasthyam labhate sā aṣṭamī tuṣṭiḥ sumārīcam iti ucyate katham sumārīcam iti ucyate arcateḥ pūjā arthasya śobhanam arcitam viṣaya saṃga nivṛttasya yoginaḥ avasthānam bhavati 
[II,347,iii]	yadā tu pūrva doṣeṣu hiṃsā doṣam upanyasyati katham anupahatya anya bhūtāni viṣaya bhoga anupapatteḥ upabhogaḥ hi nāma manojñābhyavahāraḥ strī sevā haya gaja nara ādibhiḥ yānam iti evamādi tatra manojñā abhyavahāra cikīrṣuṣā tad aṅgānām gaḥ aja avibalī varda strī puruṣa ādīnām avaśyam upaghātaḥ kāryaḥ anupaghāte vā viṣaya anupapatti prasaṃgaḥ striyam āsevamānena anyāsām strīṇām mātṛ pitṛ bhrātṛ prabhṛtīnām ca anyathā tad abhāvaḥ haya ādīnām tasmāt upabhoga arthinā avaśyam anya upaghātaḥ kāryaḥ nihita daṇḍena vā viṣaya upabhogaḥ tyājyaḥ iti āha ca yathā yathā hi viṣayaḥ vṛddhim gṛhṇāti dehinām apaghātaḥ tad aṅgānām tathā eva asya vivardhate tasmāt anicchan anyeṣām prāṇinām deha pīḍanam santoṣeṇa eva varteta tyakta sarva paricchadaḥ satya vācaḥ praśāntasya sarva bhūtāni anicchataḥ bhāva andhakāra anta jñānam acireṇa pravartate 
[II,348,i_II,349,i]	iti etasmāt darśanāt mādhyasthyam labhate sā navamī tuṣṭiḥ uttamā abhayam iti apadiśyate katham uttamam hi prāṇinām sarvebhyaḥ hiṃsā bhayam iti tad apagamāt uttamā abhayam iti āha arjana rakṣaṇa lakṣaṇayoḥ api tuṣṭyoḥ para upaghāta doṣāḥ apadiṣṭaḥ asyām api ca tatra katham anayoḥ viśeṣaḥ pratipattavyaḥ iti 
[II,349,ii]	ucyate na viṣaya bhedāt tatra yeṣām arjana rakṣaṇe pratyādriyate viṣayī tad arthinā pratyanīkānām avaśyam abhighātaḥ anuṣṭhātavyaḥ iti ādau uktam iha tu yeṣām eva arjana rakṣaṇe tad anupaghātena aśakyaḥ viṣaya upabhogaḥ iti etat vivakṣitam tasmāt asaṃkīrṇam etat iti evam ambhaḥ prabhṛtayaḥ nava viṣayebhyaḥ saṃga dveṣa nivṛtti hetavaḥ vyākhyātāḥ te jñāna virahitānām yoginām tuṣṭi śabda vācya tām labhante jñāninām tu vairāgya parva saṃjñitā svāsu svāsu tattva bhūmiṣu siddhāḥ eva iti 
[II,352,i_II,352,iii]	āha prāk apadiṣṭam aṣṭadhā siddhiḥ iti tat idānīm abhidhīyatām iti ucyate ūhaḥ śabdaḥ adhyayanam duḥkha vighātāḥ trayaḥ suhṛd prāptiḥ dānañca siddhayaḥ aṣṭau tatra ūhaḥ nāma yadā pratyakṣa anumāna āgama vyatirekeṇa abhipretam artham vicāraṇa abalena eva pratipadyate sādyā siddhiḥ tārakam iti apadiśyate tārayati saṃsāra arṇavāt iti tārakam yadā tu svayam pratipattau pratihanyamānaḥ guru upadeśāt pratipadyate sā dvitīyā siddhiḥ sutāram iti apadiśyate katham sukham anenadya tve api bhava saṅkaṭāt taranti iti yadā tu anya upadeśāt api asamarthaḥ pratipattum adhyayanena sādhayati sā tṛtīyā siddhiḥ tārayantam iti apadiśyate tat etat tāraṇa kriyāyāḥ adya tve api avyāvṛta tvāt mahā viṣaya tvāt tārayantam iti apadiśyate te ete trayaḥ sādhana upāyaiḥ ābrāhmaṇaḥ prāṇinaḥ abhipretam artham prāpnuvanti āha ca sākṣātkṛta dharmāṇaḥ ṛṣayaḥ babhūvuḥ te aparebhyaḥ asākṣāt kṛta dharmebhyaḥ upadeśena mantrān samprāhuḥ upadeśāya glāyantaḥ apare bilma grahaṇāya imam grantham samāmnāsiṣuḥ vedan ca vedāṅgāni ca iti bilmam bhāsanam samyak pratibhāsāya viśiṣṭaḥ saṃketaḥ uktaḥ eṣām tu sādhana upāyānām pratyanīka pratiṣedhāya duḥkha vighāta trayam duḥkhāni trīṇi ādhyātmika ādīni 
[II,352,iv^1]	tatra ca ādhyātmikānām vāta ādīnām siddhi pratyanīkānām āyurveda kriyā anuṣṭhānena vighātam kṛtvā pūrveṣām trayāṇām anyatamena sādhayati sā caturthī siddhiḥ pramodam iti abhidhīyate katham nivṛtta rogāḥ hi prāṇinaḥ pramodante iti kṛtvā yadā tu ādhibhautikānām mānuṣa ādi nimittānām siddhi pratyanīkānām sāma ādinā yati dharma anuguṇena vā upāyena pūrveṣām trayāṇām anyatamena sādhayati sā pañcamī siddhiḥ pramuditam iti abhidhīyate katham anudvignaḥ hi pramuditaḥ iti kṛtvā yadā tu śīta ādīni ādhi daivikāni dvandvāni siddhi pratyanīkāni svadharma anurodhena pratihatya pūrveṣām trayāṇām anyatamena sādhayati sā ṣaṣṭhī siddhiḥ moda nāmam iti abhidhīyate 
[II,352,iv^2_II,353,ii]	katham dvandvānupahatāḥ hi prāṇinaḥ modante iti kṛtvā suhṛd prāptiḥ yadā tu kṛśalam saṃspṛṣṭam sat mitram āśritya sandeha nivṛttim labhate sā ramyakam iti saptamī siddhiḥ apadiśyate ramyaḥ hi loke sat mitra samparkaḥ tasya saṃjñāyām ramyam eva ramyakam dānam yadā tu daurbhāgyam dānena atītya pūrveṣām trayāṇām anyatamena sādhayati sa aṣṭāmī siddhiḥ sadā apramuditam iti abhidhīyate subhagaḥ hi sadā pramuditaḥ bhavati tasmāt daurbhāgya nivṛttiḥ sadā pramuditam iti evam etāḥ siddhayaḥ aṣṭau vyākhyātāḥ etāsām saṃśrayeṇa abhipretam artham yatas saṃsādhayanti iti atas pūrva ācārya āgatam mārgamārurukṣuḥ tad pravaṇaḥ syāt iti āha kaḥ punar atra hetuḥ yena puruṣa artha tva aviśeṣe sati guṇānām sarva siddhi nimittam tu anubhavati iti ucyate yasmāt siddheḥ pūrvaḥ aṅkuśaḥ trividhaḥ 
[II,353,iii]	sādhya pratipatti sāmarthya sāmānyam aṅgīkṛtya āha siddheḥ iti pūrvaḥ viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭi lakṣaṇaḥ aṃkuśaḥ iva aṃkuśaḥ nivartana sāmānyāt nitya pravṛttasya api pradhānāt siddhi srotasaḥ viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭi pratibandhāt sarva prāṇiṣu apravṛttiḥ bhavati viparyayāt tāvat sthāvareṣu te hi mukhyāḥ srotasaḥ viparyaya ātmānaḥ aśakteḥ tiryakṣu te hi tiryaksrotasaḥ aśakti ātmānaḥ tuṣṭiḥ deveṣu te hi ūrdhvasrotasaḥ tuṣṭi ātmānaḥ mānuṣāḥ tu arvāksrotasaḥ saṃsiddhi ātmānaḥ tasmāt te eva tāraka ādiṣu pravartante sattva rajaḥ tamasām ca aṅga aṅgi bhāva niyamāt viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭibhiḥ pratihanyate iti na sarveṣām sarvadā siddhiḥ bhavati atas etat uktam siddheḥ pūrvaḥ aṅkuśāḥ trividhaḥ iti 
[II,355,i]	yathā ca sidddheḥ viparyaya aśakti tuṣṭayaḥ pratipakṣāḥ evam siddhiḥ api viparyaya ādīnām sā hi utpannā sarvān etān nivartayati katham aviparīta jñānam viparyayam atīta anāgata vartamāneṣu sannikṛṣṭeṣu viprakṛṣṭeṣu indriya grāhyeṣu atīndriyeṣu ca apratighātāt aśaktim puruṣasya prakṛti vikāra vyatiriktasya darśanāt sarvāsu bhūmiṣu tuṣṭim evam etāni srotāṃsi prāṇa ādayaḥ karma yonayaḥ ca vyākhyātāḥ eteṣām mārge avasthāpanāt parām siddhi kaivalya lakṣaṇām acireṇa prāpnoti āha ca yonīnām sa pramāṇānām samyak mārge niyojanāt srotasām ca viśuddha tvāt nirāsaṅga matiḥ caret iti 
[II,358,i_II,358,vi]	evam yat pūrvam apadiṣṭam saṃyoga kṛtaḥ sargaḥ iti tat vyākhyātam atra idānīm ācāryāṇām vipratipattiḥ dharma ādīnām śarīram antareṇa anutpatteḥ śarīrasya ca dharma ādi abhāve nimittantarā sambhavāt ubhayam idam anādi tasmāt eka rūpaḥ eva ayam yathā eva adya tve tathā eva atikrāntāsu anāgatāsu kāla koṭiṣu sargaḥ iti ācāryaḥ āha na etat evam kim tarhi prāc pradhāna pravṛtteḥ dharma adharmayoḥ asambhavaḥ buddhi dharma tvāt tasyāḥ ca pradhāna vikāra tvāt tatas tad vyatiriktam śabda ādi upalabdhi guṇa lakṣaṇam guṇa puruṣa antara upalabdhi lakṣaṇam ca artham uddiśya sattva ādayaḥ mahat ahaṅkāra tanmātra indriya bhūta tvena avasthāya parama ṛṣi hiraṇyagarbha ādīnām śarīram utpādayanti ṣaṣ siddhi kṣaya kāla uttaram tu guṇa vimarda vaicitryāt rajaḥ tamaḥ vṛtti anupāti saṃsāra cakram pravṛttam na vinā bhāvaiḥ liṅgam deva manuṣya tiryagbhāvena vyavatiṣṭhate iti vākya śeṣaḥ na vinā liṅgena bhāva saṃsiddhiḥ saṃsiddhiḥ atra niṣpattiḥ abhipretā liṅga ākhyaḥ bhāva ākhyaḥ tasmāt dvividhaḥ pravartate sargaḥ 
[II,358,vii]	saḥ ayam liṅga ākhyaḥ bhāva ākhyaḥ ca ṣaṣ siddhi kṣaya kālāt ūrdhvam bhavati guṇa samanantaram tu adhikāra lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt dvidhā sargaḥ adhikāra lakṣaṇaḥ bhāva ākhyaḥ ca yeṣām tu dharma adharma śarīrayoḥ paryāyeṇa hetu hetum at bhāvaḥ teṣām kāraṇam asti avyaktam iti atra prativihitam ye api ca sāṃkhyāḥ evam āhuḥ dharma adharma adhikāra vaśāt pradhānasya pravṛttiḥ iti teṣām anyatara parikalpanā narthakyam iti katham yadi tāvat adhikāraḥ eva ayam pradhāna pravṛttaye alam kim dharma adharmābhyām atha tāvat antareṇa adhikārasya pradhāna pravṛttau asāmarthyam evam api kim adhikāreṇa tayoḥ eva pravṛtti sāmarthyāt tasmāt adhikāra bhāva nimittaḥ dvidhā sargaḥ tatra yathā idam śarīram avibhaktam dharma artha kāma mokṣa lakṣaṇāsu kriyāsu vibhaktam bhavet iti atas pāṇi ādi vikalpaḥ asya bhavati evam sattva sargaḥ api avibhaktaḥ dharma artha kāma mokṣa lakṣaṇāsu kriyāsu samarthaḥ bhavet iti 
[II,362,i_II,362,iii]	aṣṭa vikalpaḥ daivaḥ tairyagyonaḥ ca pañcadhā bhavati mānuṣyaḥ ca ekavidhaḥ aṣṭau vikalpāḥ asya saḥ ayam aṣṭa vikalpaḥ aṣṭa prakāraḥ aṣṭa bhedaḥ iti arthaḥ tat yathā brahma prajāpati indra pitṛ gandharva nāga rakṣaḥ piśācāḥ tairyagyonaḥ ca pañcadhā bhavati paśu mṛga pakṣi sarīsṛpa sthāvarāḥ mānuṣyaḥ ca ekavidhaḥ ca jāti antara anupapatteḥ āha kim etāvān eva bhūta sarga vikalpaḥ āhosvit anyaḥ asti iti ucyate vikalpa antaram asti eteṣām eva sthānānām antar gaṇa bhedāt ayam tu āhosvit anyaḥ asti iti ucyate vikalpa antaram asti eteṣām eva sthānām antara gaṇa bhedāt ayam tu samāsatas bhautikaḥ sargaḥ kim upadiṣṭaḥ ita vākya śeṣaḥ tatra devānām sādhya marut rudra ādi bhedāt tiraścām grāmya araṇya ādi bhedāt mānuṣāṇām ca brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viś śūdra bhedāt udbhidbhedaḥ ca vistareṇa apadiśyamānaḥ ānantyam āpādayet tasmāt samāsatas bhūta sargaḥ apadiśyate 
[II,363,i_II,363,iii]	āha vikalpa antara vacanam srotaḥ bhedāt daiva mānuṣa tairyagyonāḥ iti trividhaḥ bhūtānām vikalpaḥ upadiśyate srotāṃsi tu catvāri uktāni tasmāt vikalpa antaram vaktavyam iti ucyate na guṇa dharma saṃgraha sāmarthāt sattva bahulāḥ ūrdhvasrotasaḥ rajaḥ bahulāḥ arvāksrotasaḥ tamaḥ bahulāḥ tiryaksrotasaḥ mukhya srotasaḥ ca tasmāt anayoḥ abhedena upadeśaḥ āha asura ādi upasaṃkhyānam kartavyam itareṣu anantarbhāvāt abhedena vā upadeśaḥ kāryā na tu daiva mānuṣa tiraḥ ca iti 
[II,363,iv]	ucyate na ukteṣu eva tad saṃgrahāt asurāṇām tāvat aindraḥ eva sthāne antarbhāvaḥ pūrvadeva tvāt pūrvadevāḥ hi asurāḥ kiṃca paryāyeṇa indra tvāt dhanvi prabhṛtīnām paryāyeṇa indra tvam śrūyate tathā yakṣāṇām rakṣassu eka rūpa tvāt kinnara vidyādharāṇām gandharveṣu samāna śīla tvāt pretānām pitṛṣu adhipati sāmānyāt tasmāt tri vikalpaḥ eva bhūta sargaḥ sa ca ayam ūrdhvam sattva viśālaḥ
[II,364,i_II,364,iv]	ūrdhvam iti anena aṣṭau deva sthānāni āha tatra ayam sargam sattva viśālaḥ piśācebhyaḥ rakṣasām rakṣobhyaḥ nāgānām nāgebhyaḥ gandharvāṇām gandharvebhyaḥ pitṝṇām pitṛbhyaḥ tridaśānām tebhyaḥ prajāpatīnām tebhyaḥ api brahmaṇaḥ evam viśāla grahaṇam samarthitam bhavati tamaḥ viśālaḥ tu mūlataḥ sargaḥ mūlataḥ tu sargaḥ tamaḥ viśālaḥ paśubhyaḥ hi mṛgāṇām prakṛṣṭataram tamaḥ mṛgebhyaḥ pakṣiṇām pakṣibhyaḥ sarīsṛpāṇām sarīsṛpebhyaḥ sthāvarāṇām madhye rajaḥ viśālaḥ
[II,364,v_II,364,vi]	devebhyaḥ tiryagbhyaḥ ca avakṛṣṭāsu bhūmiṣu yathā yathā sattva tamasaḥ nirhrāsaḥ tathā tathā rajasaḥ vṛddhiḥ manuṣyāḥ tu ubhayoḥ madhyam iti tatra paramaḥ prakarṣaḥ rajasaḥ arvāk srotasaḥ siddhi rūpa tvāt atyantam kriyā pravṛtta tvāt yathā ca mānuṣeṣu rajaḥ prakarṣaḥ evam brahmaṇaḥ sthāne sattvasya sthāvareṣu tamasaḥ sa khalu ayam brahma ādi stamba paryantaḥ caturdaśa bhedaḥ trivikalpaḥ sattva ādi atiśaya nirhrāsa viṣaya bhāvena yaḥ sargaḥ vyākhyātaḥ 
[II,367,i_II,367,ii]	atra jarā maraṇa kṛtam duḥkham prānoti cetanaḥ puruṣaḥ jarā akṛtam maraṇa kṛtam jarā maraṇa kṛtam tatra jarā akṛtam tāvat yathā balī taraṃgita gātra tvam daṇḍam antareṇa caṅkramaṇa ādiṣu apravṛttiḥ sarva indriyāṇām viṣaya upabhogeṣu asāmarthyam prabala kāsa śvāsa tā sa asra āvila īkṣaṇa tā daśanānām asthira tvam varṇa vikṛtiḥ śaithilyam abhivyāhāra saṃgaḥ mandā smṛtiḥ iti evamādi 
[II,367,iii^1]	maraṇa kṛtam api pṛthivī ādīnām śarīra bhāvena avasthitau sahabhāva pratipakṣatā svabhāva bheda vṛtti saṃgraha panthi vyūha avakāśa dāna ādeḥ upakārasya pracyutiḥ indriya adhiṣṭhāna vikārāt śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhānām satām agrahaṇam asatām ca grahaṇam abhūta ākāram sambhava viparītam vā sarva arthānām grahaṇam tat yathā paurṇamāsyām dakṣiṇatas khaṇḍasya indu maṇḍalasya piśāca ādīnām pāṇḍarasya ca nabhasaḥ ityādi 
[II,367,iii^2]	tathā vāta ādi vaiṣamyāt samupajanita aneka prakāra vyādhiḥ prabhraśyamāna sakala indriya vṛttiḥ srasta aṅgaḥ tāmra pīta asra āvila īkṣaṇaḥ bhrama dāha śvāsa ādi parigama antar marma sandhiḥ jala artham diśaḥ avalokayan sa brahma lokeṣu api lokeṣu trātāram avindan rāga ādi aneka kālāt pakvena ātma graheṇa ātma kārya karaṇa upahyimāṇa buddhiḥ manda mandeṣu api smṛti pralambheṣu dayita janasya ātmanaḥ ca anusmarandaśavidhāt kuṭumba ādyaḥ prabhraśyate saḥ ayam avaśyambhāvī sarva sattvānām prakṛṣṭa udvega kārī ca avyutpannaḥ ca aparihāryaḥ ca aniyata kālaḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ para ma ṛṣya ādibhiḥ andhatāmisra śabdena apadiṣṭaḥ maraṇa kṛtam duḥkham tat ca idam duḥkham pradhāna mahat ahaṃkāra tanmātra indriya bhūta viśeṣa lakṣaṇasya tattva parvaṇaḥ caitanyāsambhavāt puruṣaḥ eva caitanya śakti yogāt upalabhyate tat api samīkṣya uktam ācāryeṇa atra jarā maraṇa kṛtam duḥkham prāpnoti cetanaḥ puruṣaḥ iti 
[II,368,i]	āha janma kṛtasya upasaṃkhyānam yathā eva hi jarā maraṇam ca ātmanaḥ prakṛṣṭa udvega kārakam evam janma api tathā hi ayam mātuḥ udare jarāi upariveṣṭita śarīraḥ amedhya parisnutaḥ vraṇa mātrāyām garbha dhānyām yathā sukha sambhavāt paripītita gātraḥ mātuḥ aśana ādibhiḥ pīḍyamānaḥ garbha āvāse duḥkham anubhūya paścāt saṃvṛtena asthi dvaya vivareṇa nissṛtaḥ mūtra rudhira kalilaiḥ pariṣikta gātraḥ bāhyena vāyunā karaiḥ ca saṃsparśadasibhiḥ iva tudyamānaḥ sva saṃvedyam duḥkham ātmani vartamānam ākhyātum asamarthaḥ sva sukha duḥkha sāmanyāt paratra parikalpita sukha duḥkha buddhibhiḥ dṛḍha gātraiḥ upacita kleśaiḥ ca yātyamānaḥ janma duḥkham anubhavati tasmāt tat api vaktavyam iti 
[II,369,i_II,370,i]	ucyate na avyāpitavāt mānuṣa tiraścām eva janma kṛtam duḥkham bhavati na devānām katham taḍit vilasita vat kṣaṇa mātreṇa śarīra prādurbhāvāt jarā maraṇa kṛtam tu teṣu api na nivartate tasmāt prādhānyāt etat eva upadiṣṭam na itarat iti āha itara grahaṇa aprasaṃgaḥ tulya tvāt na hi deva sthāneṣu jarā maraṇam vā śrūyate tasmāt avyāpi tvāt tayoḥ api agrahaṇa prasaṃgaḥ ucyate na smṛti vacanāt jīryate anayā iti jarā kṣayaḥ iti uktam bhavati sa ca deva bhūmau api bhavati kasmāt evam hi āha rajaḥ viṣaktiḥ aṅgeṣu vaivarṇyam mlāna puṣpa tā patiṣyatām deva lokāt prāṇinām upajāyate 
[II,370,ii^1]	śakra ādīnām vyādhi śravaṇāt śarīra kṣayaḥ evam hi āha tvāṣṭrī iyam sāma bhavati indram kṣāmam api na sarva bhūtāni prasvāpayitum na aśaknuvam stam etena sāmnā tvāṣṭrīyeṇa āsvāpayat iti tathā prajāpateḥ vāyuḥ akṣayīt dakṣa abhiśāpāt ca somasya kṣayaḥ tathā prajāpatiḥ vai somāya rājñe duhitṝra dāt nakṣatrāṇi sa rohiṇyām eva avasat tāni apekṣyamāṇāni punar agacchan tasmāt svān anupeyamānā punar gacchati tāni anvāgacchat tāni punar ayācata tāni asmai na punar adadāt sā bravīt sarveṣu eva samāsata vasā atha te punar dāsyāmi iti sa rohiṇyām eva avasat tasmin anṛte yakṣmaḥ agṛhṇāt candramāḥ vai somaḥ rāja yat rājānam yakṣmaḥ gṛhṇāt tad rājayakṣmasya janma sa tṛṇam iva aśuṣyat sa prajāpatā anāthata saḥ abravīt sarveṣu eva samāvat vasā atha tvā atas mokṣyāmi iti tasmāt candramāḥ sarveṣu nakṣatreṣu samāvat vasati tam vaiśvadevena caruṇā amāvasyām rātrī mayāḥ yajante na enam yakṣmodamuñcat ityādi 
[II,370,ii^2]	tasmāt deva bhūmau api jarā akṛtam duḥkham asti tathā maraṇa kṛtam bhūmi antara gamanāt tatra utpannānām yayātiḥ udāharaṇam yathā gopatha brāhmaṇam devānām ha vā pañcadaśa śatāni āsan tāni brahma kilbiṣāt akṣīyanta tatas trayastriṃśat eva āsata tat etat ṛca api uktam sodaryāṇām pañcadaśānām śatānām trayastriṃśat udaśiṣyanta devāḥ śeṣāḥ prāsīyanta iti śveta araṇye ca antakasya rudreṇa kṛtam duḥkham asti iti udāharaṇa mātrāt vā athavā udāharaṇa mātram eva duḥkhānām ādi śabda lopaḥ vā vaktavyaḥ jarā maraṇa kṛtam eva udāharaṇa tvena abhipretam na punar duḥkha antaram kasmāt tatra api hi ādi śabda lopaḥ udāharaṇa mātra tvāt śaktyā parikalpayitum idam iti ucyate na sarva duḥkha āspada tvāt sarveṣām hi duḥkhānām āspadam jarā maraṇa kṛtam sādhāraṇam katham tad bandhu mitrāṇām api udvega hetu tvāt na tu janma kṛtam sambandhinām praharṣa nimitta tvāt yatas ca brahma ādau stamba paryante jagati jarā maraṇa kṛtam duḥkham na kaścid ativartate 
[II,371,i_II,371,iii]	liṅgasya vinivṛtteḥ tasmāt duḥkham samāsena sukhaleśasya tad vyāpta tvāt yāvat idam liṅgam na nivartate tāvat avaśyam duḥkhena bhavitavyam paryāyeṇa saṃskārasya sāmarthyāt loka antara upapatteḥ tathā ca āha sukham ca duḥkham ca hi saṃśayam vāreṇa ayam sevate tatra tatra kathampunar duḥkhena vyāptam sukham iti ced ābrahmaṇaḥ aśuddhyā atiśaya upapatteḥ tasyāḥ ca duḥkha mūla tvāt prajāpateḥ akṣi roga śravaṇāt indrasya kāma upatāpāt gautama paribhāvāt rambhāyāḥ ca abhiśāpāt pāṣāṇa bhāva upapatteḥ nāgānām sarpa satra āyāsāt vaiśravaṇasya yaska abhiśāpāt hastibhāva upapattiḥ jaratkāraḥ pitṝṇām ca garte avalambanāt piśācānām mantra oṣadhi maṅgala prayogaiḥ udvāsanāt mānuṣa tiraścām pratyakṣatas eva prāyeṇa duḥkha āspada tvāt tasmāt na asti saṃsāre kaścid pradeśaḥ yatra saha liṅgena ātmānam duḥkham na avāpnuyāt iti atas evam prayatitavyam yena liṅgasya eva atyanta ucchedaḥ tatas hi sarva duḥkhānām atyanta upaśamaḥ samāsa grahaṇam tu sukha mohayoḥ avakāśa dāna artham anyathā saṃsāre tayoḥ abhāvaḥ eva abhyupagataḥ syāt 
[II,374,i_II,374,ii^1]	evam yathāvat sargam upākhyāya upasaṃharan āha iti eṣa prakṛti vikṛtaḥ pravartate tattva bhūta bhāva ākhyaḥ prati puruṣa vimokṣa artham sva arthaḥ iva para arthe ārambhaḥ iti karaṇena sarga samāptim dyotayati eṣaḥ iti uktam api pratyāmnāya artham punar apekṣate prakṛtyā kṛtaḥ prakṛti kṛtaḥ anena vākya parisamāpti artham vīta avītābhyām siddham pradhāna astitvam aṇu ādi pratiṣedham ca apekṣate prakṛti kṛtaḥ eva na aṇu ādi kṛtaḥ pravartate iti kriyā prabandham āha pravṛttaḥ na pravartsyati kim tarhi pravartate eva anantānām śarīra ādi bhāvena paraspara anugraheṇa ca na iyam kriyā kadācid api bhūta bhaviṣyat rūpā bhavati kintarhi vartamāna rūpā yathā vahanti nadyaḥ tiṣṭhanti parvatāḥ iti tattva bhūta bhāva ākhyaḥ iti uktānām nigama artham pratyāmnāyam karoti tattva ākhyaḥ mahat ādibhiḥ bhāva ākhyaḥ vyoma ādiḥ puruṣam puruṣam prati vimokṣaḥ prati puruṣa vimokṣaḥ 
[II,374,ii^2]	tad artham prati puruṣa vimokṣa artham sarva puruṣa adhikāra nibaddhāyāḥ sarva śakteḥ nirāka aṃkṣīkaraṇa artham iti arthaḥ sva arthaḥ iva para arthe ārambhaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvena tatra kāryasya tāvat śabda ādeḥ sva arthaḥ iva indriyāṇām viṣaya bhāvaḥ indriyāṇām aprāpta viṣayāṇām laulyam adhiṣṭhāna vikāra anumeyam sva artham iva karaṇānām ca saṃkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāyānām viṣaya dvāri bhāva upagamanam manaḥ prabhṛtīnām ca sva pravṛtti viṣaya tvam manaḥ ahaṃkārayoḥ ca buddhau sva pravṛtti upasaṃhāraḥ buddheḥ ca śānta ghora mūḍha tvam vyavasāya kartṛ tvam ca sattara jaḥ tamasām ca prakāśa pravṛtti niyama lakṣaṇaiḥ dharmaiḥ paraspara upakāri tvam na ca eṣa sva arthaḥ sarvasya asya ācaitanyāt kim tarhi para arthaḥ eva ayam ārambhaḥ saṃghāta tvāt iti 
[II,376,i]	āha yat uktam prati puruṣa vimokṣa artham ayam ārambhaḥ iti tat ayuktam ācārya vipratipatteḥ prati puruṣam anyat pradhānam śarīra ādi artham karoti teṣām ca māhātmya śarīra pradhānam yadā pravartate tadā itarāṇi api tad nivṛttau ca teṣām api nivṛttiḥ iti paurikaḥ sāṃkhya ācāryaḥ manyate tad katham apratiṣidhya ekā prakṛtiḥ abhyupagamyate iti 
[II,376,ii^1]	ucyate na pramāṇa abhāvāt na tāvat pratyakṣataḥ eva tat śakyam niścetum pradhānānām atīndriya tvāt liṅgam ca asandigdham na asti āptāḥ ca naḥ na abhidadhurataḥ manyāmahe na etat evam iti kiṃca ekena artha parisamāpteḥ aparimita tvāt etat ekam pradhāna malam sarva puruṣa śarīra utpādanāya tasmāt anya parikalpanā narthakyam parimitam iti ced atha matam parimitam pradhānam iti na uccheda prasaṃgāt evam api tasya ucchedaḥ prāptaḥ kṣīra vat tathā ca saṃsāra uccheda prasaṃgaḥ kim ca anavasthā prasaṃgāt ekasya īśvarasya yoginaḥ vā icchā yogāt aneka śarīra tvam 
[II,376,ii^2]	tad parimitāt ayuktam pratiśarīram vā pradhāna parikalpane pradhāna anavasthā bhavati parimita śarīra kāraṇa tva abhyupagamāt anya parikalpanā narthakyam tatas ca pradhāna eka tvam eva tasmāt ayuktam prati puruṣam pradhānāni iti yat tu uktam māhātmya śarīra pradhāna pravṛttau itareṣām pravṛtiḥ tad nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ iti atra brūmaḥ na atiśaya abhāvāt yathā kṣetrajñānām niratiśaya tvāt itaretarā pravartaka tvam evam eṣām api sa atiśaya tve vā pradhāna anupapatti prasaṃgaḥ vaiṣamyāt tasmāt yuktam prati puruṣa vimokṣa artham ekā prakṛtiḥ pravartate iti 
[II,379,i_II,379,iii]	āha tad anupapattiḥ ācetanyāt iha acetanānām ghaṭa ādīnām uddiśya pravṛttiḥ adṛṣṭā sā ced iyam acetanā prakṛtiḥ asyāḥ api uddiśya puruṣa artham pravṛttiḥ na upapadyate bhavati ced caitanyam tarhi prāptam asya a tatra yat uktam prati puruṣa vimokṣa artha prakṛteḥ pravṛttiḥ iti etat ayuktam iti ucyate na dṛṣṭānta upapatteḥ vatsa vivṛddhi nimittam kṣīrasya yathā pravṛttiḥ ajñasya puruṣa vimokṣa nimittam tathā pravṛttiḥ pradhānasya 
[II,379,iv]	yathā kṣīram acetanam vatsa vivṛddhim uddiśya pravartate evam pradhānam api puruṣa vimokṣam uddiśya pravartate na ca asya caitanyam syāt sādhya tvāt ayuktam iti ced syāt matam sādhyam etat kim kṣīrasya uddiśya vatsa vivṛddhim pravṛttiḥ atha na iti tasmāt udāharaṇam sādhya tvāt ayuktam iti etat ca ayuktam kasmāt tad abhāve abhāvāt tad bhāve ca bhāvāt yatra na asti vatsa vivṛddhiḥ tatra na kṣīrasya pravṛttiḥ upalabdhā yatra asti tatra upalabdhā yadi asmin sati bhavati tasya tad arthā pravṛttiḥ dṛṣṭā tat yathā ghaṭe kumbhakārasya sa ca ayam īdṛśaḥ asmākam uddeśaḥ abhipretaḥ yat uta tādarthyam tasmāt na asti udāharaṇa sādhya tvam iti 
[II,380,i]	asadbhāva abhidhānāt sat kārya virodhaḥ iti ced na vyakti paryāya tvāt vyakti paryāyaḥ hi tat iti śāstra loka prāmāṇyāt śāstram tāvat sattā mātraḥ mahān vyakti mātraḥ iti arthaḥ loke api na asti asmin kūpe salilam iti ucyate na kvacid api kūpe salilam na asti abhivyaktam na tat bhavati tasmāt na satkārya virodhaḥ 
[II,380,ii]	adṛṣṭa preraṇa tvāt asiddhiḥ iti ced atha matam dharma adharma preritam kṣīram pravartate na vatsa vivṛddhi artham iti tat api ayuktam kasmāt doṣa sāmyāt dharma adharmau acetanau vivṛddhi kāle kṣīram pravartayataḥ tad avasāne ca nivartayataḥ tasamāt ittham api parikalpyamāne samānaḥ doṣaḥ īśvara preraṇāt iti ced syāt matam īśvaraḥ tatra kṣīram pravartayate vatsa artham na svayam iti tat ayuktam kasmāt pratiṣedhāt prāk pratiṣiddham īśvara karma tasmāt idam api ayuktam evam ced avasthitaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ vārṣa gaṇānām tu yathā strī puṃśarīrāṇām acetanānām uddiśya itaretaram pravṛttiḥ tathā pradhānasya iti ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
[II,381,i_II,382,i]	āha katham avagamyate tādarthyāt utpannena vyaktena puruṣasya sambandhaḥ na punar sānnidhya mātrāt bhikṣu vat iti ucyate na anapavarga prasaṃgāt sānnidhya mātrāt puruṣa upabhogam abhyupagacchataḥ na apavarga prasaṃgaḥ syāt nityasānnidhyāt tasmāt ayuktam etat apravartayitāram prati kārya kāraṇānām pravṛttiḥ ayuktā iti ced syāt matam apravartayitā kṛṣṇa ādīnām bhikṣu ḥ atas na teṣām api tam prati pravṛttiḥ evam apravartayitā kārya karaṇānām puruṣaḥ tasmāt teṣām api tam prati pravṛttiḥ ayuktā iti etat api atas eva anaikāntikam vatsaḥ hi kṣīrasya apravartayitā atha ca tam prati tasya pravṛttiḥ tasmāt yuktam eta puruṣa vimokṣa arthā prakṛtteḥ pravṛttiḥ na caitanya prasaṃgaḥ iti 
[II,384,i_II,384,ii]	āha na apravṛtti prasaṃgāt yadi pradhānasya puruṣa kaivalya arthā pravṛttiḥ tena tad abhāve kaivalyam siddham eva iti apravṛtti prasaṃgaḥ atha kevale puruṣe pradhānam pravartate na tarhi asya tad arthā pravṛttiḥ iti autsukya nivṛtti artham yathā kriyāsu pravartate lokaḥ puruṣasya vimokṣa artham pravartate tadvat avyaktam 
[II,384,iii]	prāk eva etat apadiṣṭam yathā dṛśya darśana śakti yukta tvāt anyatara abhāve ca tayoḥ ānarthakyāt pradhāna puruṣayoḥ itaretara sambandham pratyautsukyam dṛṣṭā ca uparama arthā api lokasya autsukya nivṛtti arthā pravṛttiḥ tathā pradhānasya api uparama arthā pravṛttiḥ atha dṛśya darśana śaktyā urautsukya nivṛtti artham pravartate iti ekatra kṛtārtha tvāt itareṣu apravṛtti prasaṃgaḥ iti ced syāt etat pradhānam ekasya puruṣasya ātmānam prakāśya uparamede dṛśya darśana śaktayā uḥ autsukya nivṛttiḥ bhaviṣyati 
[II,386,i_II,386,ii]	apravṛttiḥ ca iti etat api na upapannam kasmāt dṛṣṭānta antara sāmarthyāt tat yathā kim ucyate raṅgasya darśayitvā nivartate nartakī yathā nṛtyāt puruṣasya tathā ātmānam prakāśya vinivartate prakṛtiḥ tatra nānā varṇa svabhāva vijñānānām prekṣā arthinām puruṣāṇām saṃghātaḥ raṅgaḥ iti ucyate nartakyāḥ ca tad ārādhanā nṛtti kriyā aneka puruṣa arthā yadi vā atra kaścid brūyāt nṛtta ācāryeṇa kuśīlavaiḥ vā dṛṣṭā eva iyam kasmāt na nivartate katham akṛtārtha tvāt evam sarva puruṣāṇām kārya kāraṇa sambandhena autsukyavatām nirāka aṃkṣīkaraṇa artham pravṛttā prakṛtiḥ katham ekasya puruṣasya autsukya nivṛttau kṛtārthā syāt tasmāt na ekasya puruṣasya ātmānam prakāśya prakṛteḥ nivṛttiḥ yuktā iti atra ca 
[II,388,i]	 kārya kāraṇa kriyā sākṣī puruṣaḥ tasmāt ye bhautikāḥ śiraḥ pāṇi ādayaḥ ye ca ahaṃkārikāḥ śravaṇa ādayaḥ vacana ādayaḥ saṃkalpa abhimāna adhyavasāyāḥ ca te lakṣaṇa viparyayāt na aham na aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ tat etat evam tattvānām abhyāsa ekāgra manasaḥ yateḥ punar punar abhyāsāt ekasya api asmitā rūpasya parikalpita viṣaya bheda pratiṣedha mukhena na asmi na me na aham iti apariśeṣam 
[II,388,ii_II,389,iii]	āprakṛteḥ pratipakṣa grahaṇāt aviparyayāt pañca srotasaḥ asya avidyā parvaṇaḥ nivṛtteḥ śāntam dhruvam sakala bhāva anubandha pratipakṣa bhūtam dharma ādi āpyāyitasya buddhi tattvasya asan digdham aviparītam viśuddham kevalam utpadyate jñānam āha viśuddham kevalam anyatara anabhidhānam artha abhedāt yat eva viśuddham tat eva kevalam iti artha abhedāt anyatarat śakyam avaktum iti ucyate guṇa antara rūpa nivṛtti hetu tvāt rajaḥ tamaḥ dharmāṇām tāvat grahaṇāt śuddham saṃśaya viparyaya vyatiriktam ca kevalam kṣetrajña parijñāne apūrvam eva iti āha tad sama kālam eva śarīrasya pātaḥ prāpnoti sati dha vasthānena ajñāna hetukam śarīram iti 
[II,390,i_II,390,iii]	ucyate ajñāna hetukam śarīram atha ca ayam nānā tva darśī dharma ādīnām akāraṇa prāptau tiṣṭhati saṃskāra vaśāt cakra bhrama vat dhṛta śarīraḥ ya śarīra antara upārjitāḥ dharma ādayaḥ na tāvat kāraṇam buddhi mupasaṃprāptā akṛtārtha tvāt buddhiḥ ca pradhānam tadā tiṣṭhati ayam nānā tva darśī tasya saṃskārasya sāmarthyāt kaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ cakra bhrama vat dhṛta śarīraḥ tat yathā kumbhakāra prayatna viśiṣṭena daṇḍena ghaṭa ādi niṣpatti yogya kriyā cakrasya bhramaḥ tena tulyam cakra bhrama vat yathā cakra bhramaṇam ghaṭa artham niṣpanne ghaṭa ādi niṣpatti yogya kriyā cakrasya bhramaḥ tena tulyam cakra bhrama vat yathā cakra bhramaṇam ghaṭa artham niṣpanne ghaṭe pūrva saṃskāra anurodhāt na nivartate na ca tadā nivṛttam iti kṛtvā saṃskāra kṣaye api avatiṣṭhate evam samyak darśana artham śarīram samyak jñāna adhigame api na nivartate pūrva saṃskāra vaśāt na ca tadā nivṛttam iti kṛtvā saṃskāra kṣaye api avasthāpyate iti 
[II,392,i_II,392,ii]	yadā tu saṃskāra kṣaye tad nimittasya śarīrasya bhedaḥ atas prāpte śarīra bhede dharma adharmau kṛtārthau kāraṇe buddhi lakṣaṇe layam gacchataḥ yaḥ ca asya bhūta avayavaḥ śarīra ārambhakaḥ sa sarva bhūteṣu bhūtāni tanmātreṣu indriyāṇi tanmātrāṇi ca ahaṃkāre ahaṃkāraḥ buddhau buddhiḥ avyakte sā iyam tattva ānupūrvī tad artha pradhānāt utpannā parisamāpte punar pradhāne pralayam gacchati iti pradhānam api artha vaśāt eva asya śarīrāṇi teṣu teṣu jāti antara parivarteṣu karoti sa cāryaḥ caritārthaḥ 
[II,392,iii_II,392,v]	atas caritārtha tvāt pradhāna vinivṛttau atīndriyam asaṃvedya laghu sarvatra sannihitam praśastam anirmitam viśuddham akṣayam niratiśayam ekāntam ātyantikam abhayam kaivalyam āpnoti etat ca avasthānam bauddhaiḥ nirupadhi śeṣa nirvāṇa lakṣaṇam apavargaḥ vyākhyātaḥ etat param brahmam dhruvam amalam abhayam atra sarveṣām guṇa dharmāṇām pratipralayaḥ etat prāpya sarva āyāsaiḥ sarva bandhanaiḥ anādi kāla pravṛtta rāga dveṣa viyuktaḥ muktaḥ bhavati etad artham brāhmaṇāḥ dayitaputra dāra dhana sambandham apahāya guru śuśrūṣā parāḥ śarīram araṇyeṣu yātayanti katham nāma ekāntikam ātyantikam ca kaivalyam syāt iti yatra eva utthānam śāstrasya tatra eva upasaṃhāraḥ ācāryeṇa kṛtaḥ 
[II,394,i_II,394,iv]	āha kimartham punar idam śāstram kena vā pūrvam prakāśitam iti ucyate yat uktam kimartham iti puruṣa artha artham idam katham nāma ajñāna vaśāt tad saṃskāra upanipatitānām prāṇinām apavargaḥ syāt iti evam artham idam śāstram vyākhyātam yat tu uktam kena iti ucyate guhyam parama ṛṣiṇā samākhyātam 
[II,394,v_II,395,i]	guhyam iti gūhanīyam rahasyam akṛtātmanām yama niyameṣu anavasthitānām ādarāt api anadhyeyam parama ṛṣiḥ bhagavān sāṃsiddhikaiḥ dharma jñāna vairāgya aiśvaryaiḥ āviṣṭa piṇḍaḥ viśva agrajaḥ kapila muniḥ tena kapila muninā samākhyātam samyak ākhyātam cira abhyastasya vidyā srotasaḥ nirvacana sāmarthyāt syāt etat katham idam guhyam iti ucyate katham vedam guhyam na syāt 
[II,395,ii_II,395,iii]	bhava agra utpannaiḥ api sanaka sanātana sanandana sanatkumāra prabhṛtibhiḥ anityānām sthiti utpatti pralayāḥ cintyante ca yatra bhūtānām tatra sthitiḥ tāvat rūpa pravṛtti phala nirdeśena utpattiḥ api prakṛteḥ mahān iti ādiḥ pralayaḥ api avibhāgāt vaiśvarūpyasya iti vacanāt autsukya anuparamāt prakṛti puruṣayoḥ sthitiḥ utpattiḥ dṛśya darśana śaktayoḥ sa apekṣa tvāt tathā ca uktam puruṣasya darśana arthaḥ kaivalya arthaḥ tathā pradhānasya paṅgu andhavat ubhayoḥ api saṃyogaḥ tad kṛtaḥ sargaḥ iti
[II,395,iv_II,396,i]	pralayaḥ prāpte śarīra bhede caritārtha tvāt pradhāna vinivṛttau iti athavā sthiti kṣaṇa bhaṅga pratiṣedhāt kāla antareṣu asya anāśāt utpattiḥ vipariṇāma anna abhūta prādurbhāvāt akasmāt asambhavāt pralayaḥ api nimitta antarāt svābhāvyāt eva bhūtānām api vyaktānām niṣpattimatām iti yāvat evam ca mahat ādayaḥ api parigṛhītāḥ iti āha puruṣa ādayaḥ tarhi parityaktāḥ katham vā bhūta śabdaḥ iti 
[II,396,ii]	ucyate vitatha pratiṣedha artha tvāt yāvat kiṃcid avitatham bhūtam tasya sarvasya iha sthiti ādayaḥ ucyante iti utpatti vināśa pratiṣedha aviśeṣāt evam api puruṣa ādīnām utpatti pralayau api prāpnutaḥ kim kāraṇam aviśeṣāt iti ucyate sambhavataḥ viśeṣaṇam bhavati tatra sthitiḥ eva puruṣa ādīnām itareṣām tu sthiti utpatti pralayāḥ iti vijñāsyāmaḥ 
[II,397,i_II,397,iii]	āha kasmai punar idam śāstram parama ṛṣiṇā prakāśitam iti ucyate etat pravitram agryam muniḥ āsuraye anukampayā pradadau tatra pavitram pāvanāt agryam sarva duḥkha kṣapaṇa samartha tvāt pavitra antarāṇi punar eka deśam kṣālayanti adhamarṣaṇa gaṅgā ādīni tasmāt idam eva agryam muniḥ āsuraye anukampayā pradadau 
[II,397,iv]	āha sampradānasya akasmika tvam dharma ādi nimitta anupapatteḥ na tāvat parama ṛṣeḥ dharma artham śāstra pradānam upapadyate phalena anabhiṣvaṅgāt na artha kāma artham śiṣyāṇām anāyāsa prasaṃgāt na mokṣa artham sāṃsiddhikena eva jñānena tad prāpteḥ tasmāt viparīta artha asambhavāt pariśeṣāt akasmāt ācāryaḥ śāstra nidhānam pradadau iti 
[II,398,i]	ucyate na akasmāt kim tarhi anukampayā pradadau ādhyātmika ādhidaivika ādhibhautikaiḥ duḥkhaiḥ pīḍyamānam āsurim upalabhya sva ātmani ca jñāna sāmarthyāt sati kārya kāraṇa samprayoge duḥkhānām apravṛttim parijñāya śiṣya guṇān ca katham nāma yathā mama sukha duḥkheṣu jñāna upanipātāt sāmyam evam āsureḥ api syāt tad dvāreṇa ani eṣām api puruṣāṇām evam anukampayā bhagavān parama ṛṣiḥ śāstram ākhyātavān 
[II,398,ii_II,398,iv]	yathā ca parama ṛṣiḥ āsuraye tathā āsuriḥ api daśamāya kumārāya bhagavat pañcaśikhāya tena ca bahudhā kṛtam tantram bahubhyaḥ janaka vaśiṣṭha ādibhyaḥ samākhyātam asya tu śāstrasya bhagavataḥ agre pravṛtta tvāt na śāstra antara vat vaṃśaḥ śakyaḥ varṣa śata sahasraiḥ api ākhyātum 
[II,400,i_II,400,vi]	saṃkṣepeṇa tu dvau a hārīta vādhalikaiḥ āta paurika āṛṣabha īśvara pañca adhikaraṇa patañjali vārṣa gaṇya kauṇḍinya mūka ādika śiṣya paramparayā āgatam bhagavān īśvara kṛṣṇaḥ ca sāhāyakam śāstram pūrva ācārya sūtra prabandhe gurulāghava manādriyamāṇaḥ paurastyāni ākhyānavyā na garbham atipramādam dadāti iti grantha bhūyastvam upajāyate tad ced ānīntanaiḥ prāṇibhiḥ alpa tvāt āyuṣaḥ granthataḥ eva na sūpa pādam kim punar śravaṇa prayogābhyām āha ca caturbhiḥ prakāraiḥ vidyā su upa yuktā bhavati āgama kālena svādhyāya kālena prayoga kālena ca tatra ca asya āgamana kālena eva āyuḥ paryupayuktam syāt tatas ca śāstra ānarthakyam iti asya manda dhiyām api āśu grahaṇa dhāraṇa prayoga sampatsyāt iti ṣaṣṭi tantrāt upākhyāna gāthā vyavahitāni vākyāni ekatas upamṛdya śiṣya anukampā artham yāvat īśvara kṛṣṇena ca etat āryābhiḥ saptatyā saṃkṣiptam ārya matinā sarva sattva hita pravṛttena samyak vijñāya siddhāntam katham ca asya samyak siddhānta vijñānasya api aneka grantha śata sahasra ākhyeyam sāṃkhya padārtham sa tattvam akhaṇḍam ācāryāṇām saptatyā saṃkṣiptavān 
[II,402,i_II,402,ii]	āha ca saptatyām kila ye arthāḥ te arthāḥ kṛtsnasya ṣaṣṭitantrasya ākhyāyikā virahitāḥ para vāda vivarjitāḥ ca api yatas ca nārāyaṇam anujanaka vaśiṣṭhadvaipāyana pravṛttibhiḥ ācāryaiḥ pradhāna puruṣa ādayaḥ padārthāḥ parigṛhītāḥ ca upadiṣṭāḥ ca praśastāḥ ca atas svabhāvataḥ prasiddham aiśvaryasya phalatas ṛddhyā ārya mārgam alaṃkartum iti bhagavat īśvara kṛṣṇena padārtha svarūpa nirūpaṇa nipuṇa sāra matinā parama ṛṣya ādi yathā ukta āgamena pramāṇa trayam puraskṛtya tarka dṛśā vicāraḥ kṛtaḥ na ca asya mūla kanaka piṇḍasya iva su alpam api doṣa jātam asti iti 
[II,402,iii]	āha ca ajñāna dhvānta śānti artham ṛṣi candramasaḥ cyutā malinaiḥ tīrtha jaladaiḥ chādyate jñānacandrikā iti sadbhiḥ asambhrāntaiḥ kudṛṣṭi timira apahā prakāśikā iyam sargasya dhāryatām yuktidīpikā sphuṭa abhidheyā madhurā api bhāratī manīṣiṇaḥ na upakhalam virājate kṛśa anugarbha api abhitas hima āgame kaduṣṇa tām yāti divākara dyutiḥ nayanti santaḥ ca yatas sva śaktitaḥ guṇam pareṣām tanum api udāra tām iti prayātu eṣa mama śramaḥ satām vicāraṇa anugraha mātra pātra tām >
